Chapter 1580

Though the Prosperous Yellow Immortal Realm did not naturally give birth to Dao principles related to 'Intercepted Dao of Life,' Li Fan, through the Dao Refining Medicine King Scripture, imbued it with this ability by using 'Loquat' as medicine.

The modification at the Great Dao level was almost akin to innate creation. In the beginning, there might have been some awkwardness. But as time gradually passed, it would naturally become a part of the Prosperous Yellow Immortal Realm's circulating Heavenly Dao.

"Using Dao as medicine, refining Dao with medicine. The Holy Emperor Tai Wei's method bears some resemblance to Sun Pianmiao's Dao Refining Medicine King Scripture. However, Sun Pianmiao considers it the foundation of his cultivation, whereas in the eyes of Holy Emperor Tai Wei, the myriad medicinal herbs in his medicinal garden are merely tools. The foundation of the Holy Emperor's Dao path is his supreme Holy Dynasty spanning across Mountains and Seas..."

Compared to the grand Tai Wei Holy Dynasty, the Prosperous Yellow Immortal Realm crafted by Li Fan was utterly insignificant.

However, Li Fan did not consider himself crude.

"Though Prosperous Yellow is small, it holds infinite possibilities. The Holy Dynasty is vast, but its Dao path is already set."

"To be on par with Mountains and Seas, one will inevitably clash with many powerful beings in the Great World of the Other Shore. Whether one can truly take that final step is also unknown. As for my Prosperous Yellow Immortal Realm..."

Li Fan extended his palm, examining a small black dot that had quietly appeared in his palm.

It was a Dao-One Worm, which had absorbed and assimilated some of the power of Ink Slaughter.

Ink Slaughter had successfully refined the Loquat, and to prevent detection, the Dao-One Worm's covert erosion had temporarily halted.

Despite absorbing for only just over thirty days, the Dao-One Worms had undergone earth-shattering changes internally compared to before.

The most significant change, reaching a qualitative transformation, was the method by which Dao-One Worms devoured external objects. Before emulating Ink Slaughter, their method of consumption still bore the characteristics of 'biological' feeding. It was like a worm chewing, or a cultivator absorbing and refining. But after imitating Ink Slaughter, the Dao-One Worms' method of consumption had leaped to being akin to 'annihilation.'

Their feeding efficiency and assimilation capacity had increased by dozens of times.

Furthermore, due to the Dao-One Worms' inherent characteristic of constant evolution, unlike Ink Slaughter whose abilities were largely fixed and required external stimulation for further progress, the erosion capabilities of the Dao-One Worms were rapidly advancing by leaps and bounds.

"The current swarm of Dao-One Worms can almost be considered close kin to Ink Slaughter."

"Tai Yi and Eternal power provided an upgrade to Ink Slaughter, so it should similarly be effective for the Dao-One Worms." With this thought, Li Fan threw the 'Primordial Beginning of Mountains and Seas Chapter' and the Eternal power consolidated outer wear towards the Dao-One Worm swarm.

Countless black dots swarmed over, slowly engulfing both items.

Unlike Ink Slaughter, which was instantly enhanced, the metamorphosis of the Dao-One Worms was slow and steady.

Calling them 'worms' was, in reality, not related to 'worms' in the true sense. The spirits and monsters within the Prosperous Yellow Immortal Realm did not possess life; they were manifestations of the world's power. It was merely Li Fan's habitual nomenclature.

The current essence of the Dao-One Worm swarm was another form of power, extremely similar in nature to Ink Slaughter, cultivated within the Prosperous Yellow Immortal Realm as its container. Because they were born within the Prosperous Yellow Immortal Realm, they were under the control of Li Fan, the Father and Mother of Prosperous Yellow.

"The Dao-One Worms have not yet fully assimilated the inner workings of Ink Slaughter."

"We still need to find something for Ink Slaughter to do, to distract its attention as much as possible."

Within the Prosperous Yellow Immortal Realm, and even within the primordial possibility, the newly born Ink Slaughter was almost unrivaled, with few enemies. To find a suitable opponent, one had to look beyond the primordial possibility.

However, at the current level of the Prosperous Yellow Immortal Realm, it was insufficient to support Li Fan in safely traversing Mountains and Seas. Therefore, Li Fan first thought of the fishing pond.

Or rather, the Sea of Stars fishery.

However, after careful consideration, Li Fan ultimately decided not to covy the fishing pond for now.

"After all, it can connect to Mountains and Seas, and the strength of the Fishing Immortal behind the fishing pond is not trivial. Just as I could perceive the scene of the Tai Wei Holy Dynasty through Loquat, and be seen by Holy Emperor Tai Wei, when I look at or use the fishing pond, it is destined to be perceived by that Fishing Immortal."

"In the short term, I might still be able to use 'Illusion is True' for concealment. But in the long run, the risk of exposure will increase exponentially. What I need is a method to stably capture items from beyond the primordial..."

Li Fan then thought of the salvage method he had seen in the Guangwu Star Sea in his previous life.

By distributing Heavenly Pillars with different load-bearing capacities, they deliberately created weak points to attract the descent of Dao Annihilation, forming annihilation basins, in the hope that floating objects within the Dao Annihilation would be attracted.

In the 'True Return Without Interruption' reincarnation, Li Fan had successfully recreated this method.

"It's just that the salvage yields are too unstable. If luck is bad, even after a hundred years, one might gain nothing, and it would increase the risk of being devoured by Dao Annihilation for no reason."

"Fortunately, the Guangwu Star Sea has already paved the way for me. Besides the projections of the Dao Chronicle and transcendent remnants, there should be many other original items there..."

"When the first Harmonizer is born in the Prosperous Yellow Immortal Realm, and True Immortals are listed on the Investiture of the Gods, the Prosperous Yellow Expedition can officially commence."

Thinking this, Li Fan's thoughts instantly focused on Xuanyuan Tuo.

This Heavenly Transmission Venerable, almost forgotten by everyone in the Prosperous Yellow Immortal Realm, had always captured Li Fan's attention.

Knowing that before the great changes in the Prosperous Yellow heavens and earth, Transmission had already been at the Harmonization realm. With the sublimation of Prosperous Yellow and its transformation into an Immortal Realm, the Heavenly Pillar within it, 'Golden Executive,' had long been tens of thousands of times stronger than before.

Yet, Transmission remained at his past strength.

Theoretically, the moment Li Fan unsealed his confinement, Transmission should have been torn apart by the surging power within him.

But now, not only had Transmission not perished, but he had also managed to control the Golden Executive, which had transformed with the Prosperous Yellow Realm, as if using an ounce of force to move a thousand pounds.

Though, in Li Fan's view, it was at the limit, as if led by countless threads, and any slight movement of the Golden Executive risked breaking the control.

However, such control undeniably existed.

In a sense, Transmission was now the first Harmonizer in the Prosperous Yellow Immortal Realm.

"But this is only in his current state of tranquility."

"Once his understanding of Dao is disrupted, Transmission will instantly turn to dust. This is also why he has always remained in seclusion, motionless."

Under the condition of potentially perishing at any moment, Transmission not only did not panic, but instead used this special 'Harmonization' realm as a stepping stone to seek the true method of Harmonization.

"This is truly a case of 'succeed or be destroyed.' Facing such immense pressure, he can still treat it with indifference," Li Fan silently admired.

Truly worthy of being the Transmission Heavenly Venerable who would dominate the Prosperous Yellow for ten thousand years in later generations.

"Only certify Harmonization, not Longevity."

This was the most profound thought Li Fan could discern lingering in Transmission's heart.

And it was precisely by this belief as guidance that Transmission was able to maintain control over the Golden Executive through the faint connection they had in the past.

Li Fan had a premonition that Transmission was currently entangled in some internal conflict.

After a deep investigation, Li Fan finally understood the source of Transmission's hesitation.

"So, he already had a method for achieving stable Harmonization in his heart. But if he were to adopt this method, he would henceforth be limited to Harmonization within Prosperous Yellow, and would never be able to surpass the Heavens of Prosperous Yellow again. The previous new method, which defied the principles of heaven and earth and only allowed him to control the affairs of heaven and earth, would no longer be possible..." Understanding Transmission's thoughts, Li Fan couldn't help but let out a wry smile.

"He had already realized this point, yet he still hesitated as he was about to take the final step."

"It seems Transmission, like Tianyang, is unwilling to be inferior to others!"

However, the path Transmission envisioned was destined to conflict with Li Fan, the Father and Mother of Prosperous Yellow. How could Li Fan cede the Prosperous Yellow Immortal Realm?

"If you truly choose that path, then do not blame me for being ruthless."

"Of course, if you can let go of your obsessions and willingly become my lackey..."

"Then I will not be stingy and will even lend you a hand." Li Fan smiled faintly.

As if sensing Li Fan's thoughts, Xuanyuan Tuo, who had been sitting for a long time, finally made up his mind.

Letting go of his internal obsessions, he let out a long sigh, and his entire demeanor relaxed.

He opened his eyes and slowly stood up.

Because of his movement, the immensely vast Heavenly Pillar within him, far exceeding his limit of endurance, the 'Golden Executive,' instantly showed signs of losing control and exploding.

However, all anomalies were inexplicably halted by the two sentences Transmission softly chanted.

"Transform the Heavenly Pillar, merge with Dao with one's body;"

"Solidify the principles of heaven and earth, to certify Longevity!"

With just these two sentences, they resounded like thunderclaps throughout the heavens and earth, growing louder and louder, echoing relentlessly within the Prosperous Yellow heavens and earth.

The Heavenly Pillar, Golden Executive, no longer showed signs of exploding out of control.

Because Transmission, or rather Xuanyuan Tuo, had now transformed into It!

Donning a golden, radiant outer garment, and the previously faceless Heavenly Pillar, Golden Executive, gradually revealed Transmission's appearance on its face.

A moment later, Transmission took a step towards the Golden Executive ahead.

The two then merged into one!

Before taking that final step, a trace of imperceptible melancholy flashed in Xuanyuan Tuo's eyes. But it lasted only for a fleeting moment before being completely suppressed.

Since a decision had been made, there would be no regrets!

A ray of golden light shot up into the sky.

Reaching directly into the highest heavens.

Passing through the Investiture of the Gods in the heavens, it reached the four heavenly gates.

From the four heavenly gates, rays of light each shot out, converging on Xuanyuan Tuo.

The barrier between the heavens beyond the heavens and the ground was pierced by this infinitely brilliant light. All beings on the surface could see everything happening at the four heavenly gates.

Hum hum hum...

Roars from Mountains and Seas came from beyond the heavenly gates.

The gates opened, and infinite immortal power, like divine bestowment, cascaded down.

"This is..."

"Immortal?"

Xuanyuan Tuo looked at the vast landscape of Mountains and Seas that appeared before him, and was momentarily lost in thought.

For some reason, despite taking that step that countless people dreamed of, he did not feel much excitement.

And not far away, Li Fan, hidden behind the scenes, let out a hearty laugh, a sight rarely seen.

"This is truly 'the Great Dao cannot be trodden upon before you'..."

"The Prosperous Yellow Saint Venerable is above!"

Chapter 1582: The Saint Mends The Void Realm

Li Fan's unrestrained laughter was audible only to himself within the entirety of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm. The attention of all beings in heaven and earth was now focused on that brilliant figure isolated beyond the celestial realm. The Four Heavenly Gates shone with radiance, its sleeves fluttering like an Arch-Immortal. Standing proudly amidst the myriad stars and even higher than the Investiture of the Gods, the words, "Transform the souls of heaven and earth, merge with the Dao with one's body; solidify the principles of heaven and earth, to prove longevity..." continued to echo, and finally, someone among the masses, gazing upon the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm's first Dao-integrating cultivator, recalled the figure's identity.

"Transmission Immortal Venerable!"

Some wept profusely, some were in disbelief, and some nodded with excitement. "Even with the drastic changes in heaven and earth, Transmission remains the same Transmission!" In one awakening, he not only became the first to merge with the Dao and ascend to immortality but also illuminated a path to ascension for all beings in Profound Yellow.

The method of Transmission, in essence, was simple. In summary, it boiled down to six words: "If you can't beat them, join them." The Profound Yellow Realm had undergone tremendous upheaval, its overall level having leaped and sublimated immensely. The gap between heaven and earth and cultivators had been infinitely widened. The past methods of attempting to devour heaven and earth and ascend in one step were naturally no longer applicable.

Thus, Transmission shifted his approach. Since he could not contend with the world's power, he would simply pledge allegiance. He would become a part of the world's order and use its grand might to aid his own cultivation! The old method of cultivation emphasized the enlightenment of "Oneness of Heaven and Man," where cultivators and the heavens were equals. Transmission had previously innovated a method that was a strategy of "skinning and scraping," where cultivators and the heavens were adversaries.

Now, by adopting this new method, the relationship between heaven and earth and cultivators would become one of superior and subordinate. And the first to pledge allegiance was the former leader of the adversarial cultivators. How could this not bring inexplicable joy to the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao!

Within a single day and night, Transmission managed to embody the souls of heaven and earth and instantly merge with the Dao. This was undoubtedly related to his special status as the first to pledge allegiance. Under Li Fan's deliberate guidance, Transmission's two maxims echoed in the hearts of every spirit in heaven and earth. Although a tiny fraction of cultivators instinctively rejected this method of cultivating by becoming a dog of heaven and earth, the vast majority quickly accepted it without hindrance. They even extended their understanding and comprehended the cultivation methods for various realms of Dao integration. In essence, all were about merging with heaven and earth.

It was foreseeable that in a very short period, cultivators in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm would experience a blowout of breakthroughs in their realms. And among the cultivators, two naturally antagonistic factions would emerge: those who pledged allegiance to heaven and earth, and ordinary cultivators. The confrontation between the two sides would be irreconcilable until one side completely vanished. And with Li Fan operating behind the scenes, the ultimate victor was self-evident.

Above the celestial canopy, the radiance from the Four Heavenly Gates gradually dimmed. However, the gates did not immediately close, revealing the endless mountains and seas within them to the eyes of all Profound Yellow beings. The masses were awestruck, then filled with longing. Above the Endless Sea and the Overlooking Mountain—although the world did not yet know their names at this moment—they instinctively felt their own insignificance. The glimpses of mountains and seas revealed through the gates would become their lifelong pursuits.

The grand gathering finally came to an end. The Four Heavenly Gates slowly returned to their original state, disappearing from everyone's sight. Just as the Profound Yellow beings thought Transmission's Dao integration and ascension were complete, a majestic and imposing figure, familiar to all, reappeared above the celestial canopy. Even after witnessing the mountains and seas, the masses had not knelt in reverence. But now, as this figure emerged, all beings in Profound Yellow prostrated themselves. This was because this figure was the Primordial Profound Yellow Controlling the Heavens and Skies Saint Venerable!

All beings trembled, their souls surging. As if witnessing the Dao, their minds froze in fear, yet their bodies seemed to be drawn and disintegrated by the mere appearance of the Saint Venerable's phantom. They realized this was no illusion. It was because the Profound Yellow Saint Venerable was too powerful. They could not withstand the divine might of the deity; just as ice and snow inevitably melt under the sun's glare, before the magnificent Primordial Profound Yellow Controlling the Heavens and Skies Saint Venerable, they were less than ants. Even a slight fluctuation in its aura would be unbearable, causing their annihilation. The reason they were still alive was that something stood between the Profound Yellow Saint Venerable and the beings. It was a scroll, unfurled and boundless, floating in the expanse. The scroll was initially blank, but now, it bore the first name.

Su Bai!

Originally, a name was merely a designation. You could be called Su Bai, I could be called Su Bai, anyone could be called Su Bai. But from the moment this name appeared on the Investiture of the Gods, the designation of "Su Bai" became specific throughout heaven and earth. It was, and could only be, that resplendent Heavenly Benevolence Star! Those who shared the name Su Bai in the world had already vanished like dust, leaving no trace of their past existence, nor even any imprint in the memories of their closest kin. And in the future, no second Su Bai would emerge. This was the God Transformation realm of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm: entering the Saint Venerable's discerning gaze and receiving an eternal name! Of course, receiving an eternal name was merely the most direct and perceivable enhancement for outsiders after achieving God Transformation. The earth-shattering changes truly occurring within their own bodies were known only to the individuals themselves.

The Saint Venerable's grand likeness finally slowly dispersed. And without the Saint Venerable's radiant gaze, although the Investiture of the Gods remained floating in the celestial realm, it was beyond the sight of all beings. Only cultivators who had transformed into stars at the Nascent Soul stage could vaguely perceive its trace. Thus, their ambition to advance grew even stronger. Those who could cultivate to this realm naturally possessed a certain pride. If Su Bai could advance to God Transformation, why couldn't they? With the birth of the first God Transformation cultivator in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, the emergence of the second and third would not be far behind.

Su Bai seemed to have become a bridge, shortening the vast chasm between the Nascent Soul and God Transformation realms in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm. Other cultivators displayed their unique abilities, eager to become the second name on the Investiture of the Gods.

As for Su Bai himself, he showed no joy in achieving God Transformation. Instead, his face contorted in pain, deep in self-reproach. "After the great changes in heaven and earth, the number of living beings in the world has multiplied countless times. Among them, how many shared my name and surname..." "And now, they have all died because of me." Su Bai's face turned pale, his body trembling uncontrollably. "Saint Venerable, can the strong disregard the lives of the weak? Can the strong do whatever they please? Is this truly the right way?" After a long while, Su Bai finally emerged from his remorse and self-reproach. Then, a question arose in his heart. He looked up towards the highest heavens, directly asking the Profound Yellow Saint Venerable. However, he received no answer from the Saint Venerable. Instead, he learned an unexpected piece of news that turned his face pale again, and his heart turned cold.

Only those whose names are recorded on the Investiture of the Gods will be able to escape this tribulation..." Su Bai was immediately struck as if by lightning. Having already entered the Investiture of the Gods, he should have felt fortunate, free from calamity. Su Bai muttered to himself, his gaze gradually shifting from confusion to determination, fixed upon the heavens beyond. His thought was simple: as long as he could meet the Profound Yellow Saint Venerable face-to-face, perhaps he could persuade Him to retract the decree of world destruction. "Only by merging with the Dao can one cross this invisible boundary." "Merging with the Dao..." Su Bai narrowed his eyes, once again sensing the myriad Great Daos in the world. This time, his desire to delve deeper was a million times stronger than before.

... "As expected, Su Bai is still Su Bai." Having seen Su Bai's entire transformation from beginning to end, Li Fan couldn't help but sneer. "Wanting to save the world, how much can one save? Without the Great Tribulation of Profundity, there is the Tribulation of Mountains and Seas. His own strength is not enough, yet he still wants to overthink things." Li Fan naturally could not empathize with Su Bai. But if it could make Su Bai accelerate his cultivation and completely exhaust his potential, Li Fan would not prevent him from changing his mindset. "After the integration of the Dao of Eternity, the sturdiness of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm has increased by at least thirty percent. And this effect will only grow as more names are added to the Investiture of the Gods." In fact, this was an unexpected bonus. When Li Fan, under the guise of Tai Yi, drew the gaze of Eternity and it glanced at the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, carving a trace of eternal attribute into the world, the Dao of Eternity subsequently closed its eyes. Li Fan was already quite satisfied with this outcome. He then proceeded to project his divine manifestation onto the hearts of all Profound Yellow beings. As for later, when a cultivator broke through to God Transformation and had their name inscribed on the Profound Yellow Investiture of the Gods, it was all within Li Fan's plan. Li Fan's divine sense swept across the entire Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, locking onto potential candidates. Most were as expected. Only one was a slight surprise to Li Fan. The person Li Fan was focusing on was a thin man named Zhang Shangzhi. While he appeared righteous, a hint of inexplicable gloom flickered in his eyes from time to time. The so-called talent for comprehending the Dao was, in reality, the affinity with various Great Daos. Before this, Zhang Shangzhi's talent for comprehending the Dao was mediocre. The Profound Yellow Saint Venerable was Li Fan, the Father and Mother of Profound Yellow! The greatest Dao in this world, the Dao above all Daos! And Zhang Shangzhi, due to his excellent compatibility with Li Fan—acting ruthlessly to achieve his goals, never trusting anyone from the bottom of his heart, and possessing a cold, robotic indifference—shared almost identical traits and thought patterns with Li Fan. If Li Fan hadn't known for certain that there were no blood relatives of his within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, he would have almost thought that Zhang Shangzhi was his own flesh and blood. Having understood the truth, Li Fan was speechless. The reason Zhang Shangzhi's cultivation had advanced by leaps and bounds was simply because he was "lucky" to be like Li Fan. "Outside the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, he would be useless. After all, he has no True Transformation, nor does he possess infinite spiritual essence." Li Fan shook his head slightly. After settling the Dao of Eternity in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, Li Fan intended to return to the Merchant Immortal Ship to retrieve the two Cat Treasures. "So-called talent might merely be a certain degree of similarity to certain beings."

Chapter 1583: Words Are Followed by Actions

"To possess such strength before even entering the Mountains and Seas. Given time, and after you have experienced the trials within the Mountains and Seas, your future is indeed full of promise. However..."

Evil Su Bai's tone shifted, his voice growing colder. "External aid may serve as a boat, or oars. But to truly transcend, it ultimately depends on yourself!"

"You..."

"Do you possess anything unique to yourself?"

His icy whisper echoed in Li Fan's ears, like a devil's incantation. Simultaneously, a peculiar gleam appeared in Evil Su Bai's eyes.

Li Fan's mind was involuntarily drawn to it.

As their gazes met, Li Fan suddenly found himself in an unfamiliar space.

The surrounding space was a void, with only Li Fan and Evil Su Bai standing opposite each other.

"When all external things are gone, how will you contend?"

Su Bai's sinister voice swirled around him. He had clearly seen through the myriad inheritances and foundations within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, yet he did not wish to lose face before Li Fan. Fighting within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm would inevitably cause damage, so he directly pulled Li Fan into this mental space for a confrontation.

"Kid, watch closely. I won't hold back here."

Before his words could even finish, Su Bai's figure in front of him split into two, then four, then eight...

In an instant, he manifested nearly infinite illusions, filling the empty void completely.

Each Su Bai had a different expression: some were compassionate, some smiled, some had calm eyes.

Around them, various scenes from different possibilities appeared and manifested.

In some, the Immortal Realm still existed, and Su Bai was an Immortal Minister of the Immortal Domain. In others, Su Bai was merely a mortal, yet he held all beings in his heart and was revered by the masses. But all these manifested Su Bai were undoubtedly kind-hearted individuals.

Only the Evil Su Bai, clad in black, stood out amidst the myriad illusions. Like a moon surrounded by stars, he resided at the center.

The different possibilities manifested around the countless Su Bai slowly converged and connected under the will of the central Evil Su Bai.

Like countless rivers flowing into the sea, like earth and stones piling up to form mountains.

In only a moment, Li Fan felt as if he were surrounded by Mountains and Seas!

The might of the mountains, the power of the seas. It was no different from the boundless sea and the mountain above that Li Fan had witnessed before!

"Or rather, it's almost indistinguishable from the scenes of mountains and seas that I can see, not the true Mountains and Seas."

"If he could devour all his selves across all possibilities and achieve the realm of 'all selves returning to one,' then perhaps even the word 'almost' would be unnecessary."

"Manifesting the image of Mountains and Seas with the power of a single person. Is this the true state of transcendence..."

With Mountains and Seas before him, Li Fan's heart remained exceptionally calm.

Although Evil Su Bai's display was grand, Li Fan felt no fear.

Firstly, this was merely a mental space. The clash of wills between them, whether in victory or defeat, life or death, would not truly affect reality. His act of borrowing power with a tiger's skin had, to some extent, served as a deterrent.

Secondly...

Li Fan had already clashed with Evil Su Bai before.

Although the process was somewhat convoluted, the final outcome was him instantly killing Evil Su Bai.

This was within the eternal remnant left by Su Bai in the Profound Yellow Realm.

"Even if the power of the techniques Evil Su Bai unleashed here is more than a level stronger than what was left by the eternal remnant, to me, there's no essential difference."

The sounds of mountains and seas roaring, like a storm and massive waves, approached inch by inch. It seemed Evil Su Bai had done this intentionally, wishing to use this slow, increasing pressure to break Li Fan's will.

But Li Fan remained unfazed, laughing heartily amidst the wind and rain of the mountains and seas. "Senior, have you heard of the divine ability, [Words Manifest Law Follows]?"

"This junior is untalented, but most of my strength comes from divine abilities!"

His smile vanished, and Li Fan spoke word by word, sternly, "The wind and rain are coming? Then let it [Rain Sparse, Wind Stops]!"

His voice was clear and resonant, spreading through the Mountains and Seas manifested by Evil Su Bai.

It was as if an invisible hand gently pressed down upon the Mountains and Seas. The originally fierce howling sounds were immediately suppressed, becoming barely audible.

Although there were still some winds and waves within the Mountains and Seas, they were no longer a cause for concern.

Seeing this, all the Su Bai faces flashed with unconcealed astonishment.

Before they could react, Li Fan spoke again, "The realm of Mountains and Seas, though beautiful, is somewhat an eyesore. Please disperse."

In the mental space, the continuous Mountains and Seas entered a moment of stillness.

Then...

The mountains collapsed, the seas vanished.

Along with them, the countless Su Bai who had manifested the imagery of Mountains and Seas evaporated into nothingness!

Boom!

The mental space shattered instantly, and both Li Fan and Evil Su Bai were immediately returned to reality.

Although Evil Su Bai's face appeared calm, his heart was already churning with monstrous waves.

"What was that just now?"

"My manifestation of Mountains and Seas inexplicably vanished without any resistance? Even in a mental space, during a clash of wills..." Evil Su Bai was speechless, his jaw agape.

He had also sought guidance and sparred with Shou Qiu and the Three Saints.

Even before these Saints who could traverse the eternal void, he, Su Bai, would not have been so helpless.

"[Words Manifest Law Follows]? Does such a divine ability exist in the Mountains and Seas? It can even influence Mountains and Seas!"

Although it seemed incredible, upon careful consideration, the various phenomena he had witnessed in this so-called Profound Yellow Immortal Realm suddenly made sense.

"No wonder those old fellows were so generous," Evil Su Bai suddenly understood.

While Evil Su Bai was inwardly shaken, Li Fan also felt quite solemn.

"The gap in strength is still too great. True is also currently dormant, and even in the mental space, my [True is False] required two steps to eliminate it."

Li Fan did not possess the divine ability of "[Words Manifest Law Follows]."

The method he used to defeat Evil Su Bai was exactly the same as in the eternal remnant. It was the transformation of [True is False].

Based on Su Bai's eternal remnant, his understanding of Evil Su Bai, and the initial fluctuations of True and False changes released in the mental space just now, Li Fan was certain that Evil Su Bai was unaware of the existence of [True is False].

For something outside of his perception, even if Li Fan displayed it in front of Evil Su Bai, he naturally wouldn't be able to discern it or know what divine ability was being used.

And the ability to instantly dissipate the manifested imagery of Mountains and Seas within a single breath did indeed align with the four words "[Words Manifest Law Follows]."

"Firstly, it was within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm. Secondly, I already had a sufficiently thorough understanding of Evil Su Bai. That's why I dared to use [True is False]."

"Before other transcendent powerhouses, I cannot be so reckless."

"You are qualified to formally enter the Mountains and Seas."

Evil Su Bai was slightly stunned.

Chapter 1584: Machine of a Hundred Refinements at the End of Time

The evil Su Bai's eyes narrowed, scrutinizing the item in his hand. Light and shadow distorted and shifted, and the image of the towering Heavenly Pillar gradually dissipated, revealing the slumbering Starving Immortal within. Evil Su Bai looked at the person with a rather subtle expression.

"You're quite sensible, kid," was all he said after a moment of silence, without refusing Li Fan's offer. His form then faded, disappearing. In the blink of an eye, he had left the "Primordial" possibility. Just as he had arrived, silently.

Li Fan stared at the celestial dome for a long time before finally confirming that the other party had truly departed, letting out a slight sigh of relief. Even with the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm as his backing, at his current strength, facing an Transcendent expert like evil Su Bai still put considerable pressure on him. Especially after losing his greatest life-saving trump card, True Return.

"Fortunately, the outcome is satisfactory." As his spirit relaxed slightly, the countless Dao-One Worms hidden within the Profound Yellow world, which had been on high alert, returned to their original state. They re-gathered near the four celestial platforms, enhancing their adaptability to the Great Dao of the world.

Due to the premature contact with Su Bai's eternal remnants, evil Su Bai was considered the most suitable Transcendent expert for a true first encounter in the Great Dao of the world. Although he exuded an evil aura, he was not foolish or irrational. Therefore, Li Fan could use the Great Dao of Longevity, the Tai Wei Holy Medicine, and other manifested powers to deter and restrain him.

Even if Li Fan's plan failed and he was forced into a direct confrontation with evil Su Bai, within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm's domain, with the newly born Ink Slaughter, Dao-One Worms, and the Transformation of True and False as his trump cards, Li Fan was confident he could fight evil Su Bai. However, the final outcome might be quite brutal, but survival should be guaranteed.

This was why Li Fan's actions seemed like a risky gamble. The risks were extremely high, but the rewards were naturally significant. Most importantly, Li Fan gained a clear understanding of his current strength. As the saying goes, "Without climbing a high mountain, one does not know the height of heaven; without facing a deep stream, one does not know the depth of earth."

Li Fan had personally visited the Great Dao of the world several times in the past, but only for brief glimpses, never a formal crossing. He did not have a specifically quantified understanding of the immense pressure involved in crossing the Great Dao of the world. Without the ability to True Return and start over at any time, the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm's collision with the Great Dao of the world would offer no room for error. A single misstep could turn the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm into dust, and Li Fan would be severely injured, if not die.

"Using evil Su Bai as an anchor point, one can both 'see' the Great Dao and 'measure' oneself." "Even with the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm's many layers of defense, it is still not qualified to be a celestial vessel for safely crossing the Great Dao of the world."

As if sensing Li Fan's thoughts, the Dao-One Worms' efforts in erosion and learning became even more vigorous.

"Relying solely on the Great Dao transformations brought about by the Dao-One Worms is too slow." "The Profound Yellow Celestial Ship's most significant problem is its insufficient hull strength. Even though I used rare and sturdy materials to build the celestial ship, they have not fully fused with each other. It's as if they were merely roughly piled together, with many gaps remaining." "Under normal circumstances, it is perfectly fine, and even I cannot discern these gaps. However, once subjected to the pressure of colliding with the Great Dao of the world, these gaps will become the culprit behind the celestial ship's instantaneous disintegration."

"There are two ways to solve this problem. First, find more materials to fill all the gaps. Second…" "...is to re-forge the Profound Yellow heavens and earth. Each cycle of world-ending tribulation is an opportunity for a complete remolding."

With Li Fan's current insight, once the problem is identified, a solution can quickly be found. Although his realm was constrained before Transcendance, his understanding far surpassed his current strength. In a sense, Li Fan was like a legendary powerful being who had reincarnated with his memories and was undergoing a new cultivation journey. However, his advanced knowledge stemmed from continuous reincarnation.

"I will pursue both approaches." "Within the Supreme Dao Scripture, True Immortals still exist. I will capture all of them and use them as materials to fill the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm." "And I myself must re-understand the principles of elixirs to further refine the Profound Yellow."

The orange cat slumbering on Li Fan's shoulder shattered its light and shadow in an instant, transforming back into a dose of Loquat mixed with Bai Qian.

"Using the Dao to refine medicine, and medicine to understand the Dao. This method of the Holy Emperor Tai Wei bears some resemblance to Sun Piaomiao's Dao Refining Medicine King Scripture. However, Sun Piaomiao regarded it as the fundamental basis of cultivation, whereas in the eyes of the Holy Emperor Tai Wei, the myriad medicinal herbs in the medicinal garden were merely tools. The Holy Emperor's fundamental Dao path was the supreme Holy Dynasty that spanned across Mountains and Seas…"

Compared to the magnificent Holy Dynasty of Tai Wei, Li Fan's Profound Yellow Immortal Realm was insignificant. However, Li Fan did not feel crude about it.

"Although Profound Yellow is small, it holds infinite possibilities. The Holy Dynasty is vast, but its Dao path is already determined." "To be on par with the Mountains and Seas, it will inevitably clash with the various powerhouses in the Great World of the Other Shore in the future. Whether it can truly take that final step is also unknown. As for my Profound Yellow Immortal Realm…"

Li Fan extended his palm, examining a small black dot that had quietly appeared in his palm. It was a Dao-One Worm, having absorbed and assimilated some of Ink Slaughter's power. Ink Slaughter had successfully refined Loquat. To prevent it from being discovered, the Dao-One Worm's clandestine erosion had temporarily ceased.

Although it had only absorbed for over thirty days, the internal changes in the Dao-One Worms were profound, reaching a qualitative transformation. The most significant change, reaching a qualitative level, was the Dao-One Worms' method of consuming external objects. Before learning from Ink Slaughter, their erosion method still retained characteristics of "biological" feeding, like worms chewing or cultivators absorbing and refining. After emulating Ink Slaughter, the Dao-One Worms' consumption method had been elevated to near "annihilation." Their feeding efficiency and absorption capacity had increased dozens of times over.

Furthermore, due to the Dao-One Worms' inherent characteristic of constant evolution, unlike Ink Slaughter, whose abilities were already largely fixed and required external stimuli for further advancement, the Dao-One Worms' erosion capabilities were progressing at an astonishing rate.

"The current swarm of Dao-One Worms can almost be considered close relatives of Ink Slaughter." "The powers of Tai Yi and Eternity enhanced Ink Slaughter. Thus, it should also be effective for the Dao-One Worms."

With this thought, Li Fan threw the "[Primordial Beginning of Mountains and Seas]" scripture and the manifestation of Eternity's power towards the Dao-One Worm swarm. The countless black dots swarmed forward, slowly engulfing both items. Unlike Ink Slaughter, which was instantly enhanced, the transformation of the Dao-One Worm swarm was slow yet steady.

To call them "worms" was a misnomer; they had no relation to actual "insects." The spirits and monsters of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm were not living beings but manifestations of the power of heaven and earth. It was merely Li Fan's habitual way of referring to them.

Currently, the essence of the Dao-One Worm swarm was a different form of power, extremely similar in nature to Ink Slaughter, cultivated within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm as a vessel. Because they were born within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, they were under Li Fan's control as the Father and Mother of Profound Yellow.

"The Dao-One Worms have not yet fully absorbed the essence of Ink Slaughter." "We still need to find something for Ink Slaughter to do, to distract its attention as much as possible."

Within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, and even within the original possibility, the newly born Ink Slaughter was almost unrivaled, with few opponents. To find a suitable opponent, one had to look beyond the original possibility. But with the current level of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, it was insufficient to support Li Fan in safely traversing the Great Dao of the world.

Thus, Li Fan's first thought turned to the fishing pond. Or rather, the fishing grounds of the Great Dao of the world. However, after careful consideration, Li Fan ultimately decided not to act upon the fishing pond for the time being.

Li Fan then thought of the salvaging method he had witnessed in the Guangwu Star Sea in his previous life. By distributing Heavenly Pillars with different load-bearing capacities, they deliberately created weak points to attract the descent of Dao Annihilation, forming a vortex of annihilation, hoping that drifting objects within Dao Annihilation would be drawn in. Li Fan had successfully replicated this method during the illusions of True Return.

"When the first person to achieve Dao Integration is born in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, and True Immortals are listed on the Investiture of the Gods, the Profound Yellow Expedition can officially begin."

With this thought, Li Fan's focus immediately shifted to Xuanyuan Tuo. This Heavenly Venerable of Transmission, almost forgotten by everyone in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, had always attracted Li Fan's attention. After all, by the time of the Profound Yellow Heavenly Transformations, Transmission was already in the Dao Integration realm. With the sublimation of Profound Yellow into an Immortal Realm, the Heavenly Soul [Jinzhi] within him had become tens of millions of times stronger than before. Yet, Transmission remained at his past strength.

Theoretically, the moment Li Fan unsealed him, Transmission should have been crushed by the overwhelming power within him. But now, not only had Transmission not perished, but he had also, as if using immense leverage, maintained control over Jinzhi, which had transformed along with the Profound Yellow Realm's sublimation. Although, from Li Fan's perspective, it seemed to be at its limit, as if held by countless fine threads, risking rupture even with the slightest movement of Jinzhi. In a sense, the current Transmission was, in fact, the first in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm to achieve Dao Integration.

"But this is only within his current state of tranquility." "Once the balance of his enlightenment is broken, Transmission will instantly vanish. This is also why he has remained in seclusion, motionless."

Under the condition of potentially perishing at any moment, Transmission not only did not panic but instead used this special 'Dao Integration' realm as a stepping stone to seek the true method of Dao Integration.

"To prove only Dao Integration, not Longevity." This was the most profound thought Li Fan could perceive lingering in Transmission's heart. And it was precisely this belief that guided him, allowing him to maintain control over Jinzhi through the weak connection established in the past.

Li Fan had a premonition that Transmission was currently caught in some kind of internal struggle. After a deep probe, Li Fan finally understood the source of Transmission's indecision.

"It turns out he already has a method for stable Dao Integration in his heart. However, if he adopts this method, he will be permanently halted at the Profound Yellow Dao Integration realm and will never be able to surpass the Heavenly Dao of Profound Yellow. The past New Law, which defied the principles of heaven and earth and only allowed control over worldly affairs, would become impossible."

However, Transmission's ideal method was destined to conflict with Li Fan, the Father and Mother of Profound Yellow. How could Li Fan possibly hand over the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm?

"If you truly choose that path, then do not blame me for being ruthless." "Of course, if you can set aside your obsession and willingly become my dog…" "Then I will not be stingy and will even lend you a hand," Li Fan said with a slight smile.

As if sensing Li Fan's thoughts, Xuanyuan Tuo, who had been meditating for a long time, finally made a decision in his heart. Setting aside his inner obsessions, he let out a long sigh, and his entire demeanor relaxed. He opened his eyes and slowly stood up.

As he moved, the immense Heavenly Soul Jinzhi within him, far exceeding his capacity to bear, instantly showed signs of losing control and exploding. However, all the anomalies ceased as Transmission slowly uttered two sentences.

"Transform the Heavenly Soul, merge with the Dao with one's body;" "Solidify the principles of heaven and earth, to prove longevity!"

These two simple sentences resonated like thunderous roars, echoing louder and louder throughout the Profound Yellow heavens and earth. The Heavenly Soul Jinzhi showed no further signs of losing control and exploding. Because Transmission, or rather Xuanyuan Tuo, had now become it!

Donning a golden, radiant outer layer, the Heavenly Soul Jinzhi, which previously had no face, slowly revealed Transmission's appearance. Moments later, Transmission took a step towards the golden Jinzhi ahead. The two then merged into one!

Before taking the final step, a flicker of imperceptible loneliness crossed Xuanyuan Tuo's eyes. But it lasted only for a brief moment before he completely suppressed it. Since he had made his decision, there was no room for regret!

A golden light shot up into the sky, Ascending to the highest heavens. It passed through the Investiture of the Gods above and reached the Four Heavenly Gates. From each of the Four Heavenly Gates, a beam of light shot out, converging on Xuanyuan Tuo. The barrier between the outer heavens and the ground was pierced by this infinitely brilliant light. The beings on the ground were thus able to witness the events unfolding at the Four Heavenly Gates.

*Hum hum hum...* A roaring sound from the Mountains and Seas echoed from beyond the Heavenly Gates. The gates opened, and infinite immortal power, like a divine gift, cascaded downwards.

"This is..." "Immortality?"

Xuanyuan Tuo stared at the continuous panorama of Mountains and Seas that appeared before him, lost in a daze. For some reason, despite having achieved the step countless people dreamed of, he felt no great excitement.

And not far away, Li Fan, concealed behind the scenes, burst into laughter, an expression rarely seen from him. "This is truly 'the Great Dao ahead is untraversable'..." "The Profound Yellow Saint Venerable is above!"

Chapter 1585: Xuan Shang Never Leaves

"Not targeted at me, but rather repelling the mortal world, and even everything within the Mountains and Seas."

"This Great Dao of [Cone], when developed to its extreme, could carve out a piece of territory for oneself from the Mountains and Seas with sheer force!"

"But this is only theoretically possible. To reach such a realm requires countless years of effort, with not a single moment of slack. Even the slightest carelessness could lead to thousands of years of hard work going to waste."

"This is not a path that ordinary people can cultivate."

As Ink Slaughter's erosion progressed, Li Fan's understanding of the Great Dao of the Cone deepened, and he couldn't help but shake his head slightly. At the same time, he drew closer to that solitary figure.

The opposite figure did not panic. Instead, it bowed deeply towards Li Fan from afar.

Li Fan was slightly taken aback, but after a moment, he suddenly realized that for some reason, the distance between himself and the other party had inexplicably increased!

The solitary figure, which had been almost close enough to see its appearance, once again became indistinct.

Li Fan stood still, savoring the phenomenon. Through the feedback from the Dao-One Worms and Ink Slaughter, he understood the reason for this occurrence. It was: "I respect you one foot, and you must respect me one yard!"

Li Fan suddenly understood: "This is another type of Dao path. It is precisely because of possessing this divine ability that he could cultivate the Great Dao of the Cone to its current state so smoothly."

"If he only cultivated alone, he might not even have reached the Nameless Realm."

The Cone Immortal's divine ability of "I respect you one foot, and you must respect me one yard" was executed in an instant. Even the Dao-One Worms and Ink Slaughter did not sense any fluctuations in its Dao.

However, Li Fan did not mind. As long as he continued to approach the other party, for self-preservation, the Cone Immortal would inevitably have to use it again.

As expected, when Li Fan's distance to the Cone Immortal became close again. That solitary figure bowed deeply once more. In the blink of an eye, as if an illusion, Li Fan felt the other party, through continuous flashing, escape from his grasp to the horizon.

It was as if an extremely introverted person, on seeing a stranger approaching, instantly fled in panic.

Li Fan almost laughed in exasperation. And in this brief exchange, the Cone Immortal also fully understood Li Fan's incomprehensible "learning" ability. Therefore, it wisely abandoned the idea of competing with him for the Holy Merchant Lord.

After three bows, it completely disappeared from Li Fan's sight. Only the irrational Holy Merchant Lord was left standing there.

"The Great Dao of the Cone, combined with that divine ability, makes its escape speed truly remarkable. Moreover, its escape is not based solely on speed, but on the pressure I exert. In other words, the stronger my strength, the higher the pressure I exert, the faster he can escape from me."

"It's like a spring."

"Currently, there is no particularly effective method to deal with him..."

Looking in the direction the Cone Immortal had fled, Li Fan did not continue to pursue, temporarily letting him go. As long as the Cone Immortal did not leave the Primordial Realm, with the [Supreme Dao Scripture] in hand, Li Fan could always track his location from afar.

"To capture him, I need to devise a special method. For example, a dead end where there is nowhere to retreat, like the Tribulation of Annihilation..."

Li Fan's eyes flashed, and he withdrew his gaze. He then focused on his objective for this trip. The Holy Merchant Lord had indeed become completely deranged. Even though the Cone Immortal, who had restricted him, had already left, he was still within the originally designated area.

Waving his hands erratically at the void, he squandered the last of his remaining strength.

"Come here!"

Grabbing at the Holy Merchant Lord in mid-air, Li Fan intended to capture and suppress him within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

As expected, although the Holy Merchant Lord was almost at the end of his rope, his protective means were still present. With a flash of white light, Li Fan felt all his attempts to approach the other party's Dao web being imperceptibly deflected, leaving him grasping at emptiness.

"It hasn't truly disappeared, but rather…"

No matter which part of the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net Li Fan extended, like tentacles, they were all extensions of Li Fan's power. He could faintly sense that this part of his power still existed.

However, it was no longer within the Suo Xing Sea, nor even within the Primordial Realm. Instead…

"It was actually transferred to another possibility?"

Li Fan attempted to perceive the specific situation at the distant end through the disappearing power of the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net. However, the Great Dao of the world was layered with immense distances, separated by numerous Mountains and Seas. Even with his full strength, he could only sense some vague images.

Under a gloomy sky, chaotic objects were piled up mountains high, extending as far as the eye could see. The entire world resembled an endless junkyard, with no end in sight. The part of the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net that went there, without the support of Li Fan's main body, could not even remain suspended in the air and directly fell to the ground, becoming another member of the endless pile of garbage.

Instinctively, the Ink Slaughter within the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net began to devour everything around it. Although the world seemed to be filled with useless garbage, the composition of this garbage was unexpectedly refined. Ink Slaughter not only devoured it with ease but also experienced a greater degree of self-enhancement than it did in the "Primordial" realm.

The connection with the garbage mountain world was intermittent. However, it was basically confirmed that the part of the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net transferred there was thriving. Li Fan decided to let that part of his power develop on its own.

"I just don't know if the Holy Merchant Lord's protection always transfers to the same destination."

With this thought, at Li Fan's signal, Ink Slaughter surged towards the Holy Merchant Lord once more. This time, it was still silently resolved, not existing within the Primordial possibility. However, it was not transferred to the garbage mountain world, but to another, even more distant possibility. So distant that Li Fan even lost the perception of that part of the Dao Net.

Although theoretically they still existed, they were already beyond Li Fan's control, which was no different from losing them. Moreover, Li Fan was quite wary of such uncontrollable situations. After pondering for a moment, he gave up on further attempts to probe with the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net. Instead, he used other known Daos he possessed to launch a continuous, saturated attack.

With layers of immortal formations, they replaced the blockade of the Great Dao of the Cone. Infinite sword light erupted from the formations, dispelling the Holy Merchant Lord's last trace of power. Demonic sounds echoed, and a giant illusory alchemy furnace slowly took shape, enveloping the Holy Merchant Lord within.

At this moment, the Holy Merchant Lord was like a punching bag, enduring Li Fan's relentless, unrestrained onslaught. His protective means of transferring attacks finally reached their limit. The encirclement and siege by the experts of the Suo Xing Sea had already consumed most of it. After Li Fan's continuous saturated attacks, it finally reached its breaking point.

Like exploding stars, it turned into specks of white light, eventually dissipating.

Without this protective shield, the Holy Merchant Lord was no different from a mortal before Li Fan. In an instant, he was suppressed and imprisoned within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

Li Fan nodded with satisfaction, looking around. The experts of the Suo Xing Sea had long since scattered like birds and beasts. Only a few unnamed True Immortals who had been reluctant to give up on the Holy Merchant Lord had completely abandoned their intentions after witnessing Li Fan's thunderous methods of first repelling the Cone Immortal and then breaking through the defenses. They fled in panic.

"Where can they escape to?" Li Fan chuckled softly. However, he did not pursue. Even though he had gained control over all the escape routes of the celestial beings. Li Fan intended to leave these individuals for the Dao Integration True Immortals, who were about to emerge in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, for training.

The Suo Xing Sea was merely an appetizer before the main course. The Guangwu Star Sea further in the distance was Li Fan's true target for conquest.

With a thought, Li Fan had already returned to the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm. Outside the celestial heavens, he began to attempt to infiltrate the Holy Merchant Lord's thoughts. Beside him, the orange cat Loquat manifested its form and let out several calls of mocking ridicule towards the Holy Merchant Lord. In a short time, their roles had completely reversed.

However, the Holy Merchant Lord was beyond even grief and rage. When Li Fan entered his mind, he saw the moment when the Merchant Immortal Ship was destroyed, just as before. Time seemed to be frozen at this moment, trapped in this instant. The Holy Merchant Lord repeatedly relived the scene, overwhelmed by regret and helplessness.

"His thoughts were completely consumed by the desire to save the Merchant Immortal Ship, even drowning out his past memories."

"In that case…" Li Fan snapped his fingers lightly.

As the Merchant Immortal Ship was once again engulfed by the light of the explosion, and the Holy Merchant Lord shouted, "Eternity!" The Merchant Immortal Ship, which had already disappeared, miraculously reappeared in the void! The experimental space where the Cat Treasures were imprisoned, the various buildings within the Immortal Ship, and every citizen of the Immortal Ship were exactly the same as before!

Seeing all of this, the mad Holy Merchant Lord was inexplicably stunned. "It… it's back?" Tears streamed down his face. After only half a day, he slowly regained his senses. He was still somewhat disbelieving, and the Holy Merchant Lord repeatedly shuttled through every corner of the Merchant Immortal Ship, looking back and forth at the familiar people and things in his memories. He found no flaws. Everything seemed real.

"Could it be that what just happened was just a nightmare?"

"It's a reminder from the heavens, telling me that even the Great Dao of Eternity cannot be relied upon too much."

The Holy Merchant Lord felt a sense of trance. "I remembered. In fact, our Holy Ancestor had already reminded us of this long ago. Before leaving, he specifically instructed that besides the Great Dao of Eternity, we also needed a backup life-saving method. When the Immortal Ship split back then, it was actually with the Holy Ancestor's hidden push. Otherwise, even if there were disagreements about the plan to crash into the high wall, how could the Xuan-Shang Immortal Ship, whose entire strength was under the Holy Ancestor's control, possibly split?"

"If the Merchant Immortal Ship is completely destroyed, you can return within the high wall to find the Xuan Immortal Ship. The deepest part of the Xuan Immortal Ship's treasury contains the original backup of the Merchant Immortal Ship. Similarly, we also have the backup of the Xuan Immortal Ship from its split state back then. As the saying goes, Xuan is never separated from Shang, and Shang is never separated from Xuan. Although they are in different star fields, as long as one of the Xuan-Shang Immortal Ships survives, the Merchant Immortal Ship will exist forever."

"Moreover, the high wall where the Xuan Immortal Ship is located is much safer than the Suo Xing Sea. With the many treasures they obtained back then, they are sure to develop steadily. This means that the Merchant Immortal Ship will always have a retreat."

"This secret was only known to the successive Holy Lords. But over the years, the Immortal Ship's reliance and misuse of the Great Dao of Eternity have become increasingly serious. And no matter what disaster befell them, Eternity could restore the Immortal Ship. Over time, even the successive Holy Lords gradually forgot the life-saving plan left by the first Holy Ancestor..."

"In my trance, I saw the Immortal Ship destroyed. My mind collapsed, and I almost forgot this matter."

"Fortunately, it was just an illusion."

The Holy Merchant Lord muttered to himself. "Perhaps this is a hidden reminder from the first Holy Ancestor. Does it mean I should return to the high wall?"

"Right..." Recalling the inside of the high wall seemed to trigger some keywords, and a series of long-buried memories emerged from the Holy Merchant Lord's mind.

"Before the First Generation left, he also mentioned that if the Xuan-Shang Immortal Ship was in a desperate situation of complete destruction, return to the ancestral land."

"The Xuan-Shang Immortal Ship was transformed from a grotto-heaven in the ancestral land. The Immortal Ship Grotto-heaven, and all its inhabitants, except for the First Generation Holy Lord, exist as backups within the ancestral land world."

"That was a laboratory monitored by True Immortals from the upper realm."

"When the Holy Ancestor led the masses to flee back then, the defensive mechanism within the laboratory was triggered. The ancestral land has since been sealed. According to the Holy Ancestor's speculation, that laboratory is quite special, and unless it is affected by the Tribulation of Annihilation, ordinary disasters will not be able to affect it."

"It's strange. Why are these past memories surfacing today..."

The Holy Merchant Lord looked bewildered. After a moment of dazed confusion, he looked at the vibrant Immortal Ship space and comforted himself: "It seems the previous illusion had too great an impact on me."

"We have forgotten the importance of being prepared for danger even in times of peace for too long."

However, after a moment of clarity, the Holy Merchant Lord was once again lost in recollection.

… And in the reality of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, this Holy Merchant Lord had been in a state of petrified stillness from the beginning. He was immersed in the illusory world Li Fan had woven for him.

Li Fan had meticulously inspected the Merchant Immortal Ship before. With his current strength, it was possible for him to create a lifelike illusion to deceive the Holy Merchant Lord.

"Even if there are flaws, he will probably convince himself and ignore them," Li Fan commented lightly. Indeed, the Holy Merchant Lord's memories contained a lot of valuable information. Besides the arrangements made by the Holy Ancestor within the high wall, there was also a wealth of data transmitted back by successive Holy Lords who had explored other possibilities.

"A total of twenty-eight possibilities are involved."

"These are all safe havens where the Tribulation of Annihilation has not caused a world-ending catastrophe."

"In fact, if the situation were worse than the 'Primordial' Realm, the Holy Merchant Lords would not have transmitted specific details."

Li Fan roughly scanned the states of these possibilities. Every small change in the river of history would lead to a completely different outcome in the future. These possibilities were vastly different from the Primordial Realm Li Fan inhabited. Among them, Li Fan was most interested in the one where countless lower realms were attached to the Immortal Realm, and the Immortal Realm successfully withstood the great tide of Dao Annihilation.

Chapter 1586: The Immortal Boat Is About to Sink

The turning point occurred after the previous Immortal Emperor of the Immortal Realm, Emperor Zhaiyang, abdicated. His successor was not Emperor Tianluo, but [Xuan Yi].

Unlike Emperor Tianluo, who was ambitious and sought to resolve the catastrophe of the Dao Annihilation of the entire Immortal Realm in one fell swoop, Emperor Xuan Yi's goal from the beginning was clear.

To concentrate all available resources and power to ensure the survival of the nine major star regions in the central Immortal Realm.

Other star regions in the Immortal Realm, and even countless immortal cultivation worlds in the mortal realm, were targets that could be sacrificed.

Emperor Xuan Yi's strategy proved remarkably effective. The nine major star regions of the Immortal Realm, like rising highlands, stood above the tide of Dao Annihilation. Although it came at the cost of countless submerged star regions below, it at least won a temporary victory.

Compared to the vast star regions of the Immortal Realm, the fate of the countless immortal cultivation worlds in the lower realms was relatively better. Their power level was too low to even qualify as sacrifices. Therefore, they were preserved until the last moment before being absorbed into the Immortal Realm. Not only did they no longer have to worry about the catastrophe of Dao Annihilation, but the mortals of the lower realms also benefited from misfortune, ascending to immortality in a single step.

The reason why the new Immortal Realm needed to absorb the lower realms was simple. Although the Dao Annihilation catastrophe had been temporarily overcome, Emperor Xuan Yi did not relax. He knew deeply that the Dao Annihilation catastrophe had not truly disappeared. As the overall Dao Annihilation process of the Mountains and Seas deepened, the Dao Annihilation catastrophe was likely to sweep back at some point in the future.

The countless worlds absorbed from the lower realms were for preparedness. These worlds, compared to the vast star regions of the Immortal Realm, were as fragile as dust. This meant that they were more sensitive when facing disasters.

Therefore, they could serve as warning signs for the arrival of the Dao Annihilation catastrophe.

When the great tribulation approaches, the attached realms will be destroyed first.

Based on the number and speed of destroyed attached realms, the Immortal Realm could make a preliminary judgment on the power of the upcoming Dao Annihilation catastrophe.

...

"This Emperor Xuan Yi is much more reliable than Emperor Tai Tian."

"I can even learn from his warning method," Li Fan mused inwardly, nodding.

"It's just that, since there are countless possibilities between the Mountains and Seas, and there must be many who successfully resisted Dao Annihilation like Emperor Xuan Yi, why don't other possibilities simply learn and imitate them? I believe the Immortal Emperors of the Immortal Realm, even if they cannot traverse the Mountains and Seas, should possess the ability to observe other possibilities..."

"Could it be that because the situations in different possibilities are different, there is no universal method of salvation?"

Among the twenty-eight possibilities, twenty-six were quite similar to the [Primordial] realm where Li Fan was located. As for the other two...

One was that all living beings had abandoned their physical bodies and existed as pure spirits. Without the constraints of the physical body, they could attach themselves to the Great Dao of the Mountains and Seas at any time, making it easier to survive the Dao Annihilation catastrophe.

The other possibility was extremely bizarre.

It seemed that very early on, the historical trajectory had shifted. The Immortal Realm did not even exist.

There was only a vast and desolate starry sky.

This starry sky itself was connected to the Mountains and Seas. Its vitality was extremely vigorous, and it could resist the Dao Annihilation catastrophe to a certain extent. Even in some desolate star regions swallowed by Dao Annihilation, life could occasionally and slowly recover.

Therefore, although the inhabitants of this desolate starry sky were much weaker than the immortals, they could survive longer with less effort when facing the erosion of the Dao Annihilation catastrophe.

"However, it seems that this desolate starry sky is extremely resistant to cultivators. The pioneers of the Merchant Immortal Ship who infiltrated it also barely managed to survive after abandoning all their cultivation. He guessed that the stronger the cultivator, the stronger the backlash from heaven and earth they would suffer there. If a True Immortal were to go..."

Li Fan estimated that with the desolate starry sky's ability to resist Dao Annihilation to a certain extent, without Transcendent strength, anyone entering would likely die or be crippled.

"In reality, this desolate starry sky itself can be regarded as a powerful being connected to the Mountains and Seas. I just don't know what happened in the past to cause the Immortal Realm not to be born. Logically speaking, Saints Lian Shan, Gui Hai, and Tai Yi should exist in all realms..." A hint of doubt flashed in Li Fan's mind.

"However, it is also possible that the information transmitted by the pioneers of the Holy Merchant was incorrect. After all, with his strength, he might not be able to fully comprehend the entire possibility."

Li Fan shook his head slightly.

Among these twenty-eight possibilities, the pioneers of the Holy Merchant were like towering, bright lighthouses. If one possessed the ability to traverse the Mountains and Seas, one could basically reach the destination by continuously moving forward in a certain direction.

And Li Fan, in the memory of the Lord of the Holy Merchant, found the method for the pioneers to travel to other possibilities.

A crystal-clear eyeball, like a diamond!

The light projected from the eyeball seemed to traverse the Mountains and Seas. With one charge, it could send a trace of consciousness to another possibility.

However, this treasure, which could be called the ultimate treasure of the Holy Merchant, had a lamentably weak defense. It was extremely fragile and could not even withstand the impact of a Nascent Soul cultivator's power.

Therefore...

Most likely, it had completely disappeared with the destruction of the Holy Merchant.

Li Fan could not help but feel a little regretful that such a miraculous item existed within the Holy Merchant.

However, it was only regret.

When the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm was fully established and could serve as a world-traversing immortal ship, Li Fan could explore the Mountains and Seas himself.

Knowing the situation of the destination in advance was merely for convenience.

"Besides, Transcendents should have means to observe the possibilities within the Mountains and Seas, right? Otherwise, how could they accurately find their destination in the vast Mountains and Seas?" Li Fan mused.

"Even if I reach the Transcendent realm through a shortcut, and the path ahead is invisible, I can still follow these twenty-eight coordinates of the Holy Merchant. I won't be completely lost."

The path Li Fan was currently taking was probably unique in the entire Mountains and Seas.

Other Transcendent experts, and even the Saints, could not serve as a reference for Li Fan. Everything required him to take it one step at a time and observe.

After dealing with the information outside the Primordial possibility in the mind of the Holy Merchant Lord, Li Fan shifted his attention to the matters within the Primordial realm.

"Ancestor Land."

"If I remember correctly, the so-called Ancestor Land should also be within the high wall, in the Lan Ke Daoist field."

"However, my Shou Qiu inheritance has given me complete knowledge of the world within this experimental space, and there is no existence that matches the description of the Ancestor Land in his memory."

Li Fan's consciousness entered the control center of the Lan Ke Daoist field and searched again. To ensure no omissions.

"When the Xuan Shang Immortal Ship escaped, it activated its defensive measures. The Ancestor Land fell into a sealed state, perhaps this is the reason?"

Li Fan carefully examined it again.

His gaze swept across the familiar light screen composed of countless divided square spaces.

This time, Li Fan's focus was not on the areas where light flashed.

But on those black star fields, which Li Fan had initially thought were dead zones.

"These black star fields are all areas that have been swallowed by the Dao Annihilation catastrophe. With my familiarity with Dao Annihilation, I wouldn't be mistaken. Otherwise, I wouldn't have failed to discover the so-called Immortal Ship Ancestor Land for so long."

Li Fan observed each one this time.

Once, twice...

From a common sense perspective, even if hidden extremely deeply, the Immortal Ship Ancestor Land should not have been able to escape Li Fan's meticulous investigation. But Li Fan had a faint premonition.

The Immortal Ship Ancestor Land might be extraordinary.

Therefore, he patiently searched back and forth, not missing any details.

His divine sense enveloped all the black spaces for a hundred days.

Suddenly, in one location, an imperceptible fluctuation occurred inexplicably.

It vanished in an instant.

If Li Fan hadn't been constantly monitoring, he would have likely overlooked it.

"What is this..." A sharp glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes.

"Disguising the aura of being swallowed by the Dao Annihilation catastrophe?!"

"Using Ink Slaughter as a trump card, I never expected to be deceived by Ink Slaughter one day!"

Li Fan was both surprised and delighted, and immediately sent a wisp of divine sense into this black star field.

But to his surprise, as soon as his divine sense entered, it vanished instantly, as if swallowed.

Immediately after, wisps of black energy inexplicably emerged around Li Fan's main body.

"This..."

"It's not a feigned illusion, but the real Dao Annihilation catastrophe! My divine sense rashly entered, and Dao Annihilation followed the connection between the divine sense and the main body, finding its way here!"

Li Fan's hair stood on end instantly, and he instinctively used the [Illusion Is True] divine ability.

The incoming Dao Annihilation black energy instantly lost its target. But they did not become confused; instead, they turned towards the outer heavens of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

It was as if the partially constructed Immortal Ship had been gnawed through by insects, creating several holes.

The surging Dao Annihilation was slowly pouring in through these holes.

"The holes are still small now, and can be repaired. If the holes become larger..."

"My Profound Yellow Immortal Ship will sink before it even sets sail!"

Li Fan's heart tightened, and he immediately instructed Ink Slaughter and the Dao-One Worms to patch these holes.

As for himself, he quickly flashed to the Suo Xing Sea.

Following the clues from the Grand Dao Scripture, he captured and suppressed several True Immortals and the three nameless beings [Fu Gui], [Yan Jian], and [Bu Yan] to serve as pillars to fill the Heavenly Pillars.

After considerable effort, he barely managed to quell the Dao Annihilation.

Half a day later, Li Fan surveyed the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm and ensured that there were no signs of Dao Annihilation further extending. He wiped the cold sweat from his forehead and breathed a sigh of relief.

He looked at the newly added Heavenly Pillars in the heavens and earth and sighed, "Originally, these individuals were intended for the Dao Integration True Immortals of the Profound Yellow Realm to practice with. Now, I have no choice but to act according to the urgency of the situation."

Since recovering his memories in this lifetime, he had not suffered such a significant loss.

Li Fan's expression turned somewhat gloomy, and he looked again at the black-shrouded star field in the Lan Ke Daoist field.

Pitch black, swallowed by Dao Annihilation.

"The strange fluctuation I sensed earlier was definitely not wrong."

"So, was it only possible in that brief moment?"

Li Fan narrowed his eyes, concentrating his attention, waiting for the fluctuation to reappear.

This time, he waited for more than a hundred and fifty days.

With prior preparation, Li Fan observed the changes completely this time.

It was as if a black curtain was lifted, revealing the normal white vitality within.

It lasted only for a short moment before the black curtain began to fall again.

Li Fan seized the opportunity and his divine sense entered it.

Chapter 1587: Record of Survival in the Ancestral Realm

The world was dim and silent. All things seemed to be in a state of petrification.

When Li Fan entered the Ancestor Realm of the Immortal Ship, this was the scene he witnessed.

However, this deathly stillness did not last long.

Like a spring breeze, everything in the world began to awaken from its petrification. Light reappeared, and all things were revived.

The world became noisy and full of life again.

However, the inhabitants of the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm seemed to have a clear understanding of their petrified state. After escaping from desperate straits, they all knelt on the ground, singing praises of the gods' benevolence.

This world was not large, even smaller than the Profound Yellow Realm before its ascension. In an instant, Li Fan's divine sense swept across it.

Thus, he understood the background of these so-called gods.

Approximately every hundred years, a great catastrophe would be born in the heavens and earth, destroying all living beings in the world, and even the world itself.

In the despair of the people, there was a god, with great compassion. He found the only way to save the world.

Before the great tribulation arrived, the god would first petrify all living beings and even the world to resist the disaster. After the tribulation passed, they would be transformed back.

It is unknown how the beings of the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm initially viewed this somewhat insane plan. But after experiencing countless petrifications to avoid calamity, the inhabitants of this world had already become accustomed to the drastic changes that occurred every hundred years.

"The time flow in this world is different from the outside."

"One year here is only equivalent to one day in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm."

"However, the situation here is the opposite of what I observed from the outside. When it appears black with Dao Annihilation, everything here is full of vitality. When it reveals the white light of vitality, this world is in a state of extinction and petrification."

Li Fan looked up at the celestial dome.

A vast consciousness was circling there, the culprit responsible for all these anomalies.

"Vast" was only relative to the other beings in the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm. Compared to the divine sense Li Fan had separated, it was like a drop in the bucket.

There was no need for caution, Li Fan went straight to the point to investigate.

As everything revived, the "god" fell into a deep sleep. Even with some protective measures, it was impossible to stop Li Fan.

Therefore, Li Fan was able to view all of the other party's memories.

Countless scenes flowed into his mind.
