The origin of everything stemmed from the betrayal of the Xuan Shang Immortal Ship. What was originally observational experimental data had escaped from the experimental field. This triggered emergency response measures, and this experimental field was subsequently isolated and sealed.

The original monitor of this world was also punished and annihilated. If the Lan Ke Daoist field had been operating normally, a new monitor would have been appointed quickly. However, with Dao Annihilation approaching, the Daoist field had been abandoned by all parties.

The Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm had since been sealed off and isolated.

But in fact, the period without interference from the Daoist field forces was the period of the most rapid development for the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm as a whole. The various factions united to study the reasons for the Immortal Ship's betrayal and the drastic changes in heaven and earth.

They eventually discovered the shocking secret that the world they inhabited was actually an experimental field set up by the Immortal Realm.

Who would be willing to be a white rat?

Naturally, they wanted to break free from this fate, just like the Xuan Shang Immortal Ship.

They began to study and analyze the immortal restrictions and formations hidden within the world. All factions united, putting aside their previous differences, and put their efforts into using the immortal energy for themselves.

The overall strength of the cultivators in the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm thus rapidly increased.

However, they were still far from breaking through the seal of the Lan Ke Daoist field.

Just then, Dao Annihilation descended.

Strictly speaking, what the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm faced was not the true Dao Annihilation tide that destroyed the Immortal Realm. After all, being within the Lan Ke Daoist field, with the support of the Shou Qiu phantom, they only encountered some scattered droplets created by the collision between Dao Annihilation and the Shou Qiu phantom.

Even so, [Dao Annihilation] was not something that the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm could withstand.

Countless vast worlds that were once endless, like stars in the sky, were mostly swallowed in an instant.

The remaining small portion struggled desperately in fear.

Fortunately, due to their collective research on the immortal formations and restrictions in the Lan Ke Daoist field beforehand, they were able to resist "Dao Annihilation" by relying on the remaining activated immortal formations.

This was similar to how the Immortal Realm had resisted Dao Annihilation in the past.

In the years that followed, the surviving inhabitants of the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm, for the sake of their survival, made every effort to find a way to survive under the shadow of Dao Annihilation.

Perhaps in the desperate situation of life and death, human potential can be infinitely unleashed.

The cultivators of the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm actually found a possible solution.

Li Fan observed the dormant consciousness before him.

This consciousness was not that of a single being, but a fusion of thousands upon thousands of different intentions.

Each intention represented a peerlessly gifted cultivator in the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm.

"These cultivators, each comprehended their own Great Dao, all different."

"Each cultivates one path, and they interweave, forming a Dao Net. The Dao Net can bear the weight of Dao Annihilation!"

"Although the Dao principles comprehended by these mortal cultivators cannot compare to those of True Immortals in terms of depth, they are not facing the true Dao Annihilation tide. Therefore, theoretically speaking, if more and more cultivators sacrifice themselves and join this consciousness, it might actually succeed."

"It's a pity..."

Li Fan's gaze penetrated this fused consciousness and reached its core.

There, a tiny void seemed to exist.

Threads of darkness flowed out from this void, converging like a stream.

"Dao Annihilation is not a static entity. On the contrary, Dao Annihilation is also cunning, as if it has its own consciousness. In the beginning, it was merely scattered droplets, but the real Dao Annihilation, which penetrates everything, slowly infiltrated from these weak droplets."

"The people of this world could not realize this point, or rather, by the time they discovered it, it would be too late."

With the support, the originally weak droplets gradually tended to grow into a true tide.

A disaster of this magnitude was no longer something that mortal cultivators could resist, no matter how talented they were.

"However, even in such a desperate situation, they could still find a way to survive..."

"Admirable!" Li Fan did not hesitate to praise.

"Although it is just a survival method born out of desperation."

The last resort of the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm naturally could not escape Li Fan's eyes.

They adopted the strategy of "opening rather than blocking."

They would channel all the leaked Dao Annihilation to a single location. Using the collective intentions of everyone, they would forge a dam and a high wall for resistance.

When the intention reached its limit, they would actively detonate the dam, redirecting the disaster to other spaces within the Lan Ke Daoist field.

Chapter 1588: Seeking Survival in Despair

Li Fan's fleeting light observed from the outside was caused by the explosion of the collective intention dam.

"I knew it, the Lan Ke Daoist field, after all, is supported by the phantom of Duke Shou Qiu, and it shouldn't have fallen so quickly. It turns out it was these people causing trouble..."

As the actual master of the Lan Ke Daoist field, Li Fan was not angered by this. What he truly cared about was the anomaly in the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm.

Even with the protection of the collective will, the collision between the intention dam and Dao Annihilation would cause catastrophic damage to the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm. Therefore, the fused intention also had to allocate a portion of its strength to petrify the world to ensure its safety.

Every act of salvation was a great consumption for the fused intention.

Within a hundred years, when the next wave of Dao Annihilation reached its limit, there must be enough successors to sacrifice themselves and merge their intentions to ensure the strength of the fused intention. Otherwise, the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm would face the fate of annihilation.

Li Fan had previously learned from the Taoist Comprehension that the "potential" of a single possibility might be fixed. With the birth of each prodigy, a part of the potential pool would be deducted. The number of powerhouses that could be born in a single possibility was limited.

This principle can be compared to a world.

Even the Profound Yellow Realm, which was bizarre, did not have an abundance of powerhouses and prodigies in every era. Looking back at history, after a period of prosperous cultivation, it would inevitably enter a period of decline, until after many years, the birth of an unparalleled genius would herald a new era.

Logically speaking, with the Foundation of the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm, it could not support the continuous birth of so many prodigies for such a long time.

The time flow in the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm was almost a hundred times slower than in the outside world. Since the great tribulation descended, tens of thousands of years had passed in the Lan Ke Daoist field. Here, it was millions of years!

In a million years, heavenly prodigies have continuously emerged like moths flying into a flame, sacrificing themselves to save the world.

Magnificent! Wondrous! Strange!

"The fused intention Dao Net before me, although it cannot compare to my Myriad Phenomena Dao Net in all aspects, it does have its merits."

Li Fan's divine sense withdrew from the fused cloud, and he scanned the heavens and earth again, hoping to uncover the reason for the long-lasting prosperity of the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm.

But with his vision, even after repeated checks, he could not find any clues.

Even within this fused intention, there was no gain.

"To solve a problem, one must start from the person who created it. It seems that to find the answer, I must personally enter the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm!" After a moment of contemplation, Li Fan came up with a plan.

"Incarnation as a Heavenly Demon!"

To thoroughly unravel the mysteries of this realm, simply splitting his consciousness to infiltrate would not suffice. Only by using the secret art of Heavenly Demon Reincarnation, like the Heavenly Physician in the past, could he deceive the Heavenly Dao of this world. By transforming himself into a true native inhabitant, he might have a chance to unravel the mystery.

In the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm, after the prayers and worship rituals of countless beings to the "gods" ended.

A new life was born.

In Linshan City, under the management of the Yin Yang Demon Subjugation Sect of the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm.

His surname was Li, and his name was Fan.

All infants born on the day of divine revelation would be adopted and personally trained by the City Lord.

Because there was a legend that beings born on this day would receive divine favor and have boundless prospects. And past experiences and inheritance had largely confirmed this.

Therefore, from a young age, Li Fan, along with these favored children, received meticulous training from the City Lord of Linshan City.

And they did not disappoint the City Lord's expectations. A total of seventy-two people, including Li Fan.

More than half of them officially entered the Qi Refining realm before the age of one.

Whether one could reach the peak of Qi Refining at the age of one was a crucial dividing line. Only those who met this requirement had the value to continue to be cultivated as favored children. Those who failed would lose their preferential treatment from then on. However, with the support of the City Lord, their lives could still be worry-free.

A total of thirty-nine infants were accepted into the sect by the Immortal Masters of the Yin Yang Demon Subjugation Sect for formal cultivation.

The Yin Yang Demon Subjugation Sect was one of the five major immortal sects in the world. Its mission was to subjugate demons and eliminate evil.

What is a demon? What is evil?

Those who disobey are demons. Those who are disrespectful are evil.

Disciples of the Yin Yang Demon Subjugation Sect must kill a specified number of demons and evil beings each year in their cultivation journey to be qualified to continue their identity as disciples of the Demon Subjugation Sect.

When the disciples of the Demon Subjugation Sect traveled the world, evil beings trembled at the mere mention of them.

Li Fan's talent was also among the best among the favored disciples.

At the age of one and a half, he officially established his Foundation and received anointing from the Sect Master of the Yin Yang Demon Subjugation Sect.

A volume that recorded the cultivation experiences and enlightenment insights of countless predecessors of the Demon Subjugation Sect, the [Demon Subjugation Heavenly Tome], was forcibly instilled into his mind.

A total of thirteen favored disciples received the anointing. Only six survived the impact of the Heavenly Tome and remained mentally clear.

With the blessing of the Heavenly Tome, Li Fan's cultivation speed increased exponentially.

At the age of three, he officially formed his Core and descended the mountain to subjugate evil.

A three-year-old child attempting to subjugate evil spirits. It sounds like a joke.

But in the Yin Yang Demon Subjugation Sect, it was a common occurrence.

Li Fan received the Sect Master's personal favorite [Mountains and Rivers Share Grief] sword and was then thrown by him for a hundred thousand miles. He was only permitted to return to the mountain after killing ten thousand demons and evil spirits.

The journey of a hundred thousand miles had to be paved with the blood of evil spirits.

Li Fan wielded his sword and traveled the world, patrolling the realm. Whenever he encountered beings with demonic or evil appearances, he would strike with thunderous force.

When he successfully returned to the mountain gate half a year later, the Mountains and Rivers Share Grief sword was already stained crimson with blood.

The Sect Master took the Mountains and Rivers Share Grief sword. The crimson sword body slowly condensed into the name Li Fan, engraved on the sword body, emitting an eerie glow.

Li Fan then saw that besides his own name, there were hundreds of other names densely packed on the sword, all written in blood, with varying degrees of crimson color.

"Ranked among the top three." The Sect Master of the Yin Yang Demon Subjugation Sect's eyes flashed with joy, and he officially accepted Li Fan as his personal disciple.

After becoming the Sect Master's disciple, Li Fan received further preferential treatment.

The most important aspect was the opportunity to spar and exchange with disciples from other immortal sects.

"Do you know what sparring is?" the Sect Master asked, stroking his beard.

Li Fan replied solemnly, "To determine victory and defeat, and even life and death. This is sparring."

The Sect Master showed a look of relief.

In five years, Li Fan sparred nearly a thousand matches with disciples from other immortal sects, without a single defeat.

He gradually became an undefeated legend among the disciples of the five great immortal sects.

After another exhilarating victory, he finally broke through to the Nascent Soul realm.

After reaching the Nascent Soul realm, he could no longer bully the younger disciples of the Immortal Ship. Instead, he had a new goal.

Under the guidance of a mysterious man in black, the newly promoted Nascent Soul disciples of the five great immortal sects gathered in a blessed land.

The blessed land was filled with ancient formations and ruins.

It emitted a palpitating aura.

According to the mysterious man, these ruins were all the work of immortal beings.

They would be confined here for ten years.

After ten years, the restrictions in the ruins would erupt on time. If they could not comprehend the mysteries of the immortal restrictions, they would only face a tragic death.

This was the trial they had to undergo after advancing to the Nascent Soul realm.

Facing the desperate situation, all the disciples of the immortal sects remained calm. No one clamored to return to their sect. In their opinion, life and death were trivial matters. Being able to stay peacefully for ten years was already extremely fortunate.

There was no guidance from their masters within the sealed blessed land; everything relied on personal comprehension.

Some formed groups to study together, while others were aloof and dedicated themselves to research alone.

Conflicts erupted from time to time, and many died in the struggle.

However, for the most part, everyone was engrossed in studying the ruins of the immortal realm.

Just when they thought they would really have to stay in this sealed blessed land for a full ten years.

On a certain day in the sixth year, the blessed land suddenly rumbled and shook. While they were puzzled, a long-lost external light shot down from the sky.

It shone on Li Fan.

The gazes of the heavenly prodigies from the five great immortal sects all turned to Li Fan, their faces filled with disbelief.

The mysterious man in black who had led them into the blessed land reappeared.

Staring at Li Fan, he murmured, "The fifty-second generation. This result is acceptable. I hope to add another one."

The heavenly prodigies were even more shocked upon hearing the man's words. They thought that Li Fan had already broken through the secrets of the immortal realm, which was already incredibly against the natural order. They never expected that he would only rank fifty-second. What kind of monstrous geniuses were the fifty-one before him?

As everyone's minds were still reeling, they heard the man in black speak again.

"As for you..."

"Go through another cycle of reincarnation and training."

"I hope the next life, you can be born into a better family and have higher comprehension."

The man in black only took Li Fan with him. All the others were buried in the collapse of the blessed land.

Li Fan watched silently as the blessed land, which had devoured more than a hundred heavenly prodigies from various sects, transformed into a black pill in the man's hand.

"Eat it." The man in black said nonchalantly, tossing the pill over.

Li Fan swallowed it without hesitation.

In an instant, a flash of inspiration struck his mind, and countless thoughts erupted. They were all from the insights of those heavenly prodigies in the blessed land. Although their progress in comprehending the immortal ruins was not as good as Li Fan's, they still had something worth learning from.

Five years of seclusion, plus the blessed land and the pills made from heavenly prodigies.

Li Fan's cultivation reached the Soul Transformation realm in one fell swoop.

Before he could rest, Li Fan was taken by the man in black and flew towards the nine heavens above.

The fierce winds were biting, as if they had corrosive properties. The protective spiritual energy was useless, and Li Fan's face hurt from the wind.

After a while, blood began to seep from various parts of his body.

Li Fan merely narrowed his eyes slightly, brushing away the blood discreetly, and kept pace with the man in black.

They continued to fly higher and higher.

It seemed endless, and the resistance grew stronger as they ascended.

Only after surpassing a certain boundary did Li Fan's vision suddenly broaden.

A magnificent purple palace, like an immortal's palace, stood in the clouds.

The people in the palace were all in a hurry, indifferent to other things.

Li Fan followed all the way to the central hall of the palace.

What stood in the hall was not a statue of anyone.

But a strange device.

With countless rings rotating, the projection revealed was the myriad beings below.

"This is the [Heaven-Peeking Divine Ring]. You can see all the secrets of heaven and earth within it."

"But do not be greedy. Remember, even if there are thousands of Great Daos before you, you can only choose one."

"Go," the man in black instructed a few words, rarer than usual, and pointed to the Heaven-Peeking Divine Ring ahead.

He did not explain the consequences of failure.

Li Fan had no other choice but to approach the divine ring step by step.

The closer he got to the divine ring, the faster the light and shadow within seemed to flicker.

The blood in his body surged, as if it would burst and spill out at any moment.

Li Fan endured the discomfort and slowly walked into the light and shadow.

The moment his body was engulfed by the divine ring's light and shadow, Li Fan felt as if he had completely disappeared.

He seemed to have transformed into a ring, and all the people, events, and things in the world played out before his eyes.

Who was that person? What kind of life did he live? What was his talent? What were his divine abilities? All were revealed at a glance.

What happened? From the moment the Xuan Shang blessed land broke through the realm barrier and the world was sealed, all the events that had occurred in the world were presented one by one before his eyes.

What object? Its superficial form was decomposed inch by inch. Revealing its underlying foundation and the laws of the Great Dao it represented.

...

As expected of the name Heaven-Peeking Divine Ring, with its assistance, Li Fan, at the Soul Transformation realm, could glimpse the principles of a world.

However, being a mortal body, his body gradually began to fail.

The light and shadow formed by heaven and earth gradually became illusory, and the image of the ring began to manifest.

Li Fan knew that he had to make a choice.

But he did not look back at the world's myriad things; instead, his gaze was fixed on the manifesting Heaven-Peeking Divine Ring.

"If I can obtain this item, wouldn't that be equivalent to owning the world?"

"Why look farther afield?"

As if enlightened, he decisively abandoned all that he had seen with the help of the divine ring.

He only looked resolutely at the Heaven-Peeking Divine Ring, trying to comprehend its principles.

If it were a completely unfamiliar artifact beyond his cognition, Li Fan would certainly not be able to decipher it in such a short time.

But Li Fan discovered that the essence of the divine ring was not unfamiliar to him. Although he had never formally encountered it before, from the Qi Refining stage onwards, principles very close to it had appeared in his cultivation journey from time to time.

It was as if the entire world was actually transformed from this Heaven-Peeking Divine Ring, and his cultivation path was like using himself as a hand to touch and perceive a part of the divine ring.

As his thoughts stirred, the divine ring before him also transformed from illusory to real.

The pressure it brought, however, ceased to exist, because Li Fan had truly become one of the countless parallel rings within the Heaven-Peeking Divine Ring!

His vision blurred, and Li Fan arrived in a dark space.

Countless human figures sat in a ring-shaped staircase.

Towards Li Fan, the newcomer, they merely nodded in acknowledgment.

Then, they continued to focus their gaze on the center.

There, although there was no specific object visible, Li Fan keenly sensed that it was darker than elsewhere.

Even...

The darkness of the entire space originated from here.

"This is..."

"Dao Annihilation?"

A word flashed inexplicably in Li Fan's mind.

Then, like a chain reaction, it triggered all of Li Fan's previous memories.

Without anyone present noticing, Li Fan's eyes underwent a subtle change.

"It's finally awake. The cultivator selection process of this world is quite interesting. It's even a bit cruel."

"All other life forms are expendable at any time, solely for the purpose of rapidly cultivating true prodigies who can enter this place."

Chapter 1589: World Crossing Gradually Perfected

"The fused intention of the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm is extremely repellent, and it contains Dao Annihilation. If one forcibly probes, this intention will directly self-destruct. Not only will nothing be gained, but it will also re-attract Dao Annihilation. Only by using this method can its secrets be unraveled."

Li Fan had spent twenty years infiltrating the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm, while only two months had passed in the outside world. He believed it was worth it to obtain the secrets of this place.

As Li Fan in the state of "in-utero mystery," it might have taken him some effort to decipher the scene before him, but Li Fan, having awakened his main consciousness, instantly understood the greatest secret here.

"Dao Annihilation is uncontrollable. Even a sliver of it appearing can cause world-ending tremors, one after another. However, the Dao Annihilation here is so calm. Unbelievable..."

If Li Fan's previous encounter with Dao Annihilation was like surging ocean waves, then the Dao Annihilation here, surrounded by the intentions of countless monks embodying rings, was like an extremely calm pond.

"The fused intention of the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm is less like a dam or a high wall, and more like steps outside a pond. It should have no ability to resist Dao Annihilation. However..."

Li Fan found an empty spot and sat down, mimicking the other cultivators.

The originally pitch-black space instantly became bright. The thoughts and voices of all the cultivators present echoed clearly and continuously. Wherever their thoughts reached, they could be observed.

And above the Dao Annihilation they circled, thousands of light spots of different colors floated!

Reflecting the Dao Annihilation catastrophe, which was full of deathly stillness, with a different kind of vitality.

When Li Fan's divine sense came into contact with these light spots floating above Dao Annihilation, he vaguely saw the scenes of countless worlds being born and destroyed.

Then, he suddenly understood.

"The characteristics of Dao Annihilation do not change. The reason why it does not exhibit violent fluctuations is because the contact between Dao Annihilation and the entire Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm has been distributed among these countless small worlds."

"Although they appear illusory, they are actually formed from the intentions of the peerless geniuses of this place, manifesting from illusion to reality. In a sense, they are no different from real worlds. They create targets in the void and proactively allow Dao Annihilation to devour them, breaking them down into countless parts to reduce the impact of Dao Annihilation."

Li Fan had instantly understood the survival method painstakingly crafted by the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm over a million years and through the efforts of countless generations.

"Profound Yellow Immortal Realm can also learn from this."

"With this set of protective measures, the shock experienced when colliding with the Mountains and Seas in the future will be greatly reduced. And the chances of successfully traversing the Mountains and Seas will increase."

"However, these worlds used as buffers, which are destined to be sacrificed, I cannot do that. And with the scale of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, the world intentions required are tens of thousands of times that of the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm. If I have to cultivate them from scratch, it will take too long..."

Li Fan's heart stirred, and he had already made up his mind: "Let me, in my boundless compassion, save you from this endless nightmare of reincarnation!"

In the fused intention space, the Li Fan who had infiltrated his body suddenly emitted boundless light, illuminating the gloomy place completely, and attracting the attention of all the figures present.

Everyone looked up and saw a magnificent world, faintly discernible within the light.

Four Heavenly Gates stood tall in the sky. Cultivators were like stars, dotting the void. On the vast land, there was vibrant life.

Compared to this magnificent world, their world instantly paled in comparison.

"What great fortune it is to be born in this world!" As soon as this thought arose, it spread like a virus, instantly infecting all the cultivators present.

Their eyes were fixed on the image of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm above Li Fan's head, and for a moment, they even forgot to pay attention to the Dao Annihilation in the center.

As if sensing their inner desires, a light ring resembling a gate suddenly appeared from the illusory scene.

Li Fan, who infiltrated first, leaped into it.

After a distortion of light and shadow, he actually entered that magnificent Immortal Realm!

Such a scene instantly shook the hearts of everyone present.

"What... what is going on?"

However, before their minds could fully process their confusion, sentiments like "How fortunate," "This is a divinely bestowed opportunity to attain the Dao," "Missing it will lead to lifelong regret," and "The example is right before us, there is no need to hesitate" swept over them like a storm.

At that moment, one-tenth of the figures followed Li Fan, entering the light and shadow.

"No! Small..." someone suddenly realized and wanted to shout a warning, but the moment they opened their mouth, their expression changed drastically. As if they had become someone else, they also slowly walked into the illusory passage.

Even though this was the culmination of a million years of inheritance in the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm, it could not withstand the incitement of a powerful expert like Li Fan.

In just a few breaths, a large portion of the cultivators in the fused intention had been forcefully taken away by Li Fan.

As for the remaining ones who were still struggling, Li Fan did not intend to let them go. He personally took action and guided them one by one into the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

Without these heavenly prodigies maintaining the world of intention and acting as sandbags to resist Dao Annihilation, the Dao Annihilation, which was originally as calm as a pond, became violently turbulent as if it had been boiled.

The Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm instantly fell into a precarious state.

Li Fan's manifested Profound Yellow light swelled, enveloping the entire Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm.

Before the out-of-control Dao Annihilation could completely swallow the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm, he transferred them all to the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

In the Lan Ke Daoist field, the block of space representing the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm thus became completely dead and dark, with no further gleam of life.

And in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, a group of new inhabitants appeared.

However, these new inhabitants, after arriving in a homeland they had never dared to imagine, quickly became even more devout than the original inhabitants of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

In the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm, there was already a savior "god" who had been worshipped by billions of people for a million years.

But now, the so-called "god" had materialized.

Thus, the people of the Immortal Ship quickly changed their faith and became fanatical believers of the [Primordial Yuan Profound Yellow World-Ruling Spiritual Sky Holy Venerable].

After all, they had truly been saved from a world that could be destroyed at any moment.

And the vast fused intention of the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm was also forcibly divided by Li Fan into countless figures.

"These heavenly prodigies, let alone comparing them to Su Bai and Chuan Fa, are not even as good as those on the Profound Yellow Investiture of the Gods."

"But they have their own unique value."

"If Chuan Fa and the others are the helmsmen and sailors of the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship, then these people are the buffer airbags distributed around the hull. The more, the better..."

"There is no place for them in the heavens. Then let them go to the Profound Yellow continent!"

These phantoms instantly received their orders and flew to various parts of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

They became "Earth Gods" and "River Gods" who controlled a region of mountains and waters, etc.

Responsible for promoting and maintaining the great image of the Profound Yellow Holy Venerable, while using the methods of the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm to select suitable seedlings within their jurisdiction. To continuously provide Li Fan with qualified buffer intentions.

In order not to affect the normal cultivation of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, they often chose from the intentions of those who had died or were about to perish.

"This is the path of the Yin God."

"Yin and Yang coexist, and the Immortal Ship will be safe."

Li Fan sat high above the heavens, and with a single thought, the world and the human realm underwent drastic changes.

This was the majesty of being the Profound Yellow Holy Venerable.

The addition of the Yin God cultivation system seemed to be a great tonic for the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

Li Fan clearly felt that the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, this great elixir, had become more stable and rounded.

The small cracks that had been spread across the Immortal Ship were slowly being filled.

The Profound Yellow Realm was showing signs of completeness.

This was an unexpected gain for Li Fan.

"It was just a casual act, but I didn't expect such a bonus."

"It seems that this path should have originally existed in the Mountains and Seas. But for some reason, it has vanished. Now that I have recreated it..."

"It seems that the ancient ships are more suitable for sailing in the Mountains and Seas." Li Fan looked towards the endless mountains and seas beyond the Profound Yellow heavens.

His gaze seemed to penetrate Dao Annihilation, resisting the infinite mortal worlds that had already been swallowed.

"When I first entered the Infinite Sea, I didn't know how to hide myself. I was actually discovered and attracted the attention of a being in the deep sea of the Infinite Sea, which was condensed from unimaginable ancient possibilities..."

"Perhaps only sufficiently ancient ships can traverse and sail into it."

"Hmm?" Just as Li Fan was contemplating the secrets of the Mountains and Seas, a slight anomaly from the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm below interrupted his thoughts.

Logically speaking, as the Profound Yellow Holy Venerable, Li Fan, who was high above, should not be attracted by mortal ants.

But at this moment, after witnessing what happened on the continent, Li Fan was beaming with joy, as happy as drinking a bowl of iced plum juice on a hot summer day.

He hadn't felt this relaxed in a long time.

The reason for this was precisely the devout immortal ship inhabitants.

In the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, although everyone revered the Hunyuan Profound Yellow World-Ruling Spiritual Sky Holy Venerable, because the world-altering changes had not long passed, most cultivators were still struggling to survive. Influenced by the past cultivation concept of transcending the mundane, people were more inclined to pin their hopes on their own cultivation breakthroughs.

On the Profound Yellow continent, temples worshipping the Profound Yellow Holy Venerable were actually not very numerous.

But after these immortal ship inhabitants arrived, things changed. In their eyes, the Holy Venerable's temples and statues were indispensable, far more important than their own lives as ants.

So wherever they went, temples of the Holy Venerable sprang up.

In addition to the traditional title of [Hunyuan Profound Yellow World-Ruling Spiritual Sky Holy Venerable], other titles also emerged.

Such as [Primordial Beginning Profound Yellow August Father] and [Primordial Profound Sage Heaven-Opening Great Sage], etc.

Although it had no lasting impact on Li Fan himself, with the cries of "Profound Yellow Father and Mother" echoing among the beings of heaven and earth, Li Fan keenly sensed that his connection with the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm had become even closer.

"As the saying goes: Father gives birth to heaven, and everything endures; Mother gives birth to earth, and heaven and earth last forever."

"It is precisely because of my existence as Father and Mother that the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm has reached its current state. Even if you can transcend and traverse the Mountains and Seas in the future, you must always remain beneath me." Li Fan said calmly.

A faint, imperceptible hum echoed throughout the Profound Yellow heavens and earth.

As if in response.

After the trip to the Immortal Ship's Ancestor Realm, the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm reached the Transcendent realm faster than expected.

"Perhaps, after consuming the Guangwu Star Sea, it will truly be complete."

A brilliant light flashed in Li Fan's eyes as he looked towards the distant Star Sea.

The Suo Xing Sea had already been swept clean by Li Fan over the past century. The remaining scattered True Immortals could be suppressed by the Dao Integration True Immortals within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

"Coincidentally, the path to the Guangwu Star Sea is submerged by Dao Annihilation. Let's test the quality of my Immortal Ship!"

This was the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship's first official encounter with Dao Annihilation, and also a rehearsal for traversing the Mountains and Seas.

Li Fan naturally attached great importance to it.

He set the date for a hundred years later. With a mere thought, he slightly relaxed the suppression of cultivators within the Profound Yellow heavens and earth.

Cultivation became easier, and within a few days, almost a star would rise from the continent.

The sparse Profound Yellow starry sky gradually became starry and splendid.

And the names on the Profound Yellow Investiture of the Gods increased day by day.

However, the number of Daoist fields in the outer heavens had not increased much.

As the first two cultivators to achieve Dao Integration, Chuan Fa and Su Bai had a very close relationship.

Especially before, the two had joined forces to explore the Suo Xing Sea.

Although they did not find the method of longevity they sought, their horizons were greatly broadened after battling several True Immortals.

"Brother Tuo, do you feel the changes in the world recently? Could it be that the so-called world-ending tribulation is coming?" Su Bai asked quietly, filled with worry.

Chuan Fa smiled and shook his head, "Brother Su, do not worry. I think it is because that person, having been too quiet, is restless."

He pointed to the sky with his finger and said quietly.

Su Bai's eyes narrowed, and then he understood. His worried expression, however, deepened. "Even so, for the beings of Profound Yellow, it is still a disaster, not a blessing."

"We have already explored the vicinity of the Guangwu Star Sea. There is no path forward, and nowhere to go. If changes occur again, we might..."

Chuan Fa and Su Bai exchanged glances, their hearts filled with alarm. "Ride the wind and waves, traverse Dao Annihilation!"

The Daoist field fell into silence for a long time.

After a long while, it was Chuan Fa who spoke, "Although sentient beings suffer, for us heavenly beings, it is a rare opportunity that comes once in ten thousand years. Not only can we go to other star domains, but more importantly, we can observe the waves of Dao Annihilation from within this realm!"

"Brother Su, you must understand that in the past, only Transcendent experts had such an opportunity."

Su Bai nodded, "I understand this principle. With Brother Tuo's talent, you might be able to observe Dao Annihilation and comprehend the Dao, taking that final step."

Chuan Fa laughed heartily, "In terms of talent, Brother Su, you are no less than me!"

Su Bai's expression remained unchanged, implicitly acknowledging this. He did not show any pride but murmured, "However, I always have a premonition. If we truly take that step, the outcome might not be very good."

Chuan Fa was slightly startled, "What are you saying, Brother Su? I don't have such a feeling."

Su Bai frowned, hesitating several times before finally shaking his head, "I can't explain it clearly either. It's just that whenever I recall the heart-pounding feeling I suddenly had that day, strange images always appear in my mind..."

Su Bai detailed his anomalies.

Chuan Fa pondered, as if understanding something.

Chapter 1590: Yellow Gate Crossing Dao Annihilation

Because of his ancestor King Xuantian and the mysterious "Grandfather," Chuan Fa knew more about the situation in other possibilities beyond Profound Yellow than other Dao Integration cultivators in Profound Yellow.

"Brother Su's condition seems to be sensing your other selves in other possibilities. The impact is so great, even..."

"Transcendent expert?"

Chuan Fa naturally understood the paths outside the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm's cultivation system, which he could not reach and had to reluctantly abandon. His ancestor Xuanyuan Hong was a powerful being of that realm.

For a moment, Chuan Fa looked at Su Bai before him, his heart filled with mixed emotions.

However, considering the fear Su Bai sometimes felt, Chuan Fa vaguely understood that having other Transcendent selves might not be a good thing.

After careful consideration, Chuan Fa still shared everything he knew with Su Bai.

Unexpectedly, after knowing all this, Su Bai's state of mind became calmer.

"So that's how it is." His expression was calm, and he let out a long sigh.

"My other selves..."

"If I'm not mistaken, when all my selves meet, one must be devoured. And I am currently the weaker one being eaten. All this fear comes from this."

Chuan Fa nodded slightly.

"If it's just this, then there's nothing to fear. At worst, I'll just stay here forever and not go out." Su Bai smiled with洒脱.

"The world we are in is already vast enough. Perhaps we will never be able to explore it fully in our lifetime. Why would we aspire to go further and step into the Mountains and Seas? Human desires are endless. Who knows if there are other Mountains and Seas beyond the Mountains and Seas? Where will the end be?"

"Moreover, I have a vague premonition. As long as we stay within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, perhaps we don't need to take that step ourselves to see all the Mountains and Seas." Su Bai said calmly.

Chuan Fa was stunned at first, unable to quickly grasp Su Bai's meaning. However, after pondering for a moment, he gradually understood, "Perhaps your premonition is correct."

The two men looked at the Daoist fields that were gradually appearing in the outer heavens with great tacit understanding, sensing an impending storm.

A hundred years passed in the blink of an eye.

The changes in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm were not significant. The Investiture of the Gods was almost full, the stars in the sky had increased, and the palace complexes in the outer heavens had taken shape.

On this day, the number of Profound Yellow cultivators who achieved Dao Integration and ascended reached the extreme of ninety-nine.

The number of named individuals on the Investiture of the Gods had already exceeded a thousand.

The stars in the sky were countless.

Li Fan sat in the center of the Profound Yellow Realm, looking at the world-traversing Immortal Ship he had built with his own hands, his satisfaction beyond words.

The feedback effect of the [Heavenly Sitting Technique] still existed. Moreover, due to the deepening connection between him and the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, the power he received in the past hundred years was even greater than when the Profound Yellow Realm had ascended and sublimated.

A phantom flickered in his palm, displaying the current state of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, filled with immortals.

"With these feedback phantoms, the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship has almost infinite backup repair energy. Even if a certain area is damaged, as long as the overall structure of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm remains intact, I can restore it instantly."

"Traversing mountains and seas, the confidence has increased several fold."

"Now that the time has come, let's see how the Immortal Ship performs when facing the tide of Mountains and Seas."

Li Fan stood up abruptly, as if standing at the prow of the Immortal Ship, looking towards the distant Guangwu Star Sea beyond the annihilation zone.

"Ride the wind and waves, the time is now!"

Within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, it remained motionless, as if unchanged from the past.

However, in reality, the entire world, along with the Lan Ke Daoist field, had transformed into a ship and had begun to move slowly.

However, the initial movement had already stirred up immense waves!

In the past hundred years, the Suo Xing Sea had long been swept clean by the Profound Yellow immortals, but it was also a place where life gathered. Now that the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship was setting sail, the Suo Xing Sea was like ice block in front of the ship's bow.

It was easily shattered.

Although the destruction was less severe than that caused by Dao Annihilation, it would likely take millions of years for life to re-emerge in this sea.

After shattering the Suo Xing Sea, they arrived at the border of the life-filled star sea.

There was no path forward, but Li Fan waved his hand and continued to control the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship, charging straight ahead.

The speed increased, and with a fierce collision against the void boundary, they slammed into it!

The Profound Yellow Immortal Ship flickered.

The massive world then disappeared, leaving behind only the devastated and ruined remnants of the Suo Xing Sea.

Without the support of the Shou Qiu phantom, this star field could no longer withstand the pressure of Dao Annihilation.

The reaction of Dao Annihilation was also swift. Wisps of black energy soon emerged from various parts of the Suo Xing Sea.

It seemed that this star field would not live to see the day when life would be restored.

At this moment, the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship seemed to have entered a storm, its hull shaking violently, appearing on the verge of disintegration!

Li Fan vaguely remembered that in his previous life, Zi Yi had merely made a casual gesture, and a path had been forcibly opened in the void swallowed by Dao Annihilation.

He had walked freely in the void of Dao Annihilation, without any danger.

However, when Li Fan attempted to traverse the Mountains and Seas himself, the situation was completely different.

Even though, theoretically, with the current configuration of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, it was absolutely capable of safely traversing.

But that was only in theory.

The Profound Yellow Immortal Ship, facing Dao Annihilation for the first time, encountered various situations that had not appeared in previous deductions.

The most obvious was the insidious erosion and impact of Dao Annihilation.

The Profound Yellow Immortal Realm was only close to perfection, not truly perfect. The cracks on the hull, although Li Fan had filled them as much as possible through various means, had not been completely eliminated.

The moment they entered Dao Annihilation, the corrosive power flowed into the Immortal Ship through these cracks.

The Profound Yellow Immortal Realm's sky instantly became like a black cloth covering it, turning dim and lightless.

Not only in the sky, but in every corner of the world, countless tiny black fissures appeared simultaneously, emitting terrifying auras.

This was the phenomenon of Dao Annihilation engulfing everything!

As the master of the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship, Li Fan, though alarmed, did not panic. He quickly instructed Ink Slaughter and the Dao-One Worms to patch these fissures as much as possible.

At the same time, he crushed a phantom in his palm.

Infinite energy surged from the shattered phantom, pouring towards various parts of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, like lightning illuminating the dim Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

With the rapid replenishment of backup energy, the Profound Yellow world itself began to evolve rapidly, regenerating the areas devoured by Dao Annihilation.

The fissures in heaven and earth slowly diminished, and the anomaly seemed to disappear immediately.

However, these repairs and patching actions ultimately could not fundamentally prevent the erosion of Dao Annihilation, and the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm still had imperfect cracks.

After being temporarily repelled, Dao Annihilation soon returned.

It generated numerous corrosive black fissures in different areas of heaven and earth.

With the experience of the first wave of response, Li Fan was even calmer. He methodically carried out the patching.

Thus, amidst this exchange, the sky of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm continuously alternated between dimness and brightness.

"One does not know one's own mediocrity until one personally enters the Mountains and Seas."

"I thought the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm was already near perfection, but I didn't expect so many flaws upon entering Dao Annihilation. Fortunately, I was well-prepared."

"And..."

Ink Slaughter and the Dao-One Worms, on which Li Fan had placed great hope, while rapidly adapting to survival in Dao Annihilation, were also attempting to repair the small cracks in the Immortal Ship.

"The fewer cracks, the smaller the waves."

"When the hull is perfect, traversing will be worry-free."

The Profound Yellow Immortal Realm was currently fine, but the situation of the beings within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm was not optimistic.

Traversing Dao Annihilation meant officially entering the Mountains and Seas.

As a result, in the world of alternating light and darkness, illusory visions of magnificent and continuous mountains and seas appeared from time to time.

Infinite Sea, Upper Mountain.

These were things Li Fan had gradually become accustomed to.

However, for the beings of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, they were still incredibly shocking existences.

More than nine-tenths of the life forms perished instantly upon seeing the Mountains and Seas, unable to withstand the pressure of the Mountains and Seas.

They disappeared and died too quickly, leaving no residual consciousness to be preserved by heaven and earth. There was not even a possibility of re-cultivating in the Yin God state.

The once vibrant Profound Yellow Immortal Realm instantly became desolate.

Seeing this tragic scene, Li Fan, as the Father and Mother of Profound Yellow, showed no emotional fluctuation on his face.

In his view, these lives that could not withstand even the first wave of ripples had no value to him.

Let them die.

With a single thought, new life quickly regenerated.

On the Profound Yellow continent, those who survived, with sufficient strength to serve as crew and sailors, were the ones worthy of attention.

Although they barely managed to keep their lives, the vast majority were in a state of extreme panic when faced with the intermittently flashing illusory visions of the Mountains and Seas.

"What... are these things?"

"In such vast Mountains and Seas, I am not even comparable to an ant! Not comparable at all!"

"The seas are overturned, and the mountains are inverted. They are about to crush us!"

"Is this what lies beyond Profound Yellow? The Holy Venerable above, the Holy Venerable above..."

Fear, terror, and panic consumed their minds. Countless fantasies appeared chaotically in their minds.

Even though they tried their best to remain calm, they could not protect their minds completely. Inevitably, they became delirious.

Moreover, it was like sinking into quicksand; once the fear of the Mountains and Seas was generated, it would only deepen. Initially, they could still resist, but eventually, they would be completely lost.

Just as all beings were in a state of constant fear and apprehension due to the awe-inspiring power of the Mountains and Seas,

A magnificent and majestic figure reappeared in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm's celestial dome.

It was the [Hunyuan Profound Yellow World-Ruling Spiritual Sky Holy Venerable]!

Unlike before, this time, the Holy Venerable looked down at the beings below, a trace of sorrow flashing in his eyes, and let out an inexplicable sigh.

The sound was like thunder, continuous and resounding through heaven and earth.

The Holy Venerable's colossal figure emitted infinite warm light.

Sound and light converged, as if leading the remaining living beings to a warm sanctuary. The terrifying illusory visions of the Mountains and Seas in their hearts slowly disappeared.

As their minds gradually regained clarity, all beings wept tears of joy, kneeling on the ground and chanting the Holy Venerable's merits.

However, they did not know that Li Fan had only acted out of consideration for the stability of the Immortal Ship. Those who could not face the pressure of the Mountains and Seas themselves had been placed on the list of those who could be abandoned at any time.

When they officially entered the Mountains and Seas and faced the impact of Dao Annihilation, requiring buffer materials, it would be their time to contribute themselves.

"Those who did not retreat in the face of the might of the Mountains and Seas numbered seven hundred and sixty-two."

"Those who could face it with equanimity numbered one hundred and sixty-seven."

"Those who even felt a spirit of courage and pushed forward bravely numbered as many as seventy-six."

"Very good. This is the foundation of our Profound Yellow Immortal Ship."

Being able to perceive the hearts of the Profound Yellow beings at any time, Li Fan was quite satisfied with the current outcome.

Although they were under the protection of the Immortal Ship and the Mountains and Seas they saw were not the true Mountains and Seas, in reality, these individuals had met the most basic mental requirement for traversing the Mountains and Seas.

"However, this is only the first wave of wind and waves."

"The real calamity is still ahead."

Li Fan thought silently.

If traversing Dao Annihilation were so simple, then the Mountains and Seas would have produced an unknown number of Transcendent experts over the years.

Based on Li Fan's understanding of Dao Annihilation, he knew that Dao Annihilation was extremely cunning and possessed its own offensive consciousness.

When it detected foreign objects floating in Dao Annihilation, it would soon launch a more violent offensive against them.

Until it completely devoured them.

"The longer one stays in Dao Annihilation, the harder it is to survive."

"Through countless waves, just one slip-up, and all previous efforts will be in vain!"

"Fortunately, the journey this time is not too far."

As Li Fan had predicted.

After a period of peace, the erosion of Dao Annihilation not only did not cease but became even more ferocious.

Not only were anomalies occurring everywhere in heaven and earth, but the entire world began to shake violently uncontrollably.

Mountains collapsing and rivers changing course were commonplace.

Furthermore, a large number of stars fell from the celestial dome.

These were the phenomena resulting from Nascent Soul cultivators of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm being unable to withstand the pressure and perishing.

Logically speaking, once one achieved the Nascent Soul realm, they would become immortal and coexist with the Profound Yellow world. However, in the current situation, the Profound Yellow world itself was in a crisis. The areas refined by Nascent Soul cultivators had unfortunately been devoured by Dao Annihilation.

Naturally, there was no hope of survival for them.

Only those on the Investiture of the Gods and those who had achieved Dao Integration could survive safely under the protection of the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship.

"The waves are indeed a bit too strong."

Li Fan stood between heaven and earth and said so.

This traversal could be described as quite ragged.

"Constantly repairing, it consumed three Profound Yellow Immortal Ship phantoms."

"But fortunately, we ultimately held on and did not disintegrate."

"Moreover, the overall state of the Immortal Ship remained intact. As long as we get out of Dao Annihilation, it can instantly return to its full state."

"Most importantly, the initial launch exposed all the flaws of the Immortal Ship. When we return to shore, I will refine it again, and the Immortal Ship will be truly perfect."

Li Fan was quite satisfied with the results of this traversal experiment.

"Rest and resupply here for now!"

The Guangwu Star Sea had arrived.

Chapter 1591: Heavenly Book Destroys Guangwu

The Profound Yellow Immortal Ship arrived at the Guangwu Star Sea, stirring a storm with a single stone!

The colossal Immortal Ship, which appeared without warning, shook the entire starry sky with its rapid impact.

In an instant, dozens of divine lights shot out from the depths of the Guangwu Star Sea to investigate the cause. Each figure that emerged exuded an aura indistinguishable from that of a True Immortal!

"In my previous life, Zi Yi pacified the Guangwu Star Sea, leaving behind over three hundred True Immortal Purple Talismans. There were also the nameless beings guarding the embankment."

"And within the Profound Yellow Realm, there are only ninety-nine Dao Integration cultivators. However..."

"The advantage is mine!"

With a casual wave of Li Fan's hand, a beam of light soared into the sky, instantly delineating the boundary between the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm and the Guangwu Star Sea, separating this small space from the Guangwu Star Sea.

The Guangwu True Immortals who came to investigate flew to the edge of this barrier, only to find themselves as if facing a vast chasm, unable to advance even half a step.

At the same time, within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, ninety-nine Dao Integration cultivators simultaneously flew out, meeting the Guangwu True Immortals head-on. Without a single wasted word, they unleashed their full killing moves from the outset.

The Profound Yellow Dao Integration cultivators, relying on the "momentum" of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm and the connection of the Four Heavenly Gates to the infinite, achieved the realm of "Immortal." The true strength they could unleash was actually slightly weaker than that of genuine Immortals, especially after leaving the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

But under Li Fan's signal, the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship suddenly erupted with infinite light and illusions, instantly enveloping the battlefield of the immortals. They suddenly felt as if they were fighting on their home turf, while the Guangwu True Immortals were suppressed by the Profound Yellow Heaven and Earth. With the power dynamics shifting and a numerical advantage, the outcome of the battle was not in much doubt.

After ascending to the Immortal Realm, it was not so easy to be killed or subdued. Generally speaking, even if they could not win, they could escape and preserve their lives. However, the Profound Yellow Dao Integration cultivators, each holding a "Immortal Binding Lock" bestowed by the Profound Yellow Saint Venerable, were instantly rendered like mortals with their divine abilities and powers lost once restrained by the Immortal Binding Lock, even for True Immortals. Thus, in this initial engagement, the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm side achieved victory with little effort.

Under Li Fan's instruction, these first batch of captured Guangwu True Immortals were all imprisoned in a nine-story exquisite Profound Yellow Pagoda manifested by the Outer Heavens. After all the captives were imprisoned, the pagoda gate closed with a bang. Moments later, the Profound Yellow Pagoda began emitting large amounts of Profound Yellow Qi. Half of this Profound Yellow Qi dissipated into the heavens and earth. The other half flew directly towards the Dao Integration cultivators.

As the Profound Yellow Qi entered their bodies, the Dao Integration cultivators' minds were instantly flooded with the cultivation memories and enlightenment insights of True Immortals! Although not complete, merely scattered fragments, for these cultivators who had just entered the Immortal Realm, it was undoubtedly a great tonic.

"Thank you, Saint Venerable, for your benevolence!" They said with sincere reverence and gratitude. They seized the time according to the Saint Venerable's instructions to digest the gains bestowed by the Profound Yellow Pagoda.

The so-called "Immortal Binding Rope" was essentially made of Infinite Power at its core, combined with various immortal formations. Though the refining method was simple and even somewhat crude, the power level was too high, naturally possessing a restraining effect on ordinary True Immortals. The exquisite Profound Yellow Pagoda, on the other hand, was filled with Ink Slaughter and Dao-One Worms. Once True Immortals were imprisoned within, Ink Slaughter and Dao-One Worms would devour them, feeding the True Immortal foundation back to the outside. "This is called 'fighting to sustain fighting.'"

The nourishment from over thirty True Immortals was, for the current Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, merely negligible. After suffering such a significant loss all at once, the Guangwu Star Sea was clearly stunned and remained silent for a long time. There was no further probing. However, it was evident that they would not let this matter rest.

Li Fan took advantage of this time to activate the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship's anchor, attempting to root it within the Guangwu Star Sea as much as possible. "Anchoring" was essentially the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm converting the spatial area belonging to the Guangwu Star Sea into its own use. Countless imperceptible Dao-One Worms at the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm's edge frantically burrowed out, gnawing at everything outside. These Dao-One Worms were like living Profound Yellow boundaries. At a visible speed, a layer of gray "armor" appeared around the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship.

"The Immortal Ship needs further refinement to reach its perfect state. These are the materials needed for refinement."

"Of course, this alone is far from enough."

In the Outer Heavens, above the Profound Yellow Pagoda, a giant transparent furnace reappeared, visible only to Li Fan. With a gentle flick of his finger, the furnace instantly expanded outwards, enveloping the entire Profound Yellow Immortal Ship. With a flash of yellow light, Loquat leaped onto the top of the furnace, protecting the Immortal Ship. The wisps of Profound Yellow Qi emitted from the Profound Yellow Pagoda, along with the starry sky devoured by the Dao-One Worms from the outside, converged and fused within the furnace. They transformed into wisps of ethereal mist, drifting towards the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship, revealing the many flaws in the areas exposed by the Dao Annihilation.

While presiding over the refinement, Li Fan's gaze frequently drifted towards the depths of the Guangwu Star Sea. "After such a long time, there's still no movement..."

"They shouldn't be afraid, but rather want to achieve everything in one fell swoop."

Just as Li Fan had predicted, after a period of calm lasting more than half a day, a beam of light swiftly came from the Guangwu Star Sea. In an instant, it arrived at the Profound Yellow boundary, outside the surging barrier of light. The beam of light stopped, revealing its true form within. It was a pearl that looked unremarkable.

"It's indeed you, the Dao Epoch Projection Pearl!"

As this thought flashed through Li Fan's mind, infinite light and shadow erupted, from the ancient past to eternal oblivion. All the Dao techniques and divine abilities ever used by any living being in all possibilities burst forth in this light and shadow. The brilliant, dazzling light enveloped the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm. At this moment, under the full outbreak of the Dao Epoch Projection Pearl, it could easily destroy an entire possibility!

However, since Li Fan already knew of the existence of the Dao Epoch Projection Pearl, how could he not be prepared? "Although the divine abilities are vast, one ship can navigate." Facing the siege of divine ability projections from countless different prodigies, Li Fan's expression remained unchanged. Calm and composed, he watched as the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm was simultaneously struck by countless projections. Just as when they entered the Dao Annihilation, the Profound Yellow Heaven and Earth violently trembled. This time, it was not a large-scale, intense tremor, but as if being struck by billions of hailstones simultaneously. The sound of small, dense explosions mingled with occasional, massive roars. The entire heaven and earth were submerged by these noisy sounds, akin to being trapped in a torrential downpour. The Profound Yellow Immortal Ship inevitably suffered damage. But under the blessing of the Eternal Great Dao and the feedback phantom of Li Fan's Heavenly Sitting Technique, all losses existed only for a fleeting moment before being rapidly repaired. Not only that. The "imprints" left by these Dao techniques and divine abilities striking within the Profound Yellow Realm were also recorded by the giant furnace that enveloped heaven and earth. The more powerful the divine ability and technique, the deeper the damage to the Profound Yellow Realm, and the more obvious the imprint left behind. Therefore, the easier it was to replicate. With a casual wave of Li Fan's finger, in the Outer Heavens, besides the Investiture of the Gods scroll, which recorded countless names, another long scroll slowly formed. As if countless brushstrokes were rapidly writing on the scroll, the divine abilities recorded within the Dao Epoch Projection Pearl were all replicated onto this scroll.

"The Dao Epoch Projection can only be used once."

"But my 'Myriad Dao Heavenly Scroll' can be used repeatedly." Li Fan extended his palm, and a phantom of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm floated towards the scroll. The originally illusory image, after absorbing the Profound Yellow phantom, rapidly solidified. Occasionally, streaks of lightning flashed, emitting extremely dangerous auras. The divine abilities contained within the Dao Epoch Projection Pearl were not inexhaustible. After cascading down like a torrential rain for a full three years, they were finally depleted. And when the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm emerged from the engulfing light and shadow, appearing completely unharmed, the Guangwu Star Sea fell into complete silence.

Before they could react, a scroll of heavenly scripture had already arrived. The heavenly scripture stretched for billions of miles, seemingly encompassing the entire Guangwu Star Sea. With a flash of light, infinite divine ability illusions emerged, pouring down like a torrential rain, instantly engulfing the Guangwu Star Sea. "Using one's own methods against oneself!" Li Fan chuckled lightly, crushing another phantom of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm in his palm. He then threw another scroll of heavenly scripture! The torrential rain intensified, turning black, completely obscuring the original appearance of the Guangwu Star Sea. Occasionally, fluctuations in aura seemed to struggle to break free from the divine ability projections. Li Fan immediately added another scroll of heavenly scripture. After nine scrolls of heavenly scripture were cast down, the Guangwu Star Sea had no remaining trace of resistance. And this continuous downpour of divine abilities lasted for twenty years. When Li Fan finally put away his divine abilities, the Guangwu Star Sea was a scene of utter devastation. Life was extinguished, filled with an aura of death and destruction. Ruins and remnants were everywhere. Occasionally, a few surviving heavenly pillars stood, but they were also scarred and battered.

With a movement of Li Fan's will, the Profound Yellow cultivators, who had been cooped up for too long, swarmed out. They began to clean up the battlefield. In the current state of the Guangwu Star Sea, even if there were nameless survivors, they would undoubtedly be in a critically injured and near-death state. It would not be difficult for the Profound Yellow cultivators to subdue them.

Li Fan paid no attention to these insignificant matters and headed straight for the embankment of the Guangwu Star Sea. As expected, a middle-aged man, whom he had seen once before and who was suspected to be the leader of the Guangwu Star Sea, also escaped to this place, ragged and stumbling. Sensing Li Fan behind him, the middle-aged man's eyes were filled with resentment: "We have no enmity, why do you strike such a deadly blow?"

"To possess treasure is already a crime. To hold a supreme treasure and not use it is an even greater sin!" Li Fan said coldly. He didn't even bother to ask for the other party's name and simply suppressed him. "After all, he is a nameless one; he cannot be wasted." "I see his Dao is 'Restoration.'" "Heh..." Li Fan shook his head indifferently. He then focused his attention on the center of the now severely damaged Guangwu Star Sea embankment. The bombardment of the nine scrolls of heavenly scripture seemed to have had no effect on the Dao Annihilation gathered there. Instead, the increasingly intense Dao fluctuations only made the Dao Annihilation more active.

"I did not sense the aura of that Transcendent remains."

"Even the Rat Emperor is not here."

"The Rat Emperor is hard to say, but judging from the expression displayed by 'Restoration' before his death, the Transcendent remains should have been salvaged by them at this point."

"They have likely returned them to the mountains and seas to lure other drifting foreign objects." Li Fan carefully sensed the Guangwu embankment again. Indeed, within the remaining heavenly pillars in the vicinity, he found faint, almost imperceptible connections, like threads, extending towards the central Dao Annihilation. "If I hadn't had the experience of traversing the Dao Annihilation before, I would have found it difficult to detect these 'threads.'" "They should also be crafted from the remains of Transcendent beings, or those who failed to transcend." After a period of judgment, Li Fan reached out and gathered these threads into his hand. Then, with a gentle pull... The other end of the threads remained motionless. Li Fan was not embarrassed and threw these threads towards the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm. The dense swarm of Dao-One Worms was responsible for connecting the threads to the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm. Then, amidst the roaring of heaven and earth, with the power of the entire Profound Yellow Heaven and Earth, they finally slowly pulled the threads. But in just an instant, Li Fan felt a colossal resisting force from the other end of the threads. Li Fan narrowed his eyes and instantly crushed dozens of Profound Yellow Immortal Realm phantoms. His strength surged, and the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship exerted immense force, dragging out the object from beneath the embankment, from within the vortex of Dao Annihilation! It was the Sea and Mountains lone sail remains that Li Fan had seen once before. However, compared to what he had seen previously, this corpse was more complete. This was the second Transcendent expert Li Fan had faced besides Evil Su Bai. Even though the other party had already fallen, Li Fan did not dare to be careless. Moreover... Something else was attached to his body. A black box, neither jade nor gold, adhered to the head of the Transcendent remains. The parts where they made contact seemed to have merged into one. It looked peculiar, as if a person had grown a black box for a head.

"I didn't see this thing in my previous life."

Li Fan was unsure if his premature salvage had changed anything. But regardless of what was contained within the black box, Li Fan would never let go of the Transcendent remains. Because he, rarely, felt the tremor of "True Return" again. "Hungry..." This was the faint fluctuation subtly transmitted by True Return. In his previous life, when he saw the Sea and Mountains lone sail within the Transcendent remains, True Return had subtly shown a desire to devour it. Seeing it again this time, even though it was in a deep slumber, it still sent a message to Li Fan. "Perhaps, if True Return can devour it, it can awaken from its slumber." This thought flashed through Li Fan's mind, and he immediately released Ink Slaughter to test it. Rolling dark clouds enveloped the Transcendent remains and the black box. However, Ink Slaughter, which had always been effective, suddenly hit a wall. It was as if it had bitten into solid steel. Although Ink Slaughter could devour, its speed of devouring... and its consumption were immense. Before it could achieve significant progress in devouring, the Ink Slaughter clouds themselves were consumed by more than half. It was a situation that had never occurred before. "As expected of a being that could drift in the Sea and Mountains Dao Annihilation until now."

Chapter 1592: Mountain and Sea Born Year Ring

Perhaps it was because of the extremely similar characteristics of Ink Slaughter and Dao Annihilation that it triggered the defense mechanisms of the Transcendent remains and the black box. Strange changes began to occur rapidly on both.

The originally smooth surface of the black box suddenly showed numerous protrusions, like countless grotesque and painful faces. As if stimulated by something, they churned madly, trying to drill into the remains' heads.

The Transcendent remains seemed oblivious to the intrusion of the black box, only reacting to the encroachment of Ink Slaughter. Accompanying a fierce wind blowing from an unknown source, a lone sail rose, carried by the wind. The Ink Slaughter clouds were instantly repelled by an unfathomable force of isolation. If it was like biting into a steel plate before, then with the appearance of this lone sail, an insurmountable barrier seemed to form between it and the remains. Previously, it could be slowly gnawed, sacrificing eight thousand of its own for a hundred of the enemy. Now, it was completely incapable of harming the other party!

The Guangwu Star Sea, which had gradually fallen into turmoil and destruction in a crisis due to the sudden demise of the various immortals, abruptly regained its calm with the appearance of this lone sail. It seemed to have drawn all the winds and waves from the Sea and Mountains. In the star sea, only this sail rustled; all other places were silent.

"This is the Dao of Transcendence..." Li Fan stared intently at the lone sail manifested within the remains, murmuring. This was the second time Li Fan had witnessed its existence. Because he had personally traversed the Dao Annihilation, Li Fan's perception of this lone sail was now even more profound.

"However, this sail is clearly much newer than the one I saw in my previous life."

"Logically speaking, mere tens of thousands of years should not have caused the Dao of Transcendence to corrode so quickly." Li Fan's gaze narrowed slightly, and he then looked at the black box attached to the head of the remains. As the Ink Slaughter clouds approached, the myriad writhing faces that appeared on the black box's surface now seemed like countless parasitic worms, trying to invade the lone sail.

The defenses of the lone sail, capable of traversing the Sea and Mountains and resisting Dao Annihilation, were naturally not something these worms could breach. However, this remains was not a true Transcendent expert. Although it still possessed Transcendent abilities, it was now merely a corpse. Even if it could block the attacks of billions of worms, it could not completely isolate all their erosion. And if even one worm managed to enter the lone sail...

Li Fan saw that within the small holes on the lone sail, a large number of grotesque faces were gathering.

"This black box can actually erode others' Dao of Transcendence." Li Fan exclaimed in surprise. "Perhaps the black box itself does not have the ability to traverse the Sea and Mountains, but by parasitizing on the Transcendent remains, it can still survive in the Dao Annihilation."

For Li Fan, the lone sail before him was of great use for the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship's traversal of the Sea and Mountains. How could he allow these worms to gnaw at it?

"Since Ink Slaughter cannot do it..."

"Then let's use Dao-One Worms!"

With this thought, the Ink Slaughter clouds retreated like a tide. They were replaced by an endless swarm of invisible Dao-One Worms.

This time, the situation was reversed. Without sensing the threat of Dao Annihilation, the lone sail within the Transcendent remains gradually vanished. Conversely, the black box seemed to genuinely perceive the countless Dao-One Worms surrounding it. The grotesque faces let out constant roars and growls, as if issuing a threat. Dao-One Worms, naturally, were not intimidated. They collectively charged towards the black box without fear.

In an instant, they swarmed and engulfed the black box like a tide. Li Fan clearly saw that the moment they came into contact with the faces on the black box's surface, a large number of Dao-One Worms seemed to evaporate, disappearing into thin air. And on the black box's surface, some faces were added as a result!

"Even Dao-One Worms can be absorbed and transformed... this black box." Li Fan narrowed his eyes. Under his command, Dao-One Worms continuously surged from the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

"If you like to swallow, then I'll let you eat your fill!" Unlike the power of the newborn Ink Slaughter, after Ink Slaughter was consumed, it needed a certain period to recover its vitality. However, as long as Li Fan was willing and had sufficient energy supply, Dao-One Worms could grow exponentially. The erosion and consumption of a mere wooden box were completely negligible for the swarm!

Like moths drawn to a flame, the Dao-One Worms launched continuous kamikaze attacks on the black box. The principle was the same as the black box's erosion of the lone sail. Even if the black box could block most of the swarm, as long as one Dao-One Worm broke through the blockade and formally came into contact with the black box's surface, the swarm's attack efficiency would double. And with the blessing of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm phantom in Li Fan's palm, the Dao-One Worm swarm had no need to worry about its own consumption.

With the advantage shifting, the black box gradually began to struggle. Its entire surface was filled with countless terrifying faces. There was no place for new faces to appear, and the black box trembled violently as if something was trying to break free from within!

Buzzing... When the black box's high-frequency vibration reached a certain threshold, it suddenly stopped. A faint light flashed, and all the faces that had appeared on the black box's surface were as if purified, all disappearing. The Dao-One Worms that had successfully invaded also completely vanished in this purification sweep. The black box returned to its original state, as if all previous efforts had been in vain!

Not only that, but the very nature of the black box seemed to have changed inexplicably. The smooth advance of the Dao-One Worms was also hampered, as if facing something completely different, requiring a large number of "corpses" to explore again.

However, Li Fan feared consumption the least! Li Fan's will remained unchanged, and the Dao-One Worms' offensive would not weaken in the slightest. Slowly, the black box's surface was again filled with countless grotesque faces. The familiar scene replayed, a faint light flashed, and everything returned to its original state. The black box changed its appearance again.

However, a smile appeared on Li Fan's face. Because through these two observations, Li Fan was certain that the purifying and self-altering faint light emanating from the black box was consumed each time it activated.

"Then let's see who has the deeper foundation." Li Fan let out a cold snort and instantly crushed several Profound Yellow Immortal Realm phantoms. Empowered by the strength, the Dao-One Worm swarm's offensive became even more ferocious. The faint light flashes on the black box's surface appeared more and more frequently.

Li Fan watched as if he were an observer, watching the two armies battle. "I don't know what the essence of this black box is. Its foundation is even superior to my Profound Yellow Immortal Ship."

"If it weren't for the power of the feedback phantom from the Heavenly Sitting Technique, I might not have been able to compete with it." Li Fan frowned slightly and a tiny wood chip floated to his fingertip. It was a small piece gnawed off the black box by the Dao-One Worm swarm through relentless effort. From the outside, the black box appeared uniformly dark, but when peeled off, its color was like the brilliant blue sky.

"Interesting." Li Fan threw this piece of blue light into the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm and slowly refined it using the Dao refinement method. As wisps of blue Qi rose from the wooden block and were absorbed by the world, the distance between heaven and earth in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm increased slightly.

"Power of World Growth?"
