The Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao, which had long submitted to Li Fan's overwhelming power and dared not express its self-awareness, requested Li Fan for the first time in a long while. It seemed this blue Qi was a rare and potent supplement for it, comparable to the methods used during its ascension and sublimation. Since absorbing the blue Qi was beneficial to the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship, there was no reason to refuse this request.

The entire block of blue wood was thrown into the furnace, and the alchemy fire instantly blazed. The blue Qi drifted and reappeared in the Profound Yellow Heaven and Earth after being refined. This time, there were no beneficiaries among the beings in the Profound Yellow Realm. Only the Profound Yellow Heaven and Earth itself grew and absorbed it wantonly. And in Li Fan's eyes, the deck and hull of the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship gradually took on a touch of blue. As the material of the entire Immortal Ship changed, the sturdiness of its hull took another step forward.

"This is only a very small piece from the black box." Li Fan stared at the remaining part of the black box, his heart skipping a beat. "If I could completely refine and absorb it..." However, Li Fan also understood the principle of not rushing. Even if he could refine the entire black box, it would not be advisable to feed it all to the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm at once. While strengthening the Immortal Ship was a good thing, it had to be done gradually. Suddenly becoming too strong carried the risk of losing control. Furthermore, given the mysterious nature of this black box, it might possess the ability to resurrect from a corpse, and caution was needed to verify this.

Next, Li Fan directly poured the blue Qi absorbed by the Dao-One Worms into one of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm phantoms in his palm. With the blessing of the blue Qi, the phantom showed signs of slowly solidifying. Various phenomena within the world were lifelike, no different from the actual world, like a miniature sculpture.

The Ink Slaughter clouds, which had been injured and retreated previously, quietly appeared beside Li Fan. Li Fan threw this blue Profound Yellow wood carving to Ink Slaughter. He hoped that through Ink Slaughter's devouring and analysis abilities, he could understand the details of the black box. If it were the complete black box itself, it might be able to resist Ink Slaughter to a certain extent. However, this detached fragment was no match for Ink Slaughter.

Smoothly, the Ink Slaughter clouds devoured the wood carving. After a brief silence, the clouds churned turbulently. In a very short time, they rapidly expanded by about a third. As if having eaten its fill, Ink Slaughter's feedback finally arrived. A series of blurry images flashed through Li Fan's mind. It was the process of the birth of a possibility from the Sea and Mountains.

In the Sea and Mountains, countless possibilities existed. As the Sea and Mountains merged, these possibilities were fading. But in the past, many possibilities had evolved from nothingness to existence, originating from the Sea and Mountains. Even the Sea and Mountains themselves were growing and changing. Different stages of the Sea and Mountains evolved into distinct possibilities. It was like concentric rings of Sea and Mountains, which, to some extent, could reflect the state of the Sea and Mountains themselves.

"This blue Qi comes from the possibilities that evolved during the initial stage of the wild growth of the Sea and Mountains."

"There, not only was there no Immortal Realm, but there weren't even animals or humans. Everything visible was the most primal life form, green algae covering the entire world."

"But their vitality was comparable to that of ordinary True Immortals..." Li Fan saw that as the Sea and Mountains grew, this ancient possibility perished. But the green algae covering the world did not disappear. Instead, it settled, was squeezed into the depths of the Sea and Mountains, and merged with other possibilities. Like undying ghosts, they stubbornly survived, witnessing the birth and destruction of one possibility after another. All the possibilities they had experienced, the existences with vitality similar to them, were absorbed by them, becoming a part of them. Thus, they transformed from simple green algae into something more complex in composition. However, they were not the true Dao of Longevity.

After an unimaginably long time, they also slowly declined from prosperity to decline. Each possibility they parasitized on was a devastating blow to them. Not to mention, the Sea and Mountains began to merge. They could escape the changes of the Sea and Mountains themselves, but they could not escape the calamity of Dao Annihilation. Since they could not help themselves, driven by the survival instinct cultivated over countless years, they began to search for beings capable of surviving such a calamity. Transcendent experts in the Sea and Mountains. However, those who could traverse the Dao Annihilation were not beings that ancient relics like them could contend with. Thus, they had to settle for the next best thing, targeting the Transcendent remains drifting in the Sea and Mountains. The lone sail was not the first target they had parasitized. Before this, they had successfully borrowed seven drifting objects, and the newly discovered lone sail was the strongest and most suitable for parasitism. Everything proceeded smoothly, until the lone sail remains were forcibly dragged out of the Dao Annihilation by Li Fan.

Chapter 1593: Wind and a Sail Hang

The object before Li Fan’s eyes, which had turned from dark green to pitch black, was the accumulation of an ancient Mountain and Sea relic across countless possibilities. It had long since transcended the category of the primitive green algae form.

"It possesses no realm, cultivation base, divine abilities, or spells. Relying solely on the powerful survival instinct tempered over eons, it could invade the Transcendent Path of a Transcendent expert..." Li Fan couldn't help but marvel.

Yet, such an existence that he praised so highly was now slowly being transformed into nourishment for the further evolution of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm under the suicidal siege of the Dao-One Worms.

Taking a total of three years, the black box was completely consumed to fully charge and solidify sixty-seven illusory projections of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

"With these reserves, the structural strength of the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship can rise to another level. My confidence in traversing the Mountains and Seas has increased further."

Sixty-seven azure wood carvings sat in Li Fan’s palm. After a moment of contemplation, he crushed one of them. He attempted to directly use his own physical body to absorb the azure energy slowly overflowing from the carving.

After being absorbed and converted by the Dao-One Worms, the consciousness belonging to the ancient Mountain and Sea relic had completely vanished, leaving only pure, condensed vitality. Li Fan had already verified this on the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm itself, so he dared to absorb it with his true body.

"Furnace of Creation, Great Dao Manifestation."

As the azure energy was slowly inhaled, a smear of crimson appeared on Li Fan’s cheeks. Countless tiny thundering impacts resounded from all parts of his body. Using two great body-refining secret arts in tandem, Li Fan attempted to turn the abilities of the ancient Mountain and Sea relic into his own.

Although Li Fan’s Transcendent Path was currently defined as the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship—and as the "Father and Mother of Profound Yellow," he possessed absolute control over this Transcendent vessel he had built—this control was increasing daily due to the worship of countless living beings within the realm. Once he steered the ship across the Mountains and Seas, the vessel would completely become his path.

But just like True Return (还真), until it truly became his own inherent ability, there was always the risk of "losing" it at any moment. Li Fan had to plan ahead and add another layer of insurance for himself.

"Even if the traversal fails in the future and the Immortal Ship is destroyed, I will be able to survive calmly after jumping off the ship."

Every tiny particle of his body seemed to transform into a furnace supporting the heavens. The imprints engraved on these furnaces were left by the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net, ceaselessly absorbing the azure energy of the ancient relic to temper and remodel his flesh and blood.

As if swallowing many potent tonics at once, Li Fan felt his blood and energy churning violently. His heart thundered, seemingly ready to leap out of his chest. Only by personally "tasting" it could he have a truly concrete understanding of the vitality contained within this ancient Mountain and Sea relic.

"This vitality is somewhat different from the 'Life' of the Great Dao of Longevity. It is more about adaptation, evolution, and survival."

Li Fan’s body already had a small amount of residual power from the Great Dao of Longevity. Now, after absorbing this new power of life, he found there was no conflict between the two. In fact, as the residual power of Longevity merged with the survival power of the ancient relic, it became stained with azure, showing a unique transformation.

Though it still fell under the category of the Great Dao of Longevity, it seemed to have opened a completely new branch, becoming distinct.

"This is..."

Li Fan was a person who had once almost completely "attained the Dao of Longevity." His understanding of "Longevity" within the Mountains and Seas was second only to Lord Shou Qiu. Savouring it carefully now, he understood the reason for the mutation of the Longevity power within him.

"Lord Shou Qiu shares Longevity; he never minded juniors bringing forth new ideas or opening different branches. He even encouraged it—gathering under Longevity to let a hundred flowers bloom, each showing their own divine abilities. When the path matures, one can even break away from the main path of Longevity to establish a new sect and achieve a completely new Dao..."

"Lord Shou Qiu truly deserves the name 'Abundant Virtue' (盛德)," Li Fan lamented. To consider his disciples' futures so thoroughly, Lord Shou Qiu was likely the number one teacher in the Mountains and Seas.

Absorbing the azure energy of the ancient relic even helped in expelling the residual Longevity power from his body. After realizing this principle, Li Fan no longer had any reservations. He pushed his body to its absolute limit to absorb and refine the azure energy.

In any case, a single "Profound Yellow Wood Carving" was enough to satisfy his body-refining needs and wouldn't affect the strengthening of the Immortal Ship. With sufficient raw materials, the Furnace of Creation and Great Dao Manifestation arts could operate on instinct. Li Fan simply activated them and stopped paying excessive attention.

Instead, he focused his attention on the remaining objective of this harvest: the Transcendent Remains.

After removing the ancient Mountain and Sea relic that had been latched onto its head, the fallen Transcendent expert finally revealed his true face. His features looked as if he were still alive, merely fallen into a deep slumber. He was quite handsome, with an indescribable air of freedom between his brows. Only the small blood-colored hole at the center of his forehead, gnawed by the relic, was jarringly inconsistent.

Currently, without the stimulation of Dao Annihilation, the Transcendent intent within the remains did not manifest. Li Fan did not act recklessly or use Ink Slaughter to force out that "Lone Sail of the Mountains and Seas."

"The Dao-One Worms still need a period to adapt and evolve."

Li Fan was very patient. This was both a reminder to himself and a comfort to True Return. Since clearing the threat of the ancient relic, the "Lone Sail" was completely exposed, and True Return’s desire for it came in waves, far stronger than when he had glimpsed it from afar in his previous life.

"Mainly because in the previous life, Zi Yi was by my side, and True Return had reservations. Now, this Transcendent intent belongs to me alone. Moreover, True Return is still in a state of heavy slumber from its injuries and desperately needs this Transcendent intent to repair itself."

Li Fan understood this in his heart but did not lose his composure. He waited unhurriedly for the Dao-One Worms to completely digest and adapt to the ancient relic.

During the wait, the Profound Yellow immortals had unexpected gains while cleaning up the battlefield of the Guangwu Star Sea. Besides finding the "Dao Sword" and "Dao Blade" seen in the previous life, they discovered three other powerful Dao Treasures that hadn't been used in time.

They were: a severed stone hand, a blood-stained azure robe full of holes, and a withered yellow tree branch. All were remnants of other possibilities that had perished in Dao Annihilation. Li Fan glimpsed the history of the extinction of three possibilities from these items. However, having seen many such things now, he was no longer surprised. Though powerful, these items were of no use to the current Li Fan. He tossed them into the Outer Heavens of Profound Yellow as spares.

Once everything was prepared, Li Fan officially began the theft of the "Lone Sail of the Mountains and Seas." This Transcendent intent was something Zi Yi had personally made a trip to take in the previous life, indicating it had value even to Transcendent experts. Li Fan naturally treated it with the utmost caution.

He dismissed all the Profound Yellow immortals back into the realm. Standing alone, Li Fan faced the Transcendent Remains.

"Ink Slaughter!"

With a thought, the rolling clouds of Ink Slaughter surged forth. The aura, identical to Dao Annihilation, instantly forced out the "Lone Sail" suspended within the remains.

As the Lone Sail appeared, the winds and waves stilled. It was as if a giant invisible hand had pressed down heavily on the clouds of Ink Slaughter. The boundless, churning clouds completely calmed down. Ink Slaughter naturally tried to resist, but no matter how the clouds shifted, they could not damage the sail in the slightest. At most, they caused the sail to sway slightly.

Li Fan observed the power of this Lone Sail through the perspective of Ink Slaughter.

"Though the Mountains and Seas are far, I cross them with a single sail."

"One who possesses such ambition and perseverance is definitely a peerless genius. A pity he died so silently amidst the Mountains and Seas."

Unlike Zi Yi’s overbearing and exclusive Path to Heaven, the Lone Sail before him was not so domineering. From this sail, Li Fan sensed a trace of "carrying together" (同载) intent.

"If we meet by chance in the Mountains and Seas, and my light boat has not capsized, what harm is there in giving you a ride..."

A faint laugh seemed to echo in his ears, making Li Fan freeze slightly.

"This person was quite heroic. Even I wouldn't mind making friends with him. It’s just a pity... I wonder exactly how he died."

Li Fan couldn't help but feel a sliver of doubt. The Lone Sail was not completely damaged. It had enough strength to resist Dao Annihilation; he shouldn't have died.

"Dao-One..."

To pry into this secret, it was time for the Dao-One Worms to take the stage. The familiar scene replayed once more, but this time, it wasn't the ancient relic eroding the remains—it was the boundless swarm of worms!

The erosion of the Dao-One Worms was even more efficient than that of the ancient relic.

Whoosh...

A whistling sound echoed, and Li Fan’s vision blurred as if he had fallen into a vast ocean. Other than this ocean and a lone boat, there was nothing else. Around him, sometimes fierce winds howled, sometimes it was calm, and sometimes it rained incessantly. Yet the lone boat remained exceptionally stable, sailing forward.

"This is... the memory of the Transcendent remains when he was traversing the Mountains and Seas in life."

Li Fan’s heart stirred, and he observed closely. The ocean before him seemed to have no end. The scenes in the memory were almost entirely repetitive—endless ocean vistas.

The original owner of the sail had an exceptionally steady state of mind. It was Li Fan, the bystander, who gradually became restless because this journey was simply too long.

"This isn't right. How could traversing to other possibilities take this long?"

Li Fan looked into the distance, trying to find traces of other possibilities. After an unknown amount of time, he finally saw some blurry images on the distant horizon—likely the locations of other possibilities. But the Lone Sail seemed completely oblivious, ignoring them and continuing to sail forward steadily.

"I observed them; the owner of the remains couldn't have missed them. So..."

A moment later, Li Fan understood. Ordinary possibilities were not what he sought. Transcendence—what is transcendence? It is leaving the common mortal world to head toward the legendary "Other Shore."

Li Fan stared blankly at the boundless ocean. Where exactly was the Other Shore?

People he had encountered—Zi Yi, the Black Physician, Evil Su Bai—all came and went in an instant. Li Fan had naturally assumed that the distance to the Other Shore was not far. As long as one had the strength to cross the Mountains and Seas, one could naturally go there.

But now, it seemed... the truth was not so.

By now, Li Fan had a vague guess as to the cause of the Lone Sail's death, but he still needed the full memories to confirm it. As the Dao-One Worms persevered in their invasion, the memories of the Lone Sail flooded in like a tide.

The owner of the Lone Sail must have been an extremely peaceful person in life. Li Fan felt no hostility from the memories; instead, it felt like a spring breeze, refreshing to the soul. Even facing an endless ocean, he remained so.

He sailed alone in the Infinite Sea like this, his broad-mindedness not diminishing in the slightest due to the hopeless situation. Even though this ocean was vast beyond imagination—even Li Fan, watching from a bystander's perspective, began to feel despair—the Lone Sail remained optimistic.

"At least, I have seen and personally traveled this ocean."

The faint laughter echoed in his ears again. The Lone Sail continued to sail; there was no end ahead.

...

Li Fan actively withdrew from the Lone Sail's memories. Not everyone possessed such a broad-minded temperament—at least, the current Li Fan did not. Especially knowing the outcome of the Lone Sail—knowing there was destined to be no end ahead.

Staying submerged in the Lone Sail's memories for too long caused irritability and hostility to rise in Li Fan’s heart. His state of mind became unbalanced, and murderous intent surged. It reminded him of when he traveled upstream in the River of Time and almost lost himself.

"However, at least I had many familiar things at past time nodes to serve as lighthouses and beacons for navigation. But the Lone Sail, sailing on the Infinite Sea, had nothing at all. Only a blurry direction..."

Re-entering the memories, Li Fan chose not to immerse himself but to skim through, looking only for key points.

The result: there were no "key points." Or rather, that high-hanging Lone Sail was everything.

Until the Dao-One Worms completely broke through the defenses of the Transcendent intent and Li Fan mastered all the memories within. The scenes didn't change much.

Until the Lone Sail died of old age on the Infinite Sea.

It was difficult for Li Fan to estimate exactly how long that period of time was. It must have been an extremely vast span of time. It was a duration so long that even a powerhouse who could calmly face the Dao Annihilation of the Mountains and Seas could not overcome it.

"Transcendent experts... still have an end?"

Li Fan first found it somewhat unbelievable. At the same time, he truly realized the weight of Lord Shou Qiu’s "Great Dao of Longevity."

"However, the lifespan of a Transcendent expert must be extremely long. So..."

In a daze, Li Fan began to understand. The era the Lone Sail powerhouse lived in might have been the ancient period when the "Other Shore" was first being established. At that time, Transcendents were few, and few knew where the Other Shore was. They could only rely on a vague sense of direction to head there themselves.

As pioneers, naturally, no one could guide them. Thus, he had been lost and drifting in the Mountains and Seas until today.

Chapter 1594: The Truth Is Temporarily Awakened

The object before Li Fan’s eyes, which had turned from dark green to pitch black, was the accumulation of an ancient Mountain and Sea relic across countless possibilities. It had long since transcended the category of the primitive green algae form.

"Dao-One..."

To pry into this secret, it was time for the Dao-One Worms to take the stage. The familiar scene replayed once more, but this time, it wasn't the ancient relic eroding the remains—it was the boundless swarm of worms!

The erosion of the Dao-One Worms was even more efficient than that of the ancient relic.

Whoosh...

A whistling sound echoed, and Li Fan’s vision blurred as if he had fallen into a vast ocean. Other than this ocean and a lone boat, there was nothing else. Around him, sometimes fierce winds howled, sometimes it was calm, and sometimes it rained incessantly. Yet the lone boat remained exceptionally stable, sailing forward.

"This is... the memory of the Transcendent remains when he was traversing the Mountains and Seas in life."

Li Fan’s heart stirred, and he observed closely. The ocean before him seemed to have no end. The scenes in the memory were almost entirely repetitive—endless ocean vistas.

The original owner of the sail had an exceptionally steady state of mind. It was Li Fan, the bystander, who gradually became restless because this journey was simply too long.

"This isn't right. How could traversing to other possibilities take this long?"

Li Fan looked into the distance, trying to find traces of other possibilities. After an unknown amount of time, he finally saw some blurry images on the distant horizon—likely the locations of other possibilities. But the Lone Sail seemed completely oblivious, ignoring them and continuing to sail forward steadily.

"I observed them; the owner of the remains couldn't have missed them. So..."

A moment later, Li Fan understood. Ordinary possibilities were not what he sought. Transcendence—what is transcendence? It is leaving the common mortal world to head toward the legendary "Other Shore."

Li Fan stared blankly at the boundless ocean. Where exactly was the Other Shore?

People he had encountered—Zi Yi, the Black Physician, Evil Su Bai—all came and went in an instant. Li Fan had naturally assumed that the distance to the Other Shore was not far. As long as one had the strength to cross the Mountains and Seas, one could naturally go there.

But now, it seemed... the truth was not so.

By now, Li Fan had a vague guess as to the cause of the Lone Sail's death, but he still needed the full memories to confirm it. As the Dao-One Worms persevered in their invasion, the memories of the Lone Sail flooded in like a tide.

The owner of the Lone Sail must have been an extremely peaceful person in life. Li Fan felt no hostility from the memories; instead, it felt like a spring breeze, refreshing to the soul. Even facing an endless ocean, he remained so.

He sailed alone in the Infinite Sea like this, his broad-mindedness not diminishing in the slightest due to the hopeless situation. Even though this ocean was vast beyond imagination—even Li Fan, watching from a bystander's perspective, began to feel despair—the Lone Sail remained optimistic.

"At least, I have seen and personally traveled this ocean."

The faint laughter echoed in his ears again. The Lone Sail continued to sail; there was no end ahead.

...

Li Fan actively withdrew from the Lone Sail's memories. Not everyone possessed such a broad-minded temperament—at least, the current Li Fan did not. Especially knowing the outcome of the Lone Sail—knowing there was destined to be no end ahead.

Staying submerged in the Lone Sail's memories for too long caused irritability and hostility to rise in Li Fan’s heart. His state of mind became unbalanced, and murderous intent surged. It reminded him of when he traveled upstream in the River of Time and almost lost himself.

"However, at least I had many familiar things at past time nodes to serve as lighthouses and beacons for navigation. But the Lone Sail, sailing on the Infinite Sea, had nothing at all. Only a blurry direction..."

Re-entering the memories, Li Fan chose not to immerse himself but to skim through, looking only for key points.

The result: there were no "key points." Or rather, that high-hanging Lone Sail was everything.

Until the Dao-One Worms completely broke through the defenses of the Transcendent intent and Li Fan mastered all the memories within. The scenes didn't change much.

Until the Lone Sail died of old age on the Infinite Sea.

It was difficult for Li Fan to estimate exactly how long that period of time was. It must have been an extremely vast span of time. It was a duration so long that even a powerhouse who could calmly face the Dao Annihilation of the Mountains and Seas could not overcome it.

"Transcendent experts... still have an end?"

Li Fan first found it somewhat unbelievable. At the same time, he truly realized the weight of Lord Shou Qiu’s "Great Dao of Longevity."

"But Transcendent experts' lifespans are surely extremely long. So..."

In a daze, Li Fan began to understand. The era the Lone Sail powerhouse lived in was likely the ancient period when the "Other Shore" was first being established. At that time, Transcendents were few, and few knew where the Other Shore was. They could only rely on a vague sense of direction to head there themselves.

As pioneers, naturally, no one could guide them. Thus, he had been lost and drifting in the Mountains and Seas until today.

Chapter 1595: The Primordial Beginning Gives Birth to Life

"The Primordial possibility is likely unable to hold on much longer." Li Fan stood on the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship, gazing into the distance, having observed for a long time. He had reached this conclusion. Compared to ten years ago, the situation in the Primordial Starry Sky was vastly different. Whether any life still existed was a separate matter; the most crucial point was that its overall stability had drastically declined.

If before, the surviving life-filled starry skies of the Primordial realm were like countless scattered islands surrounded and divided by the Sea of Dao Annihilation, where the islands, with themselves as barriers, could barely maintain survival against occasional waves, then now, a monstrous tsunami was brewing in the Sea of Dao Annihilation. It was almost predictable that in the face of this tsunami that would engulf everything, all these islands would cease to exist.

"Fortunately, the Immortal Ship is almost complete. Even if the Primordial realm perishes, it will have no impact on me." Li Fan's actions of conquering star seas, plundering resources, and forging the ship's body had proceeded smoothly. However, his comprehension of the Loneliness Sail of the Mountains and Seas was somewhat unsatisfactory. It was not due to Li Fan's lack of understanding, but rather because Li Fan's disposition was too different from that of the Loneliness Sail. "If we were to meet by chance in the Mountains and Seas, and my small boat had not capsized, what harm would there be in carrying you along..." Li Fan savored the meaning of these words, and after a long while, he shook his head slightly. "Given my temperament, I would at least charge a boat ticket."

However, even if it went against his inner instincts, Li Fan was willing to change his thinking to fully comprehend the transcendent true intent of the Loneliness Sail. "The resources plundered by the Immortal Ship over these years are more than ample, even saturated. Next, let's try being a good person."

On the Sea of Dao Annihilation, waves churned. Yet, the Immortal Ship, like a phantom, quietly traversed. Compared to the earth-shattering might displayed during every voyage ten years ago, the current safety was a greater testament to the Immortal Ship's ability to navigate Dao Annihilation. "As the saying goes, 'Great skill requires no adornment!'" Li Fan softly chanted. The moment the carpenter's work was finished, the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship had once again pierced through Dao Annihilation, arriving in a new sea of surviving life.

"This time, we traversed through Dao Annihilation for a full half-year." "It's too far from the already perished Guangwu Star Sea, with no communication between them. This is a completely unfamiliar domain..." Even so, Li Fan's heart remained utterly unperturbed. The closer he got to the realm of transcendence, the more equal all beings appeared in his eyes. The nameless, True Immortals, and mortals were all the same.

The arrival of the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship did not attract the attention of the beings in this star sea. They were currently in a state of panic and despair, facing the sudden onset of tribulation. This star sea had no name. In their perception, they should have been the only surviving starry sky in the lower realms. When the Immortal Realm was destroyed, twelve True Immortals collectively fled to this place. After many years, under the protection of the True Immortals, the mortal civilization not only did not decline but flourished even more. Among the twelve True Immortals, half had even ascended to the Nameless Realm. The True Immortals had also attempted to search for traces of their companions, but despite possessing the power of the Nameless, they were still unable to traverse Dao Annihilation. Trapped on this isolated island, they began to seek a method to leave the Primordial possibility. However, before they could make any headway, the catastrophe of Dao Annihilation suddenly went out of control. The waves began to rise, with the momentum to engulf them in an instant.

At this moment, the twelve True Immortals gathered once more, discussing countermeasures. In this mortal star sea, their presence was so conspicuous that Li Fan, who had just arrived, saw them at a glance. Thus, he secretly spied on them. These twelve True Immortals seemed to have an extremely good relationship. Even though six of them had achieved the Nameless Realm, they did not divide into superior and inferior factions; there was a different order. This was because the one they called "Big Brother" was merely an ordinary True Immortal.

"Dao Annihilation is truly unreasonable. According to our observations and deductions, it should have at least another ten thousand years of stable existence, enough for all of us brothers to become Nameless. But now... the situation has collapsed too quickly!" "Dao Annihilation, Dao Annihilation. It reminds me of the terrifying scene of the Immortal Realm's destruction when Dao Annihilation suddenly arrived." "It was indeed our carelessness. Think about it, weren't most of the Immortals in the Immortal Realm as optimistic as us back then? They even wanted to resist and tame Dao Annihilation... No one expected it to come so quickly."

"Seventh Brother is right, Dao Annihilation is unpredictable and cannot be theorized by the norm. The current situation is likely the same as that year, with Dao Annihilation descending and being irreversible. The key is how to find a path to survival." As the Immortals spoke, they all turned their gazes towards "Big Brother." The leader of the twelve True Immortals was a dwarf elder. His beard and hair were all white, and he was full of vigor, but his physique was like that of a child. When he spoke, his voice was a combination of old and young tones, sounding quite strange. "The original plan was for us brothers to work together, using the twelve Nameless beings to achieve transcending methods and seek a sliver of hope for survival. Now, there is definitely not enough time. But we brothers have already made an oath: we do not ask to be born in the same year, month, and day, only to die in the same year, month, and day. You six, who have become Nameless, will certainly not abandon us."

"The only way forward now is to take a risk. If all twelve become Nameless, we have a sixty percent chance of survival. If only half achieve the Nameless Realm, the chance of survival plummets to one percent..." "One percent... so high, we can indeed try!" "Yes, yes! If it fails, we'll just perish in Dao Annihilation. Anyway, we've lived long enough, so it's about time." The twelve True Immortals were not intimidated by the bleak prospects; instead, their emotions were unusually excited. It was as if the chance of survival was not one percent, but ninety-nine percent.

The elder coughed lightly, suppressing the crowd's excited mood. "Although that's said, we still need to find a way to maximize our safety." "This star sea, we have managed for tens of thousands of years and have already achieved a considerable scale. Although no one has achieved True Immortal status, if utilized properly, it can increase our chances by half a percent!" Upon these words, the expressions of the others varied. Some were impatient, some were lost in thought, and some were eager and impatient. But obviously, no one stood up to object. After all, there was a distinction between immortals and mortals.

"Big Brother, do you mean, as before... destroying True Spirits completely?" The third among the twelve True Immortals asked. Upon these words, the atmosphere instantly fell silent. The dwarf elder nodded heavily, tacitly agreeing. "It harms heavenly harmony, harms heavenly harmony." "In fact, it's not impossible. Anyway, we are about to leave, and this possibility will likely have no future. Even if it cuts off the path for those who come after, it is nothing." After a round of exchanged glances, their decision was formally made.

Besides the so-called "complete destruction of True Spirits," the twelve True Immortals seemed to have other life-saving methods. One of them took out a fragment emitting different colors of light and assembled them in the center to form a circular sphere of light. Within the sphere, a slow heartbeat could be vaguely heard, as if something was sleeping. "This Primordial life form, we brothers have nurtured it separately for tens of thousands of years. Although we haven't managed to hatch it, we have each gained some divine abilities from it. It is indeed a life form that existed since the beginning of the Immortal Realm's birth," the dwarf elder sighed.

"To say we are reluctant is false. It is a pity that in this traversal, without its help, we might not even have a one percent chance of survival. So, its sacrifice is necessary." The elder's words had already set the tone. The other eleven looked at the sphere of light with reluctance, but facing such a supreme treasure, their opinions were extremely unified. There were no objectors. "Naturally, no matter how miraculous it is, it is merely an external object. Everything prioritizes our brothers' lives. If we lose this chance of transcendence, there will be others, but if we lose our lives, everything is truly lost." "Good, if that's the case, everyone act." The dwarf elder commanded sternly. With that, he was the first to sharply tap his own forehead.

The elder grunted, a trace of crimson flushed across his face. Correspondingly, the heartbeat within the sphere of light faltered, as if it, too, had suffered a severe injury. It was not only the elder and the sphere. The other eleven had not yet acted, but they seemed to have been affected by the injuries. After a brief rest, and when everyone had adjusted, the second brother continued to act. Their life forces seemed to be connected. If one was injured, the others would experience corresponding changes. But conversely, each of their life forces was far beyond the ordinary. Although none of them had attested to the Dao of Longevity, their life forces were incredibly vigorous. After a round of self-harm, none of them suffered any significant impact.

However, the sphere of light in the center was already on its last breath. Its already slow heartbeat was about to stop. Faint cries could also be vaguely heard from within. "Let's give it the final blow." The Immortals' expressions were complex, but they showed no intention of holding back. However, at this moment... A mysterious fluctuation suddenly descended, locking onto the sphere. A moment later, before the eyes of all, the sphere of light vanished! Having been in an environment ruled by twelve True Immortals for too long had made them lose sufficient vigilance towards "external enemies." At this sudden anomaly, they all froze slightly. Their first reaction was not to suspect an invasion by an outsider, but to look at the person beside them. From this subtle detail alone, it could be seen that although the twelve True Immortals were connected by some mysterious method in terms of their life force, their hearts might not have been truly united.

"Which fellow Immortal is playing a joke on us?" However, after all, they had been brothers for tens of thousands of years, and they knew each other inside out. They quickly reacted and scanned their surroundings with a mixture of surprise and anger, searching for the thief. "Fellow Immortal? Playing a joke?" In response came a faint cold snort. Without playing the role of a thief or hiding, Li Fan's figure, appearing so openly, was suddenly within the encirclement of the twelve True Immortals. He swept his gaze over everyone, finally landing on the sphere of light in his hand, whose life force was extremely weak. He did not take the twelve True Immortals seriously at all.

However, facing Li Fan's uninvited taking and disdain, the twelve True Immortals present dared not speak out in anger. This was because with Li Fan's appearance, all the Immortals felt as if an endless, magnificent mountain had been pressed upon their shoulders. This mountain was so heavy that even with the combined efforts of the twelve, they could not budge an inch. The twelve True Immortals were filled with fear and could not describe it. They had to know that six of them had already achieved the Nameless Realm. Nameless True Immortals could resist Dao Annihilation. Yet, facing the might of the person before them, they were struggling to cope. Recalling that there had been no traces of other True Immortals in this star sea for tens of thousands of years, and yet this person suddenly appeared today... They understood Li Fan's identity. "Transcendence..." "It is said that the heavens have compassion for all beings. This Primordial life form has been nurtured with difficulty. You wish to hunt and kill it for your own benefit. It is not a kind act." Li Fan shook his head and gently patted the sphere of light. The sphere, heavily injured by the twelve True Immortals, healed at a visible speed. Moreover, as if greatly nourished, its heartbeat grew faster and clearer.

The twelve True Immortals widened their eyes in astonishment. Because in just this moment, the growth of the sphere of light had surpassed their tens of thousands of years of nurturing. After all, it was with the combined efforts of all twelve of them, using the power of the entire star sea, that they had supplied it. And yet, it was less than a single pat from this transcendent expert! "This is... transcendence?" The dwarf elder was utterly stunned. As if greatly struck, his expression became somewhat dazed. Li Fan continued to feed the sphere of light with the Profound Yellow wood carvings and ancient Mountain and Sea artifacts from his palm. Meanwhile, he spoke to the twelve True Immortals, "What you seek is merely to survive in Dao Annihilation." "I still have spare capacity, and it's not impossible to give you a ride." These words were spoken very lightly, but to the twelve True Immortals, they were as heavy as thunder.

Initially, due to Li Fan's forceful taking and the vast disparity in their strength, they had resigned themselves to death today. They never expected that in an instant, the situation would take a sharp turn, and they would suddenly see a glimmer of hope. "This... Senior, are your words true?" The dwarf elder asked in disbelief. Li Fan chuckled, "Traversing Dao Annihilation, in your eyes, is an incredibly arduous task. In my eyes, it is merely a matter of sailing across without incident." As he spoke, a lone sail appeared in the eyes of the twelve Immortals. Like a divine pillar stabilizing the sea, the lone sail appeared, the wind and waves subsided. Since the anomaly of Dao Annihilation began, the sense of world-ending crisis that had been lingering in everyone's hearts instantly dissipated upon witnessing the Loneliness Sail of the Mountains and Seas.

The twelve True Immortals also had no doubt about Li Fan's strength. He was undoubtedly a transcendent expert! "This sail, you dare not gaze upon it for too long." "My Dao of Transcendence is not your path." The twelve True Immortals were immersed in Li Fan's display of the Loneliness Sail of the Mountains and Seas. Not long after, Li Fan proactively withdrew the illusory image of the sail. He kindly reminded them, "To seek transcendence, one must first carve out one's own path. The twelve of you are a single entity, which is a sort of method for traversal, albeit a flawed one." Li Fan evaluated them calmly. The twelve True Immortals' expressions turned somewhat somber. The dwarf elder smiled bitterly. "When Dao Annihilation first arrived and the Immortal Realm was destroyed. If not for this [Symbiosis] method, we would have long ago perished in the tide of Dao Annihilation, how could we have sought transcendence later?" "To be able to traverse the Mountains and Seas is already immensely satisfying. I do not seek a superior or inferior method." The elder bowed his head and said. "To have such an understanding is indeed not bad." Li Fan praised calmly. The faces of the twelve True Immortals looked somewhat better.

Chapter 1596: Flames Burn Mountains and Seas

Li Fan watched intently as the light sphere before him pulsed faster and faster, seemingly ready to hatch at any moment. The twelve True Immortals, curious about the true form of this Primordial being that they had collectively nurtured for tens of thousands of years without success, also secretly observed it.

"Tell me its origin," Li Fan asked indifferently.

Under Li Fan’s imposing presence, the twelve True Immortals dared not conceal anything and recounted their story: "When the Immortal Realm still existed, we were all immortals of the Myriad Domains Star Region. Among the boundless Immortal Realms, the Myriad Domains Star Region was a unique existence. Strictly speaking, it did not fall within the true scope of the Immortal Realm. Instead, it was a desolate star region, where no Immortal Overseer was appointed, and which successive Immortal Emperors chose to ignore…"

"Myriad Domains Star Region." Li Fan found information about this star region in his memory.

"Is that the place rumored to harbor terrifying beings, a sector that was only half-developed before being abandoned by the Immortal Realm? But it seemed to be just a legend. Until the destruction of the Immortal Realm, there was no concrete evidence of these beings truly existing."

The dwarfish elder nodded repeatedly: "Senior's insight is truly profound. Indeed, those terrifying beings never appeared from beginning to end, which gradually attracted those of us True Immortals who disliked constraints, unwilling to travel countless miles. However, the Three Saints are, after all, the Three Saints. Their foresight is beyond our comprehension."

"Those terrifying beings truly exist. And they had been in a deep slumber until the Dao Annihilation tide arrived, and they were startled awake..."

Recalling the scene they witnessed, the twelve True Immortals all showed varying degrees of fear.

"Rather than saying the Myriad Domains Star Region was swallowed by the Dao Annihilation tide, it would be more accurate to say it was annihilated in the confrontation between that terrifying being and the Dao Annihilation tide."

"We couldn't glimpse its full form, only faint glimpses of parts of it. It was as grand as mountains and seas, clashing head-on with the Dao Annihilation tide, and not falling behind..."

The dwarfish elder displayed the scene from his memory of the terrifying being confronting the Dao Annihilation. The power of this monster was truly astounding.

"We were completely unable to participate in the battle between the terrifying being and the Dao Annihilation, merely trying our best to evade and survive. The fierce battle lasted for nearly half a day, and then this stalemate brewed an even larger scale of Dao Annihilation."

"The Myriad Domains Star Region was swallowed in an instant, and the shadowy form of that terrifying being slowly disappeared into the Dao Annihilation, leaving behind only a shimmering light sphere, still struggling in its throes."

"When we saw this, during our escape, we brought it along. After all, it was left by a being capable of contending with Dao Annihilation, so it must be incredibly valuable. Perhaps it contains the path to Transcendence. And the facts proved us right. In these years in the lower realms, half of us were able to attain the Nameless Realm, all thanks to this light sphere," the dwarfish elder recounted truthfully.

Li Fan frowned, interrupting him: "How were you, then merely ordinary True Immortals, able to survive the Great Tribulation of Dao Annihilation?"

The twelve True Immortals smiled bitterly and exchanged glances, before slowly revealing the details: "To tell Senior, this is our brothers' greatest secret. The Myriad Domains Star Region was not fully opened. Therefore, it was one of the regions in the Immortal Realm most susceptible to the erosion of Dao Annihilation. The immortals within the star region, out of foresight, all had their own insights into how to survive Dao Annihilation."

"Among these, the [Complete Destruction of True Spirits] was recognized as the most effective method. However..."

The dwarfish elder hesitated for a moment before continuing: "It is too detrimental to celestial harmony and was regarded as a forbidden technique. We only jointly activated it at the very last moment, when the Myriad Domains Star Region was almost completely swallowed."

"What forbidden technique could enable True Immortals to resist Dao Annihilation? If it were truly that miraculous, why would the Immortal Realm have perished?" Li Fan's tone carried a hint of suspicion.

"This is absolutely true, junior would not dare to speak falsely."

Currently, the dwarfish elder slowly described the technique of [Complete Destruction of True Spirits].

Upon hearing it, a subtle expression flashed across Li Fan's face.

In simple terms, if Dao Annihilation were likened to a fire that consumed everything, then the Complete Destruction of True Spirits was a pre-emptive inferno that completely burned the star region, preparing it to resist that fire.

The vitality and existence of the starry sky were ignited, leaving only ashes. Even if these ashes would ultimately be swallowed by Dao Annihilation, the speed at which Dao Annihilation consumed them would be greatly reduced compared to a normal starry sky.

In fact, to some extent, these ashes, after the starry sky was burned, could serve as a crude wooden boat to traverse Dao Annihilation.

"At that time, we also knew a little about this technique of Complete Destruction of True Spirits. We persevered until the last moment before the Myriad Domains Star Region was destroyed, when there was truly no other way, no longer able to hold on. That's why we chose to burn all the remaining starry sky..."

"With a few ashes, we crafted a refugee boat. We arrived in the lower realms in disarray."

Li Fan could vaguely sense that the dwarfish elder's words still contained some inaccuracies. But Li Fan was not one to quibble over details; he had little interest in the precise manner of their survival.

Conversely, the technique of [Complete Destruction of True Spirits] that he spoke of was indeed genuine.

This method, which harmed oneself extensively to inflict minor damage on the enemy, had no practical meaning under normal circumstances. It only held value in extreme situations where a possibility was on the verge of being swallowed by Dao Annihilation.

But for Li Fan, it held significant reference value.

In fact, Li Fan had once wielded a similar divine ability.

In his previous life, when he was trapped in the tribulation of the fusion of three Dao, in order to save himself, Li Fan chose to resolutely self-detonate.

The foundation of immortality, the Great Dao of Longevity, transformed into fuel that consumed everything. Infinite light ignited the Primordial possibility and everything around it.

In a sense, it truly achieved the feat of isolating Dao Annihilation and leveling mountains to fill seas.

"However, compared to my crude method of forcibly igniting with a power equivalent to the Mountains and Seas, the ignition efficiency of this True Spirit Annihilation technique is far superior."

"Because this technique found a way to use the very foundation of a possibility as fuel..."

"True spirits. Or rather, potential, spirituality."

Li Fan covertly circulated this technique within his body. He mastered it faster than any other divine ability he had learned. Even upon initial understanding, he felt a sense of effortless mastery.

But at the same time, Li Fan also felt his spiritual intuition constantly sending frantic warnings.

"A slight misstep, and a blazing inferno will erupt instantly."

"This technique uses one's own spirituality as kindling and bait. One must first ignite oneself, leading to the ignition of the possibility one is in. Then, one must extinguish the flames within oneself as quickly as possible. If one delays, the only outcome is mutual destruction in the flames."

"And even if one is calm and swift, the consumption of one's own spirituality by this technique is evident. Each use significantly reduces one's potential. Use it too many times, and one becomes completely useless..."

Li Fan narrowed his eyes and looked at the subtly uneasy group of twelve immortals around him, suddenly understanding: "Twelve people coexisting, igniting the fire together. If shared, the loss of individual potential can indeed be minimized. Hmph, to achieve this, it's far more than merely knowing a little about [True Spirit Annihilation]."

"It's highly likely they are the creators of this technique. Their strength at that time should have been much greater. It was because they used the True Spirit Annihilation technique that their strength was greatly diminished." In an instant, Li Fan had seen through the hidden secret of the twelve True Immortals.

Perhaps these twelve True Immortals never imagined that someone with a constitution so compatible with the forbidden art of [Complete Destruction of True Spirits] would exist in the world. After all, because the execution consumed one's own potential and spirituality, the cost of cultivating this art was truly immense. There were often no opportunities for "practice."

Only someone immensely familiar with the theoretical foundations of True Spirit Annihilation could successfully perform it on their first attempt at practical application.

Under normal circumstances, even after attempting it three or five times, there would be no chance of igniting a possibility. Instead, one would only ruin oneself.

But Li Fan was an exception.

"This True Spirit Annihilation is truly an uncompromisingly evil art. I wonder who created it," a hint of displeasure seemed to flash across Li Fan's face.

"If I'm not mistaken, this evil art can ignite not just a single possibility. It might even extend to other existing possibilities."

The dwarfish elder quickly lowered his head and said: "Senior's insight is truly peerless, there is indeed such a possibility. However, it is merely a possibility. Firstly, the Mountains and Seas are too vast, yet the potential of living beings in the world is limited. The burning fire often burns for a while, and after losing the fuel of true spirits as support, it extinguishes itself."

"Secondly, between the Mountains and Seas, there is Dao Annihilation. Dao Annihilation, as a natural barrier, also has a great effect on suppressing the burning fire. Take this star sea as an example, if we were to ignite it, even a single possibility would not be affected; the fire would only be confined to this corner of the world..."

Li Fan chuckled, with a pointed meaning: "You have indeed researched this technique quite deeply."

The dwarfish elder smiled bitterly: "It's the only way to save ourselves, so we had no choice but to painstakingly research it."

Li Fan did not delve further: "Since I am here, you need not employ this malevolent art. For a mere twelve individuals, I am capable of giving you a ride."

"However, the Mountains and Seas are boundless; do you have a destination?"

"That Great World of the Other Shore, or the Grand Heaven Sacred Dynasty? Or perhaps, you simply wish to be dropped off at the nearest possibility not yet swallowed by Dao Annihilation?" Li Fan asked kindly.

Seeing that Li Fan seemed genuinely to be considering offering them a ride, the twelve True Immortals were overjoyed beyond measure.

They exchanged glances, likely communicating inwardly.

After a moment, the dwarfish elder still spoke in trepidation: "To Senior, we have indeed heard of the Great World of the Other Shore. However, we have never heard of the Grand Heaven Sacred Dynasty. Might Senior be so kind as to introduce it to us?"

Li Fan readily agreed: "The Grand Heaven Sacred Dynasty was established by a peerless powerhouse within the Mountains and Seas, Emperor Taiwei..."

His words, recounting the history of the Sacred Dynasty, left the twelve True Immortals spellbound.

"Such a powerful being exists within the Mountains and Seas! We were truly shortsighted in the past."

"However, this Emperor Taiwei is perhaps a bit too overbearing. We went to the Myriad Domains Star Region precisely because we disliked being controlled."

"The Great World of the Other Shore..."

Li Fan spoke, interrupting their reverie: "The journey to the Other Shore is distant. If you truly wish to go with me, you must be mentally prepared. The Mountains and Seas are vast, and the road ahead is long. Perhaps, by the time your lifespan ends, we will still not have reached our destination."

The twelve True Immortals did not perceive the gravity in Li Fan's words.

They automatically ignored words like "long" and "distant," and all expressed that they had made their decision.

In their view, with the long lifespans of True Immortals and Nameless True Immortals, no matter how far the Other Shore was, it would not take so long that they couldn't see it within their lifetimes.

And staying here was a dead end.

Compared to the forbidden art of True Spirit Annihilation, the survival rate of achieving a single sail across the mountains and seas was clearly much higher.

Thus, their choice was obvious.

"Since it is so, come aboard."

Li Fan spoke calmly, and a lone sail reappeared.

Beneath the lone sail was a narrow, cramped wooden boat.

Though small, the twelve True Immortals could just barely squeeze in.

"Everyone, if there are no objections, I shall depart?" Li Fan asked.

The twelve True Immortals naturally nodded in joy.

"Since that is the case..."

As if a sea breeze swept by, the lone sail suddenly billowed.

The small wooden boat vibrated violently. The surroundings seemed to churn with raging winds and colossal waves, as if about to swallow the small boat at any moment.

"Dao... Dao Annihilation."

Feeling the pervasive, familiar, and terrifying aura deeply etched in their memories, the twelve True Immortals uncontrollably showed signs of fear.

And the next scene that unfolded, however, added a touch of shock to their faces, beyond mere fear.

"Right, regarding the True Spirit Annihilation technique you just mentioned, although I heard a general outline, there are still a few uncertain points. I need to personally test and verify them. Since you are about to depart, you might as well give this star sea to me as material for an experiment."

"Hmm?" The twelve True Immortals all froze at his words.

Before they could fully comprehend the meaning behind Li Fan's words, Li Fan had already acted.

Clearly, Li Fan was not asking for their opinion but rather making a playful announcement.

A wisp of fire illuminated the starry sky.

In an instant, it ignited into a conflagration. Infinite light, with the wisp of fire as its center, spread outwards.

A moment later, this entire star sea was engulfed in dazzling brilliance!

"What a fire, what a vast expanse of fire!"

Li Fan stood upon the lone sail, marveling with a clicking tongue.

Below, the twelve True Immortals, crowded on the wooden boat, had faces ashen white as paper at the sight.

"You... you..."

As if seeing a ghost, their faces were filled with disbelief.

They were too stunned to even utter words of inquiry for a moment.

They simply couldn't comprehend why this person could successfully wield the forbidden art of True Spirit Annihilation on his very first attempt.

And even if this person possessed unparalleled talent, seldom seen in the Mountains and Seas, he clearly already had the ability to traverse the Mountains and Seas. Why would he still consume his own spirituality to ignite the starry sky before him?

One must know that even though they also researched and invoked forbidden arts, it was always out of desperate necessity for survival.

But this person before them...

The white flames stretched endlessly.

And Li Fan's face, illuminated by the firelight, flickered, becoming indistinct.

Chapter 1597: Immortal Boat Enters the Dao Annihilation

Li Fan watched intently as the sphere of light before him pulsed faster and faster, seemingly ready to hatch at any moment. The twelve True Immortals, curious about the true form of this Primordial being that they had collectively nurtured for tens of thousands of years without success, also secretly observed it.

"Tell me its origin," Li Fan asked indifferently.

Under Li Fan's imposing presence, the twelve True Immortals dared not conceal anything and recounted their story: "When the Immortal Realm still existed, we were all immortals of the Myriad Domains Star Region. The Myriad Domains Star Region was a unique existence within the boundless Immortal Realms. Strictly speaking, it did not fall within the true scope of the Immortal Realm. Instead, it was a desolate star region, where no Immortal Overseer was appointed, and which successive Immortal Emperors chose to ignore…"

"Myriad Domains Star Region." Li Fan found information about this star region in his memory.

"Is that the place rumored to harbor terrifying beings, a sector that was only half-developed before being abandoned by the Immortal Realm? But it seemed to be just a legend. Until the destruction of the Immortal Realm, there was no concrete evidence of these beings truly existing."

The dwarfish elder nodded repeatedly: "Senior's insight is truly profound. Indeed, those terrifying beings never appeared from beginning to end, which gradually attracted those of us True Immortals who disliked constraints, unwilling to travel countless miles. However, the Three Sages are, after all, the Three Sages. Their foresight is beyond our comprehension."

"Those terrifying beings truly exist. And they had been in a deep slumber until the Dao Annihilation tide arrived, and they were startled awake…"

Recalling the scene they witnessed, the twelve True Immortals all showed varying degrees of fear.

"Rather than saying the Myriad Domains Star Region was swallowed by the Dao Annihilation tide, it would be more accurate to say it was annihilated in the confrontation between that terrifying being and the Dao Annihilation tide."

"We couldn't glimpse its full form, only faint glimpses of parts of it. It was as grand as mountains and seas, clashing head-on with the Dao Annihilation tide, and not falling behind…"

The dwarfish elder displayed the scene from his memory of the terrifying being confronting the Dao Annihilation. The power of this monster was truly astounding.

"The terrifying being and Dao Annihilation's battle, we were completely unable to participate, merely trying our best to evade and survive. The fierce battle lasted for nearly half a day, and then this stalemate brewed an even larger scale of Dao Annihilation."

"The Myriad Domains Star Region was swallowed in an instant, and the shadowy form of that terrifying being slowly disappeared into the Dao Annihilation, leaving behind only a shimmering light sphere, still struggling in its throes."

"When we saw this, during our escape, we brought it along. After all, it was left by a being capable of contending with Dao Annihilation, so it must be incredibly valuable. Perhaps it contains the path to Transcendence. And the facts proved us right. In these years in the lower realms, half of us were able to attain the Nameless Realm, all thanks to this light sphere," the dwarfish elder recounted truthfully.

Li Fan frowned, interrupting him: "You were merely ordinary True Immortals back then, so how were you able to survive the Great Tribulation of Dao Annihilation?"

The twelve True Immortals smiled bitterly and exchanged glances, before slowly revealing the details: "To tell Senior, this is our brothers' greatest secret. The Myriad Domains Star Region was not fully open. Therefore, it was one of the regions in the Immortal Realm most susceptible to the erosion of Dao Annihilation. The immortals within the star region, out of foresight, all had their own insights into how to survive Dao Annihilation."

"Among these, the [Complete Destruction of True Spirits] was recognized as the most effective method. However…"

The dwarfish elder hesitated for a moment before continuing: "It is too detrimental to celestial harmony and was regarded as a forbidden technique. We only jointly activated it at the very last moment, when the Myriad Domains Star Region was almost completely swallowed."

"What forbidden technique could enable True Immortals to resist Dao Annihilation? If it were truly that miraculous, why would the Immortal Realm have perished?" Li Fan's tone carried a hint of suspicion.

"This is absolutely true, junior would not dare to speak falsely."

Hence, the dwarfish elder slowly described the technique of [Complete Destruction of True Spirits].

Upon hearing it, a subtle expression flashed across Li Fan's face.

Simply put, if Dao Annihilation were likened to a fire that consumed everything, then the Complete Destruction of True Spirits was a pre-emptive inferno that completely burned the star region, preparing it to resist that fire.

The vitality and existence of the starry sky were ignited, leaving only ashes. Even if these ashes would ultimately be swallowed by Dao Annihilation, the speed at which Dao Annihilation consumed them would be greatly reduced compared to a normal starry sky.

Indeed, to some extent, these ashes, after the starry sky was burned, could serve as a crude wooden boat to traverse Dao Annihilation.

"We also knew a little about this True Spirit Annihilation technique back then. We persevered until the last moment before the Myriad Domains Star Region was destroyed, when there was truly no other way, no longer able to hold on. That's why we chose to burn all the remaining starry sky…"

"With a few ashes, we crafted a refugee boat. We arrived in the lower realms in disarray."

Li Fan could vaguely sense that the dwarfish elder's words still contained some inaccuracies. But Li Fan was not one to quibble over details; he had little interest in the precise manner of their survival.

Conversely, the technique of [Complete Destruction of True Spirits] that he spoke of was indeed genuine.

This method, which harmed oneself immensely to inflict minor damage on the enemy, held no practical meaning under normal circumstances. It only held value in extreme situations where a possibility was on the verge of being swallowed by Dao Annihilation.

But for Li Fan, it held significant reference value.

Indeed, Li Fan had once wielded a similar divine ability.

In his previous life, when he was trapped in the tribulation of the fusion of three Dao, in order to save himself, Li Fan chose to resolutely self-detonate.

The foundation of immortality, the Great Dao of Longevity, transformed into fuel that consumed everything. Infinite light ignited the Primordial possibility and everything around it.

In a sense, it truly achieved the feat of isolating Dao Annihilation and leveling mountains to fill seas.

"However, compared to my crude method of forcibly igniting with a power equivalent to the Mountains and Seas, the ignition efficiency of this True Spirit Annihilation technique is far superior."

"Because this technique found a way to use the very foundation of a possibility as fuel…"

"True spirits. Or rather, potential, spirituality."

Li Fan covertly circulated this technique within his body. He mastered it faster than any other divine ability he had learned. Even upon initial understanding, he felt a sense of effortless mastery.

But at the same time, he also felt his spiritual intuition constantly sending frantic warnings.

"A slight misstep, and a blazing inferno will erupt instantly."

"This technique uses one's own spirituality as kindling and bait. One must first ignite oneself, leading to the ignition of the possibility one is in. Then, one must extinguish the flames within oneself as quickly as possible. If one delays, the only outcome is mutual destruction in the flames."

"And even if one is calm and swift, the consumption of one's own spirituality by this technique is evident. Each use significantly reduces one's potential. Use it too many times, and one becomes completely useless…"

Li Fan narrowed his eyes and looked at the subtly uneasy group of twelve immortals around him, suddenly understanding: "Twelve people coexisting, igniting the fire together. If shared, the loss of individual potential can indeed be minimized. Hmph, to achieve this, it's far more than merely knowing a little about [True Spirit Blaze]."

"It's highly likely they are the creators of this technique. Their strength at that time should have been much greater. It was because they used the True Spirit Annihilation technique that their strength was greatly diminished." In an instant, Li Fan had seen through the hidden secret of the twelve True Immortals.

Perhaps these twelve True Immortals never imagined that someone with a constitution so compatible with the forbidden art of [Complete Destruction of True Spirits] would exist in the world. After all, because the execution consumed one's own potential and spirituality, the cost of cultivating this art was truly immense. There were often no opportunities for "practice."

Only someone immensely familiar with the theoretical foundations of True Spirit Annihilation could successfully perform it on their first attempt at practical application.

Under normal circumstances, even after attempting it three or five times, there would be no chance of igniting a possibility. Instead, one would only ruin oneself.

But Li Fan was an exception.

"This True Spirit Annihilation is truly an uncompromisingly evil art. I wonder who created it," a hint of displeasure seemed to flash across Li Fan's face.

"If I'm not mistaken, this evil art can ignite not just a single possibility. It might even extend to other existing possibilities."

The dwarfish elder quickly lowered his head and said: "Senior's insight is truly peerless, there is indeed such a possibility. However, it is merely a possibility. Firstly, the Mountains and Seas are too vast, yet the potential of living beings in the world is limited. The burning fire often burns for a while, and after losing the fuel of true spirits as support, it extinguishes itself."

"Secondly, between the Mountains and Seas, there is Dao Annihilation. Dao Annihilation, as a natural barrier, also has a great effect on suppressing the burning fire. Take this star sea as an example, if we were to ignite it, even a single possibility would not be affected; the fire would only be confined to this corner of the world…"

Li Fan chuckled, with a pointed meaning: "You have indeed researched this technique quite deeply."

The dwarfish elder smiled bitterly: "It's the only way to save ourselves, so we had no choice but to painstakingly research it."

Li Fan did not delve further: "Since I am here, you need not employ this malevolent art. For a mere twelve individuals, I am capable of giving you a ride."

"Just, the Mountains and Seas are boundless; do you have a destination?"

"That Great World of the Other Shore, or the Grand Heaven Sacred Dynasty? Or perhaps, you simply wish to be dropped off at the nearest possibility not yet swallowed by Dao Annihilation?" Li Fan asked kindly.

Seeing that Li Fan seemed genuinely to be considering offering them a ride, the twelve True Immortals were overjoyed beyond measure.

They exchanged glances, likely communicating inwardly.

After a moment, the dwarfish elder still spoke in trepidation: "To Senior, we have indeed heard of the Great World of the Other Shore. However, we have never heard of the Grand Heaven Sacred Dynasty. Might Senior be so kind as to introduce it to us?"

Li Fan readily agreed: "The Grand Heaven Sacred Dynasty was established by a peerless powerhouse within the Mountains and Seas, Emperor Taiwei…"

His words, recounting the history of the Sacred Dynasty, left the twelve True Immortals spellbound.

"Such a powerful being exists within the Mountains and Seas! We were truly shortsighted in the past."

"However, this Emperor Taiwei is perhaps a bit too overbearing. We went to the Myriad Domains Star Region precisely because we disliked being controlled."

"The Great World of the Other Shore…"

Li Fan spoke, interrupting their reverie: "The journey to the Other Shore is distant. If you truly wish to go with me, you must be mentally prepared. The Mountains and Seas are vast, and the road ahead is long. Perhaps, by the time your lifespan ends, we will still not have reached our destination."

The twelve True Immortals did not perceive the gravity in Li Fan's words.

They automatically ignored words like "long" and "distant," and all expressed that they had made their decision.

In their view, with the long lifespans of True Immortals and Nameless True Immortals, no matter how far the Other Shore was, it would not take so long that they couldn't see it within their lifetimes.

And staying here was a dead end.

Compared to the forbidden art of True Spirit Annihilation, the survival rate of achieving a single sail across the mountains and seas was clearly much higher.

Thus, their choice was obvious.

"Since it is so, come aboard."

Li Fan spoke calmly, and a lone sail reappeared.

Beneath the lone sail was a narrow, cramped wooden boat.

Though small, the twelve True Immortals could just barely squeeze in.

"Everyone, if there are no objections, I shall depart?" Li Fan asked.

The twelve True Immortals naturally nodded in joy.

"Since that is the case…"

As if a sea breeze swept by, the lone sail suddenly billowed.

The small wooden boat vibrated violently. The surroundings seemed to churn with raging winds and colossal waves, as if about to swallow the small boat at any moment.

"Dao… Dao Annihilation."

Feeling the pervasive, familiar, and terrifying aura deeply etched in their memories, the twelve True Immortals uncontrollably showed signs of fear.

And the next scene that unfolded, however, added a touch of shock to their faces, beyond mere fear.

"Right, regarding the True Spirit Annihilation technique you just mentioned, although I heard a general outline, there are still a few uncertain points. I need to personally test and verify them. Since you are about to depart, you might as well give this star sea to me as material for an experiment."

"Hmm?" The twelve True Immortals all froze at his words.

Before they could fully comprehend the meaning behind Li Fan's words, Li Fan had already acted.

Clearly, Li Fan was not asking for their opinion but rather making a playful announcement.

A wisp of fire illuminated the starry sky.

In an instant, it ignited into a conflagration. Infinite light, with the wisp of fire as its center, spread outwards.

A moment later, this entire star sea was engulfed in dazzling brilliance!

"What a fire, what a vast expanse of fire!"

Li Fan stood upon the lone sail, marveling with a clicking tongue.

Below, the twelve True Immortals, crowded on the wooden boat, had faces ashen white as paper at the sight.

"You… you…"

As if seeing a ghost, their faces were filled with disbelief.

They were too stunned to even utter words of inquiry for a moment.

They simply couldn't comprehend why this person could successfully wield the forbidden art of True Spirit Annihilation on his very first attempt.

And even if this person possessed unparalleled talent, seldom seen in the Mountains and Seas, he clearly already had the ability to traverse the Mountains and Seas. Why would he still consume his own spirituality to ignite the starry sky before him?

One must know that even though they also researched and invoked forbidden arts, it was always out of desperate necessity for survival.

But this person before them…

The white flames stretched endlessly.

And Li Fan's face, illuminated by the firelight, flickered, becoming indistinct.

Chapter 1598: Living Beings Generate Taiji

Compared to the display of the Heaven-Destroying Divine Ability, the benevolent act of igniting a single candle to dispel the extreme cold within the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship, consuming the spirit was almost negligible. For Li Fan, it was not a burden at all. It merely served to preserve the helmsmen and crew on the Immortal Ship, and was thus done as a matter of convenience.

"This extreme cold..."

"What is its origin?"

The warmth generated by the burning True Spirit fire merely protected the beings within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm. Li Fan, as the Lord of Profound Yellow, however, actively withdrew this protection. He directly faced the cold loneliness of the mountains and seas.

The Profound Yellow Immortal Ship sailed through the darkness, silent and without a ripple. The outside world seemed to have lost the meaning of the passage of time. Li Fan stood on the high, lone sail of the Immortal Ship, as if he were the darkness before his eyes.

During the traversal of the mountains and seas, time became irrelevant. Within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, seventy years had passed in the blink of an eye. Since the moment the Immortal Ship entered Dao Annihilation, the "variables" of the entire Profound Yellow Immortal Realm seemed to have been locked in place. In these seventy years, no more cultivators at the Dao Integration realm were born. This was not Li Fan deliberately limiting the Immortal Ship's resource consumption, but rather a natural consequence of the Immortal Ship's own changes.

Immersed in an environment far removed from the mortal world for an extended period, Li Fan slowly began to understand the fundamental source of the persistent chill that clung to him like a scar. "The beings of the mountains and seas are mostly born in the mortal world. Once we beings leave the mortal world, we distance ourselves from the most basic environment that nurtured us from nothing, through cultivation. It is like a fish leaving water, a bird trapped on land, or an underground creature suddenly exposed to sunlight."

"Due to maladjustment, leading to demise. The Transcendent True Intent condensed by powerful Transcendent beings, in a sense, is the ability to adapt and safely navigate through such drastic changes."

"Although I possess infinite spiritual energy, when I distance myself from the mortal world, I still feel this sense of hesitation and discomfort..."

"Infinite spiritual energy might be related to my transmigration and my original self. As for this body, it is indeed a native being of the mountains and seas," Li Fan mused silently.

Within the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship, almost all beings, including the twelve True Immortals who boarded last, could not escape this feeling of cold loneliness.

There was only one exception. It was the unknown primordial being that had once slept in the Zhuyu Star Domain and was later jointly nurtured by the twelve True Immortals.

The energy consumption of the primordial being was indeed astonishing. For fifty years, Li Fan had fed it without pause. Over a hundred Profound Yellow wooden carvings had been crushed. Yet, the true gestation of this primordial being was still one step away. Fortunately, Li Fan had recently sensed that it was beginning to reject his feeding. It was not that it had become ungrateful before its birth, but rather that the primordial being had reached the limit of what its gestation state could absorb and could no longer consume any more!

Li Fan invited the twelve True Immortals to witness the gestation of the primordial being within the luminous orb. After all, they had diligently helped nurture it for tens of thousands of years. It was worth mentioning that even after fifty years of traversing the mountains and seas together, the twelve True Immortals had still not seen the true appearance of the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship. From beginning to end, they had been forced to huddle in the small wooden boat Li Fan had manifested. Relying on the lone sail that rose from the wooden boat, they protected themselves from the constant erosion of Dao Annihilation, never realizing that on the small wooden boat they inhabited, there existed another, immeasurably larger Immortal Ship for traversal!

Most of their minds were occupied with resisting the constant influx of loneliness within them. Any residual energy was seized to attempt to comprehend the Dao of "Traversal." Coupled with the vast disparity in strength between them and Li Fan, they found it difficult to glimpse the truth of the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship.

At this moment, seeing Li Fan suddenly appear holding the primordial being, they were all slightly taken aback. Only then did they react, looking at the luminous orb about to give birth with complex expressions.

"To be able to witness the birth of a primordial being today is truly a blessing for three lifetimes."

"It was not in vain that we labored so hard."

"I just wonder if this primordial being remembers us."

"Senior not only saved us from dire straits but also helped us fulfill our long-cherished wish. Such benevolence and magnanimity are truly admirable." The twelve True Immortals acted very naturally, showing no hint of resentment in their hearts.

Li Fan's gaze swept over them calmly, causing a shiver to run down their spines. The silence in the hall lasted for a while before Li Fan finally spoke again: "This beast should be coming out soon, so let's wait patiently."
