The twelve True Immortals all inwardly grumbled at Li Fan referring to the primordial being as a "beast," but they dared not express any dissent, only nodding and offering polite agreement.

Nine more years passed. For True Immortals, this was merely the time it took to close their eyes to meditate and then casually open them.

On this day, subtle fluctuations emanating from the luminous orb in Li Fan's hand startled everyone on the wooden boat. A black fissure appeared in the center of the orb, as if it had cracked open. Instantly, infinite light and shadow erupted from this fissure. It was the roar of mountains and seas, and the birth and destruction of countless possibilities! As if directly facing the mountains and seas, the people on the boat became immersed in this scene.

However, they did not notice a black line, hidden within the light and shadow, speeding towards the weakest among the twelve True Immortals. By the time the black line was almost upon him, this True Immortal, named Shi Qiwu, whose cultivation was in the Dao of "Nurturing," finally sensed the sudden attack in a daze. However, before he could even change his expression, in the next moment, he was about to be pierced by the black line.

"A beast is still a beast!"

At this moment, Li Fan's icy voice suddenly rang out. A hand, moving faster than the black line, firmly grasped it.

Roar!

A roar like the collision of mountains and seas erupted from the black line. The twelve True Immortals felt waves of thunder in their ears, causing dizziness. Shi Qiwu, who was closest, felt as if he had been struck a heavy blow, his Dao path showing signs of dissipating under this roar. Fortunately, the twelve True Immortals shared their life force. With the help of the other eleven, Shi Qiwu narrowly escaped death. The terror of this primordial being was evident.

However, in Li Fan's hand, the beast was unable to move. It could only emit threatening roars. The twelve True Immortals thus saw the true appearance of the black line: it resembled a smoothed wooden stick, with infinitely complex yet non-repeating patterns faintly appearing on it. Each end of the wooden stick had a face. It was not like a human face, but merely black and white expressions that constantly shifted, revealing the essence of a "face." This primordial being, rather than a living creature, was more like a refined magic artifact. Though newborn, its nature was still fierce. Now, caught in Li Fan's hand, unable to advance or retreat, it struggled unceasingly. With roars like surging mountains and seas, the patterns on its body seemed to come alive, rapidly separating and gathering at each end of the wooden stick. The primordial being instantly split into two, one completely black, the other snow-white. The two resembled two snakes, swallowing each other's heads and tails, constantly rotating rapidly. In an instant, they formed a Tai Chi diagram, swirling in Li Fan's palm. A mysterious force was born, as if someone had heavily pushed Li Fan, and the restraint he held on the primordial being loosened. The Tai Chi diagram's colors instantly darkened, as if it were escaping to another place. Outside the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship, the previously calm Dao Annihilation suddenly churned with winds and waves. It was as if something had violently plunged into the sea.

"Not good, that beast is trying to escape!" The twelve True Immortals exclaimed in alarm. Li Fan merely sneered. He beckured towards the direction the Tai Chi diagram was escaping. The clamor within Dao Annihilation instantly intensified. Wave after wave of surging water continuously struck the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship, exposing everyone on board to the greatest turbulence they had experienced since traversing the mountains and seas. It was as if two ancient behemoths were fiercely battling underwater!

This turn of events far exceeded the expectations of the twelve True Immortals. They stared intently at the void outside the ship, occasionally stealing glances at Li Fan, who stood calmly by. They wondered what divine ability their senior used to capture an enemy within Dao Annihilation, a feat unheard of. The fierce battle within Dao Annihilation did not last long. Despite its ferocity, it was, after all, in its nascent state. Soon, the commotion in Dao Annihilation slowly subsided, and the Tai Chi diagram quietly returned to the wooden boat. It spun and turned, ultimately unable to maintain its form and reverting to its stick-like appearance. The patterns on the wooden stick seemed less dense than before. The black and white expressions at each end also appeared listless.

"This object was born at the beginning of the world, imitating the birth and evolution of the Great Dao..."

"However, it ultimately lacks sentience. It knows the form but not the spirit. Thus, after such a long time, it remains in this state," Li Fan commented indifferently, tapping the wooden stick with a finger. The twelve True Immortals nodded in understanding. The one who retrieved the Tai Chi wooden stick from Dao Annihilation was naturally Ink Slaughter. After fifty years of contemplation and adaptation, Ink Slaughter had finally recognized its identity. It had completely separated itself from the omnipresent Dao Annihilation, existing solely as "Ink Slaughter," the soul of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm and Li Fan's subordinate! Unlike all other beings and powers in the mountains and seas, Ink Slaughter entering Dao Annihilation was truly like "a fish in water, moving with ease." The corrosive power of Dao Annihilation had almost no effect on Ink Slaughter. In fact, when other existences were present, Ink Slaughter could even use the power of Dao Annihilation to attack its enemies. The recent capture of the Tai Chi wooden stick was its first trial. If it had to fight the Tai Chi wooden stick with its own strength alone, it might have been a bitter battle. But with the assistance of the surrounding environment, "Dao Annihilation," capturing it was merely a matter of moments.

Li Fan's ability to so quickly discern the nature of the primordial being was also thanks to Ink Slaughter. If Dao Annihilation were a boundless ocean, then almost all beings in the mountains and seas would be unable to swim. A few Transcendent beings would possess the ability to swim. But Ink Slaughter... was a fish born to live in this ocean! "Even if the Immortal Ship capsizes, with Ink Slaughter, I can still be safe." Li Fan did not reveal Ink Slaughter's existence to the twelve True Immortals. After completing its mission, Li Fan ordered it back to the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

Sensing the departure of Ink Slaughter's aura, the Tai Chi wooden stick, which had been severely injured and seemed on the verge of death, instantly became vibrant again. However, Li Fan merely flicked his fingers several times, suppressing the accumulated strength it had regained. This cycle continued until the Tai Chi wooden stick finally recognized the gap in their strength and became temporarily docile.

"There are such wondrous beings in the mountains and seas."

"Primordial beings are sometimes even more ancient than the Immortal Realm, often symbolizing the ancient Daos of the mountains and seas. It is said that some True Immortals, after subduing primordial beings, attained enlightenment from them, reaching the realm of Transcendence the moment they attained the Nameless realm."

"I see that the Tai Chi Dao manifested by this beast is also not bad..." The twelve True Immortals, who had witnessed Li Fan's entire process of subduing the Tai Chi wooden stick, marveled.

"However, Senior is already immensely powerful, and this wooden stick is of little use to you." Shi Qiwu spoke, and the people on the ship fell silent. Shi Qiwu realized the impropriety of his words and was about to offer an apology. However, Li Fan said calmly: "Indeed, this object is of little use to my Dao path."

"But it is of great use for this journey."

The twelve True Immortals were puzzled upon hearing this. But Li Fan then threw the Tai Chi wooden stick, which had barely recovered some strength, back into Dao Annihilation. The Tai Chi wooden stick seemed in disbelief, frozen in place for a moment. Then, as if realizing what had happened, it frantically fled towards the depths of Dao Annihilation.

"Senior, this..." The twelve True Immortals were about to question him.

But suddenly, they noticed that the small wooden boat beneath them seemed to be sailing faster for some reason. Upon closer inspection, they saw that thin black lines seemed to be connected from the Tai Chi wooden stick, which had fled into Dao Annihilation, to the hull of the ship! Because of these connections, the Tai Chi wooden stick seemed to be pulling the wooden boat, allowing it to quickly navigate through Dao Annihilation.

"It can still be like this?" The twelve True Immortals were all astonished.

"Primordial beings, despite their powerful life force, ultimately cannot survive in Dao Annihilation for long."

"So, when trapped in Dao Annihilation, to survive longer, they instinctively seek 'food' for replenishment."

"Primordial beings are peculiar existences in the mountains and seas. Their perception of possibilities and life force far surpasses that of us cultivators. We, in this vast Dao Annihilation, can barely discern direction. They, however, might sense the existence of food in the distance." Li Fan stood at the prow of the ship, feeling the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship changing direction under the牵引 of the Tai Chi wooden stick, a strange expression on his face.

Recalling Li Fan's action of burning the Primordial possibility with True Spirit fire without asking for their opinion, the twelve True Immortals felt a chill in their hearts. They had agreed to be taken to the Shore of Great Dao, but now it seemed... Under Li Fan's might, the twelve True Immortals dared not show the slightest opposition, only praising the senior's unfathomable divine abilities in unison. The Tai Chi wooden stick, fleeing in panic, pulled the Immortal Ship forward for forty days. Just as it was about to run out of energy and dissipate in Dao Annihilation, Li Fan rescued it in time.

Chapter 1599: The True Appearance of Mountains and Seas

The Grand Unity Wooden Staff lay dying, the black and white faces on its ends faded as if made of paper. The patterns on its body had almost entirely vanished, leaving only a few remnants.

Having survived the ordeal, it became utterly obedient.

When Li Fan offered it a Profound Yellow phantom, it eagerly devoured it, even showing an ingratiating expression.

It only slowly recovered after a full meal, but it did not remain obedient for long.

Just three days later, the Grand Unity Wooden Staff reverted to its old ways.

Having already realized the immense power of Li Fan, this time it did not choose to attack him again. Instead, it leaped directly out of the ship, fleeing towards the source of the "scent" it had sensed earlier in Dao Annihilation.

It did not detect that the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship was following closely behind.

"Although this beast possesses intelligence, its wisdom is truly not high." The dwarfish elder, Ruan Ruiyu, the eldest of the Twelve True Immortals, joked upon seeing this.

"Senior is right, a beast is just a beast," everyone else echoed in agreement.

The Grand Unity Wooden Staff's memory was indeed poor.

Each time it was tormented to the brink of death in Dao Annihilation, yet given the slightest opportunity, it would instinctively flee back into it. It was as if something on the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship was more terrifying than Dao Annihilation itself.

After a few initial jests, the Twelve True Immortals finally realized something. Even if the Grand Unity Wooden Staff's intelligence was low, its innate survival instinct should still be present. Fleeing once or twice could be attributed to momentary desperation. But if it continued this way...

Everyone looked at Li Fan, who stood alone at the prow, his expression inscrutable. A chill once again rose in their hearts.

The questions that were on the tip of their tongues were forcefully suppressed.

The Twelve True Immortals all regretted having boarded this "pirate ship." They were told it was sailing towards the Other Shore Great World, but from all indications, their host did not seem intent on delivering them there easily.

However, besides staying on the ship and pressing forward into the unknown, they had no other choice. Entering Dao Annihilation without protection meant certain death. Resisting Li Fan would likely lead to an even swifter demise. Though bitterness filled the hearts of the twelve brothers, they could only silently endure.

The Twelve True Immortals did not know that they had misunderstood Li Fan in this regard.

It wasn't that he didn't want to take them to the Other Shore Great World.

It was that Li Fan himself didn't know where this so-called Other Shore was, or how to get there.

"Theoretically, in this vast Mountains and Seas, there should be many lighthouse-like beacons guiding the specific direction of the Other Shore. New Transcendent experts only need to find the nearest lighthouse and then continue sailing towards the next, and they will eventually reach the Other Shore Great World."

"But for some reason, I have been adrift in Dao Annihilation for so long, yet I have seen no trace of a lighthouse."

"There are two possibilities. I have not condensed my own Transcendent True Intent, so even if a lighthouse is right before me, I cannot perceive it. This possibility is not very high, as the lone sail above my head is not fake."

"The other possibility is that traversing the Mountains and Seas simply takes this much time. As I saw in the memories of the lone sail. Without directional guidance, the time required to traverse can exhaust the lifespan of a Transcendent expert. However, with clear directional guidance..."

"Even if the time needed is reduced by a hundredfold, it would still be an unimaginably long period."

Li Fan was mentally prepared for this.

He did not expect to reach the Other Shore anytime soon.

"When Zi Yi descended, he repeatedly mentioned 'not wanting to run errands' and 'not making this trip for nothing.' This indicates that even in the eyes of an experienced Transcendent expert like him, descending from the Other Shore to a possibility is not a negligible expenditure."

"Yet, earlier, when the Primordial possibility involved those Transcendent experts, they seemed to instantly sense it and descend..."

Riding the wind and waves in Dao Annihilation, Li Fan felt a faint premonition.

In this vast expanse of Mountains and Seas, it seemed as though time did not flow.

Or rather, time only affected them.

No matter how long they stayed here, it would not affect the interconnected possibilities of the mortal world.

It seemed incredible, but having once navigated against the current of the River of Time, Li Fan could barely comprehend the reason.

"Leaving the mortal world and entering the Mountains and Seas is like instantaneously leaping out of the River of Time. The moment one leaps out, the River of Time seems to freeze. Only when one re-enters does the River of Time flow again."

"If we view the Mountains and Seas as a towering tree growing upwards, with lush leaves, then the various possibilities of the mortal world are the rings of growth on its trunk."

"Below represents the past. Above indicates the future."

"The growth rings representing possibilities are not merely flat discs, but three-dimensional, connecting the top and bottom of the tree according to time."

"Originally, if there were no Dao Annihilation, the past and future of the Mountains and Seas would be completely connected and whole. Those able to travel against time could freely and smoothly move between different positions up and down the tree."

"But because of the appearance of Dao Annihilation, the Tree of Mountains and Seas was severed at its waist."

"Even with time reversal, the range of activity is limited to the segment of the trunk one is currently in."

"And between the growth rings, the original tree trunk tissue has mostly been devoured by Dao Annihilation. Ordinary beings can only survive within the lines of the growth rings."

"When I traveled against the current of the River of Time, I was traversing the Tree of Mountains and Seas longitudinally, following the traces of the growth rings, from top to bottom. Transcending and crossing, however, means leaving the growth ring line and moving across the cross-section of the Tree of Mountains and Seas, resisting Dao Annihilation."

"Whether longitudinally or transversely, it is limited to a single trunk segment."

"And the Other Shore Great World..."

Having personally traversed the Mountains and Seas, Li Fan now had a concrete understanding of their structure.

But even now, he still could not imagine what kind of existence the Other Shore truly was.

"However, one thing is certain: the Other Shore is completely independent of the many possibilities within the Mountains and Seas."

"If forced to draw an analogy, perhaps it can be seen as a place created by hollowing out a certain part of this trunk segment from top to bottom."

"Even without experiencing the River of Time, or traversing Dao Annihilation, one can smoothly travel to all time nodes of all possibilities..."

"If such a capability truly existed, it would truly live up to the name of 'Other Shore.'"

Li Fan envisioned the situation of the Other Shore, his thoughts churning.

Meanwhile, the Grand Unity Wooden Staff, fleeing frantically in Dao Annihilation through dozens of attempts, finally led the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship to a place where life converged!

It was not a complete possibility.

But an Immortal Coffin floating above Dao Annihilation!

Having drifted for an unknown period, the surface of the Immortal Coffin had turned completely black.

Even at a distance, Li Fan and the Twelve True Immortals on the wooden boat could faintly discern an ominous aura clinging to it.

The Grand Unity Wooden Staff, however, was not picky. Regardless of what lay buried within the Immortal Coffin, it transformed into a black and white Tai Chi, covering the drifting Immortal Coffin as if biting it fiercely.

The black and white Tai Chi diagram rotated rapidly, causing the Immortal Coffin's light and shadows to twist and blur. It slowly sank into the vortex formed by the Tai Chi diagram.

Although the Immortal Coffin's defenses were still intact, there were faint signs of it being swallowed by the Tai Chi diagram.

Just as the Grand Unity Wooden Staff was about to swallow the Immortal Coffin, Li Fan tugged at its invisible tether, forcibly dragging it back from Dao Annihilation.

Back on the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship, it still clung stubbornly to the Immortal Coffin.

Li Fan flicked it several times, shaking the Grand Unity Wooden Staff so violently that its patterns shattered and dispersed. Only then did it reluctantly let go.

It hid in a dark corner, glaring fiercely at Li Fan, who had snatched its prey.

Li Fan, however, paid it no mind, calmly placing the Immortal Coffin before him.

On the wooden boat, the Twelve True Immortals looked solemn. Without realizing it, they had already moved closer together.

"Senior, there seems to be something in this coffin," Ruan Ruiyu warned.

"Ominous..." Li Fan chuckled lightly, completely unconcerned.

He unsealed the coffin.

In an instant, boundless light erupted from within the coffin.

Black qi, accompanied by a bloody glow, was eerie and terrifying.

A figure clad in a bright yellow imperial robe, exuding an air of贵不可言 (noble beyond words), suddenly appeared before Li Fan and the others.

After a moment of silence, the figure coldly questioned, "Since you stand before this Emperor, why do you not bow?"

"Immortal... Immortal Emperor?" Ruan Ruiyu was startled upon seeing the figure, then blurted out in disbelief.

And just as everyone's minds were greatly shaken, this majestic figure suddenly took the opportunity to attack them.

Its imperial robes gradually became tattered.

Its human head transformed into a giant rat's head!

The hearts of the Twelve True Immortals were seized, and they seemed destined to become food for the rat-headed immortal.

"It is indeed you."

Li Fan, however, seemed to have expected it. A transparent furnace rose, surrounding the rat-headed immortal like towering walls, sealing it within.

The Twelve True Immortals, still reeling from fright, stared with lingering horror at the monster within the furnace, which had completely shed its human form and transformed into a giant rat.

Li Fan observed his old acquaintance, watching it struggle furiously within the furnace, yet unable to break through the seal.

"It seems I have truly not strayed far from the Primordial."

"I am still within the range that the Guangwu Star Sea could salvage in Dao Annihilation. To be more precise, I am still in the near-shore region."

The Rat Emperor before him was no different from what he had seen in his previous life.

Having devoured an entire possibility, the Rat Emperor's power was undeniable. Yet, before the current Li Fan, it was utterly helpless.

It was slowly refined within the furnace.

Transforming into nourishment to reinforce the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship.

Li Fan expressionlessly watched as the Rat Emperor disintegrated into countless light and shadow within the furnace.

In his mind, he was contemplating other matters: "I obtained the Sovereign of Heaven's Dao, and was thus able to travel against the River of Time. However, when I returned to ten thousand years ago, the Sovereign of Heaven at that past time node also disappeared. This proves that one who comprehends the principle of 'Reversal' becomes a special existence clinging to the River of Time, traversing the length of the Tree of Mountains and Seas."

"Transcendent experts in the Other Shore might also possess this ability, but it should be due to the unique nature of the Other Shore. If relying solely on their own Dao path, they probably cannot achieve this."

"However, whether it is a Comprehender of Reversal or a Transcendent, they should be unique existences within a severed segment of the Tree of Mountains and Seas. No matter at which time node they perish, it is a complete death. Even the so-called 'reverse flow of time' cannot alter this."

"And the True Reversion..."

Li Fan frowned slightly.

"As a force on par with the Mountains and Seas, it can directly reset and restore the state of the Tree of Mountains and Seas."

"As long as it doesn't exceed the scope of the Mountains and Seas, it will be affected by it."

"However, it is still uncertain whether the scope of True Reversion's influence is limited to the segment of the Tree of Mountains and Seas I am currently in, or the entirety of the Mountains and Seas..."

"There is a way to prove this."

"Elder Shou Qiu!"

"In the previous life, Elder Shou Qiu was not within the Mountains and Seas, but in the Eternal Void beyond the Tree of Mountains and Seas. If True Reversion did not affect him, then he must still retain some memories of my previous life with Chen Dao." At this thought, Li Fan's heart tightened.

"It seems that after reaching the Other Shore Great World, even if True Reversion awakens, it cannot be easily used. At least, before clarifying this point, I should try my best not to expose myself to those Sacred Ones."

Li Fan naturally dared not directly question Elder Shou Qiu for clarification.

Moreover, Zi Yi and Chen Dao, both figures capable of interacting with Elder Shou Qiu, could potentially become triggers for True Reversion's exposure.

Chen Dao was fine, trapped within the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship by Li Fan's "Dao-Discussion."

Zi Yi, however, was beyond Li Fan's control.

"I can only hope that True Reversion's sphere of influence is larger."

"Otherwise, I might have to flee before even reaching the Other Shore." Li Fan tried his best to calm the urgency in his heart.

Li Fan was not an alarmist.

But after his current deductions, he realized the existence of True Reversion had the potential to be exposed. Naturally, he had to make some preparations for the future.

"To give up eating for fear of choking, and not go to the Other Shore, is unacceptable."

"To be blindly optimistic and make no preparations is also unacceptable."

However, after reviewing all the forces at his disposal, Li Fan had yet to find a way to fully retreat from Elder Shou Qiu.

"The Sacred Ones are only concerned with the continued existence of the Mountains and Seas."

"The only thing that might make them somewhat wary is the [True Spirit Blaze] secret art I just learned."

"This method..."

A sharp glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes as he made a decision: "It needs to be put to good use."

"Although the True Spirit Blaze art has the effect of burning mountains and boiling seas, its drawback is that the True Spirit fire spreads too slowly."

"Unless..."

"I am prepared. I will scatter kindling throughout different possibilities and time nodes across the Mountains and Seas!"

"A single spark can start a prairie fire. And my infinite spirituality is enough for me alone to spread the kindling across the Mountains and Seas."

"Then, with a single thought, the Mountains and Seas will burn."

"Although it is highly probable that before the Mountains and Seas are completely burned, the Transcendent experts of the Other Shore will unite to extinguish the fire. And the spirituality I consume to ignite it will also become nourishment for the Mountains and Seas. However, a crippled Mountains and Seas may not survive the erosion of Dao Annihilation."

"The Transcendent experts of the Other Shore... dare not gamble!"

"This method of deterrence should be effective."

Li Fan pondered repeatedly, and the unease in his heart gradually dissipated.

"It seems that before reaching the Other Shore, I still need to make ample preparations."

"Precisely, I will proceed slowly. At each possibility I encounter, I will lay down a hidden hand."

"Other Transcendent experts integrate their many selves. But I, I will expand from one to ten thousand!"

"Hehe..."

Chapter 1600: Sparks Cover Mountains and Seas

In the Immortal Realm, the Celestial Nymph Star Domain.

Tens of thousands of True Immortals gathered, many of them being Nameless existences.

"The Immortal Prime Minister remains in seclusion; we must find a solution quickly."

"The nearby Hanging Palace Star Domain, Age Shattering Star Domain, and Dipper Handle Star Domain have all been swallowed by Dao Annihilation. It seems our Celestial Nymph Star Domain isn't far from destruction!"

"The key is that Dao Annihilation has sealed our Celestial Nymph Star Domain, leaving us nowhere to flee, nowhere to go."

"Everyone, everyone, do not panic and fall into disarray. I have long since sent a message to the Immortal Prime Minister; he has replied and will come out of seclusion in the next few days to organize measures against this calamity..."

"A few more days? By the time Lin Zhaoye comes out, we'll all be dead!"

"No, he must come out today and give us an explanation."

...

The scene was chaotic. The Nameless True Immortals could barely maintain their composure. Ordinary Immortals, however, were already disturbed by the desperate situation created by Dao Annihilation, showing signs of madness.

This was not only due to the life-and-death crisis but also because, under the siege of Dao Annihilation, the Immortals slowly discovered that their "infinite" authority was also affected.

This slow deprivation, which progressed with time, was in some ways more terrifying than an instant death.

In the center of the Immortals, a group of Nameless cultivators were discussing a completely different topic in private.

"Fellow Daoists, have you heard the rumors about the Salvation Immortal Ship today?"

"Dao Annihilation approaches, calamity looms, and the Immortal Prime Minister is dormant. This Salvation Immortal Ship is likely the only way for us to escape, so how could we not have heard of it? But..."

"This Immortal Ship is very peculiar. We've never heard of it before."

"However, the claim that the Salvation Immortal Ship can traverse Dao Annihilation should be true. Although I haven't met the Ship Master, I have encountered the twelve Nameless beings on the ship. Frankly, any one of these twelve Nameless beings is probably stronger than Lin Zhaoye."

"Is Brother Zhao serious?"

"This is a matter of life and death; how could I speak carelessly?"

"Even if the rumors of the Salvation Immortal Ship are true, the conditions for boarding are too demanding. Either offer up an ancient relic of the Mountains and Seas, or become a servant for a hundred thousand years. This..."

"Fellow Daoists, what do you think? Can we unite and seize this so-called Salvation Immortal Ship?"

The Nameless Immortals, who had been chatting idly, fell silent the moment these words were spoken.

Everyone looked at the speaker. It was the notorious Shu Hu, a Nameless True Immortal from the Celestial Nymph Star Domain. His Dao path was associated with fanning flames and shameless instigation.

Everyone who followed Shu Hu's advice invariably met a bad end.

Seeing the cold stares, Shu Hu smiled awkwardly: "My apologies, my apologies, it's just a habit."

"At this crucial juncture, some words cannot be spoken lightly. The Master of this Immortal Ship is clearly a Transcendent expert. Now that the Dao Annihilation calamity has arrived and the Immortal Realm is falling apart, each Star Domain struggles for survival. In this situation, the Salvation Immortal Ship is very likely our only way to live. Being a servant for a hundred thousand years is acceptable compared to perishing."

"Moreover, although it's said to be servitude for a hundred thousand years, according to those twelve Nameless ones, they rarely need to act. Not only can they, as un-Transcendents, personally experience Dao Annihilation and comprehend the Great Dao of the Mountains and Seas, but there's also hope of being carried with it to the legendary Other Shore Great World..."

After a discussion among the Immortals, the atmosphere became lively again. Many Nameless cultivators were clearly moved.

"But where is that Salvation Immortal Ship now?"

A group of Nameless cultivators scanned the Celestial Nymph Star Domain, trying to find traces of the so-called Salvation Immortal Ship.

Yet they found nothing.

They did not know that within the Dao Annihilation clouds surrounding the Celestial Nymph Star Domain, a magnificent giant ship was moored.

It was none other than the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm!

However, compared to before, the state of this Profound Yellow Immortal Realm was somewhat strange.

It seemed to be made of illusory projections, yet all life within the Profound Yellow world was purely tangible.

Liu Liangcai, one of the original twelve True Immortals from the Primordial possibility, had already ascended to the Nameless Realm.

He came to the Outer Heavens of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm to report his progress to Li Fan.

"So, this possibility is indeed beyond saving?" Without revealing his true form, Li Fan's voice vaguely emanated from the horizon.

Liu Liangcai, however, dared not be negligent and nodded solemnly: "According to custom, I have gathered usable individuals. In ten years, when Dao Annihilation completely swallows this possibility, the Immortal Ship 'Ren Yin' can set sail again."

No reply came from Li Fan for a long time.

Liu Liangcai's heart tightened, thinking Li Fan was dissatisfied with his progress, and added: "Five years. If Dao Annihilation is further stirred, the speed of this possibility's destruction can be accelerated."

Only then did Li Fan respond: "I'll give you half a year. Liangcai, you are still too soft."

"I have long told you that if the possibility you encounter is still in a stable and prosperous state, then quietly leave my phantom there and swiftly depart."

"If it has already been targeted by Dao Annihilation and is on the verge of peril, then help it perish as soon as possible, gather usable people and things, and strengthen the Immortal Ship."

"You have also sailed in the Mountains and Seas for many years; do you not know the immensity of the Mountains and Seas, with countless possibilities? If every one of you drags your feet like this, how long will it take for us to complete our plan and set sail for the Other Shore?"

Although Li Fan spoke calmly, cold sweat had already begun to drip from Liu Liangcai's forehead.

"Half a year... after half a year, we will certainly set sail again."

After saying this, Liu Liangcai felt his vision blur, and he was expelled from the Outer Heavens of Profound Yellow.

He breathed a sigh of relief, as if a great burden had been lifted.

"Senior's prestige is becoming more and more terrifying."

Liu Liangcai's gaze passed through the Dao Annihilation beyond the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship and landed on the Celestial Nymph Star Domain.

"May my Daoist friends not blame me for not perishing with them. You all are not to blame..."

After a slight hesitation, Liu Liangcai made up his mind.

He remembered that when he first personally facilitated the surging of Dao Annihilation, enveloping an entire possibility, and witnessed countless lives perish because of him, his heart felt as if struck by endless lightning, and he almost collapsed.

But later...

He did it many times, and slowly got used to it.

Muttering to himself, he bowed halfway towards the Outer Heavens of Profound Yellow: "Ink Slaughter Saint Body, please appear."

A moment later, a black phantom, in response, quietly appeared between heaven and earth.

Without a glance, it plunged directly into the Dao Annihilation clouds outside the Immortal Ship.

Moments later, winds and clouds surged, like a gathering storm.

Towards the Celestial Nymph Star Domain, which was already reduced to a corner of its former self, it advanced inch by inch.

"Your remaining time is not much," Liu Liangcai sighed softly.

...

Meanwhile, within the true Profound Yellow Immortal Ship, Li Fan sensed that Ink Slaughter seemed to have grown stronger and nodded slightly.

It was unknown how much time had passed since he had first conceived the plan to scatter True Spirit sparks across the Mountains and Seas. Li Fan had been implementing this plan all these years.

Initially, it proceeded quite smoothly. With the Grand Unity Wooden Staff, Ink Slaughter, and the Dao-One Worms clearing the way, the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship was able to smoothly shuttle between different possibilities, quietly leaving behind True Spirit sparks.

But later, Li Fan found that while this approach was indeed smooth, its efficiency was too slow.

Even though the Mountains and Seas were riddled with holes from Dao Annihilation, they were still too vast.

At this rate, even if Li Fan spent his entire life, he would never be able to complete the threatening plan of scattering True Spirit sparks across the Mountains and Seas.

"To create a great fire that threatens the Mountains and Seas and the Other Shore, the initial sparks must cover about one percent of the entire Mountains and Seas. Only then, when I am in danger, can these sparks ignite everywhere, burning mountains and boiling seas with the fire of True Spirits."

"One percent of the Mountains and Seas seems insignificant. However, for a cultivator, it is an unimaginably vast number."

Only by personal experience did he truly understand the meaning of the "infinite" nature of the Mountains and Seas.

Li Fan alone could not complete the predetermined plan. So he decisively changed his approach.

He used the feedback of his Heavenly Sitting Technique to create slightly weaker phantom images of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

He appointed the twelve True Immortals as helmsmen, replacing himself, to control these Immortal Ships and navigate them to various parts of the Mountains and Seas.

This was just the first step.

As Li Fan had just explained to Liu Liangcai, what the twelve True Immortals needed to do was to wander through different possibilities and place True Spirit sparks.

At the same time, they were to recruit usable individuals.

Then, these newly recruited Nameless True Immortals would pilot new Profound Yellow Immortal Ships, undertaking a new round of missions.

This cycle would repeat continuously.

"To date, I have nearly a thousand Profound Yellow Immortal Ships sailing in different corners of the Mountains and Seas."

"But even so, achieving the plan is still a distant goal."

Li Fan sighed softly.

"Fortunately, I am not without gains."

As more and more True Spirit sparks were placed, Li Fan, even in the midst of Dao Annihilation, could clearly feel "himself" from different possibilities within the Mountains and Seas.

These scattered spiritual entities across the Mountains and Seas were like his eyes and tentacles, helping Li Fan to observe the Mountains and Seas more comprehensively.

"If in the past I was a blind man touching an elephant."

"Then now, tens of thousands of people are helping me touch it."

"Though the giant elephant is vast, its true form is slowly revealing itself."

"Just as I had anticipated."

In Li Fan's mind, the image of a hollowed-out, fragmented tree trunk reappeared.

Countless red stars were scattered throughout the trunk.

Even though they didn't yet occupy the majority of the area, they were already quite substantial.

"The more I see and feel, the stronger I become."

"Just like the 'Unification of All Selves' pursued by Evil Su Bai and his kind, each placement I complete in a possibility means I absorb that self from that possibility."

"From one to ten thousand, from ten thousand to one."

"All paths lead to the same destination."

And precisely because Li Fan himself was growing stronger, the Heavenly Sitting Technique could continuously generate feedback power, condensing new phantom images of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm. This was what sustained Li Fan's plan to scatter sparks.

Of course, this plan was not always smooth sailing.

The phantom Profound Yellow Immortal Ships, without the Mountains and Seas Lone Sail to stabilize them, were significantly less stable in Dao Annihilation. If the Dao Annihilation's waves were a little stronger, they were at risk of capsizing at any moment.

However, even if a phantom Immortal Ship was swallowed by Dao Annihilation, Li Fan didn't suffer significant losses. Nameless True Immortals, who served as helmsmen, were countless in the Mountains and Seas. Even if all of them died, more could be recruited at any time.

The real variable came from the changes in Dao Annihilation itself.

Initially, Li Fan didn't feel much.

But when more and more, approximately a hundred, phantom Profound Yellow Immortal Ships capsized in Dao Annihilation, Li Fan finally noticed something was wrong.

Outside the true Profound Yellow Immortal Ship, the waves of Dao Annihilation were mysteriously growing larger.

Only then did Li Fan understand: each time Dao Annihilation swallowed a Profound Yellow Immortal Ship, even if it was just a phantom, its understanding of the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship still increased.

After more than a hundred Profound Yellow Immortal Ships were destroyed, Dao Annihilation's erosion of the true Profound Yellow Immortal Realm intensified qualitatively, reaching a new level.

This was what Li Fan perceived.

"This is truly the insidious part of Dao Annihilation."

Thus, reluctantly, while maintaining his plan to scatter True Spirit sparks, Li Fan also had to try to reduce the rate of Immortal Ship destruction. He didn't demand 100% safety for the Immortal Ships; at the very least, his own growth in strength had to outpace the growth of Dao Annihilation's erosive power.

Otherwise, before he could scatter all the True Spirit sparks, he would perish in Dao Annihilation himself.

This was why Li Fan had said so much to Liu Liangcai earlier, and with such patience.

In the past, Liu Liangcai would have been thrown into Dao Annihilation by Li Fan long ago!

With Li Fan's change in attitude, and the support of powers like Ink Slaughter and the Dao-One Worms in the phantom Immortal Ships, the accident rate significantly decreased. Not only did the efficiency of placing Li Fan's True Spirit sparks greatly improve, but it also unexpectedly led to the birth of many "Transcendent experts."

One must know that the time these "apostles" carrying Li Fan's orders spent on missions in different possibilities was an insignificant fraction of their lives.

For the vast majority of the time, they were navigating the boundless Mountains and Seas, constantly facing Dao Annihilation.

In a sense, this was an excellent place to comprehend the true meaning of Transcendence.

Such suitable places, where Nameless True Immortals could so closely encounter Dao Annihilation and cultivate peacefully, simply did not exist in ordinary possibilities.

Those chosen by Li Fan as apostles were all individuals of extraordinary talent within a single possibility.

It was not surprising that some seeds of Transcendence emerged from them.

Li Fan had also explicitly told all "helmsman apostles" that if they could attain Transcendence and reach the Other Shore independently of the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship, they were free to go.

The hundred-thousand-year agreement was thus voided.

If they met again on the Other Shore, they could still have the opportunity to discuss the Dao.

Li Fan was not afraid that his plan to scatter True Spirit sparks would be leaked, because, apart from the original twelve True Immortals, these later-added helmsman apostles did not know the fundamental reason why the Immortal Ship sailed to different possibilities.

They only believed it to be Li Fan's unique method of cultivation.

And the original twelve True Immortals remained firmly under Li Fan's control.

"The cultivation method of 'Unification of All Selves' is indeed highly efficient."

"If I were to meet Evil Su Bai again now, even without using intimidation, I could still contend with him directly."

Chapter 1601: The Other Shore Illuminates with Splendor

The Grand Unity Wooden Staff lay dying, its black and white faces at both ends faded as if made of paper. The patterns on its body had almost entirely vanished, leaving only a few remnants.

Having survived the ordeal, it became utterly obedient.

When Li Fan offered it a Profound Yellow phantom, it eagerly devoured it, even showing an ingratiating expression.

It only slowly recovered after a full meal, but it did not remain docile for long.

Just three days later, the Grand Unity Wooden Staff reverted to its old ways.

Having already realized the immense power of Li Fan, this time it did not choose to attack him again. Instead, it leaped directly out of the ship, fleeing towards the source of the "scent" it had sensed earlier in Dao Annihilation.

It did not detect that the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship was following closely behind.

"This beast, though possessing sentience, truly lacks wisdom." The dwarfish elder, Ruan Ruiyu, the eldest of the Twelve True Immortals, joked upon seeing this.

"Senior is right, a beast is just a beast," everyone else echoed in agreement.

The Grand Unity Wooden Staff's memory was indeed poor.

Each time it was tormented to the brink of death in Dao Annihilation, yet given the slightest opportunity, it would instinctively flee back into it. It was as if something on the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship was more terrifying than Dao Annihilation itself.

After a few initial jests, the Twelve True Immortals finally realized something. Even if the Grand Unity Wooden Staff's intelligence was low, its innate survival instinct should still be present. Fleeing once or twice could be attributed to momentary desperation. But if it continued this way...

Everyone looked at Li Fan, who stood alone at the prow, his expression inscrutable. A chill once again rose in their hearts.

The questions that were on the tip of their tongues were forcefully suppressed.

The Twelve True Immortals in their hearts already somewhat regretted having boarded this "pirate ship." It was said to be sailing towards the Great World of the Other Shore, but from all indications, their host did not seem intent on delivering them there easily.

But besides continuing to stay on the ship, pressing forward into the unknown, they had no other choice. Venturing into Dao Annihilation unprotected meant certain death. Resisting Li Fan would likely lead to an even swifter demise. Though bitterness filled the hearts of the twelve brothers, they could only silently endure.

The Twelve True Immortals did not know that they had misunderstood Li Fan in this regard.

It wasn't that he didn't want to take them to the Great World of the Other Shore.

It was that Li Fan himself didn't know where this so-called Other Shore was, or how to get there.

"Theoretically, in this vast Mountains and Seas, there should be many lighthouse-like beacons pointing the specific direction of the Other Shore. A new Transcendent expert only needs to steadfastly find the nearest lighthouse. Then, continuing to sail towards the next lighthouse, they will eventually reach the Great World of the Other Shore."

"But for some reason, I have been adrift in Dao Annihilation for so long, yet I have seen no trace of a lighthouse."

"There are two possibilities. I have not condensed my own Transcendent True Intent, so even if a lighthouse is right before me, I cannot perceive it. This possibility is not very high, as the lone sail above my head is not fake."

"The other possibility is that traversing the Mountains and Seas simply takes this much time. As I saw in the memories of the lone sail. Without directional guidance, the time required to traverse can exhaust the lifespan of a Transcendent expert. However, with clear directional guidance..."

"The time needed, even if reduced by a hundredfold, would still be an unimaginably long period."

Li Fan was mentally prepared for this.

He did not expect to reach the Other Shore anytime soon.

"When Zi Yi descended, he repeatedly mentioned 'not wanting to run errands' and 'not taking this trip for nothing.' This indicates that even in the eyes of an experienced Transcendent expert like him, descending from the Other Shore to a possibility is not a negligible expenditure."

"But earlier, when the Primordial possibility involved those Transcendent experts, they seemed to instantly sense it and descend..."

Riding the wind and waves in Dao Annihilation, Li Fan felt a faint premonition.

In this vast expanse of Mountains and Seas, it seemed as though time did not flow.

Or rather, time only affected them.

No matter how long they stayed here, it would not affect the interconnected possibilities of the mortal world.

It seemed incredible, but having once navigated against the current of the River of Time, Li Fan could barely comprehend the reason.

"Leaving the mortal world and entering the Mountains and Seas is like instantaneously leaping out of the River of Time. The moment one leaps out, the River of Time seems to freeze. Only when one re-enters does the River of Time flow again."

"If we view the Mountains and Seas themselves as a towering tree growing upwards, with lush leaves, then the various possibilities of the mortal world are the rings of growth on its trunk."

"Below represents the past. Above indicates the future."

"The growth rings representing possibilities are not merely flat discs, but three-dimensional, like time, they penetrate the tree from top to bottom."

"Originally, if there were no Dao Annihilation, the past and future of the Mountains and Seas would be completely connected and whole. Those able to travel against time could freely and smoothly move between different positions up and down the tree."

"But because of the appearance of Dao Annihilation, the Tree of Mountains and Seas was severed at its waist."

"Even if time can naturally reverse, the range of activity is limited to the segment of the trunk one is currently in."

"And between the growth rings, the original tree trunk tissue has mostly been devoured by Dao Annihilation. Ordinary beings can only survive within the lines of the growth rings."

"My traversal against the current of the River of Time was a longitudinal journey through the Tree of Mountains and Seas, following the traces of the growth rings, from top to bottom. Transcending and crossing, however, mean leaving the growth ring line and moving across the cross-section of the Tree of Mountains and Seas, resisting Dao Annihilation."

"Whether longitudinally or transversely, it is limited to a single trunk segment."

"And the Great World of the Other Shore..."

Having personally traversed the Mountains and Seas, Li Fan now had a concrete understanding of their structure.

But even now, he still could not imagine what kind of existence the Other Shore truly was.

"However, one thing is certain: the Other Shore is completely independent of the many possibilities within the Mountains and Seas."

"If forced to draw an analogy, perhaps it can be seen as a place created by hollowing out a certain part of this trunk segment from top to bottom."

"Even without experiencing the River of Time, or traversing Dao Annihilation, one can smoothly travel to all time nodes of all possibilities..."

"If such a capability truly existed, it would truly live up to the name of 'Other Shore.'"

Li Fan envisioned the situation of the Other Shore, his thoughts churning.

Meanwhile, the Grand Unity Wooden Staff, fleeing frantically in Dao Annihilation through dozens of attempts, finally led the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship to a place where life converged!

It was not a complete possibility.

But an Immortal Coffin floating above Dao Annihilation!

Having drifted for an unknown period, the surface of the Immortal Coffin had turned completely black.

Even at a distance, Li Fan and the Twelve True Immortals on the wooden boat could faintly discern an ominous aura clinging to it.

The Grand Unity Wooden Staff, however, was not picky. Regardless of what lay buried within the Immortal Coffin, it transformed into a black and white Tai Chi. It directly covered the drifting Immortal Coffin, as if biting it fiercely.

The black and white Tai Chi diagram rotated rapidly, causing the Immortal Coffin's light and shadows to twist and blur. It slowly sank into the vortex formed by the Tai Chi diagram.

Although the Immortal Coffin's defenses were still intact, there were faint signs of it being swallowed by the Tai Chi diagram.

Just as the Grand Unity Wooden Staff was about to swallow the Immortal Coffin, Li Fan tugged at its invisible tether, forcibly dragging it back from Dao Annihilation.

Back on the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship, it still clung stubbornly to the Immortal Coffin.

Li Fan flicked it several times, shaking the Grand Unity Wooden Staff so violently that its patterns shattered and dispersed. Only then did it reluctantly let go.

It hid in a dark corner, glaring fiercely at Li Fan, who had snatched its prey.

Li Fan, however, paid it no mind, calmly placing the Immortal Coffin before him.

On the wooden boat, the Twelve True Immortals looked solemn. Without realizing it, they had already moved closer together.

"Senior, there seems to be something in this coffin," Ruan Ruiyu warned.

"Ominous..." Li Fan chuckled lightly, completely unconcerned.

He unsealed the coffin.

In an instant, boundless light erupted from within the coffin.

Black qi, accompanied by a bloody glow, was eerie and terrifying.

A figure clad in a bright yellow imperial robe, exuding an air of nobility beyond words, suddenly appeared before Li Fan and the others.

After a moment of silence, the figure coldly questioned, "Since you stand before this Emperor, why do you not bow?"

"Immortal... Immortal Emperor?" Ruan Ruiyu was startled upon seeing the figure, then blurted out in disbelief.

And just as everyone's minds were greatly shaken, this majestic figure suddenly took the opportunity to attack them.

Its imperial robes gradually became tattered.

Its human head transformed into a giant rat's head!

The hearts of the Twelve True Immortals were seized, and they seemed destined to become food for the rat-headed immortal.

"It is indeed you."

Li Fan, however, seemed to have expected it. A transparent furnace rose, surrounding the rat-headed immortal like towering walls, sealing it within.

The Twelve True Immortals, still reeling from fright, stared with lingering horror at the monster within the furnace, which had completely shed its human form and transformed into a giant rat.

Li Fan observed his old acquaintance, watching it struggle furiously within the furnace, yet unable to break through the seal.

"It seems I have truly not strayed far from the Primordial."

"I am still within the range that the Guangwu Star Sea could salvage in Dao Annihilation. To be more precise, I am still in the near-shore region."

The Rat Emperor before him was no different from what he had seen in his previous life.

Having devoured an entire possibility, the Rat Emperor's power was undeniable. Yet, before the current Li Fan, it was utterly helpless.

It was slowly refined within the furnace.

Transforming into nourishment to reinforce the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship.

Li Fan expressionlessly watched as the Rat Emperor disintegrated into countless light and shadow within the furnace.

In his mind, he was contemplating other matters: "I obtained the Sovereign of Heaven's Dao, and was thus able to travel against the River of Time. However, when I returned to ten thousand years ago, the Sovereign of Heaven at that past time node also disappeared. This proves that one who comprehends the principle of 'Reversal' becomes a special existence clinging to the River of Time, traversing the length of the Tree of Mountains and Seas."

"Transcendent experts in the Other Shore might also possess this ability. However, it should be due to the unique nature of the Other Shore. If relying solely on their own Dao path, they probably cannot achieve this."

"However, whether it is a Comprehender of Reversal or a Transcendent, they should be unique existences within a severed segment of the Tree of Mountains and Seas. No matter at which time node they perish, it is a complete death. Even the so-called 'reverse flow of time' cannot alter this."

"And the True Reversion..."

Li Fan frowned slightly.

"As a force on par with the Mountains and Seas, it is capable of directly resetting and restoring the state of the Tree of Mountains and Seas."

"As long as it doesn't exceed the scope of the Mountains and Seas, it will be affected by it."

"However, it is still uncertain whether the scope of True Reversion's influence is limited to the segment of the Tree of Mountains and Seas I am currently in, or the entirety of the Mountains and Seas..."

"There is a way to prove this."

"Elder Shou Qiu!"

"In the previous life, Elder Shou Qiu was not within the Mountains and Seas, but in the Eternal Void beyond the Tree of Mountains and Seas. If True Reversion did not affect him, then he must still retain some memories of my previous life with Chen Dao." At this thought, Li Fan's heart tightened.

"It seems that after reaching the Great World of the Other Shore, even if True Reversion awakens, it cannot be easily used. At least, before clarifying this point, I should try my best not to expose myself to those Sacred Ones."

Li Fan naturally dared not directly question Elder Shou Qiu for clarification.

Moreover, Zi Yi and Chen Dao, these two figures able to interact with Elder Shou Qiu, could potentially become triggers for True Reversion's exposure.

Chen Dao was fine, trapped within the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship by Li Fan's "Dao-Discussion."

Zi Yi, however, was beyond Li Fan's control.

"I can only hope that True Reversion's sphere of influence is larger."

"Otherwise, I might have to flee before even reaching the Other Shore." Li Fan tried his best to calm the urgency in his heart.

Li Fan was not an alarmist.

But after his current deductions, he realized the existence of True Reversion had the potential to be exposed. Naturally, he had to make some preparations for the future.

"To give up eating for fear of choking, and not go to the Other Shore, is unacceptable."

"To be blindly optimistic and make no preparations is also unacceptable."

However, after reviewing all the forces at his disposal, Li Fan had yet to find a way to fully retreat from Elder Shou Qiu.

"The Sacred Ones are only concerned with the continued existence of the Mountains and Seas."

"The only thing that might make them somewhat wary is the [True Spirit Blaze] secret art I just learned."

"This method..."

A sharp glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes as he made a decision: "It needs to be put to good use."

"Although the True Spirit Blaze art has the effect of burning mountains and boiling seas, its drawback is that the True Spirit fire spreads too slowly."

"Unless..."

"I am prepared. I will scatter kindling throughout different possibilities and time nodes across the Mountains and Seas!"

"A single spark can start a prairie fire. And my infinite spirituality is enough for me alone to spread the kindling across the Mountains and Seas."

"Then, with a single thought, the Mountains and Seas will burn."

"Although it is highly probable that before the Mountains and Seas are completely burned, the Transcendent experts of the Other Shore will unite to extinguish the fire. And the spirituality I consume to ignite it will also become nourishment for the Mountains and Seas. However, a crippled Mountains and Seas may not survive the erosion of Dao Annihilation."

"The Transcendent experts of the Other Shore... dare not gamble!"

"This method of deterrence should be effective."

Li Fan pondered repeatedly, and the unease in his heart gradually dissipated.

"It seems that before reaching the Other Shore, I still need to make ample preparations."

"Precisely, I will proceed slowly. At each possibility I encounter, I will lay down a hidden hand."

"Other Transcendent experts integrate their many selves. But I, I will expand from one to ten thousand!"

"Heh..."

Chapter 1602: The One Who Harmonizes with Mountains and Seas

In the Immortal Realm, the Celestial Nymph Star Domain.

Tens of thousands of True Immortals gathered, many of them being Nameless existences.

"The Immortal Prime Minister remains in seclusion; we must find a solution quickly."

"The nearby Suspended Arch Star Domain, Age-Shattering Star Domain, and Dipper-Handle Star Domain have all been swallowed by Dao Annihilation. It seems our Celestial Nymph Star Domain isn't far from destruction!"

"The critical point is that Dao Annihilation has sealed our Celestial Nymph Star Domain, leaving us nowhere to flee, nowhere to go."

"Everyone, everyone, do not panic and fall into disarray. I have long since sent a message to the Immortal Prime Minister; he has replied and will come out of seclusion in the next few days to organize measures against this calamity..."

"A few more days? By the time Lin Zhaoye comes out, we'll all be dead!"

"No, he must come out today and give us an explanation."

...

The scene was chaotic. Nameless True Immortals could barely maintain their composure. Ordinary Immortals, however, were already disturbed by the desperate situation created by Dao Annihilation, showing signs of madness.

This was not only due to the life-and-death crisis but also because, under the siege of Dao Annihilation, the Immortals slowly discovered that their "infinite" authority was also affected.

This slow deprivation, which progressed with time, was in some ways more terrifying than an instant death.

In the center of the Immortals, a group of Nameless cultivators were discussing a completely different topic in private.

"Fellow Daoists, have you heard the rumors about the Salvation Immortal Ship today?"

"Dao Annihilation approaches, calamity looms, and the Immortal Prime Minister is dormant. This Salvation Immortal Ship is likely the only way for us to escape, so how could we not have heard of it? But..."

"This Immortal Ship is very peculiar. We've never heard of it before."

"However, the claim that the Salvation Immortal Ship can traverse Dao Annihilation should be true. Although I haven't met the Ship Master, I have encountered the twelve Nameless beings on the ship. Frankly, any one of these twelve Nameless beings is probably stronger than Lin Zhaoye."

"Is Brother Zhao serious?"

"This is a matter of life and death; how could I speak carelessly?"

"Even if the rumors of the Salvation Immortal Ship are true, the conditions for boarding are too demanding. Either offer up an ancient relic of the Mountains and Seas, or become a servant for a hundred thousand years. This..."

"Fellow Daoists, what do you think? Can we unite and seize this so-called Salvation Immortal Ship?"

The Nameless Immortals, who had been chatting idly, fell silent the moment these words were spoken.

Everyone looked at the speaker. It was the notorious Shu Hu, a Nameless True Immortal from the Celestial Nymph Star Domain. His Dao path was associated with fanning flames and shameless instigation.

Everyone who followed Shu Hu's advice invariably met a bad end.

Seeing the cold stares, Shu Hu smiled awkwardly: "My apologies, my apologies, it's just a habit."

"At this crucial juncture, some words cannot be spoken lightly. The Master of this Immortal Ship is clearly a Transcendent expert. Now that the Dao Annihilation calamity has arrived and the Immortal Realm is falling apart, each Star Domain struggles for survival. In this situation, the Salvation Immortal Ship is very likely our only way to live. Being a servant for a hundred thousand years is acceptable compared to perishing."

"Moreover, although it's said to be servitude for a hundred thousand years, according to those twelve Nameless ones, they rarely need to act. Not only can they, as un-Transcendents, personally experience Dao Annihilation and comprehend the Great Dao of the Mountains and Seas, but there's also hope of being carried with it to the legendary Other Shore Great World..."

After a discussion among the Immortals, the atmosphere became lively again. Many Nameless cultivators were clearly moved.

"But where is that Salvation Immortal Ship now?"

A group of Nameless cultivators scanned the Celestial Nymph Star Domain, trying to find traces of the so-called Salvation Immortal Ship.

Yet they found nothing.

They did not know that within the Dao Annihilation clouds surrounding the Celestial Nymph Star Domain, a magnificent giant ship was moored.

It was none other than the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm!

However, compared to before, the state of this Profound Yellow Immortal Realm was somewhat strange.

It seemed to be made of illusory projections, yet all life within the Profound Yellow world was purely tangible.

Liu Liangcai, one of the original twelve True Immortals from the Primordial possibility, had already ascended to the Nameless Realm.

He came to the Outer Heavens of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm to report his progress to Li Fan.

"So, this possibility is indeed beyond saving?" Without revealing his true form, Li Fan's voice vaguely emanated from the horizon.

Liu Liangcai, however, dared not be negligent and nodded solemnly: "I acted according to custom, gathering suitable individuals. In ten years, when Dao Annihilation completely swallows this possibility, the Immortal Ship 'Ren Yin' can set sail again."

No reply came from Li Fan for a long time.

Liu Liangcai's heart tightened, thinking Li Fan was dissatisfied with his progress, and added: "Five years. If Dao Annihilation is further stirred, the speed of this possibility's destruction can be accelerated."

Only then did Li Fan respond: "I'll give you half a year. Liangcai, you are still too soft."

"I have long told you that if the possibility you encounter is still in a stable and prosperous state, then quietly leave my phantom there and swiftly depart."

"If it has already been targeted by Dao Annihilation and is on the verge of peril, then help it perish as soon as possible, gather usable people and things, and strengthen the Immortal Ship."

"You have also sailed in the Mountains and Seas for many years; do you not know the immensity of the Mountains and Seas, with countless possibilities? If every one of you drags your feet like this, how long will it take for us to complete our plan and set sail for the Other Shore?"

Although Li Fan spoke calmly, cold sweat had already begun to drip from Liu Liangcai's forehead.

"Half a year... after half a year, we will certainly set sail again."

After saying this, Liu Liangcai felt his vision blur, and he was expelled from the Outer Heavens of Profound Yellow.

He breathed a sigh of relief, as if a great burden had been lifted.

"Senior's prestige is becoming more and more terrifying."

Liu Liangcai's gaze passed through the Dao Annihilation beyond the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship and landed on the Celestial Nymph Star Domain.

"May my Daoist friends not blame me for not perishing with them. You all are not to blame..."

After a slight hesitation, Liu Liangcai made up his mind.

He remembered that when he first personally facilitated the surging of Dao Annihilation, enveloping an entire possibility, and witnessed countless lives perish because of him, his heart felt as if struck by endless lightning, and he almost collapsed.

But later...

He did it many times, and slowly got used to it.

Muttering to himself, he bowed halfway towards the Outer Heavens of Profound Yellow: "Please, Ink Slaughter Sacred Body."

A moment later, a black phantom, in response, quietly appeared between heaven and earth.

Without a glance, it plunged directly into the Dao Annihilation clouds outside the Immortal Ship.

Moments later, winds and clouds surged, like a gathering storm.

Towards the Celestial Nymph Star Domain, which was already reduced to a corner of its former self, it advanced inch by inch.

"Your remaining time is not much," Liu Liangcai sighed softly.

...

Meanwhile, within the true Profound Yellow Immortal Ship, Li Fan sensed that Ink Slaughter seemed to have grown stronger and nodded slightly.

It was unknown how much time had passed since he had first conceived the plan to scatter True Spirit sparks across the Mountains and Seas. Li Fan had been implementing this plan all these years.

Initially, it proceeded quite smoothly. With the Grand Unity Wooden Staff, Ink Slaughter, and the Dao-One Worms clearing the way, the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship was able to smoothly shuttle between different possibilities, quietly leaving behind True Spirit sparks.

But later, Li Fan found that while this approach was indeed smooth, its efficiency was too slow.

Even though the Mountains and Seas were riddled with holes from Dao Annihilation, they were still too vast.

At this rate, even if Li Fan spent his entire life, he would never be able to complete the threatening plan of scattering True Spirit sparks across the Mountains and Seas.

"To create a great fire that threatens the Mountains and Seas and the Other Shore, the initial sparks must cover about one percent of the entire Mountains and Seas. Only then, when I am in danger, can these sparks ignite everywhere, burning mountains and boiling seas with the fire of True Spirits."

"One percent of the Mountains and Seas seems insignificant. However, for a cultivator, it is an unimaginably vast number."

Only by personal experience did he truly understand the meaning of the "infinite" nature of the Mountains and Seas.

Li Fan alone could not complete the predetermined plan. So he decisively changed his approach.

He used the feedback of his Heavenly Sitting Technique to create slightly weaker phantom images of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

He appointed the twelve True Immortals as helmsmen, replacing himself, to control these Immortal Ships and navigate them to various parts of the Mountains and Seas.

This was just the first step.

As Li Fan had just explained to Liu Liangcai, what the twelve True Immortals needed to do was to wander through different possibilities and place True Spirit sparks.

At the same time, they were to recruit usable individuals.

Then, these newly recruited Nameless True Immortals would pilot new Profound Yellow Immortal Ships, undertaking a new round of missions.

This cycle would repeat continuously.

"To date, I have nearly a thousand Profound Yellow Immortal Ships sailing in different corners of the Mountains and Seas."

"But even so, achieving the plan is still a distant goal."

Li Fan sighed softly.

"Fortunately, I am not without gains."

As more and more True Spirit sparks were placed, Li Fan, even in the midst of Dao Annihilation, could clearly feel "himself" from different possibilities within the Mountains and Seas.

These scattered spiritual entities across the Mountains and Seas were like his eyes and tentacles, helping Li Fan to observe the Mountains and Seas more comprehensively.

"If in the past I was a blind man touching an elephant."

"Then now, tens of thousands of people are helping me touch it."

"Though the giant elephant is vast, its true form is slowly revealing itself."

"Just as I had anticipated."

In Li Fan's mind, the image of a hollowed-out, fragmented tree trunk reappeared.

Countless red stars were scattered throughout the trunk.

Even though they didn't yet occupy the majority of the area, they were already quite substantial.

"The more I see and feel, the stronger I become."

"Just like the 'Unification of All Selves' pursued by Evil Su Bai and his kind, each placement I complete in a possibility means I absorb that self from that possibility."

"From one to ten thousand, from ten thousand to one."

"All paths lead to the same destination."

And precisely because Li Fan himself was growing stronger, the Heavenly Sitting Technique could continuously generate feedback power, condensing new phantom images of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm. This was what sustained Li Fan's plan to scatter sparks.

Of course, this plan was not always smooth sailing.

The phantom Profound Yellow Immortal Ships, without the Mountains and Seas Lone Sail to stabilize them, were significantly less stable in Dao Annihilation. If the Dao Annihilation's waves were a little stronger, they were at risk of capsizing at any moment.

However, even if a phantom Immortal Ship was swallowed by Dao Annihilation, Li Fan didn't suffer significant losses. Nameless True Immortals, who served as helmsmen, were countless in the Mountains and Seas. Even if all of them died, more could be recruited at any time.

The real variable came from the changes in Dao Annihilation itself.

Initially, Li Fan didn't feel much.

But when more and more, approximately a hundred, phantom Profound Yellow Immortal Ships capsized in Dao Annihilation, Li Fan finally noticed something was wrong.

Outside the true Profound Yellow Immortal Ship, the waves of Dao Annihilation were mysteriously growing larger.

Only then did Li Fan understand: each time Dao Annihilation swallowed a Profound Yellow Immortal Ship, even if it was just a phantom, its understanding of the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship still increased.

One hundred Profound Yellow Immortal Ships were destroyed, causing Dao Annihilation's erosion of the true Profound Yellow Immortal Realm to intensify qualitatively, reaching a new level.

This was what Li Fan perceived.

"This is truly the insidious part of Dao Annihilation."

Thus, reluctantly, while maintaining his plan to scatter True Spirit sparks, Li Fan also had to try to reduce the rate of Immortal Ship destruction. He didn't demand 100% safety for the Immortal Ships; at the very least, his own growth in strength had to outpace the growth of Dao Annihilation's erosive power.

Otherwise, before he could scatter all the True Spirit sparks, he would perish in Dao Annihilation himself.

This was why Li Fan had said so much to Liu Liangcai earlier, and with such patience.

In the past, Liu Liangcai would have been thrown into Dao Annihilation by Li Fan long ago!

With Li Fan's change in attitude, and the support of powers like Ink Slaughter and the Dao-One Worms in the phantom Immortal Ships, the accident rate significantly decreased. Not only did the efficiency of placing Li Fan's True Spirit sparks greatly improve, but it also unexpectedly led to the birth of many "Transcendent experts."

One must know that the time these "apostles" carrying Li Fan's orders spent on missions in different possibilities was an insignificant fraction of their lives.

For the vast majority of the time, they were navigating the boundless Mountains and Seas, constantly facing Dao Annihilation.

In a sense, this was an excellent place to comprehend the true meaning of Transcendence.

Such suitable places, where Nameless True Immortals could so closely encounter Dao Annihilation and cultivate peacefully, simply did not exist in ordinary possibilities.

Those chosen by Li Fan as apostles were all individuals of extraordinary talent within a single possibility.

It was not surprising that some seeds of Transcendence emerged from them.

Li Fan had also explicitly told all "helmsman apostles" that if they could attain Transcendence and reach the Other Shore independently of the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship, they were free to go.

The hundred-thousand-year agreement was thus voided.

If they met again on the Other Shore, they could still have the opportunity to discuss the Dao.

Li Fan was not afraid that his plan to scatter True Spirit sparks would be leaked, because, apart from the original twelve True Immortals, these later-added helmsman apostles did not know the fundamental reason why the Immortal Ship sailed to different possibilities.

They only believed it to be Li Fan's unique method of cultivation.

And the original twelve True Immortals remained firmly under Li Fan's control.

"The cultivation method of 'Unification of All Selves' is indeed highly efficient."

"If I were to meet Evil Su Bai again now, even without using intimidation, I could still contend with him directly."

Chapter 1603: Seeking Survival in Shanhai

"Crossing the Mountains and Seas? Devouring the Mountains and Seas, transforming the Mountains and Seas!"

"Devour! Devour! Devour..."

In Li Fan's eyes, the Mountains and Seas were no longer a vast illusion, but rather like a delectable feast exuding a fatal allure.

Those streams of black energy soaring into the sky were precisely the tempting aura rising from the Mountains and Seas!

It was the ancient taste of the Mountains and Seas themselves!

Like his first encounter with Ink Slaughter when he was still a mortal cultivator, an extreme craving, originating from the depths of his soul, suddenly emerged, threatening to completely dominate Li Fan's consciousness.

Regardless of realm or strength, ignoring innate talent or disposition. As long as one still possessed "desires," they would be ignited by the black fragments, magnified countless times, and guided into greed for the Mountains and Seas.

Cultivators in the Mountains and Seas inherently harbored a certain yearning for them. If further induced, their hidden desires would almost certainly be ignited. The higher their strength, the more likely they were to pose a substantial threat to the Mountains and Seas, and the more so!

Just as Li Fan thought now: "All that is slaughtered and killed can become my sustenance. Now that the True Spirit fire seeds have almost spread throughout the Mountains and Seas, all it takes is a single great fire, and the Mountains and Seas will be engulfed in flames!"

"Flames blazing, ashes filling the sky. Delicious, delectable..."

The more he thought, the more Li Fan felt his plan was likely to succeed, and the more impulsive he became.

"Should I, perhaps, truly give it a try?" A dangerous glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes.

One of these myriad dispersed thoughts, having been蛊惑 (gǔhuò - bewitched/tempted), was attempting to send a signal of rebellion to the main body.

"Calm down."

However, at this moment, another cold voice echoed in Li Fan's mind.

Like a distant echo across the shore, it was completely unaffected by the seductive sound.

This voice was precisely Li Fan's own!

This clear-headed Li Fan was formed from innumerable Dao-One Worms.

It was the main body, sensing something was amiss, that commanded the Dao-One Worms to the rescue.

Although it was only a dispersed thought, under the current circumstances, it was even clearer than Li Fan's dispersed consciousness.

This was the effect of the Dao-One Worm swarms constantly adapting to the frenzied蛊惑 (gǔhuò - bewitched/tempted) brought about by the black fragments!

With the reminder from the Dao-One Worms' consciousness, the Li Fan present at this location instantly regained his clarity.

Strictly speaking, he had not been completely蛊惑 (gǔhuò - bewitched/tempted) just now.

After all, the idea of attempting to ignite the Mountains and Seas had already been repeatedly simulated in his mind several times. However, each time, Li Fan had ultimately rejected it.

Even without the Dao-One Worms' consciousness, he likely would not have truly attempted to "devour the Mountains and Seas."

But it was undeniable that Li Fan had indeed been somewhat influenced by the black fragments.

To the point where he temporarily lost consideration for the future and the overall situation, only focusing on immediate gains and losses, as if his eyes were blinded.

With the calibration and assistance from the Dao-One Worm swarm's consciousness, Li Fan became completely calm. Facing the incessantly ringing seductive voices, he was no longer moved.

After the worm-formed consciousness completely devoured the source of the蛊惑 (gǔhuò - bewitched/tempted), the Mountains and Seas in Li Fan's vision finally returned to their normal appearance.

However, the faint "fragrance" emanating from the Mountains and Seas had not completely disappeared.

It still existed.

Li Fan looked at the black fragment in his hand, which had already been digested by the Dao-One Worms.

Its physical form no longer existed in the mortal world, but the outline of the fragment still depicted its original appearance.

Clutching it with his right hand, he found himself grasping at air. His five fingers passed straight through the fragment, as if its existence were merely Li Fan's illusion.

"In the eyes of the Dao-One Worms, they have completed their mission. The black fragment has already disappeared. However..."

Li Fan pondered, then summoned the True Immortal apostles from the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship docked in Dao Annihilation. He finally confirmed that, apart from Li Fan himself, others could not see this "invisible" fragment.

Moreover, this invisible fragment only attached itself to Li Fan.

No matter where Li Fan went, it would always follow.

"Does it pose a threat?"

Li Fan gently stroked the invisible fragment in his hand.

He was currently just one of his myriad dispersed thoughts. If he encountered an uncontrollable situation, this dispersed thought could instantly self-destruct, severing any possibility of it affecting the main body.
