This was Li Fan's contingency plan, made from the very beginning when he dispatched countless Profound Yellow Immortal Ships to various corners of the Mountains and Seas. Therefore, he was not worried about the safety of his main body.

The instructions from his main body also allowed him to boldly study it without reservation.

With no further concerns, he began to study the invisible fragment around him.

Only he could observe the fragment's existence, and the research could not involve others. Fortunately, it was just a dispersed thought that could be discarded at any time, so he had no worries.

"The first step is to find a way to establish substantial contact with this fragment."

Although the invisible fragment surrounded Li Fan, whether he tried to touch it or use his divine sense, he could not truly grasp the fragment itself. Even when Li Fan used the methods of the Dao Refinement Medicine King Scripture and placed it within a grand furnace, he could not perceive its existence.

"A being on par with the Mountains and Seas can only be seen and touched and comprehended by being on par with the Mountains and Seas."

Li Fan suddenly recalled his experience when he comprehended the Great Dao of Longevity in his previous life.

Cheng Dao, as Duke Shou Qiu's true disciple, had cultivated tirelessly for eons, yet his comprehension of "Longevity" was not as profound as Li Fan's acquired in an instant. This was precisely because Li Fan possessed Huan Zhen, and to some extent, was also on par with the Mountains and Seas.

"Although Huan Zhen is currently in slumber, I can still utilize some of its True and False transformations, barely achieving a state of being on par with the Mountains and Seas."

"However, the information of this fragment is unclear. If I were to act so rashly, I might repeat the past and re-experience the catastrophe of the Three Dao Convergence..."

After contemplating for a moment, Li Fan had an idea.

"Why not borrow Duke Shou Qiu's Great Dao of Longevity once more?"

During his discussions with Cheng Dao over the years, Li Fan had indirectly confirmed that Duke Shou Qiu was indeed within the Eternal Void. Even if he activated the remaining Longevity power within his body, and Duke Shou Qiu sensed it, he would not be able to return for some time.

"Moreover, according to Cheng Dao, the Mountains and Seas are boundless. Those who obtain Duke Shou Qiu's seed of Longevity might not be few. Perhaps Duke Shou Qiu even eagerly hopes that someone in this world can truly inherit his mantle, allowing him to travel to even more ancient Mountains and Seas without any worries."

After much deliberation, Li Fan had no further reservations.

After a brief communication with his main body, a surge of vitality inexplicably emerged from within him. His body, which had become incredibly solid after absorbing the Garbage Mountain possibility, became indistinguishable from his true body due to this surge of Longevity power.

Even Li Fan himself could hardly differentiate between his current state and his main body.

Adjusting his posture, Li Fan brought the invisible fragment encircling him to his front. He then spat out a mouthful of blood, its boundless vitality gushing out like a torrential river, engulfing the fragment.

As expected, the invisible fragment, which had remained unresponsive to any external existence, finally changed upon contact with the power of Longevity.

Countless lines appeared within the fragment, like myriad mirrors.

Each mirror reflected the continuous scenery of the Mountains and Seas.

What shocked Li Fan even more was that the Mountains and Seas in the mirrors were not unified!

In other words, the fusion of the Mountains and Seas had not yet reached its current extent.

The current Mountains and Seas were integrated, with each part inextricably linked.

But in the fragment's mirrors, the Mountains and Seas were merely leaning against each other!

The boundaries between the mountains and the seas were still very distinct.

Li Fan could even clearly see the countless possibilities hovering at the edge of the Infinite Sea, crashing against the mountains and seas above, turning into spray and dust!

"This is the state of the Mountains and Seas during their initial fusion, as depicted in the 'Sayings of the Mountains and Seas'!"

Li Fan's heart stirred, attempting to see more.

However, as the Longevity power he spat out gradually dissipated, the fragment returned to its normal appearance.

"How is this possible? The power of the Great Dao of Longevity disappears so quickly?"

Li Fan's heart instantly grew alert.

After all, to expel the Longevity power from his body, Li Fan had taken considerable effort. He had continuously sprayed blood and nurtured the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm for decades without stopping. Only then did he achieve some effect.

Theoretically speaking, the Longevity power contained in the mouthful of blood Li Fan had just spat out should normally last for a million years without dissipating.

But now...

"It is this fragment that is absorbing it."

Li Fan stared at the invisible fragment, which seemed no different from before, with a cold glint in his eyes.

Perhaps sensing that Li Fan was a fellow being,

The fragment's attachment and adherence to Li Fan became even closer.

Without deliberate attraction, the fragment would actively "follow" Li Fan.

Li Fan hesitated for a moment, then ultimately decided to continue.

With another infusion of Longevity power, the fragment once again revealed the initial scene of the Mountains and Seas merging.

This time, prepared, Li Fan saw even more clearly.

"There are beings in the Mountains and Seas!"

"Born from the sea, attempting to ascend the mountains..."

Although they were merely fleeting fragments, Li Fan could still glimpse events recorded in the "Sayings of the Mountains and Seas" left by Sun Piaomiao.

The sea waves crashed against the mountains, and countless civilizations and beings turned to dust.

But within the Infinite Sea, new civilizations were constantly born.

Continuously exploring and conquering the Mountains and Seas.

It was like a cycle, or perhaps a destiny that had long been predetermined.

Once again, after the Mountains and Seas had been shaken and all civilizations destroyed.

The Mountains and Seas fell into a rare period of calm.

But something extraordinary occurred.

The Infinite Sea churned as if boiling, and with the evaporation of countless possibilities, a terrifying roar seemed to emanate from the depths of the seabed.

It echoed upwards towards the mountains, reverberating through the peaks.

It was like a symphony of Mountains and Seas, grand, magnificent, and soul-stirring.

Li Fan stared blankly at this scene, only recovering his senses long after the scene in the fragment had disappeared.

"This is merely the record within the invisible fragment."

"What truly unfolded in the Mountains and Seas back then must have been far more astonishing."

Li Fan sighed deeply.

He now understood what he had just seen within the fragment.

The communication between the Infinite Sea and the Upper Mountains!

"If described in human language, it is the 'dialogue between the Mountains and the Seas' that I saw in the Sayings of the Mountains and Seas."

"However..."

"The communication between the Mountains and Seas was far from limited to this."

"This was the tendency for the Upper Mountains and the Infinite Sea to merge, and it also contained their mutual resistance to their fated merger. And..."

Even with Li Fan's current knowledge, he could not decipher its full meaning.

But merely by listening to the echoes from the Mountains and Seas, Li Fan felt that his understanding of the essence of the Mountains and Seas was constantly improving.

His efficiency in comprehending the Dao surpassed that of drifting in Dao Annihilation by thousands or tens of thousands of times.

After all, one was a macroscopic overview, while the other was being lost in the infinite microscopic interior. The insights gained were fundamentally incomparable.

"If I can comprehend the principles within, then transcending through my own power..."

"Will be a matter of course!"

Li Fan was immersed in the roaring of mountains and seas, unable to extricate himself.

Unfortunately, the scenes recorded within this invisible fragment seemed to be limited.

Subsequently, even as Li Fan continuously infused it with Longevity power, the fragment only displayed repetitive scenes.

This made Li Fan somewhat disappointed.

"It is unlikely that it is deliberately deceiving me; it has simply recorded this segment of the scene."

"From my external observation, the recorded scene can be fully played in just over ten breaths. However, if measured by the timescale of mortal possibilities..."

"It is likely billions of years long."

"This is a period of history longer than Duke Shou Qiu's lifespan."

Although Duke Shou Qiu attained the Great Dao of Longevity, the temporal node he inhabited was at the very end of the Mountains and Seas' fusion.

Compared to the long lifespan of the Mountains and Seas, it occupied an extremely insignificant portion.

"This fragment has persisted from the beginning of the Mountains and Seas' fusion until now."

"Precisely..."

Although no new scenes appeared, Li Fan still chose to continue to infuse it with Longevity power.

Because he had discovered that as the Longevity power was continuously infused, faint whispers began to emanate from the fragment.

Unlike the seductive voices before, this time, it was the fragment attempting to communicate.

Chapter 1604: The Other Shore is Far Away

The people of the [Dark] Dynasty had long since seen through life and death. For the future of the dynasty, they were willing to sacrifice themselves at any time. Whether it was the collection of all their selves in a single possibility, or the totality of their beings within the Mountains and Seas.

It was precisely because of this that the Mountain and Sea Scribes of the past had the confidence to embark on a seemingly ethereal plan at the cost of all the lives of the dynasty. Because they knew that even if only the last person of the [Dark] Dynasty remained, as long as they waited for the "Star's Gaze" to descend and successfully complete the sublimation, the [Dark] Dynasty could be rebuilt outside the Mountains and Seas!

They did not expect the calamity to arrive so quickly and so fiercely.

The plan had just begun when the tide of Dao Annihilation, like a tsunami, swallowed everything within the dynasty.

"The Mountains and Seas seem to have perceived our actions and are thus hindering us..."

Even though the Mountain and Sea Scribe was reduced to a mere fragment, he still harbored resentment for the destruction of his dynasty. He declared this to Li Fan with conviction.

Furthermore, he repeatedly recounted the timing and scale of the disaster, emphasizing how unnatural it was.

At first, Li Fan thought this was merely the Mountain and Sea Scribe's one-sided account, distorted by his unwillingness to accept the loss of his dynasty. However, as he listened further, he began to notice the peculiarities.

The calamity of Dao Annihilation was essentially the fusion of the Mountains and Seas.

This also meant that the scale of Dao Annihilation born during the early stages of the fusion of the Mountains and Seas should have been far less than it was now.

But that disaster which swallowed the [Dark] Dynasty...

"At that time, the [Dark] Dynasty was spread across the Mountains and Seas, and Dao Annihilation should only have occurred in the areas where the Mountains and Seas were initially merging."

Li Fan's expression became somewhat serious.

In the countless years spent surviving as a fragment after the calamity, the Mountain and Sea Scribe had pondered the reasons for this occurrence. Ultimately, he could only conclude that it was the consciousness of the Mountains and Seas that had perceived the plan of the [Dark] Dynasty's beings to transcend.

This was, in the eyes of the Mountains and Seas, undoubtedly a complete betrayal.

Therefore, punishment was imposed. This was one possible explanation.

This was also why Li Fan felt such an intense urge to devour the Mountains and Seas when they first encountered the fragment.

Seemingly, the beings of the [Dark] Dynasty were innocent. But upon closer consideration, the people of the [Dark] Dynasty were born from the Mountains and Seas themselves. Now, the Mountains and Seas were facing a calamity, yet instead of offering aid or making any contributions, they first thought of surrendering to an unknown entity outside the Mountains and Seas...

Even if the Mountains and Seas were no match for the [Star], could they not deal with you parasites?

"It is understandable indeed." Li Fan's perspective shifted, and he nodded inwardly.

"If this speculation is true, then it serves as a reminder. The Infinite Sea and the Upper Mountains are both great existences with their own will, not merely passive objects to be manipulated. When I undertake the act of burning mountains and boiling seas in the future, I may have to be wary of retaliation from the Mountains and Seas."

Although he thought this way, Li Fan did not show it. Instead, he posed a question to the Mountain and Sea Scribe. The [Dark] Dynasty was destroyed by Dao Annihilation, but Dao Annihilation was a force that even the Mountains and Seas could not control. The Mountains and Seas could have punished the [Dark] Dynasty in a thousand different ways. Why did they choose a method that would harm themselves?

The Mountain and Sea Scribe heard this, his incessant chatter came to an abrupt halt. Then, he remained silent for a long time.

Ultimately, he had only eliminated all possible culprits and left only the Mountains and Seas as the sole option. In reality, there was no sufficient or reasonable basis for this conclusion.

"My brother, in my humble opinion, perhaps the destruction of the [Dark] Dynasty back then was merely an accident." Li Fan sighed softly.

"Such a large-scale Dao Annihilation calamity could even shake the foundations of the Mountains and Seas. It must have involved existences on par with the Mountains and Seas, or even the [Star] outside the Mountains and Seas. The Mountains and Seas were momentarily in turmoil. Although they ultimately endured this calamity with their immense foundation, the [Dark] Dynasty, as a floating vessel within the Mountains and Seas, could not make it through..."

"Afterward, the Mountains and Seas declined, and the trend of fusion became increasingly rapid." Li Fan elaborated on his speculation.

The Mountain and Sea Scribe of the [Dark] Dynasty listened silently.

It was clear that compared to his original deduction, Li Fan's speculation was more plausible.

However, he found it difficult to accept for a moment that the demise of his dynasty and the annihilation of countless souls were merely accidents.

"Or rather, it was not an accident, but a certainty."

"When the Mountains and Seas could not even protect themselves, how could their inhabitants survive?"

"The deceased are deceased. My brother, you should let go of everything and look towards the future."

"You survived by chance and were coincidentally saved by me. Is this not a form of destiny? Perhaps you bear the mission of rebuilding and establishing the [Dark] Dynasty."

"Call upon the Star's Gaze, complete the unfinished business of the past, and transcend beyond the Mountains and Seas..."

The Mountain and Sea Scribe, who had been observing the Mountains and Seas for countless years, did not have much experience with scheming and complex interactions. Having established trust with Li Fan, he was gradually swayed by Li Fan's rhetoric.

"Even if you consider the Mountains and Seas your enemy... open your eyes and look at the surrounding Mountains and Seas. Dao Annihilation is encroaching everywhere, and the Mountains and Seas are in a precarious state. Have your grievances not been avenged?"

Sensing the change in the Mountain and Sea Scribe's emotions, Li Fan felt that he had been persuaded to some extent.

However, deeply ingrained beliefs accumulated over countless years were not so easily overturned.

Fortunately, Li Fan was persistent.

While periodically nourishing him with Longevity power to aid in his recovery, he continued his brainwashing, urging him to let go of unnecessary hatred and focus on the future.

As the saying goes, a continuous drip can wear through stone, and a steady stream can pierce metal.

One year, ten years, a hundred years, a thousand years, ten thousand years...

As Li Fan's plan to spread the True Spirit fire seeds was nearing completion, the countless resentful souls of the Mountains and Seas condensed within the fragment in the span of countless years suddenly dispersed.

Brilliant white light erupted from the fragment. As the light dissipated, a figure appeared.

It was none other than the Mountain and Sea Scribe!

However, it was not in a "human" form, but rather entirely sea-blue, with slender limbs. Though the facial features resembled those of a human, there were distinct differences. Most notably, its head was transparent.

Blue light flowed like seawater within it, seemingly allowing one to see the various brilliant and fantastical lights flashing simultaneously inside.

"My friend, allow me to formally introduce myself. My name is Xiao Wangsheng."

Li Fan could clearly see the warm hues flashing within Xiao Wangsheng's head.

He smiled slightly and cupped his fists: "Congratulations, my brother, on your rebirth and transformation today."

Half the color of pale blue sadness flashed within Xiao Wangsheng's head.

"I must also thank my friend for your tireless assistance."

The two had already formed a deep friendship through their long interactions. Li Fan, without ceremony, inquired about Xiao Wangsheng's future plans.

"The dynasty is fallen. Without the support of countless subjects, the plan to invoke the Star's Gaze must be revised," Xiao Wangsheng pondered for a moment and said slowly.

He pointed into the distance: "I can vaguely see a gathering of numerous powerful beings in that direction. Among them, there are even those comparable to my former full strength. If I can persuade them to join the plan..."

Li Fan narrowed his eyes and looked in the direction Xiao Wangsheng indicated.

It was precisely the direction of the Shore of Great Dao!

He couldn't help but let out a wry smile and recount the current state of the Mountains and Seas to Xiao Wangsheng.

"Oh? That is the Shore?" Xiao Wangsheng nodded. "It's much weaker than I imagined."

Xiao Wangsheng said this naturally with his own confidence.

There were nearly a thousand Mountain and Sea Scribes in the past, and Xiao Wangsheng was merely one of the younger ones.

The longer one could survive in the Mountain and Sea form, the stronger they were.

The strength of the Mountain and Sea Scribes of the past was evident.

"The previous Temple of Blessings was powerless in the face of the Mountains and Seas calamity. These people's so-called plan to save the world is ultimately futile," Xiao Wangsheng shook his head, commenting.

"Perhaps it is because the true powerhouses within the Shore have already crossed the Eternal Void and traveled to a more ancient past," Li Fan explained to Xiao Wangsheng.

After hearing about Duke Shou Qiu, the Three Sages Tai Shan, Gui Hai, and Taiyi, and the deeds of many other powerful beings, Xiao Wangsheng retracted his initial condescension.

"Just like you, brother Xiao. The mindset of the beings on the Shore is not something that can be easily changed. If we approach them directly and try to persuade them to carry out the Star's Gaze plan, we will undoubtedly be rejected outright."

"We must proceed slowly..."

Xiao Wangsheng, having no knowledge of the current era's beings, felt Li Fan's words carried some sense. He then asked: "My friend, what is your plan?"

In his view, Li Fan was already a "comrade-in-arms" on the same side as him.

After all, Li Fan had personally witnessed the Star's Gaze and almost became lost in it. Based on Xiao Wangsheng's experience, any sentient being that had personally experienced the power of the [Star] would resolutely implement the Star's Gaze plan.

Because apart from relying on the [Star], no other method could guarantee survival in this great calamity of the destruction of the Mountains and Seas.

Hearing Li Fan's words, Xiao Wangsheng's head immediately filled with images of sandstorms, like flying colors.

"Your plan is ingenious!"

"But I wonder, how can we join this so-called Shore?"

Xiao Wangsheng, subconsciously, still considered himself a being of ancient civilization, with insurmountable invisible barriers between him and the current beings of the Mountains and Seas. Regarding integrating into the collective of the Shore, he instinctively felt it was almost impossible.

However, Li Fan said nonchalantly: "The Shore never restricts its entry requirements. As long as one can reach it, they are considered a member of the Shore. Of course, this is merely superficial integration. To truly become part of their core and possess the ability to change their perceptions, one must make certain contributions."

Although Li Fan had not truly set foot on the Shore, he had already seen many immortals from the Shore. He could generally guess the situation within the Shore's organization.

"Just reaching it? It's that simple?" Xiao Wangsheng was somewhat surprised to hear this.

"Crossing the Mountains and Seas is a simple matter for you, Brother Xiao. However, for the vast majority of beings today, it is something they can never achieve even in a lifetime. Even I need to build a Profound Yellow Immortal Ship to travel there," Li Fan sighed with emotion, his feelings not feigned.

"Brother Xiao, please assist me in returning to my main body. It is time for us to sail towards the Shore." Li Fan bowed to Xiao Wangsheng.

Xiao Wangsheng nodded.

With Li Fan providing directional guidance, Xiao Wangsheng's gaze easily pierced through the endless barriers of the Mountains and Seas, spotting Li Fan's main body standing at the prow of the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship, smiling at him.

After giving a nod of acknowledgment, he waved his sleeve, enveloping the phantom Immortal Ship beneath him and stepping forward.

For cultivators of the current era, crossing the Mountains and Seas required comprehending the Transcendent True Intent.

But for an ancient being like Xiao Wangsheng, navigating and traversing the Mountains and Seas was an instinct.

Even with the burden of a phantom Immortal Ship, it was not a difficult task for him.

Riding the wind and waves through the Mountains and Seas, they traveled at great speed.

The true Profound Yellow Immortal Ship sensed the rising waves and waves, experiencing a slight tremor. However, after countless years of tempering and strengthening, the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship had long been able to ignore turbulence of this magnitude.

A figure shot out from the surging waves of Dao Annihilation.

The phantom Immortal Ship merged with the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship.

Xiao Wangsheng also stood before Li Fan's main body. The two had already established a tacit understanding and wasted no further words.

Manipulating the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship, they sailed towards the Shore.

If traveling at the normal speed of the Immortal Ship, it would likely take hundreds of thousands of years to truly arrive.

But now, with Xiao Wangsheng leading the way at the prow, pulling the entire Profound Yellow Immortal Ship, they advanced rapidly.

The speed of the Immortal Ship increased by more than ten thousand times!

Li Fan noticed that this was not solely due to Xiao Wangsheng's powerful strength. Instead, it was as if he possessed a natural skill for crossing the Mountains and Seas, an innate talent and instinct.

Li Fan humbly sought Xiao Wangsheng's guidance.

Xiao Wangsheng naturally did not hesitate to impart his knowledge.

"For the people of the dynasty, although this is an innate ability, it still requires strengthening through learning and practice."

"However, this was all before they reached adulthood." As if recalling a fond memory from his past, Xiao Wangsheng couldn't help but smile slightly. However, he soon realized that the dynasty of his memories no longer existed. His smile quickly vanished.

Instead, he earnestly began to teach Li Fan.

"The so-called Transcendent True Intent allows one to cross the Mountains and Seas, but ultimately, it is like using an external object, a difficult and arduous journey."

"In reality, we are beings of the Mountains and Seas, born from the Mountains and Seas. Using the power of the Mountains and Seas to cross the Mountains and Seas itself, how can there be any obstacles?"

Xiao Wangsheng attempted to help Li Fan comprehend the principle of harmonizing with the Mountains and Seas.

However, for something that seemed so simple to him, Li Fan found it impossible to learn.

Xiao Wangsheng could only console him: "Perhaps it is due to the changes in time, and beings have also changed."

Li Fan, however, remembered something and asked: "In the current era, within a single possibility, there is the concept of 'potential.' There is a certain upper limit to the number of powerful beings that a possibility can produce."

"I wonder, in the ancient Mountains and Seas, was there also such a thing as 'potential'?"

Chapter 1605: The Weakest Transcendence

"Potential?" Xiao Wangsheng seemed to have some difficulty understanding Li Fan's question.

"Within the dynasty, there did occasionally appear one or two individuals who could not fully perceive the Mountains and Seas. However, firstly, we Mountain and Sea Scribes would assist them in recovering. Secondly, with billions of people in the dynasty, even if only they remained, it would not have a significant impact."

"We have never heard of a large-scale disability occurring within a single possibility..."

It was no wonder Xiao Wangsheng spoke of "disability" repeatedly.

In his opinion, anyone who could not achieve synchronous resonance with all their selves in various possibilities was essentially "disabled."

Li Fan did not refute him, but instead pondered in his heart: "If we consider spiritual energy as a quantifiable resource, then the spiritual energy of the people of the [Dark] Dynasty, in terms of universality, was far superior to the current beings of the Mountains and Seas."

"Yet, despite both being born from the Mountains and Seas, there is such a gap..."

"It seems that the Mountains and Seas themselves have also suffered significant damage during the Dao Annihilation calamity."

Li Fan did not continue this topic with Xiao Wangsheng, but instead discussed with him the precautions needed after entering the Shore.

"Apart from our ultimate goal of instigating the immortals of the Shore to support the Star's Gaze plan, it is best not to conceal anything else, even your origin, Brother Xiao..."

"Even though it is the final era, eroded by Dao Annihilation, the possibilities within the Mountains and Seas are still endless. Strange situations can arise at any time. Survivors of ancient civilizations like yourself are not particularly rare. Moreover, among the people of the [Dark] Dynasty, apart from you, no one else survived. As long as you do not reveal any flaws, we do not need to worry about our secrets being exposed."

"Those who can reach the Shore are all beings with extraordinary talent and immense perseverance. Their perspectives are not something that can be easily changed in a short period. It may take a considerable amount of time to achieve results. Brother Xiao, please do not be impatient..." Li Fan urged endlessly.

"My friend, rest assured. I possess that much composure," Xiao Wangsheng said solemnly.

Li Fan was not truly considering the other party's welfare. He was merely finding an excuse to stall for time. It was precisely for the purpose of heading to the Shore that he had gone to great lengths to "resurrect" Xiao Wangsheng.

He had sparred with Xiao Wangsheng before. As expected of a powerhouse who had already undergone metamorphosis and become on par with the Mountains and Seas in ancient times, even though Xiao Wangsheng was currently just a remnant fragment, his strength was not to be underestimated.

Even the True Spirit fire that ignited possibilities could not harm him in the slightest.

In Xiao Wangsheng's own words, only calamities that caused large-scale collapse and annihilation of the Mountains and Seas could truly threaten him. Or perhaps the power of the [Star], which transcended the Mountains and Seas.

Besides these, he was almost invincible while standing within the Mountains and Seas.

"Most of the Mountain and Sea Scribes of the past were not skilled in combat techniques. This was because, within the Mountains and Seas, there were no opponents they could not defeat. With a single thought, they could eliminate any target. Therefore, there was no need to study any techniques," Xiao Wangsheng explained.

"This is the 'One power suppresses all techniques'!" After trying various methods, Li Fan found that he could not pose any threat to Xiao Wangsheng, and he sighed with emotion.

Although Xiao Wangsheng had nothing to teach Li Fan in terms of techniques or divine abilities, his constant clashes with beings on par with the Mountains and Seas could greatly enhance Li Fan's ability to adapt when facing the Mountains and Seas.

Gradually, the howling sounds emanating from the continuous Mountains and Seas became less jarring to the mind. Li Fan could also gradually achieve a state of calm observation, like Duke Shou Qiu, gazing at the sea from the mountains.

In fact, during the years of implementing the True Spirit seed-scattering plan, with the Profound Yellow Immortal Ships traversing every corner of the Mountains and Seas, Li Fan's own strength had also increased at an inconceivable rate day by day.

His own consciousness now covered one percent of the current Mountains and Seas. Although it had not yet reached the level of "Unity of Many Selves," it was not far from the concept of true "Transcendence" held by the powerhouses on the Shore.

This was because Li Fan differed from other cultivators who pursued the path of "Unity of Many Selves." For beings like the Black Heavenly Physician and Xie Subai, their selves in other possibilities varied in strength.

A strong one might reach the realm of Nameless True Immortal. A weak one, however, might not even have the strength of True Immortal. After all, against the backdrop of rampant Dao Annihilation, the destruction of the Immortal Realm and the severance of the path to ascension were highly probable events. Devouring other selves who had not become True Immortals would bring about a very limited increase in strength.

But for Li Fan, the phantom selves he had quietly scattered had at least possessed a certain level of strength, not weaker than True Immortals, ensuring a baseline. Especially with the support of the peculiar structure of the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net, he could even instantly lend a portion of his main body's power to his phantom selves located far away in the Mountains and Seas.

Furthermore, these phantom selves residing in different possibilities could continue to cultivate by plundering resources within their respective possibilities. The improvement in each point brought about an overall improvement. It could be said that if Li Fan had not intentionally concealed his strength, his rate of improvement would have multiplied several times over.

This was the efficient cultivation achieved through unified will and coordination, like the people of the [Dark] Dynasty.

The strength gained with every breath was incomparable to what could be achieved in tens of millions of years within a single possibility.

"This is why the realm of Transcendence represents a truly qualitative leap compared to ordinary Nameless True Immortals. It allows one to transform the infinity of the Mountains and Seas into a part of one's own foundation..."

Li Fan recalled his encounters with Xie Subai and the Black Heavenly Physician in his previous life, feeling the immense disparity, like that between an ant and the bright moon.

"No wonder Transcendents are so indifferent to matters within a single possibility."

"Everything you see is merely a negligible part of my vision."

However, Li Fan also realized that this method of rapid advancement by utilizing the infinite possibilities of the Mountains and Seas had a clear limit. Once this limit was reached, the increase in advancement from expanding to new possibilities would rapidly diminish.

And Li Fan had now officially touched this limit.

This was also why, after scattering True Spirit fire seeds to approximately one percent of the Mountains and Seas, which was sufficient to ignite the True Spirit fire at any time, Li Fan abandoned further expansion and instead focused on the true reason for the evolution of the Shore.

"To advance further and reach the realm of Saints like Duke Shou Qiu, who can traverse the Eternal Void, I wonder what method would be required."

Regarding this, Li Fan still had absolutely no knowledge. He would likely have to wait until he reached the Shore to find the answer.

Although his strength had achieved a leap, Li Fan did not become complacent. He was keenly aware that the method he employed was purely a shortcut.

Compared to the "Unity of Many Selves" practiced by the immortals of the Shore, his foundation was extremely unstable.

At the very least, compared to beings like the Black Heavenly Physician and Xie Subai, even if the Mountains and Seas were to collapse and most possibilities annihilated, their strength would not be diminished in the slightest.

But for Li Fan, the disappearance of each possibility where he had a phantom self would result in a reduction of his strength. Even without the direct intervention of Dao Annihilation, if a transcendent expert were to take action and eliminate each possibility individually.

Li Fan would almost be instantly reduced to his original state.

Without even needing to confront Li Fan directly, he could be severely wounded.

He did not have any method of resistance other than igniting the Mountains and Seas in a move of mutual destruction.

"The Transcendent who grows strongest the fastest is also the most easily killed Transcendent," Li Fan scoffed inwardly.

Furthermore, what made Li Fan most aware of his own limitations was that all of this could not be preserved or recorded by Huan Zhen.

"Huan Zhen only exists within the main body. Even with the Dao Origin Function, it is limited to the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship."

"Once Huan Zhen is gone, this grand picture I have spent countless years building will disappear in an instant."

"I will have to start accumulating again."

"My true strength is merely that of a Transcendent who has adapted to the turbulence of the Mountains and Seas."

This was the predicament Li Fan currently faced. Even if Huan Zhen awakened, it could not solve this predicament.

"The accumulation of so many years is only enough for one expenditure. Therefore, I must maximize the advantage brought by my current powerful strength."

"I even need to borrow strength from others, to leverage as much as possible," Li Fan glanced nonchalantly at Xiao Wangsheng beside him.

Then he looked in the direction Xiao Wangsheng was pointing.

"I hope to find other unclaimed Transcendent True Intents on the Shore."

"Only when Huan Zhen awakens will it be my true reliance."

Whether it was Li Fan's bad luck or the extreme rarity of Transcendent True Intents, it was hard to say.

The Profound Yellow Immortal Ship had traversed one percent of the Mountains and Seas. However, apart from the initial Sea and Mountains lone sail, Li Fan had not found any other Transcendent True Intents.

Therefore, despite the passage of a long time, the awakening of Huan Zhen remained a distant prospect.

It was clear that Huan Zhen's injuries were not something that could be healed by time alone. External power was needed for nourishment.

"A greater possibility is that the powerhouses on the Shore regularly patrol the Mountains and Seas, proactively searching for unclaimed Transcendent True Intents. This is why I have found nothing." Combining this with his memory of Zi Yi carefully putting away the lone sail in his previous life, Li Fan couldn't help but think this way.

...

"My friend, look up ahead quickly!" Amidst the long silence, Xiao Wangsheng suddenly exclaimed.

There was no need for him to be reminded; Li Fan already knew from the immense tremors the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship was experiencing.

They were not far from the Shore.

Just as the waves become more pronounced as one approaches the coast, the impact of Dao Annihilation in this region of the Mountains and Seas was far greater than in other areas due to the presence of the [Shore].

The Profound Yellow Immortal Ship had not experienced such turbulence for a long time. Fortunately, it had been tempered and strengthened by Li Fan for so long that it could withstand the storm without disintegrating.

Li Fan stood at the prow, gazing into the distance.

A colossal wall of light stretched across his field of vision.

Li Fan was certain that this wall of light did not exist in the Mountains and Seas he had seen before.

Instead, it suddenly appeared after the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship had passed through the turbulent waves of Dao Annihilation.

Li Fan reached out his hand, feeling the warm radiance emanating from the wall of light, and felt a sense of familiarity.

Although he had not observed the light wall of the Shore during his wandering through the Mountains and Seas, its radiance had indeed shone in almost every corner of the Mountains and Seas.

It was formless and intangible.

Before Li Fan had truly seen the Shore, he could not realize its pervasive presence.

Only now, upon truly seeing the Shore and recalling his past experiences, could he belatedly realize it.

"Knowledge leads to awareness. Without knowledge, one cannot see."

"This method... it feels somewhat familiar..."

Li Fan instantly thought of the various relics left behind by Sun Piaomiao.

The method Sun Piaomiao used to conceal his secrets shared striking similarities in nature with the radiance of the Shore.

As Li Fan's thoughts churned, the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship continued to advance.

When they were close enough to the wall of light, the surrounding winds and waves instantly subsided.

As if traversing through the void, just as the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship was about to collide with the light wall of the Shore,

A crisp female voice suddenly sounded.

"Wait."

Within the wall of light, layers of shadows overlapped.

A giant eye silently appeared, fixedly staring at the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship and the countless beings within it.

The forward momentum of the Immortal Ship was halted, and it stopped moving.

Li Fan, however, remained unfazed. He said in a clear voice: "Junior has endured countless hardships and searched the Mountains and Seas, finally arriving at the land of the Shore. Have I caused any offense? Why does Senior obstruct me?"

"To be able to reach this point signifies that you have already qualified to join the Shore. However... everyone else came alone, as individuals. You, bringing so many with you, are the first in the Mountains and Seas."

"The way of the boat... I need to inquire." The giant eye showed no emotion as it simply replied and disappeared from the wall of light.

Li Fan waited patiently, but in his heart, ripples began to stir.

At first, he hadn't noticed.

But as the eye spoke more, Li Fan suddenly realized that its voice was somewhat familiar.

It bore a ninety percent resemblance to "Hungry Immortal"!

"Could it be that upon arriving at the Shore, I have encountered an acquaintance?"

"Fortunately, the Hungry Immortal, sealed as a Heavenly Pillar within the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship, was given to Xie Subai long ago. Otherwise, there would likely be some trouble."

Xiao Wangsheng was unaware of Li Fan's inner thoughts. He merely stared at the wall of light. After a long while, he suddenly transmitted a message: "My friend, this wall of light has some interesting properties."

"Oh? Brother Xiao, please elaborate."

"Looking at this wall of light, I see the same sight as the Mountain and Sea Scribes of the past."

"Or rather, I see the Mountains and Seas themselves."

Li Fan narrowed his eyes upon hearing this.

However, with his current perception, he could not yet glimpse the appearance of the Mountains and Seas from it.

Xiao Wangsheng continued: "If my prediction is correct, this wall of light is formed by the combined power of many beings on par with the Mountains and Seas. Some of them are in a slumber, while the majority are still active. However... they do not seem to be within these Mountains and Seas."

"But regardless. The foundation of the Shore is far stronger than I imagined."

Li Fan and Xiao Wangsheng waited at the prow of the Immortal Ship for a long time.

It was not until thirty days and nights had passed within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm that the eye of the Hungry Immortal reappeared.

"Although your situation is extremely complex, after deliberation among the Sages, you have been granted permission to enter the Shore."

Chapter 1606: Li Fan Meets All Sages

"If I can meet the Saints, then I will be free to move around."

"However, it is limited to yourself. Your boat of crossing, however, can only be docked within the [Formless Star Pivot]." The Star Scavenger declared indifferently, leaving no room for negotiation.

"As for you..." After speaking to Li Fan, the Star Scavenger's enormous eye turned to look at Xiao Wangsheng.

"You remnant of the Mountains and Seas, there is a dedicated living area within the Shore. You can travel freely to most places within the Shore. There are not so many restrictions."

This time, it was Xiao Wangsheng's turn to be taken aback. He hadn't expected that this giant eye would discern his origins with just a single glance.

"It seems my friend was right. If we want to safely blend into the Shore, it's best not to withhold anything."

Li Fan's reaction was even quicker. Seizing the opportunity, he directly asked, "Judging from your words, Senior, it seems there are many other remnants of the Mountains and Seas within the Shore like my friend?"

It didn't seem to be a secret. The Star Scavenger smiled and said, "It's not exactly 'many.' However, compared to transcendent experts like us, these remnants of the Mountains and Seas have fundamental differences. They have more in common with each other, so we simply arranged for them to live together."

Li Fan nodded, indicating his understanding, "Thank you for the reminder, Senior. We all understand and are willing to accept all regulations within the Shore."

"That's good. It saves me from having to say more." For some reason, a hint of regret could be vaguely detected in the Star Scavenger's words.

A beam of light shot out from the giant light wall, locking onto the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship.

In a daze, Li Fan felt the scene before him suddenly change. Above the sky, countless streams of purple energy erupted from fissures in the void, transforming into glazed bridges connecting various places. These bridges seemed to lead to different regions, and one could vaguely glimpse the rapidly changing scenery beyond the purple bridges.

A figure stood silently beside him. Its appearance bore a nine-tenths resemblance to the Star Scavenger.

The moment he saw this face, Li Fan's expression showed a touch of feigned astonishment. However, he quickly suppressed it. As a cover, he bowed proactively, "Greetings, Senior!"

The Star Scavenger, however, was extremely perceptive and captured this detail. He asked playfully, "You've seen me before?"

Li Fan gave a wry smile and truthfully recounted, "Senior truly possesses eyes that see through all. In my original possibility, I did indeed have a karmic connection with Senior. I even sealed you as a Heavenly Pillar to contend with Dao Annihilation..."

A flicker of fear crossed his face as Li Fan explained the entire affair, including how he had handed over that Star Scavenger to Xie Subai.

Hearing about the tragic fate of his other self, the Star Scavenger of the Shore did not show much anger. Instead, he calmly said, "Once you enter the Shore, all past karma ceases to exist. Do not worry. No matter what enmity existed between us in the past, it will all be nullified once you join the Shore. You can rest assured on this point. I will absolutely not trouble you because of it."

"As for that 'me' you speak of..."

The Star Scavenger of the Shore furrowed his brow and looked in a certain direction, "Subai... Hmph!"

It was clear that the Star Scavenger of the Shore had not taken the Star Scavenger Heavenly Pillar, which Li Fan had handed over, back to the Shore. Instead, he had hidden it for himself.

"Let's go. I'll take you to see the Saints." Without dwelling on this issue, the Star Scavenger of the Shore quickly regained his composure and said calmly.

As she spoke, one of the countless purple energy bridges in the sky suddenly came alive, swooping down and stopping before them.

"The Shore is divided into many different regions and is immeasurably vast. Even for transcendent experts like us, traversing it on our own takes considerable time. Therefore, we need the assistance of these [Reception Rainbow Bridges]."

Standing on the purple bridge, Li Fan felt the surrounding scenery distort and twist. An indistinct trembling resonance, like the communication of mountains and seas, could be faintly heard, as if he were rapidly traversing through them. However, within the reception bridge, no matter how pronounced the external changes were, he felt no discomfort.

Only Li Fan noticed that Xiao Wangsheng's expression had become extremely abnormal since stepping onto the reception bridge.

"This purple bridge..."

"It seems to be crafted from those who are in harmony with the Mountains and Seas," Xiao Wangsheng transmitted with some difficulty.

The Star Scavenger seemed to hear his transmission, "Strictly speaking, they are fitting candidates of the Mountains and Seas. Like a bird flying in the nine heavens, or a fish leaping in the sea. Because of their innate abilities, these creatures are more efficient at traversing and roaming within the Mountains and Seas than most beings in the Shore. Therefore, the Saints borrowed their bodies to construct these reception rainbow bridges to facilitate the passage of all Immortals within the Shore."

Although there was this explanation, Xiao Wangsheng's complexion had not improved much. After all, in his view, these fitting candidates of the Mountains and Seas were almost no different from his own Mountain and Sea sacrifices. They were beings of extreme reverence in his former dynasty. Now, they had been reduced to mere mounts...

"This Shore is more perilous than I imagined!"

"No wonder my friend was so incessantly warning me." Xiao Wangsheng fell into a long silence.

He merely listened passively as the Star Scavenger occasionally shared information about the Shore.

"Actually, theoretically speaking, there's no need for me to explain everything word-for-word. For anyone who can reach the Shore on their own, all the information exchange can be completed with a single thought. However, you haven't yet met the Saints. Most of the information within the Shore cannot be told to you."

"Once you receive the recognition of the Saints, you will naturally understand all about the Shore." The Star Scavenger explained to Li Fan, who was idly waiting.

Li Fan asked curiously, "Senior, I've continually heard you mention the [Saints]. What exactly are these 'Saints'..."

"The Saints, naturally, are the Sages. Those who have crossed the Eternal Void and journeyed to the previous epoch of Mountains and Seas are what we call Saints. Before they departed, they left behind a trace of their will within the Shore. This will is devoid of any personal emotion and only serves the continuation of the Shore and the Mountains and Seas."

"Within the Shore, there have been a total of nine Saints to date. The collection of their individual wills is what I refer to as the [Saints]," the Star Scavenger of the Shore introduced Li Fan with a solemn expression.

"And the recognition of the Saints?" Li Fan's expression became somewhat subtle.

"What each person encounters is not the same. But as long as one survives after meeting the Saints, they have passed the test."

As if sensing the fleeting expression on Li Fan's face, the Star Scavenger added, "However, rest assured, the Saints are extremely tolerant. In all the countless years since I have served as a [Guardian of the Dao], only two cases have failed the test and been punished by the Saints."

"And even those extremely wicked individuals did not perish. Instead, they toiled day and night within the [Eternal Heavenly Steps] of the Shore, atoning for their sins."

The Star Scavenger of the Shore did not specify what the Eternal Heavenly Steps were, but from his tone, it was clear that the experience of being imprisoned there would not be pleasant.

Upon hearing the Star Scavenger's words, Li Fan, though regaining his composure, had already become inwardly tense.

Even though he had anticipated facing a trial after arriving at the Shore, the thought of facing a combined test from nine powerful beings like the Three Sages still filled him with a slight sense of gravity.

"I hope the 'True and False Transformation' technique can protect me."

"If all else fails, I will have to use the Mountains and Seas as a threat to secure my departure."

The True Spirit fire seeds he had planted throughout the Mountains and Seas could still be clearly sensed even after entering the Shore. This gave Li Fan a sense of relief.

Compared to Li Fan's turbulent thoughts, Xiao Wangsheng had completely calmed down by this point.

In his view, the transcendence method of having the dynasty activate the "Star's Gaze" was the only way to save everything. Since they were called Saints, they should naturally be very reasonable.

"A method that can truly save everything, there's no reason they would refuse."

"Perhaps we don't need to subtly change their perspectives. By directly meeting the Saints and explaining the pros and cons, we might be able to make them accept it." After all, as a being who had survived from the ancient era of the Mountains and Seas, Xiao Wangsheng had his own ideas. Although Li Fan was his savior and friend, he would not act like a puppet and follow the other party's instructions entirely.

In Xiao Wangsheng's view, after the destruction of his dynasty, he was the sole survivor of the Mountain and Sea sacrifices. The mission of completing the plan to transcend the Mountains and Seas and continue the dynasty outweighed all else.

Xiao Wangsheng's resolve gradually strengthened.

Li Fan, however, did not notice this subtle change.

After an unknown period of time spent on the reception rainbow bridge, the scene before him changed once again.

"I won't be going in."

"Let's continue on. The Saints are just ahead!"

The Star Scavenger's voice echoed in his ears, while Li Fan's attention had already been captured by the wondrous sight before him.

It was as if he had returned to the Mountains and Seas. The surroundings presented a scene of continuous mountains and seas.

However, unlike in the past, when he, as a single weak individual, was lost within the Mountains and Seas.

Even the sight was vastly different from what Duke Shou Qiu had seen when he sat on the mountain and gazed at the sea.

Li Fan now appeared as if he had ascended outside the Mountains and Seas, hovering high in the sky.

From top to bottom, he observed the changes of the Mountains and Seas.

Every ripple was the condensation of countless possibilities.

Above the serene and majestic mountains, one could faintly glimpse continuous celestial realms, like a sea of stars.

And the black currents, winding and coiling like dragons throughout the Mountains and Seas, were the Dao Annihilation tribulation devouring the Mountains and Seas!

The Mountains and Seas merged, and Dao Annihilation raged.

This scene appeared before Li Fan in an unprecedentedly visualized manner.

Li Fan could not only clearly feel the destruction and threat of Dao Annihilation.

He could even comprehend the Dao of the Mountains and Seas.

"This perspective... it somewhat resembles the legendary [Star]."

"It is not a realm that I can reach. But rather..."

"The Saints!"

Xiao Wangsheng, who was beside him, had disappeared. Li Fan was the only one left in the entire space.

Taking a deep breath and gradually calming down, Li Fan walked forward with a composed expression.

Above the Mountains and Seas, there seemed to be no concept of time.

Li Fan took step after step, but his perception of sight, feeling, and awareness remained unchanged. He almost felt as if he were standing still.

However, after countless years of diligently scattering True Spirit fire seeds, Li Fan had already cultivated extraordinary patience and perseverance.

"Since the Saints are just ahead, as long as I continue to walk, I will definitely see them."

It wasn't that Li Fan had changed his ways and trusted the Star Scavenger of the Shore, whom he had met for the first time, so implicitly.

It was derived from logical deduction.

The Shore, as the hope for countless beings in the current Mountains and Seas, gathered numerous transcendent experts with the aim of saving the Mountains and Seas. They would certainly not play tricks on a newcomer like him.

"Otherwise, the Shore could not have been established, nor would it have survived to this day."

Li Fan walked calmly forward, indifferent to the passage of time.

After an unknown period, until all other thoughts in his mind had quieted down.

Only the single, pure thought of moving forward remained.

The surrounding scenery suddenly shifted again.

A circle enveloped him, enclosing him within.

Nine figures stood above the halo, all looking at Li Fan in the center.

In an instant, Li Fan felt as if he were bearing the weight of the Mountains and Seas!

His body and divine senses were instantly crushed into countless fragments.

This change came too quickly, so quickly that Li Fan had not yet emerged from the obsession of "moving forward." He had no time to react at all!

He saw himself shatter into countless star-like fragments.

However, within this circle, there seemed to be a mysterious power that, even in this shattered state, maintained Li Fan's "completeness."

Li Fan, gradually recovering his senses, felt a premonition.

Even while in the "True and False Transformation" state, he felt this way.

This was because Li Fan sensed that the moment he was shattered, the nine figures outside the halo had all rippled.

With the power of the Saints, what could cause them to collectively exhibit emotional fluctuations...

"True Spirit fire, burning mountains and boiling seas. Hahaha, interesting!"

A bold laugh rang out, causing Li Fan's heart to sink to the bottom.

This sentence had completely exposed the essence of his Infinite Spirit!

Li Fan no longer pretended. His expression instantly turned grim.

The methods of the Saints were far beyond his imagination.

All the anticipated smooth talk, schemes, and strategies...

Were all useless!

The moment they met, the Saints had already shattered Li Fan's existence into countless particles.

And then they examined him.

All his past experiences, all his secrets, all his thoughts.

At this moment, none of them could be hidden!

"Is it called being a Saint to pry into one's privacy?!" Li Fan, feeling as if he had been stripped bare and was being scrutinized, said angrily.

Facing Li Fan's angry accusation, the Saints showed no emotional fluctuation whatsoever.

"Saint... is a respectful title given by outsiders. In reality, we are merely a group of pathetic souls attempting to save the world."

"The Shore is built upon the efforts of countless people and concerns the critical survival of the entire Mountains and Seas. Naturally, we cannot allow any hidden dangers to enter. Privacy... is insignificant in the face of absolute survival."

"However, when spoken from your mouth, these two words are rather comical."

...

Voices came from all directions.

Li Fan, who was initially filled with rage, gradually calmed down.

"You saw my Infinite Spirit?"

"What else did you see?"

The Saints replied, "When the true becomes false and the false becomes true. You've given 'True and False' a good name."

Li Fan could no longer hold back, and his mind seemed to explode.

Chapter 1607: Breaking Through the Mist

[True and False], as Li Fan's greatest reliance, had always been regarded by him as his deepest secret.

Especially after learning that there were legends in the Immortal Realm, dating back to ancient times, that pointed to a treasure for saving the world that was related to [True and False], Li Fan feared that [True and False] would be stolen. Thus, he tried in every way to conceal the existence of this extraordinary treasure within his body.

However, he never expected that the moment he met the Saints, [True and False] would be exposed!

As if his prey on a plate had been spotted, Li Fan's eyes turned red, and he stared vigilantly at the nine Saintly figures standing outside the light.

Although his heart was greatly shaken, Li Fan did not lose his reason. He keenly caught the hidden meaning in the Saints' words.

"Him?"

"Did you already know about the existence of [True and False]? What exactly is it?" Li Fan instinctively pressed for answers.

The Saints remained silent and simultaneously pointed a finger at Li Fan's body, which had transformed into countless fragments.

"Ahhhhhhh..."

From the billions of fragments of his body, countless brilliant lights erupted simultaneously, as if something was being extracted from them.

The very foundation of his existence became shattered, and Li Fan's consciousness was engulfed by pain that words could not describe. He couldn't even utter curses, only instinctive cries of agony.

These cries echoed within the halo.

As the extraction process continued, a silhouette seemed to flash across Li Fan's billions of fragments. With each flash, the silhouette appeared to become clearer. Correspondingly, Li Fan's fragmented body began to blur, as if melting like ice and snow.

"Burning... mountains... boiling... seas..."

As if enduring eternal torture in the lowest depths of hell, Li Fan's thoughts were intermittent. He couldn't even execute his only countermeasure—igniting the True Spirit fire seeds spread throughout the Mountains and Seas.

As if sensing Li Fan's thoughts, the Saints told him in their utterly indifferent voices, "Although the Shore is within the Mountains and Seas, it can be considered an independent existence detached from the Mountains and Seas. Furthermore, you are currently within the confinement created by our divine senses..."

"How can your thoughts be transmitted out?"

As if to make Li Fan give up struggling and thus better extract [True and False]. The Saints' torture paused.

"A bunch of scoundrels, die together!"

However, Li Fan, in extreme pain, could not comprehend what the Saints were saying. The moment his thoughts regained clarity, Li Fan was consumed by boundless rage.

Roaring, he issued the command to ignite the True Spirit fire seeds.

But the command was sent as if falling into a bottomless abyss.

Below the halo, the Mountains and Seas remained serene. Only the collisions of Mountains and Seas, representing Dao Annihilation, sounded like blooming waves.

Li Fan refused to believe it. He roared again and again.

His voice echoed like the wails of a trapped beast within the light observed by the Saints.

The Saints remained silent, merely watching Li Fan's frantic actions.

After an indeterminate amount of time, as if having exhausted his strength, Li Fan finally quieted down.

"Hehehehehe..."

"After extracting [True and False], what will be my fate?" Li Fan asked with an extremely weak, self-mocking laugh.

"Rest assured, we will not harm your life. If you are willing, there is also a place for you within the Shore. If you are unwilling, you are free to go to any possibility within the Mountains and Seas. We will not obstruct you in the slightest."

"Aren't you afraid that if I get out, I'll burn down the Mountains and Seas with a single fire!" Li Fan shouted vehemently.

"Even if you burn down the Mountains and Seas, what can it compare to the words '[True and False]'?"

Only after losing something can one truly appreciate how precious what they once possessed was. The Saints' words struck Li Fan's vulnerability.

No one in the entire Mountains and Seas understood the power of [True and False] better than he did.

Even if countless changes occurred within the Mountains and Seas, with a single thought from [True and False], all could be restored.

It was just that Li Fan, who had witnessed the changes before and after [True and False], was about to become one of those who would be subjected to [True and False].

Without [True and False], Li Fan was no different from the ants he had previously regarded as NPCs.

Li Fan's expression became dejected, and he fell silent.

He let the Saints do as they pleased.

The figures outside the halo pointed their fingers again.

[True and False] continued to be forcibly extracted from Li Fan's C body.

Immersed in boundless pain, his consciousness plunged into eternal oblivion.

When Li Fan finally regained consciousness, he was already outside the halo, no longer within the Saints' sight.

The gazes of the nine figures were now fixed upon a jade tablet in the center of the halo.

"Is that... [True and False]?"

This was the first time Li Fan had seen the true appearance of [True and False], and he was stunned.

Both sides of the jade tablet appeared completely smooth, with no symbols or patterns carved upon them.

But Li Fan vaguely saw countless figures shifting simultaneously.

Some, even if their appearances were difficult to discern, exuded an extremely powerful aura.

Some, however, made Li Fan feel a sense of familiarity.

Countless figures were condensed and gathered upon this small jade tablet.

For some reason, the Saints all wore expressions of extreme complexity.

Li Fan had initially thought that he would then have his Infinite Spirit extracted to supply [True and False].

However, he never expected that the Saints would simply say, "You may go."

And then expelled him from the halo space where they were.

Seeing Li Fan suddenly appear, the Star Scavenger of the Shore was slightly stunned. "So fast?"

Then he said with a smile, "See, I told you not to worry..."

Before he could finish speaking, his gaze met Li Fan's red eyes.

Even though the Star Scavenger's strength surpassed Li Fan's, his soul momentarily faltered, and his words were abruptly cut off.

However, the Star Scavenger did not seem to mind.

He had long been accustomed to Transcendents who had just gone through the Saints' trial, as they were all somewhat emotionally unstable.

After Xiao Wangsheng also emerged, equally dejected, the Star Scavenger sent them to the [Myriad Phenomena Heaven], the dwelling place of transcendent experts within the Shore, and then left on his own.

Li Fan, immersed in the pain of losing [True and False], was in a daze and paid no attention to where he was.

Although he desperately wished to reclaim [True and False] from the Saints' hands immediately, it was evident that the combined will of the nine Saints was far too powerful.

The current Li Fan was no match for them.

"Even if I publicize the existence of [True and False], with the strength of the Nine Saints, they can ignore it. Moreover, with [True and False] in hand, no matter how much trouble I stir up, they can restore everything in an instant."

He who had always been the master of [True and False] now found himself subjected to [True and False]. Li Fan truly felt the powerlessness he had experienced when opposing [True and False].

His heart was enveloped by despair, and Li Fan spent hundreds of years in the [Myriad Phenomena Heaven] in a daze.

Even as time flowed by, his thoughts remained fixed on the day he lost [True and False].

He relived the scene of meeting the Saints again and again, savoring his own powerlessness.

"I traveled across worlds, believing that with the help of the extraordinary treasure [True and False], I could attain eternal life and freedom. I never expected..." Li Fan smiled bitterly in his heart.

Suddenly, Li Fan jolted.

"Having traveled across worlds, having traveled across worlds..."

Reliving the scene of himself being interrogated by the Saints, Li Fan muttered, "It seems there's something wrong."

"The Saints saw my Infinite Spirit, and they saw that I possessed [True and False]."

"Why didn't they see that I had traveled across worlds?"

His identity as a traveler was a secret Li Fan considered as important as the existence of [True and False].

Yet, the Saints seemed to overlook it.

"My homeland is vastly different from these Mountains and Seas. Even though the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship has traveled through the Mountains and Seas, it has not found a similar possibility. If the Saints had seen it, they would not have simply ignored it..."

"But it was clearly in my memory, so why couldn't the Saints, who could see everything, discover it?"

Li Fan's brow furrowed deeply.

Once doubt arose, it became difficult to eradicate.

And as he repeatedly pondered, Li Fan discovered more suspicious points.

"My Infinite Spirit is absolutely an earth-shattering matter."

"Even if the Saints obtained [True and False], they would need the support of spirit to activate it. Even if their spirit were as profound as mine, I, a free and readily available activator of [True and False], have no reason to be directly let go. Given the methods of the Saints, turning me into a dedicated machine for extracting spirit would not be difficult."

"Yet the Saints merely..."

"Mentioned my plan to burn mountains and boil seas."

Li Fan suddenly looked up, his gaze fixed towards the direction of the Saints in the Shore.

After gazing for a long time, and then looking around at his surroundings, at the space he currently occupied.

"There are too many contradictions."

"To display the power of the Saints, but in reality, theory and practice diverge."

"It's like..."

Li Fan extended his hand. "The simulation and deduction have reached the limit of what they can support."

"Simulation..."

This keyword triggered a memory buried deep within Li Fan's mind.

Back then, he had just awakened from his slumber.

Amnesiac, he was captivated by the lines of characters flashing on the screen before him.

Facing several different options, he hesitated for a long time.

Finally, he decided to activate a simulation again.

Then, he returned to a month prior.

Step by step, from an ordinary person to the Grand Tutor of Great Xuan, then to the Profound Yellow Realm. He met Emperor Tai Tian and was sent to the past.

Ten thousand years ago, he regained his memory.

He explored methods of becoming transcendent and finally reached the Shore.

...

The scenes of this life flashed rapidly through Li Fan's mind.

Because an extremely long time had passed, Li Fan's head felt heavy and groggy.

But he clung to a key point: "No, no, no..."

"It was possible to activate [True and False] before."

"But after I re-entered the simulation and fell into the River of Time, wanting to activate [True and False] to save myself, it failed."

"What exactly..."

Like a bolt of lightning, it shattered the fog.

Recalling that the Saints did not glimpse his memories before he traveled across worlds.

Li Fan had a faint answer in his heart.

"Could it be like this?" Li Fan was somewhat lost in thought.

Previously, he had used the Immortal-grade Illusion Array to trap the Heavenly Physician.

However, in the end, when the Heavenly Physician faced the Star Scavenger of the Immortal Ruins, because the Illusion Array could not truly simulate the might of a True Immortal, it was ultimately seen through by the Heavenly Physician.

"The current situation is exactly the same."

"It's just that what I encountered was not an Illusion Array."

"But [True and False]'s simulation!"

"It's not that the Nine Saints are truly unable to glimpse my memories from before traveling across worlds. It's that the Nine Saints within this Mountains and Seas created by [True and False] cannot!"

"Or rather, [True and False] cannot." A glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes.

"The upper limit of time that [True and False] can backtrack is only the moment I first traveled to the Mountains and Seas. Before that, my existence was a blank slate to [True and False]!"

"My identity as a traveler, and even my Infinite Spirit, are variables that exceed this simulation. Therefore, when it pertains to the level of the Mountains and Seas, and touches the upper limit of the simulation, it can only be so vague..."

His heart, which had been deadened by the loss of [True and False], began to beat again.

Li Fan stared intently at the direction of the Saints.

"It's no wonder the awakening of [True and False] has been so difficult. Even after I traveled the Mountains and Seas, I couldn't complete it. A long time ago, I felt like it was just a little bit short... but even after arriving at the Shore, it was still like this."

"Moreover, when facing the stripping by the Nine Saints, [True and False] did not resist at all."

Like a gushing spring, thoughts surged.

Li Fan's eyes regained their color. "It's simple to verify this. We just need to meet the Saints again."

"This Mountains and Seas is almost indistinguishable from reality."

"The Saints are the only flaw."

"Even if it's just my delusion, it's fine. The Saints are merciful, they probably won't blame me!"

With this thought, Li Fan headed straight for the [Stage of Meeting Saints].

Unexpectedly, halfway there, he was blocked by the Star Scavenger.

"For the inhabitants of the Shore, there is only one chance to meet the Saints, and that is upon their initial arrival. To meet the Saints again requires making a significant contribution to the Shore."

Li Fan stared at the Star Scavenger, sensing the fluctuating aura on his body, and ultimately chose to back down.

Upon returning, Li Fan forced himself to calm down and meticulously pondered, "This simulation is very different from what I have experienced before."

"Perhaps it is due to the changes brought about by the merging of the Three Daos."

"Without the existence of [True and False], it is not what truly happened in [reality]."

"But in this life, I often feel my divine sense warning me. For example, when I was going against the current in the River of Time..."

"It seems that if I were to perish in this space-time, I would truly die."

"It is like reality."

"Even if I realize that what I am experiencing now is a simulation, it is not easy to awaken from this simulation."

"The Nine Saints are the only breakthrough."

Li Fan chose to lie low for the time being.

He began to inquire about the changes in the Shore and the Mountains and Seas over the past hundred years.

Perhaps it was the inclusion of [True and False], which exceeded the simulation's tolerance limit. Therefore, its influence was blurred again.

The Saints obtained this treasure, yet there was no change at all.

This further convinced Li Fan of his judgment.

"However, how exactly do I withdraw from this simulation?" Li Fan frowned slightly.

Chapter 1608: A Real Warning

Direct suicide was certainly not an option.

This simulation was unusual, and all indications suggested that dying within the "simulation" would likely mean true annihilation.

Although he couldn't find a solution immediately, Li Fan no longer felt the despair and anxiety he had before.

"Since it's a simulation, it means things haven't reached an irreversible point. As long as I return to reality, True Reversion will return, and all difficulties will be resolved."

At this moment, having lost True Reversion, Li Fan yearned for the mystical treasure that could defy fate more than ever before.

At the same time, this experience had subtly altered some of Li Fan's thoughts.

"A summer insect cannot comprehend ice. Humans cannot imagine things beyond their cognition. Even though I tried my best to reasonably estimate the strength of the Other Shore Sages, when I truly stood before them, I had no power to resist at all."

Recalling his encounter in the Nine Sages' Halo, even though he knew he was in a simulation, Li Fan couldn't help but feel a shiver of fear.

"If there wasn't this hurdle of meeting the Sages, perhaps I could still go to the Other Shore. But now that the Sages are present, all newcomers to the Other Shore must pass their scrutiny..."

"Until I find a way to deal with the Sages, going to the Other Shore is absolutely a dead end for me."

If someone had issued such a warning to Li Fan before he came to the Other Shore, he would have scoffed. Even with True Reversion's warning, Li Fan would at most have taken it very seriously.

He would have believed that after "sufficient" preparation, he would eventually embark on the journey to the Other Shore, just like the Li Fan in this simulation.

After all, before facing the Sages this time, Li Fan, who had spread True Spirit kindling throughout the Mountains and Seas, felt his preparations were extremely robust.

"The disparity between a Saint and a Transcendent cultivator is truly immense, almost unbelievable. Especially in the Other Shore, where the Nine Sages are gathered."

"In the past, as a mortal, I could still struggle against a True Immortal, activating True Reversion in critical moments to turn the tide."

"But now, before the Nine Sages, there is no room for resistance at all."

Li Fan continuously replayed the moment his body and soul were fragmented when he met the Sages. He re-deduced it repeatedly but couldn't find any way to break the situation.

"The power of the Sages transcends the scope of my current understanding."

"The Nine Sages float high above the Mountains and Seas, like the mysterious [Star] in the Mountains and Seas fables. If I'm not mistaken, the power of a Saint has probably reached a level on par with the Mountains and Seas. The combined strength of the Nine Sages can, to some extent, even transcend the Mountains and Seas. Moreover, this is just my inference from their performance that day. Their true strength is almost immeasurable."

"And I, I need the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship to traverse the Mountains and Seas..." Li Fan shook his head slightly.

He had completely clarified the immense gap between himself and the Other Shore Sages.

"In the face of such a disparity, all schemes, threats, divine abilities, and techniques... are merely jokes. Even True Reversion would be useless."

Suddenly, Li Fan seemed to understand the reason why this simulation was so abnormal.

"Is it... True Reversion's warning?"

"At the end of my previous life, due to a moment of carelessness, I triggered the Calamity of Three Dao Convergence. Although I miraculously survived, True Reversion was probably injured as a result."

"True Reversion knows my temperament well and can even deduce what I will experience when I eventually go to the Other Shore. In the face of the Other Shore Sages' power, once danger strikes, it can no longer save me. Even it itself would be subdued by the Sages. So, it used this method to make me fully understand..."

Realizing this, a strange feeling suddenly welled up in Li Fan's heart.

The exotic treasure, True Reversion, which had accompanied him throughout his growth and seemed omnipotent, finally could no longer protect him.

Next, he would have to find a way to overcome the hurdle of meeting the Sages himself.

"Or... hide within the Mountains and Seas forever, never entering the Other Shore."

This thought was extinguished by Li Fan the moment it arose.

With True Reversion in hand, yet choosing to be a perpetual coward. This was absolutely not an option Li Fan would consider.

"I can come step by step from that land of Immortal Annihilation in Great Xuan to where I am now. Why can't I find a way to contend with the Sages?!"

The confidence that had been crushed by the Nine Sages of the Other Shore slowly rebuilt itself within Li Fan.

"The Other Shore is a creation of the Sages. Since I can't find a way to exit the simulation for now, I might as well properly research the Other Shore. Perhaps I can catch a glimpse of some clues from this creation of the Sages."

Li Fan composed himself and began to explore the Other Shore for the first time since arriving a century ago.

His current location was called the [Myriad Phenomena Heaven].

It was the dwelling place for many Transcendent experts in the Other Shore.

Within the Myriad Phenomena Heaven, a single thought could manifest a world from one's mind. Moreover, there was no need for self-consumption; it completely relied on the inherent evolutionary capabilities of the Myriad Phenomena Heaven. The Myriad Phenomena Heaven seemed boundless, and the worlds created by the Other Shore's Transcendent experts were like stars, scattered sparsely throughout.

However, Li Fan could detect that only a minority of these stellar worlds actually had Transcendent experts residing in them.

"The Myriad Phenomena Heaven is largely empty. Most Transcendent experts are either within the Mountains and Seas, pursuing the path to sainthood, or in other areas of the Other Shore."

After observing for a while, Li Fan reached this conclusion.

Choosing not to expend effort in manifesting his own dwelling world, Li Fan, with a thought, summoned a Reception Rainbow Bridge, preparing to observe other areas of the Other Shore.

Within the Myriad Phenomena Heaven, a stream of purple qi suddenly appeared, transforming into a Rainbow Bridge.

It came and went silently.

Had Li Fan not been constantly vigilant, he would have barely noticed its movements.

"Perhaps that day, when I first saw the Reception Rainbow Bridge, I should have already realized the Sages' power."

Li Fan sighed inwardly.

How could the true creators of the Other Shore, who could use the so-called Mountains and Seas' "fitting candidates" to construct transportation routes, be weak?

Next, he planned to explore the [Eternal Heavenly Steps].

Before setting off, Li Fan suddenly had a thought and sought out Xiao Wangsheng.

A century had passed, yet Xiao Wangsheng remained exactly as he was when he left the Nine Sages' Halo.

It seemed the blow he suffered was even greater than Li Fan's loss of True Reversion, and he still hadn't recovered from his distraught state.

"Brother Xiao, there's no hurdle you can't overcome. Why are you so troubled?" Li Fan patiently tried to console him.

Li Fan was, after all, Xiao Wangsheng's savior, and the two had shared conversations spanning an extremely long period.
