After a long silence, Xiao Wangsheng finally spoke, his voice filled with bitterness: "The Dynasty's Mountain and Sea Scribes all believed that by using the Star's Gaze, we could transcend the Mountains and Seas. However, that day, when I truly looked at the Star through the Sages' power..."

"I realized it was fundamentally wrong!"

Xiao Wangsheng's face showed an uncontrollable horror.

He shared his experience in the Nine Sages' Halo with Li Fan.

In a trance, Li Fan felt as if he had returned to that deep, dark space. Outside the halo, nine figures stood.

The pain of having True Reversion extracted felt as if it were assaulting him again. Li Fan instinctively shivered.

Fortunately, it was just his subconscious reaction.

This time, he was an observer, watching the scene unfold.

The Nine Sages of the Other Shore were already high above the Mountains and Seas.

But as the Nine Sages pointed their fingers, Xiao Wangsheng within the halo seemed to be pulled, slowly raising his head.

Thus, he could see higher.

A lonely star hung high, like the Eye of God, indifferently gazing upon the beings of the Mountains and Seas!

As his gaze met the Star head-on, Xiao Wangsheng felt as if he was once again witnessing the annihilation of his ancient dynasty, and even the collapse of the Mountains and Seas themselves!

Even under the Sages' protection, Xiao Wangsheng's recently reconstructed body began to decay.

Small holes, seemingly corroded by Dao Annihilation, appeared on his body without warning.

Xiao Wangsheng was terrified, like a drowning man, struggling for help. He wanted to avert his gaze from the Star.

But his eyes seemed to be tightly adsorbed, utterly unable to move.

His body's surface turned a strange purplish-black.

More and more holes appeared on Xiao Wangsheng, as if he were being consumed by Dao Annihilation.

He was on the verge of completely dissipating within the Mountains and Seas.

At this moment, the Nine Sages' Halo erupted with dazzling light, filling Xiao Wangsheng's vision and shielding the lone [Star] hanging above.

Only then was Xiao Wangsheng able to avert his gaze.

Even though gazing at the Star was what he had painstakingly yearned for.

"The endless changes of the Mountains and Seas are but an instant in the eyes of the [Star]."

"To attempt to peek into the mysteries of the Star with our transient concept of time is no different from suicide."

As the Sages' calm words echoed, Xiao Wangsheng's injuries were fully restored.

The Nine Sages' figures faded, but he couldn't extricate himself from the encounter with the Star.

He had been in this state of profound despair for a century.

And it was clear that he would continue to sink deeper.

"We were wrong, my friend, our ideas were all wrong."

"An ant trying to shake a tree; how foolish and arrogant!"

"How foolish and arrogant!"

Xiao Wangsheng refused Li Fan's suggestion to explore the Other Shore together.

Instead, he returned to the Myriad Phenomena Heaven, creating a world for himself, recreating his ancient dynasty, and once again serving as a Mountain and Sea Scribe.

Li Fan did not press him. He watched Xiao Wangsheng immerse himself in "role-playing" and quietly departed.

"When the true is false, the false is also true."

"True or false, who can truly distinguish?"

With a sigh of emotion, Li Fan stepped onto the Reception Rainbow Bridge and headed towards the Eternal Heavenly Steps.

This journey was subtly different from his previous one.

As he traveled, fragments of light, imbued with images of the Mountains and Seas, burst forth from the purple bridge.

They were like ripples stirred by swift movement across water.

Li Fan casually collected a few fragments. It felt as if he himself was rapidly traversing through the Mountains and Seas.

"With these fragments, one can clearly perceive the Dao of Transcendence. For cultivators who haven't yet transcended, these are treasures of immeasurable value. But for those who have already transcended and forged their own Dao path, their value is not as great."

"Yet, they are perfectly suited for me."

Li Fan felt little joy, merely absorbing them as circumstances allowed.

After all, if he couldn't find a way to escape this simulation, he would probably be trapped in the Other Shore for the rest of his life. He would have plenty of time to slowly comprehend.

But if he could successfully leave, he could always return to comprehend the Dao of Transcendence whenever he wished.

The Reception Rainbow Bridge flew ceaselessly, stirring up waves of the Mountains and Seas, with no sense of time's passage.

On this day, as the solidified purple qi beneath his feet suddenly dissipated, Li Fan finally reached his destination.

A familiar, endless river flowed down from the heavens.

Roaring and surging, without end.

"This is..."

"The River of Time?"

Having once struggled against its current, Li Fan recognized the true nature of the river before him almost instantly.

"It's not an illusion. Rather, it's the truly existing River of Time, concretized and fixed here by an inscrutable power."

"Passing through this projection, one can truly plunge into it."

Li Fan marveled inwardly.

What caught his attention even more were the ancient, rustic stone slabs suspended above the river!

Like steps, they spanned past and present!

Li Fan instantly understood the meaning of the Eternal Heavenly Steps.

"Not all Transcendent experts in the Other Shore comprehend the Dao of Reversal. If they wish to travel to different time nodes in the Mountains and Seas, they need the help of these Eternal Heavenly Steps."

Li Fan scanned the vast River of Time, trying to find the beings who forged these steps.

"Hungry Immortal once said that two Transcendent experts who failed the Sages' test were imprisoned here."

"My plan to burn mountains and boil seas was forgivable in the eyes of the Sages. I wonder what unspeakable atrocities these two committed."

Li Fan truly wished to meet and learn from them.

However, a seemingly short segment of the river, flowing from heaven to earth, contained an infinity of detail in each section. Like the boundless Mountains and Seas, it was impossible to survey in a short time.

But apart from exiting the simulation, Li Fan had no other immediate goal. So he simply stood by the River of Time, patiently observing.

Previously, after absorbing the power of the Heavenly Demon within his body, Li Fan had felt that his progress in the Dao of Reversal had advanced further. However, he had never had the chance to verify it within the River of Time.

Now, standing by the river, bathed in the fragments of time occasionally spewing forth, he confirmed his judgment.

"It seems the Heavenly Demon is indeed closely related to the River of Time. Perhaps it is even a 'fitting candidate' for the river."

The term "fitting candidate" referred to an existence whose very being could perfectly adapt to its environment.

The Reception Rainbow Bridge was constructed from fitting candidates of the Mountains and Seas. It could rapidly traverse the Mountains and Seas.

And after absorbing the Heavenly Demon, the ease Li Fan felt when facing the River of Time was proof that the Heavenly Demon was a fitting candidate for the river.

"Perhaps it hasn't reached the point where I can freely traverse it, but it's much stronger than ordinary Dao of Reversal."

"Even without fully comprehending the Dao of Reversal, I can navigate it without the need for these Eternal Heavenly Steps."

As he pondered this, a thunderous rumble suddenly echoed from the illusory River of Time.

Li Fan looked intently, only to see that one of the ancient stone slabs, originally suspended outside the river, had somehow fallen into it. It splashed countless fragments of time.

This also caused the myriad intricate paths flowing beneath the river to change.

Li Fan keenly observed that along with the falling stone slab, a figure also plunged into the river.

"The Eternal Heavenly Steps are consumables. After being used and leveraged by Transcendent experts, they are depleted." Li Fan mused thoughtfully.

Chapter 1609: All Sceneries on the Other Shore Are Marvelous

Direct suicide was certainly not an option.

This simulation was unusual, and all indications suggested that dying within the "simulation" would likely mean true annihilation.

Although he couldn't find a solution immediately, Li Fan no longer felt the despair and anxiety he had before.

"Since it is a simulation, it means things haven't reached an irreversible point. As long as I return to reality, True Reversion can return, and all difficulties will be resolved."

"The Eternal Heavenly Steps are consumables. After being used and leveraged by Transcendent experts, they are depleted." Li Fan mused thoughtfully.

Chapter 1610: Deceiving the Saint by Tactics

A crisp bell chime echoed in Li Fan's ears, lingering like a persistent melody.

Since entering the Shore, a series of anomalies had occurred: his Infinite Spirit had been detected, True Return had been confiscated, and in his despair and numbness, he had discovered it was all a simulation…

These intense emotions, brought about by these events, had now quietly faded with the resonant chimes of the bell.

Li Fan’s heart settled into a state of peace he hadn't felt in a long time.

Even the faint joy of discovering this transcendent intent, which promised an escape from the simulation, had vanished.

Absolute peace, devoid of any personal emotion, allowing for a more comprehensive and rational analysis.

"Calamity-Quelling Focused Mind…"

As the bell's chime reverberated, the name of this transcendent expert's ancient bronze bell surfaced in Li Fan's mind.

Along with it came endless streams of light and shadow, depicting the life deeds of this transcendent.

Li Fan marveled as he reviewed them: "Like a smoothly paved road, without a single ripple. From Foundation Establishment to Dao Integration, from True Immortal to the Nameless realm. All setbacks, all tribulations, this person calmly and steadily navigated them."

"Even after leaving their original possibility and facing the continuous tidal waves of Dao Annihilation in the boundless Mountains and Seas, they remained as placid as an ancient well. Even in the most perilous moments, when Dao Annihilation had already engulfed more than half of their body, they were still thus."

"In truth, this person also possessed emotions and desires, but with paramount willpower, they dissolved all distracting thoughts. Numerous calamities were all overcome with the aid of Focused Mind…"

Slowly opening his eyes, emerging from the immersive light and shadow, Li Fan uttered with a solemn expression, "Detached from external things, without self, without ego. This person, I am inferior!"

"Fan Wunian…" Li Fan committed the name of this fallen transcendent expert to memory and reverently put away the ancient bell, Calamity-Quelling Focused Mind, preparing to return to the Shore.

This time, traveling to the Shore would not be like before, searching aimlessly like a headless fly in the Mountains and Seas.

Having already visited the Shore and passed the recognition of the Nine Saints, Li Fan could now gaze into the heavens from any corner of the Mountains and Seas and faintly perceive the shadow of the Shore. It was like the great sun in the sky, radiating endless warm brilliance. Li Fan merely needed to follow the direction of the light to quickly return to the Shore.

Li Fan leaped, returning to the Mountains and Seas. Looking back, the original possibility, due to the deaths of numerous True Immortals, had become precarious. It could be engulfed by Dao Annihilation at any moment.

"The outcome is irrelevant."

Li Fan's heart remained unmoved, and he flew towards the Shore without looking back.

Under the influence of the immense tidal waves stirred by his traversal of Dao Annihilation, the already unstable possibility completely collapsed. Innumerable beings, countless True Immortals, were annihilated in an instant.

But this was merely an insignificant spray of ripples kicked up in the Mountains and Seas.

The Calamity-Quelling Focused Mind emitted continuous bell chimes, directly counteracting the Dao Annihilation tides. The Dao Annihilation seemed to strike an invisible barrier and was repelled.

Li Fan moved with unrestrained freedom, riding the waves.

Even without the assistance of the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship this time, his journey was far smoother than during his first exploration of the Mountains and Seas.

The feeling of desolate coldness from being far from the mortal world was gone. Even when facing the threat of Dao Annihilation, Li Fan could calmly cope, as if Dao Annihilation were no longer a fatal crisis to him, but rather a source of immense opportunities!

"When I escape this simulation and return to reality, I must immediately acquire the ancient bell, Calamity-Quelling Focused Mind. Even among the myriad stone tablets in the Boundless Mountains and Seas Forest, this transcendent intent is undoubtedly of the highest caliber."

"I just don't know how Fan Wunian met his demise back then."

Empowered by the ancient bell, Li Fan's return speed was much faster than anticipated.

As he traversed the Mountains and Seas at high speed, Li Fan always felt the warm radiance of the Shore shining upon him. It not only pointed the direction but also increased his speed in traversing Dao Annihilation.

"This should be the Boundless Light Chain."

"The faster I traverse, the greater the auxiliary effect of the Light Chain."

"That scroll of the Mountains and Seas that I glimpsed vaguely within the Light Chain that day, perhaps only Saints could have drawn it. Its power permeates the entire Mountains and Seas…"

On this journey through the Mountains and Seas, Li Fan became increasingly certain of his judgment. The Nine Saints, and the Shore guarded by them, had, to some extent, surpassed the Mountains and Seas.

"But currently, this segment of the Mountains and Seas I am in…"

"According to what I know from the phantom River of Time within the Shore, this segment of the Mountains and Seas, from its beginning to its end, spans at most fifty thousand years. Compared to the vast history of the Mountains and Seas, this is but a drop in the ocean."

"The complete Mountains and Seas, compared to the segment we inhabit, possess countless times more power. And even so, they have been shattered and broken by the calamity of Dao Annihilation."

"To completely resolve the scourge of Dao Annihilation, even the Nine Saints are powerless!" Li Fan realized.

Time flows without leaving a trace in the Mountains and Seas.

When Li Fan returned to the Shore, only then did the collapse of the Calamity-Quelling Focused Mind's possibility occur in the phantom River of Time.

Li Fan clearly saw that because of that spray of ripples, the course of the surging river had changed minutely. Innumerable possibilities were affected.

But this aligned with the four words, "The outcome is irrelevant."

At the origin and end of the long river, two dark abysses still stood silently.

No matter how the river flowed, they remained unchanged.

Taking a deep breath, Li Fan proceeded to the Boundless Mountains and Seas Forest. With some reluctance, he handed over the Calamity-Quelling Focused Mind ancient bell, "It's a pity that True Return is not with me now. Otherwise, by borrowing the ability of 'Shifting Perspectives,' I could have mastered its power myself."

As the ancient bell left his hand, as if sensing the myriad transcendent intents similar to itself above, it instantly emitted a faint green light and ascended.

Bell chimes echoed, permeating the stone tablet forest, causing countless tablets to jointly radiate brilliance.

From the sky, a finger suddenly descended.

It gently pressed upon the ancient bell.

The bell's chime was instantly silenced. Then, the green ancient bell transformed into the appearance of a stone tablet and flew into the myriad Boundless Mountains and Seas Forest.

The phantom finger disappeared, leaving only a lingering echo.

Li Fan once again chose to hand over the Lone Sail of the Mountains and Seas.

Compared to the Calamity-Quelling Focused Mind, the disturbance caused by this Lone Sail was much smaller.

There was only a localized resonance of transcendent stone tablets, and no fingers descended from the sky to suppress it.

The Lone Sail flew into the Boundless Mountains and Seas Forest and spontaneously transformed into a stone tablet.

After submitting two transcendent intents, Li Fan's heart also received a flash of information.

His accumulated "merits" were enough to meet the Saints once!

The so-called merits within the Shore had no specific quantifiable data, but they were indeed quite useful.

Apart from being able to meet the Saints, the most significant use was to exchange for "privileges" in various regions of the Shore.

For example, within the Boundless Mountains and Seas Forest, after the Saints' will judged, one could find the transcendent stone tablet most likely to allow for future Dao comprehension. And for a period of time, one could exclusively access the comprehension derived from this tablet.

Another example was using the observational ability of the "Tidal Pivot of Birth and Death" to approach the Eternal Silence Void up close. After all, if one were to truly get trapped within it and be powerless, they might not even have time to regret before perishing. By observing through the Tidal Pivot of Death and Birth, one could, to a certain extent, determine how close they were to successfully traversing the Eternal Silence Void.

… Besides the various uses within the Shore, merits could also be exchanged for rare artifacts from other forces. For instance, the Grand Dao Medicine of Saintly Fortune refined by Emperor Tai Wei!

"The so-called Grand Dao Medicine of Saintly Fortune is, in essence, no different from the Loquat and Bai Qian I encountered before. It's just that the materials used for refining medicine are not the Great Dao of the Mountains and Seas, but the destiny of the Saintly Dynasty! With the Saintly Dynasty stretching across the Mountains and Seas, the accumulated destiny is said to even aid in achieving Sainthood."

"The Grand Dao Medicine of Saintly Fortune is difficult to refine. Even Emperor Tai Wei does not have many in stock. What the merits on the Shore can exchange for are naturally items that the Saints had traded with the Emperor at a certain cost. Moreover, the Saints have also stated that what is exchanged by merits is not a complete portion of the Grand Dao Medicine of Saintly Fortune, but rather pills divided into nine parts by them. Even so, the Immortals on the Shore are eager for this Saintly Medicine…"

"If it weren't for the pressing need to escape this simulation, I would also consider accumulating more merits to exchange for a Saintly Medicine to try." Li Fan suppressed his surging desire and accessed the Boundless Light Chain with his divine sense.

Perhaps due to the blessing of his merits, the scroll of the Mountains and Seas that Li Fan saw this time was clearer than before. It depicted the scene of continuous mountains and seas.

And the giant sphere of light leaping above the mountains symbolized the Shore!

Li Fan's divine sense came into contact with this sphere of light, and information about himself appeared.

Past experiences, even his thoughts at the time, were all meticulously recorded.

At this moment, Li Fan felt as if he had returned to that instant when he was scrutinized by the Saints. Even though he knew it was a simulation, a surge of unbridled anger rose within him again.

But clearly, now was not the time to lose his temper. Li Fan forcefully suppressed his anger and, after all his information had been completely presented, he then looked toward the merit data.

A white halo, like the ring of the Nine Saints, represented one portion of merit.

Li Fan's accumulated merits from retrieving two transcendent intents were just barely enough for one portion.

"Exchange for an audience with the Saints."

After confirmation, this white halo instantly dimmed.

And Li Fan also perceived that he could now see the Saints again at any time.

"True Return says it's a simulation, but it's almost indistinguishable from what actually happened in the Mountains and Seas."

"Only my Infinite Spirit and the addition of True Return itself would cause things to exceed the simulation's tolerance. This is the key to my escape."

"Now that True Return is held by the Nine Saints, its impact has been deliberately obscured. To break this gap…"

Li Fan re-examined the plan he had already set in his mind.

Even with a ninety-nine percent certainty that the plan would succeed, at the critical moment of taking the final step, he hesitated.

One reason was the immense psychological shadow cast by the Nine Saints before, which had not yet subsided.

Secondly, Li Fan had now completely lost the protection of True Return. If he perished in the simulation, he would truly die in reality. He was no different from ordinary transcendent cultivators. Facing the might of Saints, an action that could endanger his life naturally made him hesitate.

But Li Fan did not hesitate for too long.

As if hearing the faint chant of the ancient bell, Calamity-Quelling Focused Mind, once again, Li Fan’s expression slowly turned resolute.

"After much contemplation, this is the only way to escape this simulation."

"Besides, with such a high probability of success, why should I be so fearful!" Li Fan chuckled self-mockingly.

"When I first arrived in Great Xuan, as a mortal with no treasures, I was not so timid!"

"Meet the Saints!" Li Fan looked towards the sky of the Shore and said with unwavering determination.

As if divine beings in the heavens cast their gaze downwards, Li Fan's vision instantly shifted.

Below was the continuous expanse of mountains and seas, above was a solitary star hanging high.

Before him stood the Nine Saints in a halo!

Nine figures stood silently, silently observing Li Fan.

Li Fan took a deep breath, calming himself. Then, he asked in a deep voice, "May I ask the Saints, do you truly wish to save the Mountains and Seas?"

"We have sacrificed our lives, moving forward relentlessly, heading to the Eternal Silence Void precisely to save the Mountains and Seas from Dao Annihilation. We can even discard our own lives, so why would we refuse?" The Saints' voices responded calmly.

"May I ask again, are you Saints, does True Return still exist?" Li Fan asked resonatingly, scanning the nine Saints surrounding him.

The simulation of True Return was based on reality.

Even if the influence of True Return could be obscured, True Return would only appear where it should appear.

The Nine Saints' figures rippled slightly.

But in the end, they replied, "It exists."

"If True Return exists, why not use it to save the Mountains and Seas?" Li Fan questioned.

"After a hundred years, have the Saints ever used True Return? Even once!"

As this question was uttered, Li Fan's heart felt as if it were being clutched.

He feared that the Saints would become enraged and unleash their wrath, or that the Saints might reply that True Return had been used countless times, and he was simply unaware.

But to his relief, the Saints remained silent.

Li Fan secretly rejoiced and struck while the iron was hot, pressing on, "With the ultimate treasure True Return in hand, why ignore it and not use it?"

"Is it because the Saints are merely lingering remnants of will, devoid of spirit to utilize it?"

Without waiting for the Saints' answer, Li Fan solemnly cupped his fists and bowed, slowly stating, "If that is the case, I, Fan, am willing to offer my Infinite Spirit for the Saints to utilize, in order to save the Mountains and Seas!"

His voice thundered, echoing incessantly within the halo.

The figures of the Nine Saints, as if struck by a tsunami, became turbulent.

This time, the Saints could no longer respond with silence. Li Fan's request was righteous and awe-inspiring.

Even if this were reality, the next step would undoubtedly be for the Saints to extract Li Fan's Infinite Spirit and utilize True Return to save the Mountains and Seas step by step.

But…

This was within True Return's simulation!

Chapter 1611: The Situation is Broken and Finally Returns to True

"To burn mountains and boil seas!"

"Devour! Devour! Devour..."

In Li Fan's eyes, the Mountains and Seas were no longer a vast illusion but rather a delectable feast exuding a fatal allure. Those streams of black energy soaring into the sky were precisely the tempting aura rising from the Mountains and Seas! It was the ancient taste of the Mountains and Seas themselves! Like his first encounter with Ink Slaughter when he was still a mortal cultivator, an extreme craving, originating from the depths of his soul, suddenly emerged, threatening to completely dominate Li Fan's consciousness. Regardless of realm or strength, ignoring innate talent or disposition. As long as one still possessed "desires," they would be ignited by the black fragments, magnified countless times, and guided into greed for the Mountains and Seas.

Cultivators in the Mountains and Seas inherently harbored a certain yearning for them. If further induced, their hidden desires would almost certainly be ignited. The higher their strength, the more likely they were to pose a substantial threat to the Mountains and Seas, and the more so! Just as Li Fan thought now: "All that is slaughtered and killed can become my sustenance. Now that the True Spirit fire seeds have almost spread throughout the Mountains and Seas, all it takes is a single great fire, and the Mountains and Seas will be engulfed in flames!" "Flames blazing, ashes filling the sky. Delicious, delectable..." The more he thought, the more Li Fan felt his plan was likely to succeed, and the more impulsive he became.

"Should I, perhaps, truly give it a try?" A dangerous glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes. One of these myriad dispersed thoughts, having been bewitched/tempted, was attempting to send a signal of rebellion to the main body.

"Calm down."

However, at this moment, another cold voice echoed in Li Fan's mind. Like a distant echo across the shore, it was completely unaffected by the seductive sound. This voice was precisely Li Fan's own! This clear-headed Li Fan was formed from innumerable Dao-One Worms. It was the main body, sensing something was amiss, that commanded the Dao-One Worms to the rescue. Although it was only a dispersed thought, under the current circumstances, it was even clearer than Li Fan's dispersed consciousness. This was the effect of the Dao-One Worm swarms constantly adapting to the frenzied bewitchment/temptation brought about by the black fragments!

With the reminder from the Dao-One Worms' consciousness, the Li Fan present at this location instantly regained his clarity. Strictly speaking, he had not been completely bewitched/tempted just now. After all, the idea of attempting to ignite the Mountains and Seas had already been repeatedly simulated in his mind several times. However, each time, Li Fan had ultimately rejected it. Even without the Dao-One Worms' consciousness, he likely would not have truly attempted to "devour the Mountains and Seas." But it was undeniable that Li Fan had indeed been somewhat influenced by the black fragments. To the point where he temporarily lost consideration for the future and the overall situation, only focusing on immediate gains and losses, as if his eyes were blinded.

With the calibration and assistance from the Dao-One Worm swarm's consciousness, Li Fan became completely calm. Facing the incessantly ringing seductive voices, he was no longer moved. After the worm-formed consciousness completely devoured the source of the bewitchment/temptation, the Mountains and Seas in Li Fan's vision finally returned to their normal appearance. However, the faint "fragrance" emanating from the Mountains and Seas had not completely disappeared. It still existed.

Li Fan looked at the black fragment in his hand, which had already been digested by the Dao-One Worms. Its physical form no longer existed in the mortal world, but the outline of the fragment still depicted its original appearance. Clutching it with his right hand, he found himself grasping at air. His five fingers passed straight through the fragment, as if its existence were merely Li Fan's illusion.

"In the eyes of the Dao-One Worms, they have completed their mission. The black fragment has already disappeared. However..." Li Fan pondered, then summoned the True Immortal apostles from the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship docked in Dao Annihilation. He finally confirmed that, apart from Li Fan himself, others could not see this "invisible" fragment. Moreover, this invisible fragment only attached itself to Li Fan. No matter where Li Fan went, it would always follow.

"Does it pose a threat?" Li Fan gently stroked the invisible fragment in his hand. He was currently just one of his myriad dispersed thoughts. If he encountered an uncontrollable situation, this dispersed thought could instantly self-destruct, severing any possibility of it affecting the main body. This was Li Fan's contingency plan, made from the very beginning when he dispatched countless Profound Yellow Immortal Ships to various corners of the Mountains and Seas. Therefore, he was not worried about the safety of his main body. The instructions from his main body also allowed him to boldly study it without reservation.

With no further concerns, he began to study the invisible fragment around him. Only he could observe the fragment's existence, and the research could not involve others. Fortunately, it was just a dispersed thought that could be discarded at any time, so he had no worries.

"The first step is to find a way to establish substantial contact with this fragment." Although the invisible fragment surrounded Li Fan, whether he tried to touch it or use his divine sense, he could not truly grasp the fragment itself. Even when Li Fan used the methods of the Dao Refinement Medicine King Scripture and placed it within a grand furnace, he could not perceive its existence.

"A being on par with the Mountains and Seas can only be seen and touched and comprehended by being on par with the Mountains and Seas." Li Fan suddenly recalled his experience when he comprehended the Great Dao of Longevity in his previous life. Cheng Dao, as Duke Shou Qiu's true disciple, had cultivated tirelessly for eons, yet his comprehension of "Longevity" was not as profound as Li Fan's acquired in an instant. This was precisely because Li Fan possessed Huan Zhen, and to some extent, was also on par with the Mountains and Seas.

"Although Huan Zhen is currently in slumber, I can still utilize some of its True and False transformations, barely achieving a state of being on par with the Mountains and Seas." "However, the information of this fragment is unclear. If I were to act so rashly, I might repeat the past and re-experience the catastrophe of the Three Dao Convergence..."

After contemplating for a moment, Li Fan had an idea. "Why not borrow Duke Shou Qiu's Great Dao of Longevity once more?" During his discussions with Cheng Dao over the years, Li Fan had indirectly confirmed that Duke Shou Qiu was indeed within the Eternal Void. Even if he activated the remaining Longevity power within his body, and Duke Shou Qiu sensed it, he would not be able to return for some time. "Moreover, according to Cheng Dao, the Mountains and Seas are boundless. Those who obtain Duke Shou Qiu's seed of Longevity might not be few. Perhaps Duke Shou Qiu even eagerly hopes that someone in this world can truly inherit his mantle, allowing him to travel to even more ancient Mountains and Seas without any worries."

After much deliberation, Li Fan had no further reservations. After a brief communication with his main body, a surge of vitality inexplicably emerged from within him. His body, which had become incredibly solid after absorbing the Garbage Mountain possibility, became indistinguishable from his true body due to this surge of Longevity power. Even Li Fan himself could hardly differentiate between his current state and his main body. Adjusting his posture, Li Fan brought the invisible fragment encircling him to his front. He then spat out a mouthful of blood, its boundless vitality gushing out like a torrential river, engulfing the fragment.

As expected, the invisible fragment, which had remained unresponsive to any external existence, finally changed upon contact with the power of Longevity. Countless lines appeared within the fragment, like myriad mirrors. Each mirror reflected the continuous scenery of the Mountains and Seas. What shocked Li Fan even more was that the Mountains and Seas in the mirrors were not unified! In other words, the fusion of the Mountains and Seas had not yet reached its current extent. The current Mountains and Seas were integrated, with each part inextricably linked. But in the fragment's mirrors, the Mountains and Seas were merely leaning against each other! The boundaries between the mountains and the seas were still very distinct. Li Fan could even clearly see the countless possibilities hovering at the edge of the Infinite Sea, crashing against the mountains and seas above, turning into spray and dust!

"This is the state of the Mountains and Seas during their initial fusion, as depicted in the 'Sayings of the Mountains and Seas'!" Li Fan's heart stirred, attempting to see more. However, as the Longevity power he spat out gradually dissipated, the fragment returned to its normal appearance. "How is this possible? The power of the Great Dao of Longevity disappears so quickly?" Li Fan's heart instantly grew alert. After all, to expel the Longevity power from his body, Li Fan had taken considerable effort. He had continuously sprayed blood and nurtured the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm for decades without stopping. Only then did he achieve some effect. Theoretically speaking, the Longevity power contained in the mouthful of blood Li Fan had just spat out should normally last for a million years without dissipating. But now...

"It is this fragment that is absorbing it." Li Fan stared at the invisible fragment, which seemed no different from before, with a cold glint in his eyes. Perhaps sensing that Li Fan was a fellow being, the fragment's attachment and adherence to Li Fan became even closer. Without deliberate attraction, the fragment would actively "follow" Li Fan. Li Fan hesitated for a moment, then ultimately decided to continue. With another infusion of Longevity power, the fragment once again revealed the initial scene of the Mountains and Seas merging. This time, prepared, Li Fan saw even more clearly.

"There are beings in the Mountains and Seas!" "Born from the sea, attempting to ascend the mountains..." Although they were merely fleeting fragments, Li Fan could still glimpse events recorded in the "Sayings of the Mountains and Seas" left by Sun Piaomiao. The sea waves crashed against the mountains, and countless civilizations and beings turned to dust. But within the Infinite Sea, new civilizations were constantly born. Continuously exploring and conquering the Mountains and Seas. It was like a cycle, or perhaps a destiny that had long been predetermined. Once again, after the Mountains and Seas had been shaken and all civilizations destroyed. The Mountains and Seas fell into a rare period of calm. But something extraordinary occurred. The Infinite Sea churned as if boiling, and with the evaporation of countless possibilities, a terrifying roar seemed to emanate from the depths of the seabed. It echoed upwards towards the mountains, reverberating through the peaks. It was like a symphony of Mountains and Seas, grand, magnificent, and soul-stirring.

Li Fan stared blankly at this scene, only recovering his senses long after the scene in the fragment had disappeared. "This is merely the record within the invisible fragment." "What truly unfolded in the Mountains and Seas back then must have been far more astonishing." Li Fan sighed deeply. He now understood what he had just seen within the fragment. The communication between the Infinite Sea and the Upper Mountains! "If described in human language, it is the 'dialogue between the Mountains and the Seas' that I saw in the Sayings of the Mountains and Seas." "However..." "The communication between the Mountains and Seas was far from limited to this." "This was the tendency for the Upper Mountains and the Infinite Sea to merge, and it also contained their mutual resistance to their fated merger. And..." Even with Li Fan's current knowledge, he could not decipher its full meaning. But merely by listening to the echoes from the Mountains and Seas, Li Fan felt that his understanding of the essence of the Mountains and Seas was constantly improving. His efficiency in comprehending the Dao surpassed that of drifting in Dao Annihilation by thousands or tens of thousands of times. After all, one was a macroscopic overview, while the other was being lost in the infinite microscopic interior. The insights gained were fundamentally incomparable.

"If I can comprehend the principles within, then transcending through my own power..." "Will be a matter of course!" Li Fan was immersed in the roaring of mountains and seas, unable to extricate himself. Unfortunately, the scenes recorded within this invisible fragment seemed to be limited. Subsequently, even as Li Fan continuously infused it with Longevity power, the fragment only displayed repetitive scenes. This made Li Fan somewhat disappointed. "It is unlikely that it is deliberately deceiving me; it has simply recorded this segment of the scene." "From my external observation, the recorded scene can be fully played in just over ten breaths. However, if measured by the timescale of mortal possibilities..." "It is likely billions of years long." "This is a period of history longer than Duke Shou Qiu's lifespan." Although Duke Shou Qiu attained the Great Dao of Longevity, the temporal node he inhabited was at the very end of the Mountains and Seas' fusion. Compared to the long lifespan of the Mountains and Seas, it occupied an extremely insignificant portion. "This fragment has persisted from the beginning of the Mountains and Seas' fusion until now." "Precisely..." Although no new scenes appeared, Li Fan still chose to continue to infuse it with Longevity power. Because he had discovered that as the Longevity power was continuously infused, faint whispers began to emanate from the fragment. Unlike the seductive voices before, this time, it was the fragment attempting to communicate.

Chapter 1612: Li Fan Grinds True Return

"The power of Longevity and the Mountains and Seas are of the same grade." The answer was obvious. Only power of the same grade as the Mountains and Seas could support a "simulation" of the same grade.

"But how is this easy? Last life, even on the Shore, I probably only found traces related to it from the Nine Saints. To steal power from the Nine Saints?" Li Fan's eyelids twitched. Not only because of the psychological trauma of the experience with the Nine Saints, but also because of the tribulation of the merging of the Three Daos. It was foreseeable that even if Li Fan were lucky enough to obtain energy of the same grade as the Mountains and Seas, the tribulation of the merging of the Three Daos would likely be triggered again due to the presence of Huan Zhen. Neither Li Fan nor Huan Zhen would want to see this situation again.

"Unless I can resist the temptation of the merging of the Three Daos with astonishing perseverance. My current self-control is still somewhat lacking."

"Tribulation-Calming Steadfastness..." Having learned from the previous simulation, Li Fan, who had a realistic understanding of himself, immediately thought of this transcendent true intent that could help calm all desires.

"It is not difficult to find its location now that it is known. However, only this one safeguard is not enough. During the period of re-cultivation in this life, I still need to cultivate and strengthen my state of mind as much as possible, to the point where I can face the Saints with an unchanged expression. Moreover, it is best to make further preparations. If I still lose control and insist on performing the merging of the Three Daos, I will forcibly interrupt this process..."

Since he could foresee what would happen after obtaining energy of the same grade as the Mountains and Seas, Li Fan naturally made various preparations in advance.

The potential future troubles had seen a glimmer of hope for a solution, but where to find energy of the same grade as the Mountains and Seas remained a mystery. "I can't possibly go and shake down Duke Shou Qiu again, can I?" Li Fan shook his head slightly, quickly dismissing the idea. From the current situation, Huan Zhen's influence was limited to the "current" Mountains and Seas. It should not include the Eternal Void where the Saints resided.

"After all the effort to escape from Duke Shou Qiu's gaze, how could I easily go back?"

"I need to find a foolproof plan." In his study, Li Fan fell into deep thought. The current situation was that with Li Fan's current strength, the moment he entered the Saints' sight, his secrets would be instantly exposed. Therefore, he needed to use Huan Zhen's simulation ability to find a way to break through.

However, to activate Huan Zhen's simulation, which could accurately deduce the actions of cultivators at the Saint level, he needed support from energy of the same grade as the Mountains and Seas, thus falling into a vicious cycle. After a long time, Li Fan finally thought of a possible answer.

"Energy of the same grade as the Mountains and Seas is not specifically for the Saints of the Shore."

"Emperor Taiwei's Sacred Luck Elixir can promote the birth of Saints, which is definitely one part. And..." Li Fan couldn't help but recall Duke Shou Qiu's experience of becoming a Saint.

"Duke Shou Qiu was originally just a small guardian of a mountain in the Immortal Realm. Although his aptitude was extraordinary, and he could observe the Mountains and Seas to comprehend the Dao, he was ultimately limited by his lifespan. In the end, he sank into the Infinite Sea. There, facing death, Duke Shou Qiu encountered fragments of the Great Dao of Longevity, and thus his destiny was reversed, and he had the opportunity to become a Saint."

"Therefore, theoretically speaking, energy of the same grade as the Mountains and Seas might be obtainable from the infinite Mountains and Seas."

"Of course, this is only theoretical," Li Fan's eyes flickered. Forget about energy of the same grade as the Mountains and Seas, even finding a transcendent true intent was extremely difficult, let alone searching the entire Mountains and Seas.

"Not to mention the Nine Saints, even the many powerful beings on the Shore basically have the ability to turn the Mountains and Seas upside down. Over the years, even if there were remnants of energy of the same grade as the Mountains and Seas in the world, they must have been discovered by them."

Li Fan's thoughts paused. "Unless..."

"They, like Huan Zhen, did not want to be discovered and would actively hide themselves." Li Fan's eyes suddenly lit up. "This way, I am not without a chance."

"The reason why the Saints on the Shore were able to achieve the Saint realm is probably related to energy of the same grade as the Mountains and Seas."

"Already known: Lian Shan, Shang Fang Shan. Gui Hai, Infinite Sea. Shou Qiu, Longevity."

"Tai Yi, born before the Immortal Realm existed. If there is indeed energy of the same grade as the Mountains and Seas, he would be the easiest to find."

"As for the three Saints, Xing Cha, Ye Pan, and Qie Ji, I only know their names, but know nothing specific. I can only infer from their names."

"My guess is probably correct. The Shore did not have nine Saints from the beginning. There are still legends of becoming a Saint circulating in the Boundless Forest of Mountains and Seas. And they are rarely seen on the Shore. Most transcendent experts roam the mortal world of the Mountains and Seas. The stronger they are, the more so. It's probably not just to collect transcendent true intents..." Li Fan speculated that becoming a Saint might only be a prerequisite, and energy of the same grade as the Mountains and Seas might be an indispensable material to become a Saint comparable to or even transcending the Mountains and Seas.

Although he had entered the Shore, Li Fan still had no knowledge of how to advance further. The people on the Shore also maintained a tacit silence, and no kind person took the initiative to guide Li Fan.

"If only I had asked the Nine Saints for clarification during the simulation earlier," Li Fan quietly shook his head. "Even if my guess is correct, it is still difficult to find energy of the same grade as the Mountains and Seas." In the face of such a small probability, luck becomes insignificant.

"Actually, I already possess the most important condition for becoming a Saint: Huan Zhen."

"As long as I continuously understand the transformation of true and false, and turn it into my own divine ability, even half of Huan Zhen's power will be enough to face the Saints calmly."

"True and false, all depends on the heart. The Mountains and Seas are boundless, and can be overturned in an instant..." Li Fan savored these sixteen characters from Huan Zhen's reply, filled with joy.

"Unfortunately, the comprehension of the Dao of True and False is not that easy."

"Ordinary insights are like reflections in the water, completely ineffective. Mostly, only during the brief time after Huan Zhen is activated is the efficiency highest."

After fantasizing for a long time, Li Fan, who had returned to reality, sighed with emotion. The scope of the transformation of true and false increased as his knowledge grew. When he first came into contact with the Xuanhuang Realm, Li Fan already felt that he had roughly grasped the threshold of the transformation of true and false. But later, as his vision gradually expanded to the Dark Star Sea, the Primordial Possibility, and even the mortal world of the Mountains and Seas, and the Shore, he realized how laughable his previous feelings were.

"The Mountains and Seas are boundless, and the Shore's transcendence. To what extent must the comprehension of true and false reach in order to overturn it with a single thought?" Li Fan couldn't help but feel a sense of powerlessness. Ultimately, the transformation of true and false was based on the cognition of the foundation of things. Li Fan, as a True Immortal, could create and destroy the Xuanhuang Realm with a single thought. In his eyes, everything in the Xuanhuang Realm could naturally be achieved by "true and false, all depends on the heart." But the Mountains and Seas, and the Shore, had already surpassed his cognitive scope.

"The road ahead is indeed there, but the road ahead is dim." Li Fan didn't know what to do next for a while. Huan Zhen's prompt reappeared. Li Fan looked at the two options in front of him, and his myriad chaotic thoughts slowly subsided.

"An inaccurate simulation is not only unhelpful, but also a poison that kills people. If I misjudge the strength of the Saints, and rush into the Shore, I will truly fall into a situation where there is no possibility of turning back."

"Undoubtedly, before finding energy of the same grade as the Mountains and Seas, I will not choose this again." Understanding this, Li Fan canceled the idea of activating Huan Zhen with a single thought. Then he tried to ask Huan Zhen for advice, hoping that it would point him in the right direction.

Huan Zhen remained silent. However, Li Fan knew that Huan Zhen could definitely sense his thoughts and did not give up, but relentlessly continued to ask. And explained his difficulties.

"The strength of the Saints is truly terrifying. Even with your help, it is still quite difficult for me to contend with the Saints!"

"Or, I could just stay in Xuanhuang Realm, within the high walls, and be a local emperor. I will not leave Primordial from now on, and quietly wait for them to complete the saving of the Mountains and Seas."

"Since you are here, I can wait safely forever."

Huan Zhen remained silent.

"At the very least, you should tell me what you want."

"Saving the Mountains and Seas? Or restoring your own strength?"

"With the Saints ahead, without more help, I really can't do it." Li Fan shrugged, saying nonchalantly.

Outside the door, his aunt, who saw Li Fan talking to himself through the crack in the door, looked worried and hurried to find the village witch. Li Fan could naturally sense this, but he didn't care and continued to confront Huan Zhen.

If it were in the past, even if Huan Zhen didn't respond, he would just assume that Huan Zhen couldn't hear him. But after Huan Zhen maliciously initiated the simulation, Li Fan was now certain that Huan Zhen was much more "rational" than he had imagined. Moreover, with his current divine sense intensity, there was no situation where he could not withstand Huan Zhen's contemplation. Therefore, he had to stubbornly seek further communication with Huan Zhen, and must get an answer! It was both to get an explanation for the suffering he had experienced in the previous simulation, and to extract more help from Huan Zhen.

Li Fan secretly glanced at the completely clean Huan Zhen panel. The two divine skills, [Illusion of True and False] and [From the Heart Transformation], were clearly listed. They did not disappear even after the tribulation of the merging of the Three Daos. Even [From the Heart Transformation] was awakened during the simulation. This was enough to show that they existed solely because of Huan Zhen's existence.

"Since this is the case, Huan Zhen can definitely provide more support."

"The Infinite Sea has a vague similarity to Huan Zhen, and its subtle connection with the [Star] isolated in the Mountains and Seas..."

"There are too many secrets that are hidden." Li Fan snorted coldly and lay back on the bed. He stopped moving. Even when his aunt came back with the witch to feed him rune water, he did not refuse. He drank it clean and neat. Since then, except for necessities, he basically never left the house. He just slept all day. His aunt was kind-hearted and only needed Li Fan to stay alive, so she didn't say much, serving him meals daily.

Twenty-three years later, his aunt finally passed away due to daily overwork. Li Fan was too lazy to prepare his own food and shouted, "Huan Zhen!" Instantly, he returned to the anchor point of 1 year.

"Let's continue." Li Fan snorted coldly and declared. In his heart, he was slowly savoring the subtlety of Huan Zhen's activation just now.

"Either you actively tell me more."

"Or I'll wait until I fully comprehend the transformation of true and false. It might be slow, but eventually, I will completely absorb you."

Huan Zhen remained silent, and Li Fan couldn't be bothered to say more. He simply continued to live a life of reclusion, waiting for twenty-three years to pass. Another twenty-three years later, his aunt passed away.

"Huan Zhen!" Li Fan activated Huan Zhen again.

"Huan Zhen!"

"Huan Zhen!"

"Huan Zhen!"

...

Twenty-three years as a mortal was only an instant for Li Fan. Like the hundred lifetimes of foundation building in the past, Li Fan repeatedly performed retrospection. Besides using it to comprehend the transformation of true and false, he also wanted to wear down Huan Zhen's temper. Because Li Fan was certain that Huan Zhen attached to him must have a corresponding purpose. And his current passive behavior was definitely contrary to Huan Zhen's purpose.

"If you're not in a hurry, I'm even less so."

"If you have the ability, find someone else!" Li Fan contentedly finished the meal his aunt had made and said this inexplicably at the dinner table. His aunt was already accustomed to Li Fan's muttering and pretended not to hear, just silently clearing the dishes.

Huan Zhen also remained silent. Li Fan simply stopped asking and waited for twenty-three years to pass before immediately performing retrospection and starting the next round. Tens of millions of times, repeating the monotonous life again and again. At first, Li Fan felt a little bored. But later, he slowly got used to it. Twenty-three years to decipher the transformation of true and false. Activate retrospection, and then repeat the cycle. Besides this, his life had no other content.

Everything in Xuanhuang Realm, the people and things within the high walls, the secrets of Primordial, and even the Shore of the Mountains and Seas. All of this was put aside by Li Fan. He no longer inquired.

"Does the survival of the Mountains and Seas have anything to do with me?" Adhering to this philosophy, Li Fan spent one lifetime after another in his small hut. After an unknown period, when he activated retrospection again. Something slightly different happened. Among the three options saved, the third one, which he had never chosen, the line of characters that designated a close relative to inherit his memories, was flashing with light. It seemed to be reminding Li Fan to choose it.

"Hmm?" Li Fan narrowed his eyes. Based on his personality, he would never have chosen this option. However, now, it seemed that Huan Zhen had compromised and made a change on its own. Therefore, he might as well try. Li Fan thought so and chose the only suitable candidate. His aunt, Bai Wuyue, who had taken care of him for countless twenty-three-year cycles.

A moment later... As if having a nightmare, his aunt woke up in a cold sweat, looking at her body and the familiar yet unfamiliar environment with disbelief. And Li Fan, with a look of joy. "It can actually be like this!"

Chapter 1613: Self-Harm to Create Saints

"The simulation results of a close relative in this simulation..."

"And this memory can be inherited by this person."

Li Fan repeatedly pondered the description of the third option and showed a look of "I see."

"The information on Huan Zhen's panel, such as my previous bound items and divine abilities, are not arranged randomly. Instead, they are arranged in a specific order. For example, the order of binding, or the difference in strength."

"Following this logic..." Li Fan looked at the three options again.

"The first choice is items, the second is cultivation. Inheriting memories is the third."

"If it were me, with the divine ability of true and false transformation, the difficulty of replicating cultivation would be more challenging than that of items."

"This difference in difficulty does not change regardless of the preciousness of the item or the height of the cultivation realm, but rather because of their fundamental differences. Items are, after all, just items. While cultivation is more mysterious, involving the power of the Infinite Sea and the Upper Mountain."

"And the third option, inheriting memories..."

"Its difficulty, or value, is even higher than inheriting cultivation!"

"In fact, this option being on par with inheriting items and cultivation is already very telling."

"I actually ignored it all along."

In the previous life, all of his aunt's memories appeared in Li Fan's mind, from the initial anchor point to her final demise. All the thoughts and memories during this period were fully grasped by Li Fan, without any omission. From another perspective, it was almost as if Li Fan had personally experienced the entire simulation process as his "aunt." His aunt had no secrets from Li Fan.

And from a swapped perspective, his aunt's genuine, lifelong love and concern for "Li Fan," which even persisted until her death, caused ripples in Li Fan's extremely indifferent heart, which had become numb from countless retrospections.

However, these ripples only lasted for a moment and soon dissipated. An eternity of ice could not be melted by a fleeting candle flame. Li Fan still suppressed these unnecessary emotions and focused on the key change brought about by the third option.

Since Li Fan chose to have his aunt inherit the memories of the previous life, Li Fan could now clearly sense the subtle changes occurring in his aunt after the indirect "retrospection."

Before this, his aunt was just a mortal. Moreover, her cultivation talent was extremely low, and even reaching the Qi Refining stage was difficult for her in her lifetime.

But now... She could barely officially begin cultivating!

It was as if the aunt in the previous life and the aunt in this life had overlapped.

"Spiritual enhancement! The carrier of simulated memories is actually spirituality!"

Li Fan's eyes gleamed, and in an instant, he understood the core of the matter: "Spirituality cannot be generated out of thin air. Even retrospection cannot create something from nothing. Therefore, in essence, this extra spirituality is provided by me. Just like the activation of retrospection consumes my Infinite Spirit."

Even though it was his own choice, Li Fan still felt a little uncomfortable after realizing this. After all, sacrificing himself for others was something he had never done before.

"But perhaps this is the key to breaking the predicament!"

Thinking this, Li Fan could only endure it forcefully.

With the memories of the previous life, the reborn aunt spent more than half a day before finally calming down completely. She quietly walked outside Li Fan's room and, through the crack in the door, looked at the side profile of Li Fan who was still sleeping peacefully on the bed.

A look of excitement and tears flashed in her aunt's eyes.

After gazing for a long time, she finally made up her mind.

"This life, I can't let Brother Fan suffer with me anymore."

"At the very least, I can let him eat more fish and meat."

With Li Fan's current strength, it was not difficult to clearly sense the thoughts of others.

Li Fan seemed to see his kind-hearted aunt, in one reincarnation after another, gradually improving her understanding of the world bit by bit, and finally coming into contact with the secrets of immortal cultivation.

"However, Auntie is limited in her knowledge and doesn't have my strong drive for cultivation. I still need to help her!"

Li Fan smiled slightly, revealing a profound smile.

With the memories of the previous life, his aunt cleverly escaped the covetousness of the village chief's younger brother over the ancestral land, successfully protecting her family's property. Every time at a critical moment, she helped the villagers solve disasters. Moreover, she secretly joined forces with the witch, using the concept of ghosts and gods to predict a great drought in Jiangnan four years later, successfully helping the villagers survive the disaster and thus establishing her authoritative position among the villagers.

Later, she led the villagers through one natural disaster after another, her reputation spreading far and wide, even alarming the authorities. Even the county magistrate humbled himself to visit, asking about ghosts and gods instead of the common people's affairs. After a few pointers from his aunt, the county magistrate achieved remarkable political achievements and was promoted to prefectural magistrate a few years later.

In return, he reported the aunt's virtuous reputation to the higher authorities. Because of this, his aunt was granted the title of Lady of the Imperial Command, completing the leap from commoner to official. From then on, she lived a life of no worries about food and clothing, and just as his aunt was about to fulfill her wish, at this critical juncture, Li Fan suddenly fell ill for some unknown reason. His aunt invited many famous doctors to treat Li Fan, but Li Fan's condition continued to worsen day by day, his body becoming thinner and thinner, and finally died of illness. The white-haired elder burying the black-haired youth, his aunt was heartbroken and turned white-haired overnight. Two years later, his aunt also passed away due to grief. The people of the prefecture mourned together, and every household enshrined a memorial tablet for his aunt, revering her as the "Mother Spirit Who Protects the World."

...

"Huan Zhen!"

A soft chant echoed in the darkness.

Mirror flowers and water moon, broken and reappeared.

His aunt woke up from her nightmare again. However, this time, a look of greater confusion and doubt flashed in her eyes.

Li Fan was also impacted by his aunt's memories. The ripples in his calm heart became even more frequent. Having fully inherited his aunt's memories and lived a lifetime from her perspective, Li Fan deeply felt the pain of an elder burying a younger one. This was one of the most intense emotions in life, like a giant stone thrown into a calm lake, splashing ripples.

Even though Li Fan quickly suppressed this emotion, he still slightly frowned.

When simulated, he could naturally manipulate everything from behind the scenes as an observer. But when the memories of a participant became something he had to experience, the situation became somewhat different.

"Is doing this..." The thought had just surfaced when it was extinguished invisibly.

"Without experiencing all kinds of pain, how can one achieve the steadfastness of seeking the Dao?"

Li Fan looked at his aunt, who was slowly recovering, his expression turning cold again.

"Let me see the changes in your spirituality in this life."

"As expected, it has increased a bit more. The cultivation limit can barely touch the threshold of the Foundation Establishment stage."

Li Fan nodded slightly.

"This is only the third inheritance superposition. It can be imagined that if it goes through more cycles..."

"It is not impossible to create an transcendent expert by my own hand!"

"Moreover, advancing further to the Saint realm..."

"Through them, to probe the reality of the Saints on the Shore. This is the way to break the predicament!"

"I'm not afraid of losing control. I just need to hide and wait until everything is settled, then activate retrospection, and I can obtain their memories..."

Hope was within reach, and Li Fan's mood greatly improved. However, after a moment, he frowned.

"But there are also many issues that need attention. The Saint Creation Plan, like alchemy, cannot be stopped midway until the trial is successful. Otherwise, all efforts will be in vain. How can I ensure that the target will always be under my control during repeated reincarnations? As the target gets stronger and stronger, how can I ensure that I won't be discovered by them?"

"Once discovered by the target, even if I can perform retrospection with a single thought. The efforts of the past will be instantly annihilated. Even I would be heartbroken."

"Therefore, before formally launching the plan, I probably need to restore my transcendent realm strength first. To have the qualifications of a behind-the-scenes manipulator."

"Furthermore..." Li Fan swept his divine sense over his body.

"The Saint Creation Plan, the continuous superposition and enhancement of the target's spirituality, comes at the cost of reducing my Infinite Spirit. Although I have Infinite Spirit, but..."

"The Mountains and Seas are also named infinite, but they were still devoured by Dao Annihilation. Sometimes, infinite is not infinite. This is what I need to pay close attention to. If the cost is too high, I may need to change my methods."

"And..." Thinking of this last point, Li Fan's expression also changed subtly. He even felt a trace of fear in his heart. The fear was even greater than the potential loss of his Infinite Spirit.

"The target reincarnates and becomes a Saint, but at the same time, I have to bear the impact of their memories."

"..."

Although he was unwilling to admit it, Li Fan also realized deep down that after completely accepting the memories of the participant, he could no longer completely regard the other party as a mere NPC. They had become real, living "people" with distinct images. Although he did not yet know what specific impact this would have on him. But the unknown was precisely what Li Fan feared most.

"No matter what, the plan must continue."

"After all, this is the only path to breaking the predicament that Huan Zhen has personally designated, and that I have found."

"The Saints on the Shore..." Li Fan's expression became indifferent again, and his gaze drifted beyond Primordial Possibility towards the Shore.

This time, Li Fan interrupted the Saint Creation Plan targeting his aunt. Instead, he began to restore his strength. As before, he created the Profound Yellow Immortal Ship, broke out of Primordial Possibility. After finding the transcendent true intents like the Lone Sail and Tribulation-Calming Steadfastness, he hid in the Mountains and Seas, no longer heading towards the Shore.

After a long period of time had passed, and he had almost completely comprehended the essence of these two transcendent true intents. His strength had almost reached the peak achievable by a transcendent expert who had not entered the Shore and was roaming the Mountains and Seas.

With a single thought of retrospection, he returned to the anchor point of 1 year. Li Fan chose to preserve his cultivation. Then, a new anchor point fell into place!

"This will be the starting point of my Saint Creation Plan from now on."

The descent of a transcendent expert was like stirring up great waves in Primordial. But all the turmoil was contained within half a foot of Li Fan by himself. It was imperceptible to others.

Li Fan's gaze was deep, looking at his aunt.

"Let's continue now."

"Bai Wuyue."

Bai Wuyue was naturally Li Fan's aunt's name. It was given by a scholar in the village, unlike ordinary women's names. At this moment, after Li Fan's soft call, Bai Wuyue began her retrospective reincarnation experience again. Just like before.

Saint Creation Plan - First Life: Li Fan stayed at home for twenty-three years, and Bai Wuyue died of exhaustion.

Saint Creation Plan - First Life: Reborn Bai Wuyue went through hardships, protecting Li Fan from starvation and cold. However, in the end, she buried a black-haired youth with white hair and died in grief.

Saint Creation Plan - Third Life!

Bai Wuyue, who had regained consciousness, still looked at Li Fan, who was sleeping soundly on the bed, through the crack in the door. A trace of tenderness flashed in her eyes.

"Brother Fan, Auntie will definitely find a way to cure you."

The naive Bai Wuyue naively believed that the heavens gave her one reincarnation after another to save her pitiful nephew. Therefore, she was extremely determined in her heart.

In the next few years, Bai Wuyue, while growing her influence according to the memories of her previous life, also studied medical books in secret, trying to find a way to cure Li Fan's "strange illness." In the previous life, she had consulted many famous doctors but found no cure for Li Fan. This life, she decided to find a solution herself.

"Even if Brother Fan dies, I can't die. I will dedicate my life to studying medicine. After all, I don't know how many such reincarnations can be repeated."

Although this life had just begun, Bai Wuyue already felt a sense of urgency in her heart. In her previous life, Bai Wuyue leaped from commoner to official and deeply understood the difference in resources between commoners and officials. Even trying to find and read medical books as a mere commoner was not easy. Therefore, in this life, in order to maximize her "official power," she set her sights on the future emperor. Although she was a woman, Bai Wuyue also knew the principle that merit for assisting the emperor was the greatest. First, she created immense influence in the prefecture under the guise of "communicating with gods and spirits." Then, in the fifth year, amidst the impact of refugees, she saved the family of the King of Langya.

Chapter 1614: Bai Shuyue's Cultivation Journey

Bai Wuyue truly had some talent for pretending to be a deity. After successfully "predicting" the natural disasters that would occur in the next few years, her status in the royal mansion grew daily. Coupled with Bai Wuyue's almost complete detachment from worldly affairs, spending all her time with books, she only offered pointers at critical moments. This behavior made the King of Langya trust her even more. More importantly, such a mysterious figure actually had a fatal weakness. That was her sickly nephew, who was always bedridden. The King of Langya saw the importance Bai Wuyue placed on Li Fan. With the power of the royal mansion, let alone one Li Fan, even a hundred or a thousand Li Fans could be supported for a lifetime! Thus, a special garden was built to house Li Fan. One day, the King of Langya was discussing Bai Wuyue's future. Bai Wuyue, hidden behind a veil, slowly replied amidst flowing mist and clouds: "Your Highness is destined for supreme greatness. You only need to wait for the opportune time when the hidden dragon emerges from the abyss. You need not do anything else." "The more you do, the more mistakes you make." The King of Langya pondered for a long time, cupped his fists, and retreated.

Three years later, an imperial decree came from the capital. The Emperor had actually passed on the throne to the King of Langya, who had always been low-key, shortly before his death! Various forces stirred. And the King of Langya, who had received Bai Wuyue's reminder, was already prepared for this. While everyone was still searching for him in Langya Prefecture, Jiangnan, he had already appeared in the palace with three hundred elite soldiers. With lightning speed, before any forces could react, he successfully inherited the throne! He changed the reign title to Xuanjing. The world praised Emperor Xuanjing for his decisive actions, which resolved the internal crisis without bloodshed. Only a few people knew that the mysterious woman in the King's mansion, and now in the palace, was the greatest contributor to all this!

"Despite inheriting the throne, the world is not yet stable. Hidden dangers abound, and we must guard against them." Bai Wuyue handed a note to Emperor Xuanjing. Emperor Xuanjing, following the list on the note, secretly investigated and indeed discovered signs of rebels plotting to usurp the throne. Thus, before they could make a move, he wielded his butcher's knife, crushing all threats in their cradle. Emperor Xuanjing's bloody methods completely shocked the court. And the existence of Bai Wuyue, who was said to have the power of ghosts and gods, finally became known to all the officials. Hiding all their scheming thoughts, the court became temporarily stable.

On Bai Wuyue's side, she could finally focus all her attention on studying how to solve Li Fan's strange illness. Just like in the previous life, Li Fan's strange illness had struck on time. Even though she was prepared and had read countless medical books, Bai Wuyue could not find a way to cure her nephew. Even alleviating it was impossible; she could only watch Li Fan grow thinner day by day. Emperor Xuanjing heard of this and summoned imperial physicians to treat Li Fan together. However, all were helpless. Just like in the previous life, Bai Wuyue watched Li Fan die with her own eyes. Only this time, Bai Wuyue had slowly gotten used to it. She no longer turned white-haired overnight, but silently prepared Li Fan's burial.

After losing her nephew, Bai Wuyue had no more attachments to the world. She devoted herself entirely to the study of medicine. Even when Emperor Xuanjing repeatedly summoned her for matters of ghosts and gods, Bai Wuyue only demurred. Even when the increasingly enraged Emperor Xuanjing threatened her life, she calmly refused. Emperor Xuanjing was extremely frustrated, but ultimately did not harm Bai Wuyue's life. He simply ordered people to completely seal off Bai Wuyue's palace, forbidding any outsiders from entering. As long as there were medical books, Bai Wuyue didn't mind.

The palace gates were closed for thirty years. Thirty years later, as Bai Wuyue was approaching the end of her life, the long-sealed wooden door opened again. Emperor Xuanjing, with white hair all over his head, slowly came before Bai Wuyue. After dismissing all the servants, Emperor Xuanjing looked at the dying Bai Wuyue. The request he originally wanted to make, the method to extend life, could no longer be spoken. "You understand matters of ghosts and gods, yet you have met the same fate." Emperor Xuanjing said with a bitter smile. Bai Wuyue remained silent. "Have you found a way to treat the illness?" After a long silence, Emperor Xuanjing looked at the countless medical books piled up around them, but asked neatly. "Mortal methods may be difficult to treat his illness." Bai Wuyue finally spoke, her voice somewhat hoarse. Emperor Xuanjing stared at Bai Wuyue with hope, awaiting her next words. "But how can mortal know about immortal secret arts?" Bai Wuyue said with some dejection. Emperor Xuanjing was stunned. He let out a few bitter laughs, waved his hand, and turned to leave. This time, the palace gates were not sealed again. However, Bai Wuyue had no intention of leaving. Feeling that she was nearing the end of her life, Bai Wuyue's heart was completely calm. She lay quietly on the bed and lost consciousness.

"Huan Zhen!"

The fourth generation of the Saint Creation Plan. This time, Bai Wuyue no longer confined herself to ordinary medical practices. Instead, she set her sights on various folk remedies and mysterious witchcraft. Since ordinary methods could not cure Li Fan, Bai Wuyue decided to take a different approach. "Brother Fan, be good. Listen to Auntie and drink this bowl of medicine." Bai Wuyue held a bowl of black, foul-smelling "medicine" and handed it to Li Fan. Li Fan pinched his nose and drank it. Half a day later, his face turned purplish-black, and he bled from all seven orifices and died. Bai Wuyue stared blankly at Li Fan's corpse, a hint of annoyance flashing in her eyes.

"Huan Zhen!" "The progress is too slow. In the end, she is just a mortal. It seems I need to find a way to speed things up."

The fifth generation of the Saint Creation Plan! This time, Bai Wuyue adopted a multi-pronged approach, drawing on the strengths of various families, and developed a method that could successfully extend Li Fan's life. She used the King of Langya's power to collect numerous young and strong individuals. Their vital blood was extracted and infused into the ailing Li Fan. This vital blood from the strong individuals was carefully selected by Bai Wuyue, ensuring it would not clash with Li Fan's fate. With nourishment, Li Fan's complexion indeed improved. This was a historic breakthrough! Bai Wuyue was overjoyed. However, to extend Li Fan's life, a large amount of vital blood from the young and strong was needed for sustenance. Although the King of Langya's power could easily provide for a few strong individuals, extracting vital blood from people to treat an illness was a shocking act. Furthermore, for some reason, the news leaked out, becoming widely known. The common people were in an uproar, and the officials were indignant, and the Emperor was furious. Under pressure, the King of Langya had no choice but to hand over Bai Wuyue to take the blame. Fortunately, Bai Wuyue was vigilant and had long placed spies throughout the royal mansion. Receiving the news in advance, she hurriedly fled with Li Fan. Although they were not caught, they had become notorious "demons" in Great Xuan, and could only hide in the deep mountains and old forests.

With Bai Wuyue's medical knowledge accumulated over several lifetimes, totaling hundreds of years, the two would not starve to death. However, in the harsh environment of the mountains and forests, and without vital blood to sustain Li Fan's life, Li Fan's originally relatively healthy body slowly deteriorated. "It seems that next time, I must learn from this lesson. I need to establish my own power and not place all my hopes on others." After giving Li Fan a dose of medicine, Bai Wuyue looked at her nephew, who was gradually falling asleep, and thought to herself.

Bai Wuyue no longer expected Li Fan to last much longer, so she gave up the idea of treating him. She simply took Li Fan with her to travel the mountains and rivers, living a life completely different from before. Just when she thought Li Fan would soon die, and she would begin her next reincarnation. One day, they accidentally discovered a cave. "Auntie, I feel better when I stay here." Li Fan's words greatly surprised Bai Wuyue. This had never happened in previous reincarnations. She immediately began to carefully examine the cave. It seemed to have been someone's dwelling, but there were not many items left behind. Only half a stone emitting a strange aura and a jade slip.

Bai Wuyue, who considered herself knowledgeable, was confused by these two items. Although she didn't know what the stone and jade slip were, they would definitely help with her nephew's illness. As if seeing hope, Bai Wuyue decided to live in this cave. She tried to decipher the secrets of the jade slip and stone. Unfortunately, even until Li Fan's death, she gained nothing. After cremating Li Fan's remains and carrying them with her, Bai Wuyue solemnly put away these two items and traveled the world, seeking someone who might know their secrets. However, she found nothing. Just as Bai Wuyue was nearing the end of her life in this lifetime, a sensational rumor reached her ears. Immortals descended from the east, bringing heavenly punishment, and the capital of Xuanjing turned into ruins. Countless deaths and injuries!

Bai Wuyue was shocked, as this had never happened in her long reincarnations. "How could this be?" Bai Wuyue was first confused, and then she suddenly realized. "My lifespan this time, for some reason, is much longer than in the past?" "This year is..." "Fifty years later?" "I lived so long without realizing it?" Bai Wuyue was astonished, and then quickly took out the strange item she carried with her. The jade slip remained unchanged. However, the jade stone... seemed to have shrunk compared to when she first discovered it. Bai Wuyue's heart suddenly had a guess. From then on, she began to move towards Xuanjing City, trying to gather more information about the immortals, while also trying to further "absorb" the jade stone. It was a pity that before she could return to the capital, her lifespan had run out.

"Huan Zhen!"

The sixth generation of the Saint Creation Plan! This time, Bai Wuyue was no longer bewildered and had a goal. Before her nephew fell ill, she went to the deep forest and retrieved the jade slip and the jade stone. She gave the jade stone to Li Fan to wear close to his body. She herself continued to study the jade slip. "If I guessed correctly, these two items might be from immortals." Bai Wuyue pondered while playing with the jade slip in her hand. "Perhaps we can only learn more from the two immortals who descended fifty years later." Suddenly, Bai Wuyue's expression flickered slightly. For some reason, she felt that the jade slip in her hand seemed somewhat different compared to the previous life. But she couldn't tell exactly how it was different. But Bai Wuyue was certain that this was not her imagination!
