With the jade stone to extend her life early, Li Fan lived longer in this life than in any previous life. Bai Wuyue was very pleased. However, Li Fan did not live to see the arrival of the immortals and died of illness. Bai Wuyue then began to study the stone, which was now only a small piece. "It seems there is some kind of mysterious energy within it." Bai Wuyue closed her eyes. She could feel that the unique substance contained within the stone, she seemed to be able...

to activate it? After hundreds of attempts, Bai Wuyue actually succeeded in absorbing the spiritual energy from the spirit stone into her body. In an instant, Bai Wuyue's appearance rapidly aged. Her remaining lifespan was instantly burned away. Bai Wuyue died in shock.

"Huan Zhen!" "Still too slow!" "But I can't be too hasty. The path to creating Saints requires ten thousand reincarnations, and there can be no flaws." "Otherwise, all efforts will be in vain just before dawn!" Li Fan's voice echoed in the darkness.

The seventh generation! Because of the terrifying encounter at the end of the previous life, Bai Wuyue had developed a fear of immortal items in this life. But to save Li Fan's life, she still chose to continue her research. She temporarily gave up on touching the spirit stone. Instead, she used the method of activating the spiritual energy in the spirit stone from the previous life to activate the jade slip. At this moment, Bai Wuyue endured the fear in her heart and was prepared to age instantly again. But the anticipated disaster did not happen. Instead, a piece of text appeared in Bai Wuyue's mind. "I tried this before, but the jade slip did not react at that time." "It seems my feeling was not wrong." Although she didn't know what the changes in each reincarnation meant, from the current perspective, it seemed to be a good thing.

Bai Wuyue carefully read the contents of the jade slip. Her expression gradually became shocked. "Minor Five Elements cultivation technique?" "What is this..." Bai Wuyue took a deep breath, calmed her emotions, and then continued to read after completely settling down. From Bai Wuyue's perspective of having read countless books, although some of the vocabulary in this cultivation technique was unclear, the overall content was not difficult to understand. "The five elements of spiritual energy in heaven and earth can be absorbed into the body to strengthen the five internal organs..." "In medical books, there is indeed a division of the five elements and attributes of the internal organs, but where does the five elements spiritual energy come from?" Bai Wuyue frowned slightly. "Spiritual energy, spiritual energy..." She thought of the spirit stone again. "According to the cultivation method, spiritual energy is indispensable for cultivation." "But from my previous experience, spiritual energy seems to be a deadly poison to me..." Bai Wuyue was puzzled. In the end, she could only place her hope on the two descending immortals fifty years later.

Time passed quickly. One day, two streaks of light came from the horizon. Thunderous sounds reverberated throughout the world. "Dao Xuanzi! Don't push your luck too far!" ... Bai Wuyue, hiding in a safe place outside Xuanjing City, looked at the two figures in the sky and became inexplicably excited. This was the first time she had truly seen the existence of immortals. However, she did not rush to pay her respects to the immortals, but waited patiently. Bai Wuyue knew that the two immortals would have a fierce battle next, and that would be her chance to appear. "I hope it's useful." Bai Wuyue glanced secretly at the surroundings of Xuanjing City. For fifty years, she had not just been waiting.

Chapter 1615: The Old Woman Seeks Immortality

In every corner of Xuanjing City, Bai Wuyue had buried various poisons collected from her travels across the world. The most important among them was the [Blood Dripping Zither], made primarily from human vital blood. Once triggered by an explosion, it would burst into a mist of blood.

That's right, after fifty years of research, Bai Wuyue had reached an astonishing conclusion: the reason she could never absorb the spiritual energy from the spirit stone was not because the spiritual energy was poisonous. Instead, humans had a strong repulsive reaction to spiritual energy, like a deadly poison. The toxicity was far greater than any other poison in the world. Through a series of experiments, Bai Wuyue had verified this point.

"I just don't know how effective it will be against immortals."

The conversation between the immortals drifted down from the sky. Bai Wuyue silently memorized every word.

"Land of Immortal Termination, Golden Core Method."

"Immortal-Mortal Miasma..."

"It's just seeking a sliver of survival!"

Amidst insane laughter, a fire dragon descended from the sky, engulfing Xuanjing City. Continuous explosions resounded through the heavens. The vast Xuanjing City, like a toy, instantly turned into ruins. Even though she had known in advance what would happen, Bai Wuyue was still trembling with fear at the might displayed by the two immortals with every move.

At the same time, the effect of the [Blood Dripping Zither] was unexpectedly good! Accompanied by blood and flames, a dense blood mist instantly rose into the sky, as if condensing the vengeful souls of hundreds of thousands of innocent citizens of Xuanjing City, soaring upwards! Dao Xuanzi and Kou Hong, caught off guard, were enveloped by large swathes of blood mist, both letting out muffled groans. Bai Wuyue held her breath and observed.

A moment later, two figures, one after the other, rushed out of the blood mist and fled westward!

"Their speed is much slower than before! And..."

"They seem on the verge of collapse!"

Bai Wuyue did not rush to chase. Although severely injured, the speed at which immortals fled was not something a mortal like her could match. However, she had long since set up informants throughout Great Xuan. As long as the immortals were still in Great Xuan, she would definitely find them! These people were all saved by Bai Wuyue during her travels as a physician and were loyal and reliable.

Waiting for half a day, a carrier pigeon arrived from the horizon, bringing news of the immortals' whereabouts. A horse-drawn carriage carried Bai Wuyue, slowly setting off, following the footprints of the immortals.

Three months later.

"Grandma Bai, according to the investigation by my brothers, the two immortals finally disappeared in this mountain forest."

"However, the Black Water Mountain spans hundreds of miles and is sparsely populated. My brothers have tried their best, but still haven't..."

A man in black knelt on one knee, reporting to Bai Wuyue with a look of guilt.

"It's alright." Bai Wuyue gazed at the secluded mountain forest ahead, interrupting the man in black. "Tell them all to come back. From now on, I'll find them myself."

The man in black was slightly stunned, but saw Bai Wuyue walking step by step into the mountain forest. After a moment of hesitation, the man in black ultimately did not choose to follow, because he knew that Grandma Bai always kept her word. Moreover, tracking immortals was indeed a terrifying matter...

With her medical skills reaching the peak of perfection, Bai Wuyue had no problem surviving in the wilderness. More importantly, she could clearly sense the spiritual energy fluctuations left by the two immortals' flight, which clearly indicated the direction in this vast wilderness.

"They haven't been able to get out of this mountain forest for a long time, perhaps they are still healing from serious injuries. Who knows when they will recover..." Bai Wuyue's brows flashed with determination. She swallowed a black pill, and within a few breaths, an unusual redness appeared on her cheeks. This was a method of greatly enhancing her mobility at the cost of consuming her lifespan. Following the direction indicated by the spiritual energy residue, Bai Wuyue moved quickly.

Fifteen days later, three hundred miles deep into Black Water Mountain, in a mountain valley.

"The spiritual energy traces stop here."

"And ahead... there is a spiritual energy fluctuation."

When she was truly about to face immortals, Bai Wuyue couldn't help but feel a surge of apprehension. But in the next moment, she suppressed her hesitation. She slowly approached.

The river flowed gently, and a man sat by the stream, with his eyes closed in meditation, not far from a tomb. Bai Wuyue recognized him at a glance: it was Kou Hong, one of the two immortals. However, he was no longer the middle-aged man he was before. His hair was white, and his face was covered with wrinkles. He looked like an old man on the verge of death!

"Could this be the effect of the Immortal-Mortal Miasma?" Bai Wuyue secretly marveled, while glancing at the tomb beside Kou Hong. "Not only can it injure immortals, but it can also kill them?"

The approach of a mortal naturally could not escape Kou Hong's senses. The moment he opened his eyes, Bai Wuyue felt her body stiffen, unable to move. Fortunately, it seemed that Kou Hong saw that Bai Wuyue was just a simple mortal with no threat, and soon closed his eyes again.

"A mere mortal, why do you pursue me to this place?"

As a healer, Bai Wuyue could hear the weakness in Kou Hong's voice, but he was not someone she, a mere woman, could contend with. After weighing the options, she took out the remaining spirit stone, bowed her head, and said softly, "This old woman's lifelong pursuit is only immortal cultivation and longevity. However, after searching the world, I have found no true immortal methods. A few days ago, I was shocked to hear of two immortals appearing in Xuanjing..."

Kou Hong was not interested in Bai Wuyue's words, but kept his eyes fixed on the spirit stone in her hand. He levitated it and, with a flash of surprise in his eyes, said, "Top-grade spirit stone?" After playing with it for a while, he showed a look of joy. "Although only a little residue remains, it is enough for me to barely recover my injuries." Looking at Bai Wuyue, he asked, "Where did you find this spirit stone?" It seemed he had already believed Bai Wuyue's words.

"Replying to the Immortal Master, this stone was found by this old woman in a mountain tomb." Bai Wuyue answered truthfully.

"Besides this spirit stone, are there any other things?" Kou Hong quickly asked.

"Uh..." Bai Wuyue pretended to recall. After a long while, she replied, "It seems there are no other special items. Oh, right, there is also a jade slip. But there are no words engraved on it, and it does not have the strange aura of this stone."

Kou Hong was overjoyed. "Where is that jade slip?" Anyone who could possess a top-grade spirit stone would surely carry a jade slip that was no less extraordinary.

"Indeed, after surviving a great disaster, one must receive blessings! Although I was severely injured by the Immortal-Mortal Miasma in this battle, as long as I can break through the Golden Core stage, I can extend my lifespan by hundreds of years!" At this moment, he stopped meditating, flashed beside Bai Wuyue, and said in a deep voice, "Point the way!"

Riding the wind and waves, flying across the nine heavens. Kou Hong took Bai Wuyue and flew across the sky.

"Your aptitude..."

"Is actually quite good." On the way, Kou Hong examined Bai Wuyue's body and said with some surprise.

"Unfortunately, you are too old, and the Immortal-Mortal Miasma is deeply entangling you. There is no hope for the Dao path." Bai Wuyue showed a look of disappointment.

"But don't worry, thanks to this jade stone and jade slip, I will bestow upon you a method. Although you cannot cultivate, you can extend your lifespan without question." Kou Hong said.

"Thank you for your immortal master's compassion!" Bai Wuyue was filled with gratitude.

Thousands of miles away, it took only half a day to arrive!

"My home is right below!" The appearance of an immortal caused the common people below to panic, and they all knelt on the ground. Kou Hong took Bai Wuyue and landed in a courtyard. His divine sense scanned and quickly locked onto the location where the jade slip was stored. He strode in and quickly examined the contents: "Minor Five Elements Art?" "It actually leads directly to Dao Integration?" Kou Hong exclaimed in shock.

"Immortal Master, this old woman has a nephew..." Seeing the extraordinary nature of the jade slip she presented, Bai Wuyue seized the opportunity to ask. Having obtained the Dao Integration method by chance, Kou Hong was in a great mood. After pondering for a moment, he said, "Show me."

Bai Wuyue was overjoyed and led Kou Hong to Li Fan's bedside. Kou Hong took a look: "Hmm?" He frowned deeply.

"Immortal Master, do you have any clues?" Bai Wuyue asked hopefully.

"Uh... this..." Kou Hong hesitated. Bai Wuyue naturally saw Kou Hong's meaning and found it difficult to accept: "My nephew's strange illness, even an immortal master like you cannot cure it?"

Kou Hong coughed lightly. "It's not that it cannot be cured, but rather that its origin is unknown. If I were to inject my spiritual energy, his illness would naturally be cured. However, mortals all have the Immortal-Mortal Miasma in their bodies. Before removing the miasma, injecting spiritual energy would actually harm him."

"I implore the Immortal Master to bestow the method for removing the miasma..." Bai Wuyue knelt and begged. The [Five Spirits Qi Attraction Method] was not a secret, and Kou Hong naturally had no reason to refuse.

"However, being in this Land of Immortal Termination, even if one can remove the miasma from their body, they cannot embark on the path of cultivation without the support of spiritual energy." Kou Hong warned.

"I only wish to save my nephew's life." Bai Wuyue, having obtained the method, thanked him profusely.

"Immortal Master's grace of rebirth is unforgettable. Please stay at this old woman's home for a few more days..." Kou Hong hesitated for a moment, considering that his injuries had not fully recovered, and finally agreed. He still had enough spirit stone reserves and spent his days researching the [Minor Five Elements Art].

"What a shame. If I had known there was a Dao Integration technique here earlier, I wouldn't have fought so desperately with Dao Xuanzi."

"However, now that I have the Dao Integration technique, I can consider selling the [Thousand Mechanisms Jade Harmony Golden Chapter]. I might have hope of reaching the Nascent Soul stage..."

Just as Kou Hong was immersed in pleasant fantasies about the future. He did not know that Bai Wuyue had already quietly shed all the miasma from her body.

"It seems it's not as difficult as he said." Bai Wuyue felt that her cultivation speed was much faster than she had expected. In just three months, relying solely on the spirit stone left by Kou Hong, she had already cultivated to the peak of Qi Refining.

"However, to advance further, I need celestial treasures."

"Not something that can be found in the Immortal-Absolute Land of Great Xuan." Bai Wuyue traveled east to the edge of the Abyss. Without hesitation, she leaped down. Qi Refining peak could not break through the Immortal-Absolute Array for the first time. Bai Wuyue's will vanished into the Abyss.

"I should thank you all, Kou Hong and Dao Xuanzi."

"Huan Zhen!" Li Fan's voice echoed faintly. Saint Creation Plan - Eighth Generation!

After Li Fan's revival, Bai Wuyue first retrieved the top-grade spirit stone and jade slip. Then she cultivated at lightning speed to the peak of Qi Refining.

"It's not my imagination."

"This time, cultivation has become much easier." Bai Wuyue was stunned into speechlessness.

Chapter 1616: The Terror of Accumulated Spirituality

"Every rebirth increases my cultivation talent. If I go through countless cycles of reincarnation, won't I achieve longevity?" Bai Wuyue had never imagined that she would one day reach the realm of [Longevity].

From beginning to end, she only wanted to save her pitiful nephew's life.

A Qi Refining stage cultivator is an "Ascended Immortal" to mortals!

With a few minor tricks, Bai Wuyue intimidated the entire village. Li Fan found a stable place. Although Bai Wuyue was reluctant to part with him, she embarked on the path to explore the Immortal Absolute Array alone.

This time, with the experience of breaking the array from her previous life, Bai Wuyue successfully passed through the outermost gale layer of the array, saw through the illusion of flowing light, crossed the upside-down layer, and carefully avoided the fiery layer, ultimately perishing in the profound ice layer.

Ninth life!

"According to Kou Hong, after the profound ice, there are thunderstorms and darkness."

"Soon, it's even easier than I imagined." Bai Wuyue was exhilarated.

Perhaps it was because her cultivation talent had accumulated to a considerable level through continuous rebirth and reincarnation. The Immortal Absolute Array, which Kou Hong described as extremely dangerous, did not seem so difficult to break through?

She didn't even understand formations, yet she successfully passed through more than half of the array relying solely on intuition.

Bai Wuyue stood at the edge of the Abyss again, but this time she didn't rush to break the array. Instead, she observed from a distance.

Although she had no master to guide her, after watching for a long time, Bai Wuyue truly saw some tricks!

"So this is what a formation is." Bai Wuyue mused, then leaped down.

She traversed like a stream of light, breaking through obstacles with unstoppable force.

She reached the darkest layer at the very bottom of the Immortal Absolute Array!

In a daze, Bai Wuyue sensed that many terrifying unknown creatures were hidden in the boundless darkness around her. But they seemed to have no malice towards her.

After pausing for a moment, she hesitated no longer.

She flew towards the light spot below.

When she felt the extremely abundant spiritual energy around her, Bai Wuyue knew that she had finally arrived in the cultivation world!

Not letting herself be overwhelmed by temporary success, Bai Wuyue followed her previous plan, found the cultivators of the Myriad Immortals Alliance stationed on the nearest island, and applied to join the Myriad Immortals Alliance.

She did not conceal her background from the mortal world, only saying that she had been guided by an immortal master from the outside world and had been gifted with spirit stones, which allowed her to embark on the immortal path.

He Zhenghao smiled and welcomed Bai Wuyue to Myriad Immortals Island: "Although you are a bit old, it's not too late. If you work hard, you still have hope of successfully reaching the Foundation Establishment stage. Once you reach Foundation Establishment, the heavens and earth will be vastly different."

"I know it's not easy for you to be alone. Here are five hundred contribution points. Please accept them. They will help you get started, and you can return them when you have a surplus later."

For a Qi Refining cultivator just arriving, five hundred contribution points were not few, and it could save a lot of trouble. Bai Wuyue quickly thanked him.

After that, Bai Wuyue settled down on Myriad Immortals Island, aiming to break through to the Foundation Establishment stage.

"Kou Hong said that at the very least, one needs to reach the Golden Core stage to pass through the Immortal Absolute Array. I think late-stage Foundation Establishment should be enough."

Her realm and comprehension both met the requirements for a breakthrough. The only thing she lacked was the rare item needed for Foundation Establishment.

Bai Wuyue diligently accumulated contribution points while paying attention to news of cultivators discovering Foundation Establishment rare items in the wild.

"Foundation Establishment rare items often require four to five thousand contribution points to exchange. If each one requires saving for several years, it's too time-consuming. It's best to find them in the wild."

Three years later, Bai Wuyue, who had been training almost non-stop, finally exchanged for a [Life Lotus] in the Heavenly Profound Mirror.

She successfully advanced to the Foundation Establishment realm!

He Zhenghao immediately sent his congratulations. After a brief reply, Bai Wuyue continued to cultivate non-stop.

As it turned out, the various breakthrough materials required by the new method were the biggest limitation for Bai Wuyue.

In seven days, she broke through to the mid-stage Foundation Establishment.

In ten days, she broke through to the late stage.

In just one month, Bai Wuyue had already reached the peak of Foundation Establishment!

"If I could cultivate this fast all the time, it would be great."

"This Heavenly Venerable who transmits the law doesn't seem like a good person. He created a path and then insisted that everyone in the world walk his path..." Bai Wuyue muttered to herself inwardly.

"It's time to go back. I wonder how my nephew has been all these years."

Bai Wuyue used her remaining contribution points to buy a flying boat and several defensive spirit talismans, then prepared to return to Great Xuan.

She happened to run into He Zhenghao.

Seeing Bai Wuyue, He Zhenghao's eyes lit up, and he congratulated her repeatedly.

Bai Wuyue didn't know why He Zhenghao was so excited. However, he had helped her in many ways before, so she couldn't just be rude.

Upon learning that Bai Wuyue intended to return to the mortal world to pick up her nephew, He Zhenghao proactively offered to accompany her.

"Don't worry, Daoist Bai. I'm familiar with this matter. It's absolutely foolproof! I can even handle introducing and recommending him to the Myriad Immortals Alliance in the future!"

After some hesitation, Bai Wuyue agreed to He Zhenghao's request.

With the combined efforts of two Foundation Establishment cultivators, they traveled without any accidents. Li Fan was successfully brought to the Profound Yellow Realm.

Since he was not yet a cultivator, he was temporarily settled on Glazed Island.

"Strange, I don't see any serious illness on your nephew's body." He Zhenghao re-examined Li Fan's body and shook his head slightly.

"It's called a difficult and complicated disease." Bai Wuyue's eyes also flashed with a hint of helplessness.

"Don't worry, Daoist. Once one enters the immortal path, all illnesses disappear. As long as we help this brat successfully cultivate, he can defy fate. This time, when the Body Cleansing Spiritual Pool Array is activated, I will personally protect him!" He Zhenghao patted his chest and guaranteed.

Bai Wuyue thanked him again: "Daoist He, thank you for your great kindness. I will definitely repay you generously in the future!"

Half a year later, Li Fan inexplicably died in the Body Cleansing Spiritual Pool Array.

Upon hearing the news, Bai Wuyue rushed over. Li Fan, who was relatively healthy before, was now just a pool of blood and flesh.

Looking at the blood and flesh, He Zhenghao's face turned as pale as paper.

Seeing Bai Wuyue's extremely grim expression, He Zhenghao's heart skipped a beat, and he hurriedly explained: "Daoist Sister, please accept my condolences, Daoist Sister, please accept my condolences!"

"It's all my fault. I thought I could help him overcome this hurdle, but I didn't notice that he had already reached his limit..."

After listening to He Zhenghao's account, Bai Wuyue took a deep breath and slowly calmed down.

"So, it seems that the mortal has no talent for cultivation?"

He Zhenghao wiped the cold sweat from his forehead and nodded: "It should be so. After all, among all mortals, only a minority can embark on the path of cultivation."

Recalling her own repeated rebirths, which gradually improved her cultivation talent, Bai Wuyue sighed again.

"Relying on Li Fan himself seems unlikely."

"I can only help him change his fate after my cultivation is a bit higher."

Without Li Fan as a burden, Bai Wuyue focused her mind entirely on cultivation.

In ten years, she achieved Golden Core.

While accumulating resources and preparing to break through to Nascent Soul...

Disaster struck from the heavens, and she died inexplicably!

"True indeed!"

"The progress in this life is quite satisfactory."

"Daoist He was a great help."

Tenth life!

Bai Wuyue, who had regained consciousness, still had the terror from the previous life lingering on her face.

She didn't even know how she had died in the previous life.

She only remembered losing consciousness inexplicably while in seclusion in the Heavenly Profound Mirror.

"Didn't they say that the Heavenly Profound Mirror is absolutely safe?"

"As expected, the Myriad Immortals Alliance cannot be trusted entirely!"

Forcing herself to calm down, Bai Wuyue considered how to proceed in this life.

"I can cultivate, but mortals cannot."

"If I force him to change his fate, I will need at least Nascent Soul stage cultivation."

"Moreover, I can wait, but Fan'er cannot. I don't have much time left, unless I exchange for some lifespan-extending treasures..."

"But they are more expensive than cultivation techniques, which is somewhat unrealistic."

At most, fifty-six years to break through from an ordinary mortal to Nascent Soul.

It sounded incredible, but Bai Wuyue was very confident.

However, her cultivation talent was already sufficient. What limited her were those damned materials for the new method's breakthrough.

After taking care of her nephew, whom she hadn't seen for a long time, for a month, Bai Wuyue returned to the Profound Yellow Realm.

As before, she asked He Zhenghao for an introduction.

Although he had inadvertently caused her nephew's death in the previous life, it was an unintentional mistake.

Overall, he had earned Bai Wuyue's trust.

With the information she had carefully recorded from the previous life, Bai Wuyue's path to advancement became smoother.

She reached Foundation Establishment in one month and Golden Core in half a year.

She reached Nascent Soul in ten years.

Bai Wuyue became a genius that the entire Congyun Sea looked up to.

She even attracted the attention of the Myriad Immortals Alliance headquarters.

And these ten years were not spent on cultivation, but on completing missions and earning contribution points!

"If there were no resource constraints, I could have been even faster!" Bai Wuyue lamented inwardly.

Before Nascent Soul, she could indeed be very fast.

But the hurdle of the Divine Transformation stage was not so easy to overcome.

First, the news of the Heavenly Changes at the beginning of the world was mostly controlled by the various factions of the Myriad Immortals Alliance and would not be leaked.

Second, when the changes occurred, the world would undergo drastic changes, attracting the attention of surrounding cultivators, inevitably leading to fierce competition.

"No matter what! Anyone who dares to block me..."

"Die!" A cold glint flashed in Bai Wuyue's eyes.

While secretly inquiring about news of the Heavenly Changes, Bai Wuyue waited for the day of the inexplicable calamity to descend.

This time, she specifically left Myriad Immortals Island in advance and came to the frontier of Congyun Sea, hiding herself.

She wanted to glimpse the truth.

Only when that strand of crimson figure appeared did Bai Wuyue finally understand the source of the so-called calamity.

She was not afraid but instead rejoiced.

"I didn't expect it to be the 'Essence of Heaven and Earth'!"

"Doesn't this mean that as long as I can break through to Divine Transformation, I have a great chance of reaching the Dao Integration stage?"

"The Dao Integration realm increases the probability of changing the fate of mortals."

The flames burned the sea, and Bai Wuyue perished under the might of the crimson flames.

"The superposition of spirituality is more terrifying than I imagined."

"With Auntie's current talent, if all the resources were sufficient, she could even prove the Dao as a True Immortal. And this is only after reincarnation ten times..."

"What about a hundred times, a thousand times?"

In the dried-up bottom of Congyun Sea, Li Fan appeared beside Bai Wuyue's skeleton, his expression solemn.

"Speaking of which, others' spirituality is almost only linked to their cultivation talent."

"But in me, Infinite Spirituality seems to be just spirituality."

"Why is this?"

Li Fan frowned in deep thought. After a long time, the words "True and False" finally came out.

Chapter 1617: New Law Opens a Dead End

“What exactly is that ink-colored figure?”

Bai Wuyue was drenched in sweat. Even though a long time had passed since her rebirth, she still hadn't fully recovered from the lingering terror of her previous life.

“Could it be that the so-called Primordial Essence of Heaven and Earth is merely bait to lure us Nascent Soul cultivators to our deaths? But that makes no sense. With the power to merge with the Dao, Nascent Soul cultivators are like ants before them, dead with a wave of their hand. Why would they need bait for hunting?”

“Furthermore, the saying that one merges with the Dao by sacrificing the Primordial Essence of Heaven and Earth is not mere rumor…”

Bai Wuyue couldn’t figure it out no matter how hard she thought. She looked at Li Fan, who was still sleeping soundly in the room, and a flicker of guilt crossed her mind. “Originally, I was thinking of bringing my nephew to the Profound Yellow Realm to change his fate and extend his lifespan. But I never expected that it would be better for him to live as an ordinary mortal in the Great Xuan minor world.”

After much deliberation, Bai Wuyue made up her mind.

This lifetime, she would change her plan!

Her cultivation speed would be further accelerated. She would reach the Nascent Soul stage in fifteen years!

After helping Li Fan change his fate, she would directly send him back to the Great Xuan minor world.

She would create a secular dynasty, solely dedicated to serving Li Fan.

Furthermore, she left behind over a thousand mechanical puppets to protect Li Fan.

“I have already made arrangements for enough spirit stones to be sent every ten years, for five hundred years.”

“Auntie…” Li Fan was deeply grateful and ashamed at the same time. “It’s my fault for always being a burden to you.”

Seeing Li Fan’s expression, Bai Wuyue felt deeply comforted. She stroked Li Fan's head. “Don’t worry, this is just a temporary measure. Once I uncover the truth, I will surely bring you out eventually. How can my nephew be confined to this small world his entire life!”

The domineering aura in her words was no longer something the simple and honest woman of the past could utter.

“To become an emperor, revered by billions of people. My nephew is already very content.” Li Fan said gratefully again.

Bai Wuyue smiled and said no more. She leaped away.

Li Fan knelt and bowed, not rising for a long time.

Only after Bai Wuyue left the Great Xuan did Li Fan return to normal.

“The superposition of spirituality is indeed terrifying. However, the Profound Yellow Realm is also full of unfathomable dangers. Not to mention the restrictions of the Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerate and the suppression of the Starved Immortal. Breaking through this predicament will likely not be easy. Let alone the fact that the Immortal Path is broken. Without True Return, aiming for the Upper Mountain is almost a laughable endeavor.”

Within Li Fan’s thoughts, countless scenarios of Bai Wuyue unfolded.

But none showed her successfully leaving the high walls. Let alone escaping the Primordial, reaching the Shore, and transcending to become a Saint.

“Unless…”

“The superposition of spirituality reaches an extremely terrifying level, enough to disregard all of this.”

“I shall wait.”

Although he was based in the Great Xuan, all matters within the high walls were under Li Fan’s observation!

Having learned from the lessons of the previous lifetime, Bai Wuyue naturally did not dare to plot against Red Flame again.

But the truth behind that ink-colored figure truly piqued her curiosity.

So, she chose to sit back and watch the tigers fight.

She secretly sold the news of Red Flame’s impending appearance, earning a substantial amount of contribution points.

Then, Bai Wuyue waited outside the Congyun Sea, observing from a distance.

Just as she had experienced in her past lives, after Red Flame was killed, Ink Slaughter descended, destroying everything in its path.

“It’s confined to the Congyun Sea region.”

Bai Wuyue watched the writhing shadows, just within reach, that were ferociously destroying everything. She slowly began to grasp some understanding.

“It seems that some secret is buried within the Congyun Sea.”

Witnessing the demise of billions of living beings, the current Bai Wuyue could remain impassive. She quietly retreated.

This lifetime, she lived for over eight hundred years.

Until her death, she had not found the opportunity to break through to merge with the Dao.

But she was not in the least bit anxious. “According to the information I gathered, sixteen Primordial Essences of Heaven and Earth descended during those eight hundred years.”

“Among them, the most suitable for me, and with the least competition, should be [Blue Flame].”

“Sixty-two years after rebirth, it appeared beneath the Great River in Lingze Prefecture, freezing ten thousand miles, turning a vast marsh into a snowy realm.”

“Sixty-two years… I actually have to wait this long…”

Although Bai Wuyue felt unwilling, she could not find a faster method to merge with the Dao at the moment.

Thirteenth Life!

Before the destruction of the Congyun Sea, Bai Wuyue searched within it, trying to uncover its hidden secrets.

Through meticulous searching, she indeed discovered many strange anomalies.

“The Congyun region, was it forcefully shoved into the Profound Yellow Realm with a single palm strike? A place from the outside, not the native land of the Profound Yellow Realm. No wonder the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao insists on its demise.”

“In the vast Profound Yellow Realm, is the Congyun Sea the only place like this? What happened to cause these?”

As one mystery was solved, more questions emerged in her mind.

Sending a chill down her spine.

“And Master Yin’s New New Law…”

“Using a Foundation Establishment base…”

“During the sixty-plus years of waiting, I might as well ponder it. If I can break free from the constraints of the Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerate…”

However, the difficulty of the New New Law far exceeded Bai Wuyue's imagination.

With her talent, after sixty years, she had gained nothing!

This made her doubt her own aptitude for the first time.

“Is there really such a law in the world? Ten lifetimes of me stacked together, yet I can’t make any progress!”

But Bai Wuyue did not give up because of this.

These sixty-plus years of pondering made her vaguely feel that the New New Law was not a dead end but rather something truly promising.

In the sixty-second year, Bai Wuyue successfully slew Blue Flame and proved herself as a Dao Merging Immortal Venerable!

This shocked the Myriad Immortals Alliance.

Her status and position underwent a qualitative leap after merging with the Dao. She no longer needed to worry about cultivation resources, and she even qualified to know many of the Profound Yellow Realm's profound secrets.

Bai Wuyue then brought Li Fan to the Profound Yellow Realm to help him with his cultivation.

As the only close relative of a Dao Merging cultivator.

Even though Li Fan was merely a mortal, no cultivator in the Myriad Immortals Alliance dared to show him any disrespect.

Li Fan lived a life of debauchery and pleasure.

With his mortal body, he controlled female cultivators far surpassing his realm, living a life of great joy.

As long as her nephew was happy, Bai Wuyue didn't mind.

She even proactively helped him find suitable partners, wanting to add more bloodline to the Li family.

Unfortunately, it seemed to be the consequence of changing fate; despite all her efforts, no descendants were born.

Bai Wuyue felt relieved and no longer forced the issue.

This lifetime seemed perfect enough.

But all this happiness ended with Li Fan’s lifespan reaching its end.

“Auntie, I don’t want to die…”

On the verge of death, shedding the youthful appearance forcibly maintained by heavenly treasures, Li Fan revealed an aged face.

Yet, he cried like a child.

Seeing this, Bai Wuyue’s heart ached, and in a daze, she seemed to have returned to the year she had just been reborn.

“Don’t be afraid, Fan’er. Auntie will definitely save you!”

Bai Wuyue tried to use heavenly treasures to extend Li Fan’s life again, but in the end, it was futile.

“Aunt…”

A tear streak crossed her face, and Li Fan perished before Bai Wuyue’s eyes once more.

As if instantly drained of her vitality and spirit, this powerful Dao Merging cultivator also aged.

Bai Wuyue’s heart was filled with a sense of powerlessness.

“Everything was already so good…”

With no further motivation, and her heart and spirit exhausted, Bai Wuyue died of grief ten years later.

“True Return!”

Li Fan, who had already died before her, whispered softly in the darkness.

Although he no longer cared for mortal desires of the flesh, occasionally revisiting them was not bad.

“However, my dear aunt seems to have encountered a bottleneck. Should I give her a push?”

“Forget it, I’ll wait and see. If there are any flaws, and all efforts are in vain, it wouldn’t be good.”

The Saint Creation Plan, the fifteenth life!

Reborn Bai Wuyue remained motionless for a long time.

“After merging with the Dao, there seems to be no hope for longevity.” She suddenly sighed.

The closer she got to the realm of Longevity, the more she felt the terror of the Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerate.

The vast gulf between merging with the Dao and Longevity made Bai Wuyue lose confidence in being able to advance further.

“Especially under the system of the Myriad Immortals Alliance, there is simply no opportunity for advancement from merging with the Dao.”

“I have heard that the Five Elders Association…”

“Could it be that this lifetime requires a change of location?”

After careful consideration, Bai Wuyue shook her head and dismissed the idea.

“Fundamentally, there should be no difference.”

“To break this kind of constraint…”

“Perhaps only the New New Law can achieve it.”

It took her a year to regain her spirit.

During her regular cultivation, she dedicated almost all her free time to comprehending the New New Law.

At the same time, she felt that relying on herself alone might not be enough.

Thus, she shared her insights with Master Yin.

Bai Wuyue's talent and knowledge astonished Master Yin. He was completely convinced and willingly helped her refine her ideas.

During their exchange, he also revealed many secrets about the Profound Yellow Realm to Bai Wuyue.

However, even with their combined efforts, the New New Law could not advance an inch.

The fifteenth, sixteenth, seventeenth life…

When Bai Wuyue’s reincarnation count crossed the threshold of twenty,

Perhaps it was a qualitative change brought about by the superposition of spirituality, and a flash of inspiration struck Bai Wuyue’s mind, finally offering a glimpse of the path ahead.

“After establishing my foundation…”

“It is the Primordial Golden Core!”

“Primordial, from which all things arise, created by the Great One, transformed by Yin and Yang.” At this moment, Bai Wuyue was far from the crude farmer’s wife she once was.

Having read through countless scriptures, her knowledge and understanding far surpassed most people in the Profound Yellow Realm.

“The boundless primordial chaos, originating from the innate, the beginning of the limitless. Then Yin and Yang separated, Heaven and Earth took their positions, cycling between stillness and motion.”

“Kan and Li swapped, fire flies in the Azure Sea to refine the void. The Great One contains truth and form, the Jade Cauldron drips pearls to condense, divine transformation merges with the profound and communicates.”

…

Her accumulated experiences of thousands of years, as if tempered by the fire of inspiration, finally erupted with an immensely powerful force.

It swept away the boulders blocking her path,

Revealing a wide and smooth avenue!

“With my nephew’s talent, any cultivation method that is too difficult will certainly not work.”

“The saying goes, one must see their true nature to understand their heart. To establish my foundation, while feasible, it is extremely difficult to truly understand oneself, let alone mortals. Therefore, the initial threshold for cultivation should not be set too high.”

“It can be divided and implemented!”

In Bai Wuyue’s mind, myriad ideas converged at this moment.

“Each stage of the New New Law should be cultivated simultaneously.”

“Establish foundation during Foundation Establishment, still establish foundation during Golden Core, and even during Nascent Soul. At every step of cultivation, one must repeatedly establish their foundation until finally, it becomes the true ‘Establishing My Foundation’.”

“The word Primordial, itself, encompasses everything. Starting with absolute cultivation, one can control it. Initially, it is just a nascent core. With each advancement, more ingredients are added, and further refinement is carried out.”

“The same applies to every realm after the Golden Core!”

“The New New Law should be a cultivation method where all realms are cultivated simultaneously.”

“Every improvement in self-cognition, every elevation in the understanding of the principles of Heaven and Earth, becomes the driving force for advancing the realm.”

“Like a galloping horse, moving forward relentlessly until…”

“The moment of completion, Foundation Establishment complete, Golden Core complete, Nascent Soul complete… and ultimately, Longevity!”

Bai Wuyue dissolved her own realm and returned to the state of a mortal.

Then, she walked the path of the New New Law again.

If the method she created was something even she lacked the confidence to follow through, how could her resolve be firm?

Bai Wuyue did not seek complete self-knowledge, but rather used her current understanding of herself to establish her own foundation.

It was like carving a stone statue of oneself in a mountain forest.

Once the Foundation Establishment statue was formed, the next step was to achieve the Golden Core Dao.

After twenty reincarnations, all the sights, knowledge, and experiences were gathered in her mind.

Ultimately, it transformed into a seven-colored Golden Core.

Floating above the glabella of the stone statue of herself.

“This is the sum of all my insights into the world, harmonizing with the Dao and resonating with it.”

“As I continue to reincarnate, my understanding will continue to increase. This Golden Core will become even more vibrant and colorful.”

With a single thought, the Golden Core was formed.

As the Golden Core was formed, the stone statue of herself instantly became ten thousand times more vivid.

Just like Bai Wuyue herself.

“After the Golden Core, comes Nascent Soul.”

Bai Wuyue felt her inspiration flowing like a torrent, so she continued to deduce the next steps.

“Nascent Soul, like a fetus not yet condensed, resembling the formation of Heaven and Earth from the Taiji. Humans embody the body of Heaven and Earth, harboring pure essence, the most spiritual of life…”

“Using the true self to deconstruct the observed Heaven and Earth!”

“However, most people are foolish. Even with their own bodies, they may not be able to fully see and know. How can they see the true Heaven and Earth?”

“Heaven and Earth are boundless and infinite, regardless of their true form, they will inevitably change as one’s realm and strength increase. Therefore…”

Bai Wuyue seemed to sense something. Within the stone statue, beneath the seven-colored Golden Core.

At the location of the Zhong Court acupoint, a Nascent Soul appeared.

However, this Nascent Soul was different from the Nascent Souls created in the Heaven and Earth realms of the Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerate, and the classical Nascent Souls recorded in ancient texts.

Instead, it was completely transparent, like a white mirror.

It seemed to reflect the world it saw.

“Establishing my foundation, Primordial Golden Core. Following this, it is the Spiritual Mirror Nascent Soul!”

“When a precious mirror is polished clean, it only reflects one room; when the heart mirror is polished clean, it can reflect the Six Directions! The more one sees, the wider the reflection. The larger Heaven and Earth, the more concrete it becomes in the mirror!”

Bai Wuyue’s Spiritual Mirror Nascent Soul emitted a faint glow.

Scenes from her past twenty lifetimes flashed by.

The stone statue of herself, along with this reflection, also acquired a touch of ‘mortal’ aura.

Bai Wuyue, who had dispelled her own realm and was cultivating anew, although only in the Nascent Soul stage.

Yet, with the formation of the stone statue, Golden Core, and Spiritual Mirror, her own aura rapidly returned to its peak within a short period.

In the Nascent Soul stage, she was comparable to a Dao Merging cultivator!

However, moments later…

Bai Wuyue’s vitality, just as it reached its peak, suddenly declined.

Her Dao comprehension and willpower were depleted, her spirit scattered, and her soul perished!

Chapter 1618: Li Fan Sees His True Self

The Saint Creation Plan, twenty-first life!

"With my foundation establishment, Primordial Golden Core, Spiritual Mirror Nascent Soul..."

Merely extending the New New Law to the Nascent Soul realm seemed to have completely drained Bai Wuyue's spiritual energy, leaving her feeling utterly exhausted even after a rebirth. She spent several days resting in bed, a rare occurrence.

"Auntie, are you alright?" Li Fan asked, his eyes full of concern as he brought a bowl of freshly cooked hot porridge.

Bai Wuyue's spirit perked up. After drinking the porridge, she replied, "Don't worry, Fan'er. Auntie is just feeling a bit tired. I'll be fine after a few days of rest."

Li Fan paused, a strange expression on his face. "Why has Auntie's speech become so refined..."

Bai Wuyue's heart skipped a beat. She chuckled dryly to cover her lapse.

"It seems that what has changed within me is not just my spirituality, but also many subtle influences. Fortunately, the continuous cycle of rebirth is too outlandish for my nephew to even consider."

What amused Bai Wuyue was that although her nephew seemed to be fooled by her on the surface, he still secretly worried and even went to invite the village witch to "treat her illness."

Looking at the bowl of rune water the witch handed her and Li Fan's expectant gaze, Bai Wuyue helplessly drank it.

After the charade, Bai Wuyue settled Li Fan and, instead of rushing to the Profound Yellow Realm, headed to the nearest spiritual mountain to meditate.

Dismantling the Mountain Peak!

"To see the heart and awaken the nature, to establish the foundation with myself. With a new birth, I have once again become different from my past self..."

Bai Wuyue sat by the cliff, gazing at the vast, boundless sea of clouds before her, and introspected. It was as if the heavens themselves held the reins, an invisible knife carving profoundly intricate trajectories in the void. Bai Wuyue's own statue slowly materialized from the darkness. Compared to the end of the previous life, this self-statue resembled Bai Wuyue even more.

Within a few breaths, Bai Wuyue had already reached the peak of Foundation Establishment!

"This is the superiority of the New New Law. If I were still cultivating the Heavenly Venerate's methods, I would have to painstakingly search for heavenly treasures. Though, with the convenience of continuous rebirth, I could find increasingly better quality treasures, the earthly treasures are already the limit. Most of them are controlled by the Law-Transmitters. As for heavenly treasures, they are even beyond imagination..."

"Moreover, even heavenly treasures might not compare to [Establishing Myself Foundation Establishment]."

Bai Wuyue looked at the self-statue within her body with great satisfaction, took a deep breath, and clenched the top-grade spirit stone in her embrace. In her sea of consciousness, countless colorful beams of light shifted and intertwined, soon forming a Primordial Golden Core. The volume of the spirit stone instantly reduced by more than half.

"Although it is the Land of Immortal Termination, it is not absolutely devoid of spiritual energy. It is just that the quantity is too scarce, negligibly small." Bai Wuyue sat on the mountain peak, her gaze sweeping across the entire Great Xuan minor world.

"Hmm? There are actually a few places with spiritual energy fluctuations?"

With a flicker of her form, Bai Wuyue investigated these locations.

"Tomb of Taiyan Sect disciple Yi Xingzhi."

"Tomb of Qian Hong."

"...These are all burial sites of cultivators who perished here."

"Apart from this item, nothing else has any value." Bai Wuyue shook the Heavenly Lock Treasure Box in her hand.

"I wonder what treasures are hidden within."

As a former Dao Integration cultivator, Bai Wuyue's standards were already exceptionally high; ordinary treasures rarely caught her eye. However, after unlocking the Heavenly Lock Treasure Box with the Heavenly Profound Mirror and discovering the Dao Dissolution Stone within, Bai Wuyue was still somewhat excited.

"I never imagined that my homeland would hide such a treasure." She had long heard of the peculiar nature of the Dao Dissolution Stone. Even as a Dao Integration expert in the Immortal Alliance, she had no way to obtain one. "The Dao Dissolution Stone can increase deductive calculation power severalfold. If used to assist in creating a Spiritual Mirror Nascent Soul..."

"The effect is extraordinary!" In Bai Wuyue's middle dantian, the mirror-like body of her Nascent Soul seemed to have been polished anew. In an instant, it became several times clearer. Furthermore, the world it reflected also revealed more details. The clouds in the sky, the grasses on the ground, all moved with the wind, everything as if real. Bai Wuyue was immersed in it, feeling as if the world had never been so bright before.

"If I had this item in my previous life, I wouldn't have exhausted my heart and soul to death." After a long while, Bai Wuyue exhaled, sighing inwardly.

"It's a pity it's only of lower grade. If it were of higher grade, or even the legendary Dao Dissolution Stone Mother, I wonder how much it would help me."

"However, it reminds me that within the Profound Yellow Realm, there are many treasures like the Dao Dissolution Stone that can enhance comprehension. For example, the Enlightenment Pill of the Grand Supreme Sect, the Heavenly Profound Spirit Enlightenment, and so on. Appropriately borrowing external forces might lead to twice the result with half the effort."

Bai Wuyue lingered in the Great Xuan minor world, illuminating every corner of this world. After finding nothing else, she then gracefully headed towards the Profound Yellow Realm.

Shortly after Bai Wuyue's departure, not far from where she had meditated on the mountain peak, a figure suddenly appeared! It was Li Fan.

"Spiritual Mirror Nascent Soul..."

"The twenty lives of spirituality superposition are indeed extraordinary. She has forged a path entirely different from the vague framework proposed by Su Bai, or the deductions of the Saint Emperor."

"Su Bai only proposed a vague framework, which is irrelevant for now. The Saint Emperor's deductions were likely influenced by Emperor Taiwei the Sacred. The importance of the Sacred Dynasty rested entirely on Emperor Taiwei. Therefore, his new law completely disregarded transmissibility. But my aunt, for my sake, has truly exhausted herself..."

Li Fan chuckled softly and flicked a finger towards the void ahead. A phantom image of Li Fan appeared, mimicking Bai Wuyue's posture, facing the sea of clouds and sitting cross-legged. Although it was a phantom, within the interplay of light and shadow, it was indistinguishable from a real flesh-and-blood body. The phantom closed its eyes, its chest rising and falling with each breath, as if it were another Li Fan!

"True and false in a single thought, transformation follows the heart~" Li Fan chanted softly, quite pleased with his performance. After twenty cycles of reincarnation, his aunt had transformed from a mere mortal into a Dao Integration grand cultivator, and had even deduced and comprehended three levels of the New New Law. Li Fan, naturally, had not gained nothing. The semi-real, semi-virtual body before him was a creation born from his manipulation of true and false.

"My body in a mortal state."

"Ignoring the influence of Huan Zhen's existence." Li Fan walked around the phantom-virtual body, nodding constantly. "Except for the impact of Infinite Spirituality, it is almost indistinguishable from my true self."

"Even if placed before my aunt, she would not recognize it as merely my creation."

"My understanding of spirituality is still too superficial. I'll put that aside for now."

"Using this body as an experiment, anything that happens within it can be replicated perfectly and without loss within my own body."

"Establishing my foundation..." A faint light flashed in Li Fan's eyes. An invisible blade rapidly carved within the phantom Li Fan. Carving a statue of himself within a phantom of himself. It seemed awkward, but with each carving, Li Fan's self-understanding seemed to deepen.

"Laughter and scolding are me, greed and fear of death are also me."

"Worrying about the world is me, disregarding all beings is also me."

"Extravagance is me, obsession with longevity is also me..."

The scenes of past reincarnations flashed before Li Fan's eyes. His statue became increasingly angular and complex. While Bai Wuyue could complete her Foundation Establishment in a single thought, Li Fan's first step alone would require at least a hundred years. But Li Fan was patient.

...

After Bai Wuyue returned to the Profound Yellow Realm, she followed her usual routine and found Master Yin. Although she didn't mention reincarnation, she generously shared her newly comprehended cultivation method. Master Yin was so moved that he danced with joy. Having been on the verge of breakthrough in the New New Law for years, Bai Wuyue's insights had pushed him over the edge. In just a few days, Master Yin, like Bai Wuyue, reached the Nascent Soul stage. The old injuries from his Foundation Establishment were also healed, and he no longer spoke with a faltering voice.

"Regarding this Dao Dissolution Stone you mentioned, I might have some clues."

"I vaguely recall that the Taiyan Sect was still hidden within this world in the past. As for its specific location..." Master Yin scratched his head, unable to recall.

Bai Wuyue comforted him, "It's alright. As long as they are still alive, we will find them eventually. It is said that the Dao Dissolution Stone Mother, with its deduction power millions of times greater than an ordinary Dao Dissolution Stone, could help us easily perfect the New New Law."

Master Yin heartily agreed. "Besides the Dao Dissolution Stone Mother, we could also try other possibilities."

"For example, the Enlightenment Infinite Wall and the Mortal Deification Wall..." Master Yin offered various suggestions.

Bai Wuyue sighed, "The Profound Yellow Realm holds so many unbelievable wonders. It's truly hard to imagine how magnificent the vast Sea of Stars beyond the Profound Yellow Realm must be..."

Master Yin shook his head. "Perhaps the entire Sea of Stars combined cannot compare to even a corner of the Profound Yellow Realm."

Bai Wuyue was stunned. Master Yin then recounted the calamity that had befallen the world, the destruction of the Sea of Stars. Bai Wuyue's heart trembled. "Previously, I had heard of ancient calamities, but I always thought that after so many years, life would have revived beyond the Sea of Stars. I never expected..."

"Furthermore, there is the Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerate, collecting remnant realms and stitching together the Profound Yellow Realm." The true face of the Profound Yellow Realm began to be revealed to Bai Wuyue. Bai Wuyue knew that there were too many secrets within the Profound Yellow Realm. But she also firmly believed that with her infinite rebirth ability, these secrets would become a catalyst to break the constraints of the Law-Transmitter.

"One step at a time." In the eyes of the Spiritual Mirror Nascent Soul, a miniaturized image of the Profound Yellow Realm, shrouded in mist, appeared. Bai Wuyue's first destination was the Enlightenment Infinite Wall in Tianliang Prefecture.

"It is said that comprehending the Dao before this wall has a certain chance of being drawn into it. Although the flow of time is different from the outside, and there is the danger of dying of old age within, the enlightenment bonus inside is several times greater than the Heavenly Profound Spirit Enlightenment..."

"It's perfect for me!" Bai Wuyue stared intently at the smooth stone wall before her. In a trance, she sensed the heartbeat of the stone wall.

"It's not my imagination." Bai Wuyue reached out and gently stroked it. The next moment, the scenery before her changed, and she entered the Infinite Wall. Just as the rumors outside suggested, upon entering, she felt a boost. Her mind became thousands of times more active. Past knowledge and experiences were reorganized and gathered towards the primordial Great Dao of heaven and earth. However, the price was the rapid depletion of her vitality. As the saying goes, "Hear the Dao in the morning, and die in the evening." Clearly, cultivators immersed in enlightenment here would not care about this, allowing their life force to drain away, engrossed in their comprehension. This place was indeed useful to Bai Wuyue. But she saw something others could not. Above each cultivator's head, an invisible tentacle seemed to extend from the void, deeply inserted into the cultivator's head, occasionally wriggling. As the absorbed cultivators appeared entranced, this scene seemed particularly bizarre. It was as if these tentacles were helping the cultivators within the Infinite Wall achieve enlightenment.

"Hmm? You can see me?" A soft whisper sounded beside Bai Wuyue. Bai Wuyue was not startled, only nodded. "Then, what do I look like in your eyes?" Bai Wuyue replied truthfully. "Tentacles..." The voice sounded somewhat disappointed, then said, "It's already good." Hearing these words that seemed to be meant as consolation, Bai Wuyue felt curious. "Is this not your original form?" The voice chuckled. "A frog in a well sees only the small patch of sky above its head, thinking that's all there is to the sky. A bird flying in the sky, though it sees the boundless firmament, also believes that's the true appearance of the sky." "In reality?" "Beyond the sky, there are more skies; the mountains and seas are infinite, beyond the comprehension of mortals..." Although mocked as a frog in a well, Bai Wuyue was not angry. "Listening to your words, senior, you seem incredibly knowledgeable, able to see things we cannot. Yet, why are you trapped here?" "Trapped? What do you mean? I am merely feeding. Ever since I was thrown here years ago, cultivators have continuously entered my belly. I don't need to move, and food comes to me. Since there's such good fortune, why should I toil?" The voice spoke boastfully. "Endless eating?" Bai Wuyue mused. "Indeed, just like you. Do you think your enlightenment is stimulated by me? In fact, I am merely accelerating the loss of your life force, concentrating a lifetime's worth of thoughts into this moment!" "A lifetime, hundreds or even thousands of years, should have been gradual. This is the truth of this place." "You cultivators are often impatient. You would achieve it on your own eventually, but you always seek external help. You play right into my hands!" It seemed the voice hadn't spoken to anyone in a long time and rambled on to Bai Wuyue. At the same time, the tentacle inserted into Bai Wuyue's head was continuously drawing her life force. "Hmm? Why, after hearing so much, does your heart remain completely unmoved?" The voice sounded surprised. Bai Wuyue stared at the tentacle above her head, which seemed to be changing shape, and suddenly chuckled. "It seems your knowledge is also limited."

Chapter 1619: I Am the Revered One

In every corner of Xuanjing City, Bai Wuyue had buried various poisons collected from her travels across the world. The most important among them was the [Blood Dripping Zither], made primarily from human vital blood. Once triggered by an explosion, it would burst into a mist of blood. That's right, after fifty years of research, Bai Wuyue had reached an astonishing conclusion: the reason she could never absorb the spiritual energy from the spirit stone was not because the spiritual energy was poisonous. Instead, humans had a strong repulsive reaction to spiritual energy, like a deadly poison. The toxicity was far greater than any other poison in the world. Through a series of experiments, Bai Wuyue had verified this point.

"I just don't know how effective it will be against immortals." The conversation between the immortals drifted down from the sky. Bai Wuyue silently memorized every word.

"Land of Immortal Termination, Golden Core Method."

"Immortal-Mortal Miasma..."

"It's just seeking a sliver of survival!" Amidst insane laughter, a fire dragon descended from the sky, engulfing Xuanjing City. Continuous explosions resounded through the heavens. The vast Xuanjing City, like a toy, instantly turned into ruins. Even though she had known in advance what would happen, Bai Wuyue was still trembling with fear at the might displayed by the two immortals with every move. At the same time, the effect of the [Blood Dripping Zither] was unexpectedly good! Accompanied by blood and flames, a dense blood mist instantly rose into the sky, as if condensing the vengeful souls of hundreds of thousands of innocent citizens of Xuanjing City, soaring upwards! Dao Xuanzi and Kou Hong, caught off guard, were enveloped by large swathes of blood mist, both letting out muffled groans. Bai Wuyue held her breath and observed. A moment later, two figures, one after the other, rushed out of the blood mist and fled westward!

"Their speed is much slower than before! And..."

"They seem on the verge of collapse!" Bai Wuyue did not rush to chase. Although severely injured, the speed at which immortals fled was not something a mortal like her could match. However, she had long since set up informants throughout Great Xuan. As long as the immortals were still in Great Xuan, she would definitely find them! These people were all saved by Bai Wuyue during her travels as a physician and were loyal and reliable. Waiting for half a day, a carrier pigeon arrived from the horizon, bringing news of the immortals' whereabouts. A horse-drawn carriage carried Bai Wuyue, slowly setting off, following the footprints of the immortals. Three months later.

"Grandma Bai, according to the investigation by my brothers, the two immortals finally disappeared in this mountain forest."

"However, the Black Water Mountain spans hundreds of miles and is sparsely populated. My brothers have tried their best, but still haven't..." A man in black knelt on one knee, reporting to Bai Wuyue with a look of guilt.

"It's alright." Bai Wuyue gazed at the secluded mountain forest ahead, interrupting the man in black. "Tell them all to come back. From now on, I'll find them myself." The man in black was slightly stunned, but saw Bai Wuyue walking step by step into the mountain forest. After a moment of hesitation, the man in black ultimately did not choose to follow, because he knew that Grandma Bai always kept her word. Moreover, tracking immortals was indeed a terrifying matter... With her medical skills reaching the peak of perfection, Bai Wuyue had no problem surviving in the wilderness. More importantly, she could clearly sense the spiritual energy fluctuations left by the two immortals' flight, which clearly indicated the direction in this vast wilderness.

"They haven't been able to get out of this mountain forest for a long time, perhaps they are still healing from serious injuries. Who knows when they will recover..." Bai Wuyue's brows flashed with determination. She swallowed a black pill, and within a few breaths, an unusual redness appeared on her cheeks. This was a method of greatly enhancing her mobility at the cost of consuming her lifespan. Following the direction indicated by the spiritual energy residue, Bai Wuyue moved quickly. Fifteen days later, three hundred miles deep into Black Water Mountain, in a mountain valley.

"The spiritual energy traces stop here."

"And ahead... there is a spiritual energy fluctuation." When she was truly about to face immortals, Bai Wuyue couldn't help but feel a surge of apprehension. But in the next moment, she suppressed her hesitation. She slowly approached. The river flowed gently, and a man sat by the stream, with his eyes closed in meditation, not far from a tomb. Bai Wuyue recognized him at a glance: it was Kou Hong, one of the two immortals. However, he was no longer the middle-aged man he was before. His hair was white, and his face was covered with wrinkles. He looked like an old man on the verge of death!

"Could this be the effect of the Immortal-Mortal Miasma?" Bai Wuyue secretly marveled, while glancing at the tomb beside Kou Hong. "Not only can it injure immortals, but it can also kill them?" The approach of a mortal naturally could not escape Kou Hong's senses. The moment he opened his eyes, Bai Wuyue felt her body stiffen, unable to move. Fortunately, it seemed that Kou Hong saw that Bai Wuyue was just a simple mortal with no threat, and soon closed his eyes again.

"A mere mortal, why do you pursue me to this place?" As a healer, Bai Wuyue could hear the weakness in Kou Hong's voice, but he was not someone she, a mere woman, could contend with. After weighing the options, she took out the remaining spirit stone, bowed her head, and said softly, "This old woman's lifelong pursuit is only immortal cultivation and longevity. However, after searching the world, I have found no true immortal methods. A few days ago, I was shocked to hear of two immortals appearing in Xuanjing..." Kou Hong was not interested in Bai Wuyue's words, but kept his eyes fixed on the spirit stone in her hand. He levitated it and, with a flash of surprise in his eyes, said, "Top-grade spirit stone?" After playing with it for a while, he showed a look of joy.

"Although only a little residue remains, it is enough for me to barely recover my injuries." Looking at Bai Wuyue, he asked, "Where did you find this spirit stone?" It seemed he had already believed Bai Wuyue's words.

"Replying to the Immortal Master, this stone was found by this old woman in a mountain tomb." Bai Wuyue answered truthfully.

"Besides this spirit stone, are there any other things?" Kou Hong quickly asked.

"With your talent, I can confidently entrust it to you." Although it said this, the Boundless Wall's large eyeball still looked somewhat reluctant.

It slowly and sluggishly revealed the "[Seize]" technique. Bai Shuyue saw its behavior and felt strange. It had not even concealed the Saint Monarch's Palace plaque, so there was no reason for it to hide a mere True Immortal Seal Script.

It was only after Bai Shuyue deciphered the "[Seize]" technique that she understood why. With flowing strokes, a golden True Immortal Seal Script instantly formed in the air. The Boundless Wall's eyes flickered, having already retreated far away before the "[Seize]" technique appeared.

"Miss Bai! We agreed that the [Seize] technique was to deal with that brat with the golden hair. Why are you using it on me now?"

Bai Shuyue did not answer, merely waving her other hand. The "[Restrain]" technique in the air instantly appeared. Like two suns shining together, they illuminated the nine heavens!

The Boundless Wall's eyes showed panic as it retreated even further.

"The '[Restrain]' and '[Seize]' characters both belong to the unique seal scripts of the Immortal Court. They were special means used by the Immortal Court to suppress the myriad immortals. When combined, they are like immortal soldiers and generals setting up a formation to search for enemies, their power being several times greater than any individual character."

"By casting these two talismans, I can not only suppress and plunder the Boundless Wall but also plunder its private collection. The Saint Monarch's Palace plaque..." For a moment, Bai Shuyue did consider such a thought. However, in recent lives, memories of spending time with the Boundless Wall flashed through her mind. She ultimately did not act.

"Humans are not insensible beings; how can one be without feelings? In this life, it has shown me kindness. I cannot repay kindness with enmity. When the next life begins anew, with no past ties and debts between us, it will be time enough." Thinking this, the '[Restrain]' and '[Seize]' characters in the air hovered gently and then dissipated.

Bai Shuyue looked at the Boundless Wall, still hiding far away, and chuckled, "It's just my divine ability at its nascent stage; I was merely testing its feel. Why are you so nervous? We are life-and-death allies; how could I possibly harm you!"

The Boundless Wall observed for a while longer, and seeing that Bai Shuyue showed no signs of hostility, it finally relaxed. It said smugly, "I was merely testing you. Since I dared to teach you these two characters, naturally I have a way to break them. If you had truly attacked me, hmph..." Whether its words were true or not, Bai Shuyue silently bore them in mind.

"With my divine ability formed, it's time to seek revenge on that brat. He caused us such a mess; it’s simply outrageous!" the Boundless Wall said excitedly. In its view, being humiliated by a mortal was absolutely unacceptable. It had to reclaim its honor, or its title of 'Before the Saint Monarch's Gate' would be meaningless!

Bai Shuyue, however, remained calm. "There's no need to seek him out. We just need to wait here, like a hunter waiting for prey." Bai Shuyue's premonition was not wrong. Ou Shangtian seemed to possess a special tracking method; even from a great distance, he could easily pinpoint their location. After ambushing them for less than three days, Ou Shangtian's aura was faintly detected on the horizon, rapidly approaching.

However, strangely, just as he was about to enter the ambush zone, Ou Shangtian stopped without warning. After a brief pause, he turned and left without hesitation.

"Such sharp intuition!" Bai Shuyue was greatly surprised and no longer hesitated. The two True Immortal Seal Scripts were unleashed simultaneously. Myriad golden chains and a pale, massive hand suddenly appeared in the sky, trapping Ou Shangtian within.

"Invert the Heavens and Earth!"

A furious roar resounded, attempting to scatter the sealing power of the True Immortal Seal Scripts. However, seemingly affected by the "[Seize]" technique, the immortal bone within Ou Shangtian's body rapidly retracted its golden light. His divine power vanished instantly, as if it had never existed.

Empowered by immortal bone, Ou Shangtian became ordinary! Like falling from the clouds to the earth, having lost the enhancement of the two immortal artifacts, Ou Shangtian was, without suspense, successfully suppressed and captured by Bai Shuyue.

"Good, good, good! I'll let you chase again!" The Boundless Wall, which had disappeared during the battle, now revealed itself triumphantly, wielding dozens of tendrils and incessantly tormenting the tightly bound Ou Shangtian.

"I'll slowly dig out your immortal bone, inch by inch, later!" the Boundless Wall whispered with a hidden laugh, its single eye pressed close to Ou Shangtian's face.

"Kill me or dismember me, as you wish! Don't think I'll fear you two wicked thieves!" Ou Shangtian, unfazed, cursed them.

The Boundless Wall flew into a rage, and five tendrils plunged into Ou Shangtian's body, churning vigorously. Ou Shangtian nearly convulsed in pain, yet he endured it, not uttering a single sound, let alone begging for mercy. This stubbornness only further enraged the Boundless Wall. It resolved to employ more brutal methods, determined to make the mortal boy submit.

Compared to this, Bai Shuyue frowned slightly while watching Ou Shangtian's display. A wave of emotion washed over her. "Wicked thieves... I never thought that one day, others would call me by such a name."

"Speaking of which, we were in the wrong initially, accidentally killing his father. Seeking revenge for a loved one is only natural. Moreover, this youth, despite suffering such cruel punishment, remains steadfast."

"Yes, he's a good child, just like Fan'er."

"Let's just give him a quick end." With this thought, Bai Shuyue interrupted the Boundless Wall's torment. The tendrils instantly drained Ou Shangtian's lifespan, and after extracting the two immortal artifacts from his body, Bai Shuyue intended to leave. To find a safe place and meticulously study the spoils she had obtained.

However, she hadn't flown far when a strong sense of unease surged within her. She scanned her surroundings with suspicion but found no source of the unease. Judging by the Boundless Wall's reaction, it was clearly not her imagination.

"Hurry and escape! We seem to be targeted by something!" Bai Shuyue's expression turned grim as she fled with all her might, but the unease in her heart only intensified. Finally, nine golden needles descended from the sky, instantly sealing off Bai Shuyue from all directions!

After a moment of stunned silence, Bai Shuyue reacted. She intended to use the True Immortal Seal Script again to defend herself. Unexpectedly... A pale hand silently appeared above her head. It gently pressed a long golden needle into her Baihui acupoint.

The golden needle entered her body, piercing her skull. Her entire being seemed frozen, her expression caught between shock and panic. Not only could her entire body not move, but even her thoughts were sealed in ice. The Boundless Wall, disregarding any camaraderie, let out a startled cry and prepared to flee. But it was interrupted by a light hum.

Two fingers gently pinched the jade tile. The Boundless Wall trembled and struggled incessantly, its jade surface revealing the blurred outline of the Saint Monarch's Palace plaque.

"Hmm?" After a voice filled with both surprise and delight, the Heavenly Physician slowly revealed himself. He quickly tapped the surface of the Boundless Wall several times. The Saint Monarch's Palace plaque, which had been trying to break free, trembled slightly and then fell silent again. The Boundless Wall itself seemed to have fallen into a slumber, just like Bai Shuyue.

Looking at the temporarily sealed person and artifact before him, the Heavenly Physician pondered. Not long ago, he had been searching near the remnant Great Wall beneath the high walls for suitable fragments of cultivation worlds. Unexpectedly, he suddenly sensed fluctuations in True Immortal Seal Script energies from the Profound Yellow Realm. Although it wasn't the same one that caused the catastrophe in the Heavenly Law Realm years ago, the Heavenly Physician decided to return and investigate. After all, the Profound Yellow Realm was of great importance, and no mistakes could be tolerated.

Later, sensing the appearance of a second True Immortal Seal Script, the Heavenly Physician's return speeded up. "The Profound Yellow Realm has been peaceful for a long time. Now, within a short period, two True Immortal Seal Scripts have appeared... What exactly happened?" The Heavenly Physician was filled with doubt and uncertainty.

Upon arriving near the Profound Yellow Realm, the two True Immortal Seal Scripts erupted once more. The Heavenly Physician followed the trail, pinpointing the source of the True Immortal Seal Scripts. "This jade tile seems to be an item from the Immortal Realm. And that plaque on the jade tile just now..."

"The Tai Yi Palace?" The Heavenly Physician's expression turned grave. Although the Boundless Wall's origin was extraordinary, the Heavenly Physician's gaze remained fixed on Bai Shuyue. "In the moment before I sealed her, this woman's thoughts were rather strange."

"On the surface, she seemed shocked and fearful, but deep down..." The Heavenly Physician frowned, flying around the immobilized Bai Shuyue several times. "Fearless?"

"Does she have some other reliance?" The more the Heavenly Physician observed, the more he felt his intuition was correct. Golden needles of various lengths were arranged, and the Heavenly Physician prepared to conduct a more thorough examination of Bai Shuyue.

"If the Heavenly Demon were still here, this wouldn't be so troublesome. Alas, I need his power to suppress the transmission of the Dao." Thinking this, the Heavenly Physician held the needle, preparing to pierce Bai Shuyue's forehead.

Just as the golden needle was about to penetrate, a crisp snapping sound echoed through the heavens and earth. The Heavenly Physician's movement instantly halted. His expression, like Bai Shuyue's before him, became frozen in time. In fact, it wasn't just the Heavenly Physician; the entire Profound Yellow Realm fell into a state of stagnation with that light sound.

Li Fan's figure appeared on the scene. Looking at the scene before him, he shook his head slightly. "Fortunately, I was vigilant back then. Otherwise, this would be the end of the line."

"But it's alright. Auntie, I'll help you!" Li Fan took the Heavenly Physician's hand and forcefully thrust the uninserted golden needle into him. In an instant, many scenarios were filled in. Then...

"True and False!" The Saint Creation Plan, the twenty-eighth generation!

Bai Shuyue woke up from her nightmare, unable to recover for a long time. This time, the shock she felt was even more intense than during her first "rebirth." She subconsciously touched her head, as if the pain there had not yet dissipated.

After the golden needle pierced her, her consciousness had frozen, so she did not know how she had died. However, she still retained some vague images in her mind. Treated like an object, golden needles filled her entire body. And later, she was dismembered into countless pieces... Even recalling the faint residual memories of the previous life, Bai Shuyue's face turned instantly deathly pale.

"Ugh..." Instinctively bending over, she vomited uncontrollably. Her body trembled violently, unable to stop. Months passed, and she still hadn't recovered.

After all, despite Bai Shuyue's twenty-plus layerings of spirituality, making her incredibly talented, her experiences could not match her current aptitude. It was fine if she died normally before, but after encountering the Heavenly Physician in the previous life and undergoing such inhuman torture, Bai Shuyue became terrified.

She did not want to, nor dared to, nor wished to venture into the Profound Yellow Realm again. "The Profound Yellow Realm is simply too dangerous and terrifying."

"Living as a mortal emperor in Great Xuan, staying put, wouldn't that be good too." Once this thought arose, it spread like wildfire, impossible to extinguish.
