Bai Shuyue dared not even speculate about the true identity of the figure who appeared at the end of the previous life. She chose to bury her head in the sand and escape.

Chapter 1623: Auntie Encounters Heavenly Doctor

The fear of being inexplicably sealed by a powerful figure subsided somewhat with the second rebirth. Seeing Li Fan alive and well again, Bai Shuyue felt a long-lost joy. Revitalized, Bai Shuyue embarked on the path of cultivation once more.

The fact was that even with such a "slothful" approach as in the previous life, only living for a few months in a daze, her cultivation talent had still increased with each rebirth. A dangerous thought arose in Bai Shuyue's mind: "If this is the case, why don't I just commit suicide after each revival? Quickly start the next life. By using this method, I can first increase my cultivation talent to an unimaginable level. Then, cultivation will be as easy as eating and drinking. Deriving the New New Method will also be a matter of moments..." Honestly, Bai Shuyue was quite tempted.

In her past twenty-plus reincarnations, she had deeply experienced the benefits of outstanding cultivation talent. The initial difficulty of cultivation was incomparable to the later twenty lives. Even now, Bai Shuyue could hardly imagine what cultivation would be like if her talent were to increase tenfold or a hundredfold.

However, after careful consideration, Bai Shuyue ultimately abandoned this seemingly extremely tempting idea. The reason was fundamental: Bai Shuyue's rebirth was uncontrollable. After each death and loss of consciousness, Bai Shuyue could not be certain if she would be able to revive in the next life. Nor could she be sure how long this cycle of rebirth and reincarnation would last.

"If, in reality, my rebirth has a limit, say fifty times, one hundred times, and I use them all to stack talent, without any effort towards my and Fan'er's future, I would likely regret it terribly." "It's better to proceed steadily, step by step. After all, although the path ahead is arduous, it's not entirely impossible to overcome."

Bai Shuyue took a deep breath, calming the restlessness in her heart. "If, in the future, I truly encounter a situation where there is no hope of breaking through, perhaps then I can adopt this method."

Bai Shuyue did not rush to the Profound Yellow Realm, but habitually ascended to the peak of Solitude Mountain, reviewing her experiences from the life before the last. "How was that mysterious powerhouse with the golden needles attracted?" "Could it be Ou Shangtian's elder? The elder coming after the junior?" She quickly dismissed this speculation. "If that were the case, he would have appeared long after I killed Ou Daozi."

"It seems it was the fluctuations from my use of the True Immortal Seal Scripts that attracted him." "Although True Immortal Seal Scripts are powerful, they create too much disturbance..."

Bai Shuyue mentally estimated the time it took for the golden-needled expert to appear after she first used the True Immortal Seal Script. "After using it, I must relocate quickly and hide in a safe location. Furthermore, I cannot use it again for a long time." "Until I find a way to counter that golden-needled expert." Bai Shuyue formulated a guiding principle for her future actions.

"I wonder how the strength of this mysterious expert compares to the Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerable whom I suppressed? Or perhaps, he *is* the Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerable?" "Did the Boundless Wall escape again at the end of the penultimate life?"

Carrying this question, Bai Shuyue sought it out again. Relying on her familiarity with the Boundless Wall accumulated over several lifetimes, combined with her transcendent talent, Bai Shuyue regained its trust without much effort. "What is your current strength? According to the Saint Monarch's doorstep, you should easily be able to block a true immortal." Bai Shuyue asked.

"Hehehe, naturally!" the Boundless Wall said smugly.

Seeing the Boundless Wall's performance, Bai Shuyue stared at it suspiciously. "What is that look?" the Boundless Wall roared. "How could I, when I make my move, be unable to stop even a common true immortal?" Bai Shuyue continued to stare, confronting it.

Slowly, the Boundless Wall's imposing aura weakened, and it admitted guiltily, "Alright, when I was at my peak, I could indeed easily suppress a true immortal. But currently..." "As you know, the Immortal Realm was destroyed. To escape disaster, I was forced to shed my immortal realm foundation. Furthermore..." The Boundless Wall lowered its voice. "I am suppressing the Saint Monarch's Palace plaque within me. Although the writing on the plaque has long since departed, its spiritual essence remains. Naturally, it is unwilling to be perpetually suppressed by me. Thus, I must also divert a significant portion of my power to counter it."

"You have such talent; just cultivate diligently and avoid provoking any major figures. Otherwise, I may not be able to save you." Hearing the Boundless Wall's explanation, Bai Shuyue understood its fate in the penultimate life. "Rest assured, I won't do anything so foolish." "Besides, the one I need to deal with is currently just a child."

Bai Shuyue looked into the distance. Guanglan Prefecture, Baoyuan Mountain. With ease, Bai Shuyue found Ou Daozi and Ou Shangtian. Ou Shangtian at this moment was unlike the majestic figure Bai Shuyue saw in her previous life. Due to his immortal bone not yet fully integrating with his body, he frequently suffered from pain and was extremely weak.

Bai Shuyue, acting as a senior, offered to treat Ou Shangtian's illness. Although Ou Daozi was skeptical, facing Bai Shuyue, whose strength far surpassed his own, he had no choice but to accept. Bringing Ou Shangtian back into the Boundless Wall, the two worked together to finally extract the immortal bone from his body. After exchanging the restored and healthy Ou Shangtian, Ou Daozi expressed his profuse gratitude.

The Boundless Wall, however, was in an uproar. "Good heavens, what a marvel!" "It actually brought an immortal bone, and its rank from its true immortal life was not low!" "Fortunately, it's only a small piece of bone left. Otherwise, I really wouldn't have been able to suppress it!" Having not seen an old acquaintance from the Immortal Realm for a long time, the Boundless Wall was exceptionally excited. It worked diligently, helping Bai Shuyue deal with this extremely dangerous immortal bone.

"Remember, never let your consciousness come into contact with the remains. Although the true immortal is deceased, their influence lingers. There is bound to be a remnant will within the bones, and perhaps it could possess a body through resurrection..." Bai Shuyue was already aware of the immortal bone's power and naturally acted cautiously, leaving its handling entirely to the Boundless Wall.

After being digested and absorbed by the Boundless Wall, the immortal bone ultimately transformed into two silver, shimmering characters. "[Turn]" and "[Foresee]." "True Immortal Seal Scripts again," Bai Shuyue sighed, not as excited as the Boundless Wall. "Although the power is immense, I can't use it." A feeling of frustration arose within her.

"Why the long face?" the Boundless Wall asked, noticing Bai Shuyue's odd demeanor. After Bai Shuyue's explanation, the Boundless Wall scoffed, "You are more cautious than I imagined. However, caution is never a bad thing." "You're right; True Immortal Seal Scripts are indeed too flashy. But..."

After a period of contemplation, countless tendrils extended from the void, rewriting the two True Immortal Seal Scripts. "If they, like me, transform into mortals, they naturally won't attract so much attention!" Looking at the masterpiece before him, the Boundless Wall preened with satisfaction.

Bai Shuyue examined the "[Turn]" and "[Foresee]" characters modified by the Boundless Wall. Although their power had significantly decreased, their core characteristics remained unchanged. They still retained the properties of altering the trajectory of power and foreseeing one's own death. "If you're still not at ease, you could integrate your Dao with the items, transforming these two True Immortal Seal Scripts into magical treasures! While in their normal state, their power will remain below the True Immortal level. However, in critical moments, you can unseal them and reveal their true forms," the Boundless Wall elaborated endlessly.

"Truly worthy of being from before the Saint Monarch's gate; you do have some skills," Bai Shuyue praised sincerely. Transforming into mortals and integrating with objects—these two methods finally allowed Bai Shuyue to find a way to greatly increase her combat power without attracting the attention of the mysterious golden-needled expert. Restrain, Seize, Turn, Foresee. Understanding these four True Immortal Seal Scripts greatly broadened Bai Shuyue's horizons.

From then on, Bai Shuyue settled within the Boundless Wall, diligently consolidating her gains, striving to deduce the next level of the New New Method. Unexpectedly, after only fifty years, the Boundless Wall began to grow impatient. "Why has it been so long, and your cultivation is still stagnant?" "At this rate, when will you reach the stage of Transcendence?"

Bai Shuyue also felt a sense of helplessness. "The immortal path is broken; the method of transmitting laws is blocked. I can only forge a new path. Creating something from nothing, how can it be so simple?"

After a moment of silence, the Boundless Wall grumbled, "Regardless, this isn't working. It's too slow, far too slow. Your so-called New New Method has an incredibly high conception. Even in the Immortal Realm back then, it would be considered quite remarkable, worthy of the Saint Monarch's attention. Although your talent is high, it's still not enough to fully deduce it." "Let me think..."

After a long while, the Boundless Wall's single eye turned, and it had an idea. "The reason you are forced to create a new method is because the cultivation path of this realm is suppressed by the Law Transmission. As long as the Law Transmission exists, you cannot see the way forward, correct?" Bai Shuyue nodded.

"In that case, let's leave this damned place!" the Boundless Wall exclaimed, excitedly waving its tendrils. "As long as we leave here, there will be no cultivation restrictions. Then, I'll help you, and perhaps in less than a hundred years, you'll touch the Mountains and Seas and ascend to the immortal realm!"

"Leave... the Profound Yellow Realm?" Hearing the Boundless Wall's suggestion, Bai Shuyue was slightly stunned. She had never considered this before. "Didn't they say the starry sky was shattered, and all worlds except the Profound Yellow Realm were destroyed and desolate?"

The Boundless Wall scoffed, "How is that possible? If the lower realms were truly that desolate, they couldn't possibly support a single cultivation world. When I arrived, I clearly saw it. This place is vast; there must be other places with life..." Swayed by the Boundless Wall's words, Bai Shuyue was genuinely moved. After all, the situation in the Profound Yellow Realm was dire. If she could break free from its confines and find a pure land...

"But if it were so easy to leave the Profound Yellow Realm, I'm sure many cultivators would have fled already. I've never heard of such a thing before." The Boundless Wall sneered, "How can ordinary cultivators compare to one standing before the Saint Monarch? Rest assured, I will definitely protect your safety and get you out of here!"

Seeing the Boundless Wall's confident declaration, Bai Shuyue decided to trust it for the time being. Her only concern was whether her reincarnation rebirth would still be effective after leaving the Profound Yellow Realm. "Worrying is useless. Let's go out and see first. If it doesn't work, we can always come back." After a fierce internal struggle, Bai Shuyue finally agreed to the Boundless Wall's proposal.

After another ten years of preparation, and having absorbed enough cultivators' lifespans, the Boundless Wall's radiance surged, transforming into a green streak that soared into the sky. It ascended to the ninth heaven at extreme speed. In an instant, it reached the edge of the Profound Yellow Realm. "How is it? I can't say for sure about other things, but my escape skills are top-notch."

As it spoke, the Boundless Wall had already taken Bai Shuyue completely out of the Profound Yellow Realm. Looking at the receding light point in the distance, Bai Shuyue felt a complex mix of emotions. Both reluctance and relief. Just then...

"Hmm? Something's not right!" the Boundless Wall suddenly exclaimed. Its green light surged again, its speed increasing. Bai Shuyue keenly noticed that the Boundless Wall's flight trajectory had shifted inexplicably! "A true immortal is comprehending the Dao nearby?" the Boundless Wall's surprised voice came, but without much panic.

Revealing its true form, a line of characters quietly appeared on the jade tile. The surrounding invisible suction seemed to disappear instantly. Returning to its normal trajectory, the Boundless Wall did not slow down. Instead, it accelerated again, as if fleeing for its life. Until two withered, bony fingers materialized out of thin air. They gently pinched the jade tile. No matter how hard the Boundless Wall struggled, it could not move.

"How dare you! I am before the Saint Monarch; how dare you be so rude!" Even while restrained, the Boundless Wall's arrogance remained undiminished as it yelled at the hungry immortal. Bai Shuyue, hidden within the Boundless Wall, who had been frozen in terror since the hungry immortal's appearance and dared not move, could no longer contain herself upon hearing the Boundless Wall's words. She almost rolled her eyes. Calling itself "Grandfather" to her, calling itself "Young Master" to a true immortal, and now it was bragging about its supposed background. It seemed the Boundless Wall's inability to exert its full strength was because it had "eaten too much" and was stuffed.

"There are but a few sentences you've spoken that are true." If it weren't for the dire situation, Bai Shuyue would have already schemed to torment it in various ways in future reincarnations. The emotional fluctuations of mortals naturally did not enter the hungry immortal's eyes. However, after careful consideration, she agreed to the Boundless Wall's request. This was because, to the hungry immortal, the Boundless Wall and its internal treasures were ultimately dispensable. She was only one step away from achieving the nameless True Immortal realm. Having forged her own Dao path, external possessions were no longer that important. Compared to that, she was more interested in information about the True Immortal "[Effortless]."

With this in mind, the hungry immortal spoke, "I will choose three treasures from within your belly. Then, tell me what you know about my master. If it is true..." "I will let you go."

"Three items?!" the Boundless Wall's voice suddenly became louder. "Hmm?" The Boundless Wall's voice then weakened. "Three it is. No backing out!" The hungry immortal merely let out a cold snort. Her proud expression already spoke volumes.

The Boundless Wall, seeing this, finally relaxed. It began to scan its internal treasures with some heartache, while organizing its thoughts. After a moment, it said, "With True Immortal [Effortless]'s strength and talent, it's naturally not a problem for him to transcend." "However, his repeated interventions to save the Immortal Realm from annihilation were contrary to his Dao path of '[Effortless]'. Each interference was equivalent to a severe blow to his own Dao path. Therefore..." "It is highly likely that he has not left."

The hungry immortal's expression immediately changed upon hearing this. Recalling the fragmented information she had gathered about her master, the hungry immortal began to believe these words. The logic was actually not complicated. However, because "[Effortless]" was her master, she had always seen him as invincible before her. Hence, the hungry immortal had not considered this aspect. "With the Master's strength, he would certainly not perish in the tribulation of the Immortal Realm's destruction. Thus, perhaps the Master is also in the lower realm?"

Thinking this, the hungry immortal's heart trembled. Like wanting to tell one's parents the moment of success, the hungry immortal's desire to achieve enlightenment and break through now was stronger than ever before. "If the Master were to see me achieve the nameless True Immortal realm, he would surely be surprised, right?" the hungry immortal couldn't help but think. In comparison, the treasures of the Saint Monarch's Palace within the Boundless Wall became insignificant.

"Be gone, do not disturb my secluded cultivation." Throwing the Boundless Wall towards the distance, the hungry immortal said coldly. The binding force disappeared. The Boundless Wall did not reply, afraid that she would go back on her word and demand more treasures. It pushed its speed to the limit and fled in a sorry state.

Bai Shuyue, having narrowly escaped death, finally let out a long sigh of relief. Although the Boundless Wall had protected her, and the pressure from the hungry immortal was less than that from the mysterious golden-needled expert, being at someone else's mercy right after leaving the Profound Yellow Realm still made Bai Shuyue very uneasy. She said weakly, "It's too dangerous outside. I think we should return to the Profound Yellow Realm. At least, as long as we're careful..."

Before she could finish speaking, the Boundless Wall's response made Bai Shuyue's heart stop. "The Profound Yellow Realm? Where is there any Profound Yellow Realm now? That woman destroyed the Profound Yellow Realm with a casual flick when she was awakened!" As it spoke, the Boundless Wall showed Bai Shuyue the direction they came from. The cluster of light that represented the Profound Yellow Realm had vanished. The starry sky was dark and silent, with only a few small points of light remaining.

"Fan'er..." Bai Shuyue was completely dumbfounded. She had never imagined that the destruction of the vast Profound Yellow Realm was merely a casual act of a true immortal. "You shouldn't think about revenge now. Once we reach a safe place, let's focus on cultivating. See if your cultivation restrictions have disappeared? With your talent, perhaps you can even surpass that woman and achieve Transcendence before her. Then, you can help us get revenge!" the Boundless Wall said fiercely.

Bai Shuyue, however, turned a deaf ear, still shaken by the destruction of the Profound Yellow Realm. In her past reincarnations, it was at most her own death. The destruction of an entire world was the first time. Half a day later, Bai Shuyue finally recovered. Temporarily suppressing the urge to self-terminate and restart, Bai Shuyue forced herself to calm down and began to comprehend the Great Dao in the dark starry sky.

A moment later... "Such clear Great Dao!" Bai Shuyue exclaimed in shock. If comprehending the Great Dao in the Profound Yellow Realm was like looking through layers of misty fog, then comprehending it in this sea of stars was like viewing an incredibly clear painting up close. As if heaven and earth had suddenly become clear. "The difference is this huge?" Somewhat surprised and delighted, Bai Shuyue immersed herself in the unprecedented comprehension.

At this moment, she keenly sensed a faint will in this sea of stars! "This is..." "The consciousness of the Star Sea?" Bai Shuyue's heart trembled. This was a novel experience for her, something she had never encountered before. She had never imagined that the vast Star Sea beyond the Profound Yellow Realm could actually possess its own consciousness. Naturally, Bai Shuyue wanted to establish a deeper connection with it.

"Go there!" Bai Shuyue pointed to a spot in the darkness. "What for..." the Boundless Wall grumbled unhappily. However, at Bai Shuyue's repeated insistence, it changed direction. As they approached the center of the Star Sea, in Bai Shuyue's eyes, the originally pitch-black Star Sea gradually brightened. She also keenly sensed a burgeoning vitality within this dead Star Sea! However, this wisp of vitality was still extremely weak, so weak that any further disturbance could extinguish it in its cradle. The fragile life, like an infant, evoked pity and tenderness in Bai Shuyue.

A resonance... It was precisely this peculiar emotion that allowed Bai Shuyue to make her first contact with the True Intent of the Origin of the Uttermost Dark Star Sea. The originally vibrant, boundless starry sky. Everything was peaceful. However, dark clouds occasionally flashed by—disturbances from the upper realm. Meteors from the Immortal Realm became increasingly frequent. But they had no significant impact on the survival of the Star Sea itself. Until that day. The immortal Dao collapsed, the Star Sea was destroyed, and calamity spread. A figure, whose face and details were unclear, becoming increasingly faint. It completely disappeared. Only the sound of its light laughter echoed in the Star Sea, on the verge of widespread catastrophe. "What does it have to do with me..." "What does it have to do with me..." "Hahahaha..."

... As if witnessing baby Li Fan being strangled in his cradle, Bai Shuyue's heart suddenly surged with anger. It made her even disregard the gap between immortal and mortal techniques. Towards the direction where the figure disappeared, she questioned, "Who are you!" "Who are you?" Bai Shuyue's voice echoed continuously in the memories of the Star Sea's True Intent. Like ripples upon ripples.

The figure that had completely disappeared actually reappeared, stimulated by the continuous reverberations! No longer laughing wildly, it simply looked at Bai Shuyue. Its expression was somewhat enigmatic. "Interesting." A faint voice sounded, which fell upon Bai Shuyue's ears like thunder. "This... is not in the memories of the Star Sea. It's speaking to me?" "How is that possible?" The illusory existence in her memory had actually become reality. This was a divine ability Bai Shuyue could not even imagine. Like being doused with a basin of cold water, her anger instantly extinguished. Afterward, boundless fear arose. She wanted to escape from the Star Sea's memories. However, she found she could not move.

As if reliving the day the Star Sea calamity struck, the figure approached Bai Shuyue. It attempted to gently stroke her. Just then... "Ah, ah, ah! It's you, you villain!" the Boundless Wall's furious voice suddenly erupted. A plaque, like a flying sword, tore through space and time, smashing into the figure's face.

Seeing the Saint Monarch's Palace plaque, the figure's expression fluctuated slightly. It cautiously scanned its surroundings. Discovering that the attacker was merely a tile, it relaxed. Before it could speak, several streams of light, like a meteor shower, arrived. All targeted the same point. During their flight, they erupted into flames. Upon closing in, they detonated with a resounding boom. Amidst the series of explosions, the illusory space shattered into countless pieces, like glass dropped on the ground. "A pity." "Too far away." As its form vanished, it sighed softly.

Chapter 1624: Boundless Departure from Xuanhuang

The fear of being inexplicably sealed by a powerful expert gradually subsided with the second rebirth. Seeing the revitalized Li Fan, Bai Shuyue felt a long-lost joy surge within her. Her spirits lifted, and Bai Shuyue once again embarked on the path of cultivation.

The fact proved that even with such a "lazy" approach as in the previous life, only living for a few months in a daze, her cultivation talent had still increased with each rebirth. A dangerous thought arose in Bai Shuyue's mind: "If this is the case, why don't I just commit suicide after each revival? Quickly start the next life. By using this method, I can first increase my cultivation talent to an unimaginable level. Then, cultivation will be as easy as eating and drinking. Deriving the New New Method will also be a matter of moments..."

Honestly, Bai Shuyue was quite tempted. In her past twenty-plus reincarnations, she had deeply experienced the benefits of outstanding cultivation talent. The initial difficulty of cultivation was incomparable to the later twenty lives. Even now, Bai Shuyue could hardly imagine what cultivation would be like if her talent were to increase tenfold or a hundredfold.

However, after careful consideration, Bai Shuyue ultimately abandoned this seemingly extremely tempting idea. The reason was fundamental: Bai Shuyue's rebirth was uncontrollable. After each death and loss of consciousness, Bai Shuyue could not be certain if she would be able to revive in the next life. Nor could she be sure how long this cycle of rebirth and reincarnation would last.

"If, in reality, my rebirth has a limit, say fifty times, one hundred times, and I use them all to stack talent, without any effort towards my and Fan'er's future, I would likely regret it terribly."

"It's better to proceed steadily, step by step. After all, although the path ahead is arduous, it's not entirely impossible to overcome." Bai Shuyue took a deep breath, calming the restlessness in her heart.

"If, in the future, I truly encounter a situation where there is no hope of breaking through, perhaps then I can adopt this method."

Bai Shuyue did not rush to the Profound Yellow Realm, but habitually ascended to the peak of Solitude Mountain, reviewing her experiences from the life before the last. "How was that mysterious powerhouse with the golden needles attracted?"

"Could it be Ou Shangtian's elder? The elder coming after the junior?" She quickly dismissed this speculation. "If that were the case, he would have appeared long after I killed Ou Daozi."

"It seems it was the fluctuations from my use of the True Immortal Seal Scripts that attracted him."

"True Immortal Seal Scripts are powerful, but they create too much disturbance..." Bai Shuyue mentally estimated the time it took for the golden-needled expert to appear after she first used the True Immortal Seal Script.

"After using it, I must relocate quickly and hide in a safe location. Furthermore, I cannot use it again for a long time."

"Until I find a way to counter that golden-needled expert." Bai Shuyue formulated a guiding principle for her future actions.

"I wonder how the strength of this mysterious expert compares to the Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerable whom I suppressed? Or perhaps, he *is* the Law-Transmitting Heavenly Venerable?"

"Did the Boundless Wall escape again at the end of the penultimate life?" Carrying this question, Bai Shuyue sought it out again. Relying on her familiarity with the Boundless Wall accumulated over several lifetimes, combined with her transcendent talent, Bai Shuyue regained its trust without much effort.

"What is your current strength? According to the Saint Monarch's doorstep, you should easily be able to block a true immortal." Bai Shuyue asked.

"Hehehe, naturally!" the Boundless Wall said smugly. Seeing the Boundless Wall's performance, Bai Shuyue stared at it suspiciously.

"What is that look?" the Boundless Wall roared.

"How could I, when I make my move, be unable to stop even a common true immortal?" Bai Shuyue continued to stare, confronting it.

Slowly, the Boundless Wall's imposing aura weakened, and it admitted guiltily, "Alright, when I was at my peak, I could indeed easily suppress a true immortal. But currently..."

"As you know, the Immortal Realm was destroyed. To escape disaster, I was forced to shed my immortal realm foundation. Furthermore..." The Boundless Wall lowered its voice.

"I am suppressing the Saint Monarch's Palace plaque within me. Although the writing on the plaque has long since departed, its spiritual essence remains. Naturally, it is unwilling to be perpetually suppressed by me. Thus, I must also divert a significant portion of my power to counter it."

"You have such talent; just cultivate diligently and avoid provoking any major figures. Otherwise, I may not be able to save you." Hearing the Boundless Wall's explanation, Bai Shuyue understood its fate in the penultimate life.

"Rest assured, I won't do anything so foolish."

"Besides, the one I need to deal with is currently just a child." Bai Shuyue looked into the distance.

Guanglan Prefecture, Baoyuan Mountain. With ease, Bai Shuyue found Ou Daozi and Ou Shangtian. Ou Shangtian at this moment was unlike the majestic figure Bai Shuyue saw in her previous life. Due to his immortal bone not yet fully integrating with his body, he frequently suffered from pain and was extremely weak.

Bai Shuyue, acting as a senior, offered to treat Ou Shangtian's illness. Although Ou Daozi was skeptical, facing Bai Shuyue, whose strength far surpassed his own, he had no choice but to accept. Bringing Ou Shangtian back into the Boundless Wall, the two worked together to finally extract the immortal bone from his body.

After exchanging the restored and healthy Ou Shangtian, Ou Daozi expressed his profuse gratitude. The Boundless Wall, however, was in an uproar.

"Good heavens, what a marvel!"

"It actually brought an immortal bone, and its rank from its true immortal life was not low!"

"Fortunately, it's only a small piece of bone left. Otherwise, I really wouldn't have been able to suppress it!" Having not seen an old acquaintance from the Immortal Realm for a long time, the Boundless Wall was exceptionally excited. It worked diligently, helping Bai Shuyue deal with this extremely dangerous immortal bone.

"Remember, never let your consciousness come into contact with the remains. Although the true immortal is deceased, their influence lingers. There is bound to be a remnant will within the bones, and perhaps it could possess a body through resurrection..." Bai Shuyue was already aware of the immortal bone's power and naturally acted cautiously, leaving its handling entirely to the Boundless Wall.

After being digested and absorbed by the Boundless Wall, the immortal bone ultimately transformed into two silver, shimmering characters. "[Turn]" and "[Foresee]."

"True Immortal Seal Scripts again," Bai Shuyue sighed, not as excited as the Boundless Wall. "Although the power is immense, I can't use it." A feeling of frustration arose within her.

"Why the long face?" the Boundless Wall asked, noticing Bai Shuyue's odd demeanor. After Bai Shuyue's explanation, the Boundless Wall scoffed, "You are more cautious than I imagined. However, caution is never a bad thing."

"You're right; True Immortal Seal Scripts are indeed too flashy. But..." After a period of contemplation, countless tendrils extended from the void, rewriting the two True Immortal Seal Scripts.

"If they, like me, transform into mortals, they naturally won't attract so much attention!" Looking at the masterpiece before him, the Boundless Wall preened with satisfaction.

Bai Shuyue examined the "[Turn]" and "[Foresee]" characters modified by the Boundless Wall. Although their power had significantly decreased, their core characteristics remained unchanged. They still retained the properties of altering the trajectory of power and foreseeing one's own death.

"If you're still not at ease, you could integrate your Dao with the items, transforming these two True Immortal Seal Scripts into magical treasures! While in their normal state, their power will remain below the True Immortal level. However, in critical moments, you can unseal them and reveal their true forms," the Boundless Wall elaborated endlessly.

"Truly worthy of being from before the Saint Monarch's gate; you do have some skills," Bai Shuyue praised sincerely. Transforming into mortals and integrating with objects—these two methods finally allowed Bai Shuyue to find a way to greatly increase her combat power without attracting the attention of the mysterious golden-needled expert.

Restrain, Seize, Turn, Foresee. Understanding these four True Immortal Seal Scripts greatly broadened Bai Shuyue's horizons. From then on, Bai Shuyue settled within the Boundless Wall, diligently consolidating her gains, striving to deduce the next level of the New New Method.

Unexpectedly, after only fifty years, the Boundless Wall began to grow impatient. "Why has it been so long, and your cultivation is still stagnant?"

"At this rate, when will you reach the stage of Transcendence?"

Bai Shuyue also felt a sense of helplessness. "The immortal path is broken; the method of transmitting laws is blocked. I can only forge a new path. Creating something from nothing, how can it be so simple?"

After a moment of silence, the Boundless Wall grumbled, "Regardless, this isn't working. It's too slow, far too slow. Your so-called New New Method has an incredibly high conception. Even in the Immortal Realm back then, it would be considered quite remarkable, worthy of the Saint Monarch's attention. Although your talent is high, it's still not enough to fully deduce it."

"Let me think..." After a long while, the Boundless Wall's single eye turned, and it had an idea. "The reason you are forced to create a new method is because the cultivation path of this realm is suppressed by the Law Transmission. As long as the Law Transmission exists, you cannot see the way forward, correct?"

Bai Shuyue nodded.

"In that case, let's leave this damned place!" the Boundless Wall exclaimed, excitedly waving its tendrils. "As long as we leave here, there will be no cultivation restrictions. Then, I'll help you, and perhaps in less than a hundred years, you'll touch the Mountains and Seas and ascend to the immortal realm!"

"Leave... the Profound Yellow Realm?" Hearing the Boundless Wall's suggestion, Bai Shuyue was slightly stunned. She had never considered this before.

"Didn't they say the starry sky was shattered, and all worlds except the Profound Yellow Realm were destroyed and desolate?"

The Boundless Wall scoffed, "How is that possible? If the lower realms were truly that desolate, they couldn't possibly support a single cultivation world. When I arrived, I clearly saw it. This place is vast; there must be other places with life..."

Swayed by the Boundless Wall's words, Bai Shuyue was genuinely moved. After all, the situation in the Profound Yellow Realm was dire. If she could break free from its confines and find a pure land...

"But if it were so easy to leave the Profound Yellow Realm, I'm sure many cultivators would have fled already. I've never heard of such a thing before."

The Boundless Wall sneered, "How can ordinary cultivators compare to one standing before the Saint Monarch? Rest assured, I will definitely protect your safety and get you out of here!" Seeing the Boundless Wall's confident declaration, Bai Shuyue decided to trust it for the time being. Her only concern was whether her reincarnation rebirth would still be effective after leaving the Profound Yellow Realm.

"Worrying is useless. Let's go out and see first. If it doesn't work, we can always come back." After a fierce internal struggle, Bai Shuyue finally agreed to the Boundless Wall's proposal.

After another ten years of preparation, and having absorbed enough cultivators' lifespans, the Boundless Wall's radiance surged, transforming into a green streak that soared into the sky. It ascended to the ninth heaven at extreme speed. In an instant, it reached the edge of the Profound Yellow Realm.

"How is it? I can't say for sure about other things, but my escape skills are top-notch." As it spoke, the Boundless Wall had already taken Bai Shuyue completely out of the Profound Yellow Realm. Looking at the receding light point in the distance, Bai Shuyue felt a complex mix of emotions. Both reluctance and relief.

Just then... "Hmm? Something's not right!" the Boundless Wall suddenly exclaimed. Its green light surged again, its speed increasing. Bai Shuyue keenly noticed that the Boundless Wall's flight trajectory had shifted inexplicably!

"A true immortal is comprehending the Dao nearby?" the Boundless Wall's surprised voice came, but without much panic. Revealing its true form, a line of characters quietly appeared on the jade tile. The surrounding invisible suction seemed to disappear instantly. Returning to its normal trajectory, the Boundless Wall did not slow down. Instead, it accelerated again, as if fleeing for its life.

Until two withered, bony fingers materialized out of thin air. They gently pinched the jade tile. No matter how hard the Boundless Wall struggled, it could not move.

"How dare you! I am before the Saint Monarch; how dare you be so rude!" Even while restrained, the Boundless Wall's arrogance remained undiminished as it yelled at the hungry immortal.

Bai Shuyue, hidden within the Boundless Wall, who had been frozen in terror since the hungry immortal's appearance and dared not move, could not help but roll her eyes upon hearing the Boundless Wall's words. It called itself "Grandfather" to her, "Young Master" to a true immortal, and now it was bragging about its supposed background. It seemed the Boundless Wall's inability to exert its full strength was because it had "eaten too much" and was stuffed.

"There are but a few sentences you've spoken that are true." If it weren't for the dire situation, Bai Shuyue would have already schemed to torment it in various ways in future reincarnations.

The emotional fluctuations of mortals naturally did not enter the hungry immortal's eyes. However, after careful consideration, she agreed to the Boundless Wall's request. This was because, to the hungry immortal, the Boundless Wall and its internal treasures were ultimately dispensable. She was only one step away from achieving the nameless True Immortal realm. Having forged her own Dao path, external possessions were no longer that important. Compared to that, she was more interested in information about the True Immortal "[Effortless]."

With this in mind, the hungry immortal spoke, "I will choose three treasures from within your belly. Then, tell me what you know about my master. If it is true..."

"I will let you go."

"Three items?!" the Boundless Wall's voice suddenly became louder. "Hmm?" The Boundless Wall's voice then weakened. "Three it is. No backing out!" The hungry immortal merely let out a cold snort. Her proud expression already spoke volumes.

The Boundless Wall, seeing this, finally relaxed. It began to scan its internal treasures with some heartache, while organizing its thoughts. After a moment, it said, "With True Immortal [Effortless]'s strength and talent, it's naturally not a problem for him to transcend."

"However, his repeated interventions to save the Immortal Realm from annihilation were contrary to his Dao path of '[Effortless]'. Each interference was equivalent to a severe blow to his own Dao path. Therefore..."

"It is highly likely that he has not left." The hungry immortal's expression immediately changed upon hearing this. Recalling the fragmented information she had gathered about her master, the hungry immortal began to believe these words. The logic was actually not complicated. However, because "[Effortless]" was her master, she had always seen him as invincible before her. Hence, the hungry immortal had not considered this aspect.

"With the Master's strength, he would certainly not perish in the tribulation of the Immortal Realm's destruction. Thus, perhaps the Master is also in the lower realm?" Thinking this, the hungry immortal's heart trembled. Like wanting to tell one's parents the moment of success, the hungry immortal's desire to achieve enlightenment and break through now was stronger than ever before.

"If the Master were to see me achieve the nameless True Immortal realm, he would surely be surprised, right?" the hungry immortal couldn't help but think. In comparison, the treasures of the Saint Monarch's Palace within the Boundless Wall became insignificant.

"Be gone, do not disturb my secluded cultivation." Throwing the Boundless Wall towards the distance, the hungry immortal said coldly. The binding force disappeared. The Boundless Wall did not reply, afraid that she would go back on her word and demand more treasures. It pushed its speed to the limit and fled in a sorry state.

Bai Shuyue, having narrowly escaped death, finally let out a long sigh of relief. Although the Boundless Wall had protected her, and the pressure from the hungry immortal was less than that from the mysterious golden-needled expert, being at someone else's mercy right after leaving the Profound Yellow Realm still made Bai Shuyue very uneasy. She said weakly, "It's too dangerous outside. I think we should return to the Profound Yellow Realm. At least, as long as we're careful..."

Before she could finish speaking, the Boundless Wall's response made Bai Shuyue's heart stop. "The Profound Yellow Realm? Where is there any Profound Yellow Realm now? That woman destroyed the Profound Yellow Realm with a casual flick when she was awakened!" As it spoke, the Boundless Wall showed Bai Shuyue the direction they came from. The cluster of light that represented the Profound Yellow Realm had vanished. The starry sky was dark and silent, with only a few small points of light remaining.

"Fan'er..." Bai Shuyue was completely dumbfounded. She had never imagined that the destruction of the vast Profound Yellow Realm was merely a casual act of a true immortal.

"You shouldn't think about revenge now. Once we reach a safe place, let's focus on cultivating. See if your cultivation restrictions have disappeared? With your talent, perhaps you can even surpass that woman and achieve Transcendence before her. Then, you can help us get revenge!" the Boundless Wall said fiercely.

Bai Shuyue, however, turned a deaf ear, still shaken by the destruction of the Profound Yellow Realm. In her past reincarnations, it was at most her own death. The destruction of an entire world was the first time. Half a day later, Bai Shuyue finally recovered. Temporarily suppressing the urge to self-terminate and restart, Bai Shuyue forced herself to calm down and began to comprehend the Great Dao in the dark starry sky.

A moment later... "Such clear Great Dao!" Bai Shuyue exclaimed in shock. If comprehending the Great Dao in the Profound Yellow Realm was like looking through layers of misty fog, then comprehending it in this sea of stars was like viewing an incredibly clear painting up close. As if heaven and earth had suddenly become clear. "The difference is this huge?"

Somewhat surprised and delighted, Bai Shuyue immersed herself in the unprecedented comprehension. At this moment, she keenly sensed a faint will in this sea of stars! "This is..."

"The consciousness of the Star Sea?" Bai Shuyue's heart trembled. This was a novel experience for her, something she had never encountered before. She had never imagined that the vast Star Sea beyond the Profound Yellow Realm could actually possess its own consciousness. Naturally, Bai Shuyue wanted to establish a deeper connection with it.

"Go there!" Bai Shuyue pointed to a spot in the darkness. "What for..." the Boundless Wall grumbled unhappily. However, at Bai Shuyue's repeated insistence, it changed direction. As they approached the center of the Star Sea, in Bai Shuyue's eyes, the originally pitch-black Star Sea gradually brightened. She also keenly sensed a burgeoning vitality within this dead Star Sea! However, this wisp of vitality was still extremely weak, so weak that any further disturbance could extinguish it in its cradle.

The fragile life, like an infant, evoked pity and tenderness in Bai Shuyue. A resonance... It was precisely this peculiar emotion that allowed Bai Shuyue to make her first contact with the True Intent of the Origin of the Uttermost Dark Star Sea.

The originally vibrant, boundless starry sky. Everything was peaceful. However, dark clouds occasionally flashed by—disturbances from the upper realm. Meteors from the Immortal Realm became increasingly frequent. But they had no significant impact on the survival of the Star Sea itself. Until that day. The immortal Dao collapsed, the Star Sea was destroyed, and calamity spread.

A figure, whose face and details were unclear, becoming increasingly faint. It completely disappeared. Only the sound of its light laughter echoed in the Star Sea, on the verge of widespread catastrophe. "What does it have to do with me..." "What does it have to do with me..." "Hahahaha..."

... As if witnessing baby Li Fan being strangled in his cradle, Bai Shuyue's heart suddenly surged with anger. It made her even disregard the gap between immortal and mortal techniques. Towards the direction where the figure disappeared, she questioned, "Who are you!"

"Who are you?" Bai Shuyue's voice echoed continuously in the memories of the Star Sea's True Intent. Like ripples upon ripples. The figure that had completely disappeared actually reappeared, stimulated by the continuous reverberations! No longer laughing wildly, it simply looked at Bai Shuyue. Its expression was somewhat enigmatic.

"Interesting." A faint voice sounded, which fell upon Bai Shuyue's ears like thunder. "This... is not in the memories of the Star Sea. It's speaking to me?" "How is that possible?" The illusory existence in her memory had actually become reality. This was a divine ability Bai Shuyue could not even imagine.

Like being doused with a basin of cold water, her anger instantly extinguished. Afterward, boundless fear arose. She wanted to escape from the Star Sea's memories. However, she found she could not move. As if reliving the day the Star Sea calamity struck, the figure approached Bai Shuyue. It attempted to gently stroke her.

Just then... "Ah, ah, ah! It's you, you villain!" the Boundless Wall's furious voice suddenly erupted. A plaque, like a flying sword, tore through space and time, smashing into the figure's face.

Seeing the Saint Monarch's Palace plaque, the figure's expression fluctuated slightly. It cautiously scanned its surroundings. Discovering that the attacker was merely a tile, it relaxed. Before it could speak, several streams of light, like a meteor shower, arrived. All targeted the same point. During their flight, they erupted into flames. Upon closing in, they detonated with a resounding boom.

Amidst the series of explosions, the illusory space shattered into countless pieces, like glass dropped on the ground. "A pity." "Too far away." As its form vanished, it sighed softly.

Chapter 1625: Seeing He Ganxian Again

"With your talent, I can confidently entrust it to you." Although it said this, the Boundless Wall's large eyeball still looked somewhat reluctant. It slowly and sluggishly revealed the "[Seize]" technique. Bai Shuyue saw its behavior and felt strange. It had not even concealed the Saint Monarch's Palace plaque, so there was no reason for it to hide a mere True Immortal Seal Script. It was only after Bai Shuyue deciphered the "[Seize]" technique that she understood why. With flowing strokes, a golden True Immortal Seal Script instantly formed in the air. The Boundless Wall's eyes flickered, having already retreated far away before the "[Seize]" technique appeared.

"Miss Bai! We agreed that the [Seize] technique was to deal with that brat with the golden hair. Why are you using it on me now?" Bai Shuyue did not answer, merely waving her other hand. The "[Restrain]" technique in the air instantly appeared. Like two suns shining together, they illuminated the nine heavens! The Boundless Wall's eyes showed panic as it retreated even further.

"The '[Restrain]' and '[Seize]' characters both belong to the unique seal scripts of the Immortal Court. They were special means used by the Immortal Court to suppress the myriad immortals. When combined, they are like immortal soldiers and generals setting up a formation to search for enemies, their power being several times greater than any individual character." "By casting these two talismans, I can not only suppress and plunder the Boundless Wall but also plunder its private collection. The Saint Monarch's Palace plaque..." For a moment, Bai Shuyue did consider such a thought. However, in recent lives, memories of spending time with the Boundless Wall flashed through her mind. She ultimately did not act. "Humans are not insensible beings; how can one be without feelings? In this life, it has shown me kindness. I cannot repay kindness with enmity. When the next life begins anew, with no past ties and debts between us, it will be time enough." Thinking this, the '[Restrain]' and '[Seize]' characters in the air hovered gently and then dissipated. Bai Shuyue looked at the Boundless Wall, still hiding far away, and chuckled, "It's just my divine ability at its nascent stage; I was merely testing its feel. Why are you so nervous? We are life-and-death allies; how could I possibly harm you!" The Boundless Wall observed for a while longer, and seeing that Bai Shuyue showed no signs of hostility, it finally relaxed. It said smugly, "I was merely testing you. Since I dared to teach you these two characters, naturally I have a way to break them. If you had truly attacked me, hmph..." Whether its words were true or not, Bai Shuyue silently bore them in mind.

"With my divine ability formed, it's time to seek revenge on that brat. He caused us such a mess; it's simply outrageous!" the Boundless Wall said excitedly. In its view, being humiliated by a mortal was absolutely unacceptable. It had to reclaim its honor, or its title of "Before the Saint Monarch's Gate" would be meaningless! Bai Shuyue, however, remained calm. "There's no need to seek him out. We just need to wait here, like a hunter waiting for prey." Bai Shuyue's premonition was not wrong. Ou Shangtian seemed to possess a special tracking method; even from a great distance, he could easily pinpoint their location. After ambushing them for less than three days, Ou Shangtian's aura was faintly detected on the horizon, rapidly approaching. However, strangely, just as he was about to enter the ambush zone, Ou Shangtian stopped without warning. After a brief pause, he turned and left without hesitation.

"Such sharp intuition!" Bai Shuyue was greatly surprised and no longer hesitated. The two True Immortal Seal Scripts were unleashed simultaneously. Myriad golden chains and a pale, massive hand suddenly appeared in the sky, trapping Ou Shangtian within.

"Invert the Heavens and Earth!"

A furious roar resounded, attempting to scatter the sealing power of the True Immortal Seal Scripts. However, seemingly affected by the "[Seize]" technique, the immortal bone within Ou Shangtian's body rapidly retracted its golden light. His divine power vanished instantly, as if it had never existed. Empowered by immortal bone, Ou Shangtian became ordinary! Like falling from the clouds to the earth, having lost the enhancement of the two immortal artifacts, Ou Shangtian was, without suspense, successfully suppressed and captured by Bai Shuyue.

"Good, good, good! I'll let you chase again!" The Boundless Wall, which had disappeared during the battle, now revealed itself triumphantly, wielding dozens of tendrils and incessantly tormenting the tightly bound Ou Shangtian. "I'll slowly dig out your immortal bone, inch by inch, later!" the Boundless Wall whispered with a hidden laugh, its single eye pressed close to Ou Shangtian's face. "Kill me or dismember me, as you wish! Don't think I'll fear you two wicked thieves!" Ou Shangtian, unfazed, cursed them. The Boundless Wall flew into a rage, and five tendrils plunged into Ou Shangtian's body, churning vigorously. Ou Shangtian nearly convulsed in pain, yet he endured it, not uttering a single sound, let alone begging for mercy. This stubbornness only further enraged the Boundless Wall. It resolved to employ more brutal methods, determined to make the mortal boy submit.

Compared to this, Bai Shuyue frowned slightly while watching Ou Shangtian's display. A wave of emotion washed over her. "Wicked thieves... I never thought that one day, others would call me by such a name." "Speaking of which, we were in the wrong initially, accidentally killing his father. Seeking revenge for a loved one is only natural. Moreover, this youth, despite suffering such cruel punishment, remains steadfast." "Yes, he's a good child, just like Fan'er." "Let's just give him a quick end." With this thought, Bai Shuyue interrupted the Boundless Wall's torment. The tendrils instantly drained Ou Shangtian's lifespan, and after extracting the two immortal artifacts from his body, Bai Shuyue intended to leave. To find a safe place and meticulously study the spoils she had obtained. However, she hadn't flown far when a strong sense of unease surged within her. She scanned her surroundings with suspicion but found no source of the unease. Judging by the Boundless Wall's reaction, it was clearly not her imagination.

"Hurry and escape! We seem to be targeted by something!" Bai Shuyue's expression turned grim as she fled with all her might, but the unease in her heart only intensified. Finally, nine golden needles descended from the sky, instantly sealing off Bai Shuyue from all directions! After a moment of stunned silence, Bai Shuyue reacted. She intended to use the True Immortal Seal Script again to defend herself. Unexpectedly... A pale hand silently appeared above her head. It gently pressed a long golden needle into her Baihui acupoint. The golden needle entered her body, piercing her skull. Her entire being seemed frozen, her expression caught between shock and panic. Not only could her entire body not move, but even her thoughts were sealed in ice. The Boundless Wall, disregarding any camaraderie, let out a startled cry and prepared to flee. But it was interrupted by a light hum. Two fingers gently pinched the jade tile. The Boundless Wall trembled and struggled incessantly, its jade surface revealing the blurred outline of the Saint Monarch's Palace plaque.

"Hmm?" After a voice filled with both surprise and delight, the Heavenly Physician slowly revealed himself. He quickly tapped the surface of the Boundless Wall several times. The Saint Monarch's Palace plaque, which had been trying to break free, trembled slightly and then fell silent again. The Boundless Wall itself seemed to have fallen into a slumber, just like Bai Shuyue. Looking at the temporarily sealed person and artifact before him, the Heavenly Physician pondered. Not long ago, he had been searching near the remnant Great Wall beneath the high walls for suitable fragments of cultivation worlds. Unexpectedly, he suddenly sensed fluctuations in True Immortal Seal Script energies from the Profound Yellow Realm. Although it wasn't the same one that caused the catastrophe in the Heavenly Law Realm years ago, the Heavenly Physician decided to return and investigate. After all, the Profound Yellow Realm was of great importance, and no mistakes could be tolerated. Later, sensing the appearance of a second True Immortal Seal Script, the Heavenly Physician's return speeded up. "The Profound Yellow Realm has been peaceful for a long time. Now, within a short period, two True Immortal Seal Scripts have appeared... What exactly happened?" The Heavenly Physician was filled with doubt and uncertainty. Upon arriving near the Profound Yellow Realm, the two True Immortal Seal Scripts erupted once more. The Heavenly Physician followed the trail, pinpointing the source of the True Immortal Seal Scripts. "This jade tile seems to be an item from the Immortal Realm. And that plaque on the jade tile just now..." "The Tai Yi Palace?" The Heavenly Physician's expression turned grave. Although the Boundless Wall's origin was extraordinary, the Heavenly Physician's gaze remained fixed on Bai Shuyue. "In the moment before I sealed her, this woman's thoughts were rather strange." "On the surface, she seemed shocked and fearful, but deep down..." The Heavenly Physician frowned, flying around the immobilized Bai Shuyue several times. "Fearless?" "Does she have some other reliance?" The more the Heavenly Physician observed, the more he felt his intuition was correct. Golden needles of various lengths were arranged, and the Heavenly Physician prepared to conduct a more thorough examination of Bai Shuyue. "If the Heavenly Demon were still here, this wouldn't be so troublesome. Alas, I need his power to suppress the transmission of the Dao." Thinking this, the Heavenly Physician held the needle, preparing to pierce Bai Shuyue's forehead. Just as the golden needle was about to penetrate, a crisp snapping sound echoed through the heavens and earth. The Heavenly Physician's movement instantly halted. His expression, like Bai Shuyue's before him, became frozen in time. In fact, it wasn't just the Heavenly Physician; the entire Profound Yellow Realm fell into a state of stagnation with that light sound. Li Fan's figure appeared on the scene. Looking at the scene before him, he shook his head slightly. "Fortunately, I was vigilant back then. Otherwise, this would be the end of the line." "But it's alright. Auntie, I'll help you!" Li Fan took the Heavenly Physician's hand and forcefully thrust the uninserted golden needle into him. In an instant, many scenarios were filled in. Then... "True and False!" The Saint Creation Plan, the twenty-eighth generation! Bai Shuyue woke up from her nightmare, unable to recover for a long time. This time, the shock she felt was even more intense than during her first "rebirth." She subconsciously touched her head, as if the pain there had not yet dissipated. After the golden needle pierced her, her consciousness had frozen, so she did not know how she had died. However, she still retained some vague images in her mind. Treated like an object, golden needles filled her entire body. And later, she was dismembered into countless pieces... Even recalling the faint residual memories of the previous life, Bai Shuyue's face turned instantly deathly pale. "Ugh..." Instinctively bending over, she vomited uncontrollably. Her body trembled violently, unable to stop. Months passed, and she still hadn't recovered. After all, despite Bai Shuyue's twenty-plus layerings of spirituality, making her incredibly talented, her experiences could not match her current aptitude. It was fine if she died normally before, but after encountering the Heavenly Physician in the previous life and undergoing such inhuman torture, Bai Shuyue became terrified. She did not want to, nor dared to, nor wished to venture into the Profound Yellow Realm again. "The Profound Yellow Realm is simply too dangerous and terrifying." "Living as a mortal emperor in Great Xuan, staying put, wouldn't that be good too." Once this thought arose, it spread like wildfire, impossible to extinguish. Bai Shuyue dared not even speculate about the true identity of the figure who appeared at the end of the previous life. She chose to bury her head in the sand and escape. Li Fan's actions were within Bai Shuyue's expectations. After all, Li Fan had personally implanted the images in Bai Shuyue's mind. "This is her inner demon." "As long as she overcomes this hurdle, her path ahead will be clear, and nothing will hinder her. Even if she encounters any danger in the future, she will not despair but will still press forward." "And if she cannot overcome it..." "Heh heh, with my help, how could she possibly not overcome it?" To resolve Bai Shuyue's inner demon, Li Fan made a dramatic appearance. Bai Shuyue was terrified. During the months she was bedridden, it was Li Fan, who acted completely out of character, who diligently cared for her, without complaint. Bai Shuyue's complexion slowly improved. However, Li Fan, overworked and exhausted, grew thinner day by day. Yet, he still forced a smile, not wanting Bai Shuyue to worry. Until... "Auntie, lunch is ready. I learned a new dish, bean rice and wild greens. Come and try it quickly." Li Fan, holding a wooden tray filled with dishes, entered Bai Shuyue's room. Bai Shuyue looked at him, her heart aching, and was about to speak. She saw Li Fan, staggering with unsteady steps, fall to the ground. The shattering of the porcelain bowl sounded like thunder, striking Bai Shuyue's heart. "Fan'er!" The roles reversed. Now, it was Li Fan who was bedridden. "This is exhaustion taking its toll; the illness of natural decline has struck prematurely." Bai Shuyue, having mastered medicine, immediately recognized the cause of Li Fan's illness. Guilt flashed in her heart. "If I hadn't been so flustered and fearful, unwilling to pay attention to the world around me, Fan'er wouldn't have ended up like this in this life. He's only twenty years old!" Accompanying Li Fan through the final period of his life, Bai Shuyue stood before Li Fan's grave six months later, her expression grief-stricken. It had been a long time since she had experienced the sorrow of an elder burying a younger one. And after going through this ordeal, Bai Shuyue finally understood that even after so many reincarnations, the seemingly weakened familial affection had not diminished in the slightest! Li Fan was still as dear to her as her own flesh and blood. She was still the only relative Li Fan could rely on in the world! "Fan'er, it's okay." "Auntie will come find you now." At Li Fan's grave, Bai Shuyue took her own life. The twenty-ninth generation of the Saint Creation Plan began.

Chapter 1626: Faceless Virtuous Immortal

"Ah, ah, ah, this time it's a real heavy loss..." The wailings of the Boundless Wall continuously echoed in Bai Shuyue's ears.

Like striking copper bells, they slowly brought back Bai Shuyue's lost divine soul.

As if waking from a deep dream, she cleared her mind from the terrifying experience she had just endured.

Just as she was about to speak, she suddenly found that she couldn't speak at all!

"Wuwuwu..." Terrified, Bai Shuyue instinctively reached out to touch her face, wanting to see what was happening.

It was better not to touch, but the moment she did, her heart was even more shocked.

She quickly used the Water Mirror Technique to check, and this time she finally confirmed.

Her facial features had all disappeared!

Even the curve and appearance of her entire face were vaguely similar to the figure she encountered in the memories of the Star Sea Origin True Intent just now!

"It's just losing your face, what's there to be afraid of? At least you saved your life." The comforting voice of the Boundless Wall came in time, making Bai Shuyue feel a little relieved.

"It's really bad luck. I just escaped from that hateful woman. Then I met this great evildoer! I almost lost my pants! I say, when you transcend in the future, you must repay me handsomely!"

"To save you, I've really suffered heavy losses. I'm not lying this time. You must be careful next time..." The Boundless Wall babbled, sighing.

Knowing the Boundless Wall's greedy nature, yet it was willing to give up a pile of treasures from its belly to save her, Bai Shuyue couldn't help but feel a warmth in her heart.

"Don't worry, if I have the day of transcendence, I will never forget your past help." Bai Shuyue said very solemnly.

The Boundless Wall was overjoyed upon hearing this.

Little did it know that Bai Shuyue's promise was far more significant than it imagined, because Bai Shuyue was not referring to this life, but to every life since their contact and in the future.

In adversity, the relationship between the two deepened.

With the Boundless Wall leading Bai Shuyue to flee at extreme speed, they soon arrived at the fringe of the Utmost Dark Star Sea.

Seeing the continuous world remnants in the distance, Bai Shuyue was filled with shock.

"As long as we cross the formation ahead, we should be able to escape from here."

"But..."

"This formation seems to have a dual guiding path, pointing to different locations." The Boundless Wall pondered after observing for a while.

"Forget it, it's better not to attract trouble. Finding a safe place to cultivate is the most important thing." Soon, the Boundless Wall came to a conclusion.

Without consulting Bai Shuyue, it charged towards the high wall.

A green light flashed, and they crossed over.

In the next instant, Bai Shuyue had already left the Utmost Dark Star Sea.

"The Great Dao... seems to be a bit richer." Bai Shuyue sensed it keenly.

However, due to the lesson just learned, she was very cautious and did not immediately comprehend the Great Dao. Instead, she observed carefully first.

The Boundless Wall sped towards the vibrant area in the distance.

"I knew it! There must be other places suitable for cultivation outside the Profound Yellow Realm!"

Seeing that the Northern Star Sea was getting closer, the Boundless Wall became a little too conceited.

"Cultivate well, and transcend as soon as possible."

It exhorted Bai Shuyue.

Suddenly, for some unknown reason, the speed of the Boundless Wall's flight slowed down.

Innumerable crisscrossing thin lines appeared around, like a giant net, blocking the Boundless Wall.

Before the Boundless Wall and Bai Shuyue could react, they had already plunged headfirst into the Dao net.

"Immortal artifact?" With a cold snort, a transparent giant hand appeared in the void and instantly grabbed the Boundless Wall.

Having escaped from the Hungry Immortal and Ho Gan Immortal, the Boundless Wall had exhausted its foundation. At this moment, it could no longer struggle and was slowly suppressed by the Dao net.

"Damn it! How could this be!" Before the Boundless Wall's consciousness disappeared, it cried out in rage.

Inside the Boundless Wall, looking at the layered defensive formations that were about to shatter around them, Bai Shuyue sighed.

"It's too dangerous outside. It's better to just stay honestly in the Profound Yellow Realm."

Her eyes flickered, and she made up her mind.

Bai Shuyue died by suicide for the second time!

However, the reincarnation did not end here.

A green light flashed, and the Boundless Wall, which was clearly suppressed by the Dao net, instantly escaped.

It disappeared in an instant without a trace.

The transparent giant hand was full of surprise. It searched around for a long time, but ultimately could no longer find the trace of the Boundless Wall.

In the center of the Utmost Dark Star Sea, where the Star Sea Origin True Intent was most active.

The Boundless Wall suddenly appeared.

"Hahaha, I knew I wouldn't die!"

Overjoyed at regaining its freedom, the Boundless Wall was extremely proud.

When it checked its surroundings, it was suddenly alarmed: "Oh no, why did I come back here?"

Then, it let out a muffled cry: "Ah, alas, little girl, why did you die so easily! It's over, it's all over..."

Just as the Boundless Wall was unable to accept it and kept wailing.

Li Fan quietly appeared beside his aunt's corpse, looking at her face that had been stripped of its features. He gently placed his hands on it.

"Presumptuous! Who are you, to dare defile..." The Boundless Wall hadn't finished speaking before its voice abruptly stopped, as if its mouth had been gagged.

But it wasn't Li Fan who stopped him. Li Fan was examining his aunt's memories from before her death.

Instead, upon seeing Li Fan, the Boundless Wall was so terrified that it couldn't speak.

Having seen countless True Immortals in the Immortal Realm, even successive Immortal Emperors.

Its intuition told the Boundless Wall that the person before it was very dangerous.

Extremely dangerous!

The Boundless Wall's intuition was not ordinary. It was able to survive the great tribulation of the Immortal Realm's destruction and even plunder the Dao Palace, all thanks to its intuition.

And the reason it was willing to reveal its treasured possessions to Bai Shuyue was because its intuition told it that Bai Shuyue was a good person. Helping her once would bring ten times the reward in the future! However, it never expected that Bai Shuyue would die so easily.

Moreover, she encountered such an extremely dangerous individual...

"Don't see me, don't see me, don't see me..." The Boundless Wall repeatedly recited in its heart, not daring to make any sound.

It was like the days when it lay still on top of the Taiyi Palace years ago.

Li Fan naturally noticed the Boundless Wall's small movements.

However, at this moment, he no longer needed to concern himself with it. If the Saint Monarch himself were present, he would have taken it seriously.

It was merely a tile used by the Saint Monarch to build a Dao Palace in one of the countless possibilities...

It would be beneath Li Fan to even acknowledge it.

"Ho Gan Immortal."

"Virtuous Immortal."

"What does it have to do with me? What a Virtuous Immortal!"

Exiting from his aunt's memories, Li Fan gently brushed his hand, expelling the residual influence of immortal energy.

The blank face slowly recovered its original appearance.

The figure that his aunt had encountered just now was the Virtuous Immortal who had transformed the previous Hungry Immortal into a heavenly pillar to resist the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation!

"The Immortal Realm is in ruins, and the lower realms will not last long. Someone has to step forward and hold on for everyone, to resist the Dao Annihilation. Why can't it be you?!"

"Sacrifice the individual for the greater good. We survivors will remember you."

The Virtuous Immortal spoke these hypocritical words, and then casually killed the old Hungry Immortal.

What's more, after arriving in the lower realm, he unleashed a world-ending catastrophe.

"With the strength of a Virtuous Immortal, even destroying the lower realms would be as easy as waving a hand. However, he did not act personally, but wrote many True Immortal Seal Scripts and used their power..."

Li Fan frowned slightly.

When one's strength reaches the level of a Virtuous Immortal, they would certainly not do meaningless things.

"It seems it's related to his method of transcendence."

"And..."

With a thought, a statue appeared before Li Fan.

It was the Profound Sky God Statue, buried in the Profound Yellow Realm, beneath the old home of Su Bai.

When Li Fan had carelessly touched it in the past, he had lost his face due to its influence, which was exactly the same as his aunt's encounter.

Li Fan's appearance this time was also due to this reason.

"My previous guess was actually correct."

"Ho Gan Immortal is the Faceless Immortal. And he is also the Virtuous Immortal."

"But..."

Li Fan fell into confusion.

The Faceless Immortal had once saved the life of King Profound Sky, and even maintained contact with him after King Profound Sky returned to the Profound Yellow Realm.

His actions were completely unlike the arbitrary Virtuous Immortal.

Moreover, when Li Fan was a mortal, he had once utilized the immortal power of the Faceless Immortal and successfully escaped under its influence.

If the Faceless Immortal were truly the Virtuous Immortal, with the power he displayed, the Li Fan of that time would have had no chance of escape.

"To find the answer..."

Li Fan looked at the Profound Sky God Statue before him, and sent a wisp of his divine sense into it.

It seemed to have traversed a long stretch of darkness.

"Who?"

A vigilant voice came.

"An old friend of King Profound Sky." Li Fan said casually.

"A friend of Xuanyuan Hong?" The voice on the other side sounded somewhat confused.

"He doesn't know me, but I know him, and I've received his help many times." Li Fan explained. This statement was not a lie.

"I see."

After saying only this, the other side fell silent.

It seemed to be somewhat wary of the suddenly appearing Li Fan.

Li Fan didn't mind and asked, "Your state seems a little off? Do you need help?"

"You? Help?"

"If Xuanyuan Hong is the purest and most sincere person I have ever met, then you are the most evil and wicked person!" The Faceless Immortal coldly sneered.

Hearing this, Li Fan's eyes narrowed slightly.

"It seems you have the ability to discern people's character."

The Faceless Immortal remained silent.

"You say I am the most evil and wicked person, but I disagree. Not to mention the two suppressed in the Eternal Heavenly Steps of the Shore. Just the Virtuous Immortal I know, his actions are no less than mine! I really can't bear the title of most evil and wicked!"

"It seems your divine abilities have not been fully cultivated!" Li Fan smiled.

"..."

Like a stone cast into a calm lake, Li Fan could feel the emotional fluctuations transmitted from the Faceless Immortal.

"So you came to test me."

After a long time, the Faceless Immortal snorted coldly.

"The Virtuous Immortal is long gone."

"If you have any grievances, find him yourself."

"It has nothing to do with me!"

"It has nothing to do with me, what's it to me? You're still not him?" Li Fan said sternly.

"No wonder. Originally, King Profound Sky ordered many statues of you to be erected and worshipped by his followers in gratitude for saving his life. Later, he strictly ordered his subordinates to stop worshipping the Profound Sky God statue..."

"It must be that you discovered that you, your savior, were the culprit responsible for the catastrophe in the lower star sea!" Li Fan mused thoughtfully.

"I said, that's not me!" The Faceless Immortal retorted angrily.

"The Virtuous Immortal is not you, are you the Virtuous Immortal?" Li Fan countered.

"..."

"No." It seemed he hesitated slightly, and the Faceless Immortal paused for a long time before finally answering.

"It seems, friend, you've encountered a problem in your cultivation." Li Fan suddenly realized.

"Friend, you may not know this, but I am adept at the medical principles of heaven and earth. Even incurable diseases in the Mountains and Seas can be treated by me. If you have a problem, feel free to speak. Perhaps I can lend you a hand." Li Fan said very sincerely.

"Heh heh..." The Faceless Immortal certainly wouldn't believe Li Fan's nonsense.

However, for some unknown reason, he still explained: "It's not really a problem with cultivation. It's just an inevitable part of the path to transcendence."

"I was once the renowned [Virtuous Immortal] of the Immortal Realm. The Dao is formless and shapeless, it gives birth to heaven and earth, and the heart is free from defilement. Virtue is encompassing and glorious, cultivating harmony and acting without regret. Dao and Virtue are one, with the mind and nature as the root."

"What I follow is not worldly morality in the usual sense, but the principles circulating in heaven and earth. However..."

The Faceless Immortal sighed with emotion: "The erosion of Dao Annihilation and the collapse of heaven and earth. Even heaven and earth themselves can hardly circulate completely, so the [Virtue] I cultivate naturally developed various loopholes. To repair these loopholes, I began to seek solutions."

"I never expected to embark on an unexpected path."

"Consciousness split and out of control?" Li Fan asked.

"Far more than that. It's that Dao and Virtue have separated." The Faceless Immortal's words were somewhat helpless.

"Dao, Virtue, separated, family?" Li Fan savored these four words carefully.

"I am Virtue, he is Dao. We cannot have both Dao and Virtue, so we parted ways."

"He lost the constraints of Virtue, acted recklessly and without fear. He considered his own actions and thoughts as Virtue, and surprisingly achieved complete Virtue and even advanced further."

"As for me..."

"His actions became my demonic obstacle. Virtue is no longer Virtue, hence the loss of my face."

"I can't even take care of myself, how can I still seek the Dao? Compared to him, I have fallen far behind." The Faceless Immortal said with some melancholy.

Li Fan was not a dull person. With the Faceless Immortal's explanation, he quickly understood.

But recalling his aunt's experience just now, he quickly discovered a flaw in the Virtuous Immortal's possible reasoning.

He couldn't help but laugh heartily: "I think you are trapped in the situation and do not understand it clearly!"

"What do you mean?" The Faceless Immortal asked in surprise.

"Dao and Virtue. Although Dao and Virtue are separated, they are ultimately interdependent. If Virtue is no longer Virtue, then the face is lost. But if Dao loses Virtue, what then?"

"I think, in the end, you still can't escape the fate of being 'faceless'." Li Fan said with a light smile.

"If I'm not mistaken, that Virtuous Immortal should also be looking for you, right?"

The Faceless Immortal remained silent.

Li Fan's heart became even more certain.

"Dao and Virtue separated, perhaps allowing temporary transcendence."

"However, to truly achieve perfection, you two will eventually have to reunite."

Chapter 1627: Intuition Jumps Across Reincarnation

"True perfection..." The Faceless Immortal murmured, unable to hide his longing.

"What you said is indeed reasonable. But now, he is strong and I am weak. If so-called [perfection] truly requires us to merge again, I'm afraid I will be the one being hunted."

"You probably already know this in your heart, which is why you've been hiding." Li Fan's words pierced through the veil of truth.

"As for him being strong and you being weak... You don't need to worry. With my help, that mere Ho Gan Immortal is nothing to fear."

The Faceless Immortal had a clear understanding of the specific strength of his other self. As for Li Fan, they had only communicated remotely through the stone statue of the Faceless Immortal.

Therefore, he still harbored some doubt about Li Fan's confident attitude: "The Virtuous Immortal has long since transcended. What kind of strength and realm do you possess to be so confident?"

Li Fan smiled: "I am merely a minor transcended being. The reason I say he is nothing to fear is not because of me, but because of you."

"Me?" The Faceless Immortal was slightly taken aback.

"To attack the enemy's vital point. With you here, I don't have to search the entire Mountains and Seas for him. I just need to deliberately expose your whereabouts, then set a trap, and wait for the rabbit. By planning with intention while he acts without, we will naturally have the upper hand." Li Fan said indifferently.

"Why would you choose to help me? Are you enemies with him, or is it because of King Profound Sky?" The Faceless Immortal was somewhat confused inside.

"Neither, neither. I simply want to meet this Virtuous Immortal."

Li Fan's answer was somewhat unexpected to the Faceless Immortal, so he fell into a long silence.

"Although he is immoral and lawless, his own flow of virtue approaches perfection. He is extremely sensitive to all disharmonious malevolence in the outside world. Trying to scheme against him... is probably extremely difficult."

"The more information you give me about him, the higher our chances of victory."

Li Fan's words left the Faceless Immortal speechless.

Not agreeing to Li Fan immediately, the Faceless Immortal, after a period of silence, simply replied, "I need to consider it carefully."

"It's fine, I was just struck by a sudden impulse. When you've made up your mind, you can contact me again through this stone statue anytime."

"Oh, and one more thing..." Just as the aura in the stone statue was about to disappear, Li Fan suddenly asked again.
