"Back when the Profound Sky Sect was destroyed and King Profound Sky mysteriously disappeared, the head of your statue in the Profound Sky Sect inexplicably cracked open. Then, the Kui Beast even sent a message towards your location..."

"Do you know what King Profound Sky encountered back then? And what message did he convey to you?" Li Fan's gaze was deep.

The response was a long silence.

"When he encountered danger back then, I did indeed help him. But the one who truly protected him was someone else. As for what he told me..."

"I cannot tell you this." After saying these words, the aura in the Profound Sky stone statue completely disappeared.

Li Fan chuckled: "As expected of the [Virtue] within the [Virtuous Immortal]."

He put away the stone statue of the Faceless Immortal at will. This life was not in a hurry to end the True Reversion. He would see if there was an opportunity to meet that Virtuous Immortal.

"Don't see me, don't see me, don't see me..." The Boundless Wall was still frantically muttering in its heart, praying for Li Fan's departure.

And as if it were meant to be, Li Fan's figure flickered and disappeared.

The Boundless Wall, which had been frozen in fear the moment before, now instantly wrapped around Bai Shuyue's corpse and fled madly towards the high wall.

"I knew I would be able to turn misfortune into fortune in the end."

"But it's really been unlucky recently, encountering dangers repeatedly. It's best to find a safe place and hide for a while."

"When crossing the Star Sea formation, there will be a dual guiding path. Since the Star Sea outside the formation is inaccessible, let's go to another place..." Having made up its mind, the Boundless Wall hurried to escape.

Just as the high wall was in sight, a figure appeared in front of them again, blocking their path.

It was Li Fan again!

The Boundless Wall's heart tightened, and its body abruptly stopped.

"Why did this ominous god come back again?"

"Don't see me, don't see me..."

Having no other way to cope, the Boundless Wall could only brace itself and recite in its heart once more.

However, this time, the incantation was ineffective.

"I'm a little curious why you're so nice to her?"

"You don't seem like the type to give without expecting anything in return. Although her talent is indeed extraordinary, and she has hope of transcending. But that's something that will happen years later. For a hypothetical future, you're even willing to deplete all your accumulated treasures..."

"Could it be that in this short time, you've developed genuine feelings for her?"

Li Fan flicked his finger slightly, and the Boundless Wall fell into his palm.

The "she" in his words naturally referred to Bai Shuyue.

Although the Boundless Wall's own value was no longer considered by Li Fan.

But after seeing the Boundless Wall, upon escaping, still wanting to take his aunt's corpse with it, Li Fan became interested in the Boundless Wall's motivations.

He had long seen through the Boundless Wall's personality.

Under normal circumstances, it would never have put in such a great effort for Bai Shuyue, who was still a mortal. But it did so...

When something unusual happens, there must be a reason.

Although he was asking, Li Fan did not expect the Boundless Wall to answer honestly.

His fingers tightened slightly, and wisps of faint light penetrated into the Boundless Wall.

All of the Boundless Wall's thoughts turned into flowing light, which were then mastered and absorbed by Li Fan.

"Helping her a little will bring ten times the reward in the future. This kind of intuition..." Reading the Boundless Wall's motives, Li Fan's eyebrows couldn't help but lightly raise.

As the manipulator behind the scenes, Li Fan naturally knew that the Boundless Wall's intuition was extremely accurate.

Li Fan, whose intuition for warning was also incredibly accurate, naturally became interested in this kind of "intuition."

"One part of effort, ten parts of reward. It's both accurate and inaccurate. Currently, my aunt's talent is not enough to reach transcendence in this life. Therefore, the probability of her bringing sufficient rewards to the Boundless Wall in this life tends towards zero."

"But the Boundless Wall's intuition is so strong."

"Could it be that its direct foreseen reward is not directed at this life, but rather..."

"Dozens of lives after continuous True Reversion?"

Li Fan's eyes narrowed slightly.

He couldn't help but gently stroke the surface of the Boundless Wall with his hands.

At first glance, this guess might seem absurd.

What right did a mere tile used to build a Dao Palace have to foresee the future after True Reversion?

But...

The reason why Li Fan could think of this wildly was also guided by his own intuition!

Li Fan trusted his intuition implicitly.

"Infinite Spirituality is the fundamental reason for True Reversion attaching itself to me."

"And my intuition is also extraordinary, but I have never found a reasonable explanation."

"This Boundless Wall might be the key to a breakthrough."

"Intuitive warning, to this extent?" Li Fan tapped the Boundless Wall with his fingers continuously, pondering in his heart.

Such spiritual sense seemed extremely rare in the Mountains and Seas.

But perhaps it was just normally imperceptible.

"With the infinity of the Mountains and Seas, it is common for creatures to have moments of inspiration and avoid misfortune by instinct at critical junctures."

"Avoiding misfortune, avoiding misfortune..."

Li Fan suddenly thought of Yin Yuzhen, the shopkeeper of the Heavenly Treasure Pavilion on Glazed Island, whom he had met when he first started cultivating.

Although she was a mortal, she possessed the ability to avoid misfortune and seek good fortune.

It was precisely because she foresaw the infinite benefits of helping Li Fan in the future that she repeatedly gave generously without reservation.

"A mortal body naturally cannot perceive that I possess True Reversion."

"But it can point to my future."

"..."

Li Fan then thought about how, later, when he established the Bright Moon Palace on Bright Moon Lake and lent money extensively to collect contribution points, which eventually attracted the attention of Dao Integration cultivators for cleanup.

Yin Yuzhen had also predicted great fortune at that time.

Later, the Dao Integration cultivators sensed Lan Yu's Devouring Origin Samsara Array and left at the critical moment, sparing everyone's lives.

At that time, Li Fan also thought that this great fortune corresponded to this event.

But...

"Although we narrowly escaped death, we still went through great danger, which can hardly be called great fortune."

"The true great fortune refers to..."

Relying solely on his own thoughts to deduce, he could hardly find an answer.

But if he followed his intuition and reasoned accordingly, Li Fan once again arrived at an unimaginable conclusion.

"This great fortune also points to me!"

"Before this, the Yin sisters were always under my control, being exploited by me. They worked tirelessly every day managing the Bright Moon Palace affairs, and although their cultivation talent gradually improved, they ultimately could not advance further."

"But after this near-death escape..."

"I encountered that Nascent Soul cultivator. Although I defeated the Nascent Soul cultivator with the cultivation of Foundation Establishment, it ultimately ended in mutual destruction, ending that life."

"My death was a great fortune for Yin Yuzhen."

"This is only natural. Just like a bird leaving its cage, or a tiger returning to the mountains. From then on, the sisters were no longer oppressed and enslaved by me."

"But..."

Li Fan was slightly stunned: "After I perform True Reversion, everything in the Mountains and Seas is reset. Everything returns to its starting point."

"Where does the great fortune come from?"

"Am I overthinking it, or..."

As if touching upon the secret of True Reversion, Li Fan's heart involuntarily beat violently.

He re-organized his thoughts from the beginning. Not relying on ordinary logical reasoning, but more on his keen inner intuition. Li Fan arrived at another incredible conclusion again.

When he performed True Reversion, the original possibilities seemed to still exist and continue to develop in the direction of the river of time.

But this deduction was completely contradictory to Li Fan's own experience.

"Why?"

"Does True Reversion reset the Mountains and Seas or not?"

Before this, Li Fan had no doubt about this point.

After all, powerful beings of various possibilities, roaming between the Mountains and Seas, all returned to their initial anchor points with his "True Reversion."

But when his own intuition pointed to a completely opposite conclusion.

Li Fan was somewhat bewildered.

Based on his current understanding of "intuition," he could not explain such a contradiction at all.

"Fortunately, I have discovered the trick."

"It's a pity that the Profound Yellow Realm has already been destroyed in this life, otherwise, I could have captured Yin Yuzhen and studied her carefully."

"This Boundless Wall is also a subject worth paying attention to."

In Li Fan's past reincarnations, there were not many beings with such extremely sharp intuition as him.

The Boundless Wall's own attributes were mediocre, but this intuition was perhaps rare in the Mountains and Seas.

"Do Yin Yuzhen and the Boundless Wall in other possibilities also have this intuition?"

"Or..."

Li Fan's gaze suddenly sharpened.

He had traveled through one percent of the Mountains and Seas, and various possibilities of the Profound Yellow Realm existed in different circumstances.

"Perhaps, in these Profound Yellow Realms, there are no other Yin Yuzhens."

"Just like me."

"The Li Fans in other possibilities are not Li Fan."

"Intuition originates from [Uniqueness of the Mountains and Seas]?" Li Fan's heart stirred.

"The current Mountains and Seas are not complete Mountains and Seas, not the true [Infinity], but a remnant eroded by Dao Annihilation, riddled with holes."

"Theoretically, there are indeed some beings that are unique to the Mountains and Seas."

"This Uniqueness of the Mountains and Seas is similar to the perfect transcendence realm of unifying oneself, but fundamentally different."

"Transcendence is complete because of the Uniqueness of the Mountains and Seas."

"And these special beings are weak because of the Uniqueness of the Mountains and Seas."

"Of course, I am not among them."

"These beings, although destined to have no chance of transcending, have awakened extremely special divine abilities as a blessing in disguise. Perhaps, every perfected transcended expert possesses this ability?" Li Fan did not know.

The most crucial point was that this peculiar intuition sensed the abnormality in the True Reversion cycle.

"It seems that the mechanism of True Reversion is not as simple as I imagined."

"What is true becomes false, and what is false becomes true..."

Li Fan repeated these seven characters internally, concealing his figure, and released his finger from the Boundless Wall.

As if waking from a deep sleep, the Boundless Wall remained stunned for a long time before finally regaining consciousness.

"I'm actually fine? That villain actually let me go?"

The Boundless Wall was stunned for a moment, then overjoyed: "As expected, good fortune favors the lucky!"

Looking around, it found that Bai Shuyue's corpse was still there.

After a pause, its heart became entangled.

Ultimately, it followed its instincts, wrapped Bai Shuyue's corpse, and continued to flee madly towards the high wall.

"There should still be a chance to save her."

Soon, the Boundless Wall, carrying Bai Shuyue, crossed the high wall again.

This time, a radiant green light surged from the Boundless Wall.

Revealing its true form as an immortal artifact, it traversed and arrived at a ruined Ke Dao field!

"Where is this?"

The Boundless Wall scanned its surroundings, somewhat surprised and uncertain.

"It looks somewhat familiar..."

"Fortunately, there seems to be no threat."

Muttering to itself, the Boundless Wall delved deeper into the Ke Dao field.

It arrived at the control center of the Dao field.

Looking at the various objects scattered on the ground, the Boundless Wall identified them carefully and couldn't help but be delighted: "The facilities are actually still in good condition."

A deep green light swept across the surrounding space.

The originally static inanimate objects seemed to come alive,

Presenting phantom images of their past.

"So this is how it's done, and so it's done."

The Boundless Wall recorded the manipulation methods for each object, feeling extremely smug.

"I was chosen by the Saint Monarch, how could I not have some skills!"

Chapter 1628: Mountains and Seas Die and Revive

As the Boundless Wall continued to manipulate, a miraculous sight suddenly appeared on the cylindrical hall walls of the Ke Dao field.

Countless diced blocks stood side by side, coexisting in dark, dim, and flashing states.

In just a moment, the Boundless Wall understood the meaning represented by these different blocks.

"My premonition was correct, there are still so many thriving star seas! I can just hide in any one of them and wait for the wind to pass."

The Boundless Wall's green light swept across the cylindrical hall walls, selecting a suitable target.

Naturally, it also noticed the conspicuous large white circles.

"Drawing a circle to create a prison. It should be for selection and screening. This Dao field was inexplicably abandoned. Could it be that they have already found their target?"

"Regardless, the star seas within the white circles are superior in all conditions to those outside. We should prioritize them."

After careful selection, the Boundless Wall finally chose a peculiar world of Mountains and Seas!

A vast blue ocean, stretching endlessly. The seawater overflowed, occupying the entire star field. And its source was actually a mountain peak no bigger than a palm.

Spring water flowed down from the summit, continuously flowing day and night, turning into a star sea!

"Although this Mountains and Seas is not *that* Mountains and Seas, its shape, image, and essence coincide with the Mountains and Seas, so it must have its unspeakable profoundness."

"Moreover, this spring of life on the mountain peak might be able to bring the young lady back to life!"

The Boundless Wall transformed into a streak of green light and entered it.

It arrived directly at the summit.

From the outside, the mountain in the Star Sea world appeared to be merely a rather low peak. However, upon entering the realm, one discovered that this mountain was actually over ten million feet tall.

It was just that apart from the vast blue ocean covering the star field, there were no other reference points, which made the mountain appear short.

The mountain was not short, and the water was naturally not simple stream water.

It was like a great river or ocean, rumbling and roaring, emitting a deafening sound like thunder.

It wasn't just a simple sound, but it was accompanied by the rhythm of this star field's Great Dao.

Even the Boundless Wall, as it passed through, was inevitably affected. The sound and water rhythms were like carving knives, trying to etch marks on the surface of the Boundless Wall.

A faint light flashed, and the Boundless Wall blocked all anomalies, continuing to fly towards the summit.

"Strange, I was clearly flying directly towards the summit, but I landed halfway up..."

"Could it be that I've been damaged too severely, and can't even grasp this bit of precision?"

The Boundless Wall, climbing slowly, fell into a brief period of self-doubt.

However, after flying towards the summit for a while longer, it finally realized: "This mountain peak is actually inhabited?!"

The Boundless Wall's flight abruptly halted. Amidst the roar of the cascading spring water, it hesitated for a long time. Finally, the Boundless Wall gritted its teeth and decided to continue.

"In front of the Saint Monarch, I borrow this treasure land. I believe the owner of this place will not blame me."

The Boundless Wall's vision was extraordinary, and it could naturally discern the sophistication of the formation that had silently repelled it, capable of astonishing the summit.

"Although not transcended, at least it's a strong individual with no name. What a hell, even when the Immortal Realm still existed, there weren't many experts of this level. How is it that after the destruction of the Immortal Realm, this corner of the lower realm is full of them!" The Boundless Wall felt depressed in its heart.

"However... there should be no great risk."

While flying and observing, the Boundless Wall finally reached a conclusion.

Its intuition was indeed very accurate.

For nine consecutive times, the Boundless Wall was repelled, but it persisted relentlessly and continued to ascend.

On the tenth attempt, the formation finally ceased to activate.

The Boundless Wall was thus able to bring Bai Shuyue to the summit.

"Such vigorous life force..." The Boundless Wall looked at a small spring eye ahead, which was the source of the ocean covering this world, and was awed by the vast life force contained within.

At the same time, it did not forget to throw Bai Shuyue's corpse onto it.

The corpse blocked the spring eye. The surging water flow gradually weakened, and the roaring sound of the water subsided.

When the Star Sea world that formed its own cycle finally fell into silence, no more spring water flowed from the mountain peak.

The cycle of Mountains and Seas that was self-contained was broken. The vast life force that was originally concentrated in the Mountains and Seas now slowly focused on Bai Shuyue's corpse.

A mere mortal corpse should not be able to suppress the spring eye of the Mountains and Seas world.

Seeing Bai Shuyue's corpse, which could be washed away by the spring water at any moment, the Boundless Wall revealed its original form.

It gently pressed down on it.

A divine stone fell, and the Mountains and Seas were suppressed.

With Bai Shuyue's corpse as the core of the cycle, this Star Sea world entered a new balance.

"Sigh, I hope this works."

The Boundless Wall felt the changes in Bai Shuyue's body under the impact of the vast life force.

"Hmm, it's good that I came in time, she wasn't completely dead yet."

"In a hundred years, she should be able to come back to life."

"It's a pity that I, this great master, can't get half the benefits from this spring of life. Little lady, when you become successful in the future, don't forget me!" The Boundless Wall kept muttering.

The Boundless Wall did not notice that the moment it and Bai Shuyue occupied the spring eye at the summit, a divine sense had already noticed them.

Naturally, it was the owner of this Mountains and Seas world, the disciple appointed by Duke Shou Qiu, Cheng Dao.

However, Cheng Dao had already left the Star Sea and was outside the high wall. He had no intention of occupying the sacred land that had nurtured his consciousness. Since another fated person had found it, and it was for saving a life, Cheng Dao did not drive them away.

Of course, if it were ordinary mortal objects, Cheng Dao would definitely not be so polite.

The most crucial point was that Cheng Dao sensed the aura from the Immortal Realm's Saint Monarch on the Boundless Wall.

Cheng Dao was a disciple of Duke Shou Qiu. The other party was from before the Saint Monarch's gate.

Naturally, he would give some face.

The phrase "before the Saint Monarch's gate" was sometimes worthless, and sometimes worth a thousand pieces of gold!

In addition to considering the other party's origin, as the one guarding the back of the Star Sea Dao Net, Cheng Dao also discovered that the Boundless Wall currently appearing in the Mountains and Seas was an immortal artifact that had suddenly appeared in the Dao Net not long ago and then suddenly disappeared after being captured.

According to the residual fluctuations of the Dao Net at that time, Cheng Dao found that the person behind the scenes who helped the Boundless Wall escape at that time was actually not weaker than himself.

Since they possessed such strength, it was natural to resolve enmity rather than forge it.

Cheng Dao had always been principled.

...

Bai Shuyue lay quietly in the Star Sea world for more than fifty years, and her life force gradually recovered.

However, the Boundless Wall, which had witnessed all the changes from life and death, discovered something strange.

"Life force has slightly recovered, and consciousness has been reborn from dissipation."

"But..."

"After experiencing this life and death tribulation, her ignorant consciousness has not shown the slightest fear?"

The Boundless Wall gasped.

One must know that to have experienced life and death and yet not fear it is truly rare in ancient times.

"Coupled with her almost heaven-defying talent..."

"My premonition was indeed correct!"

"Transcendence is within reach!"

Chapter 1629: He Ganxian's Cultivation

Just as Bai Shuyue was gradually coming back to life, Li Fan finally received the reply from the Faceless Immortal.

"The Virtuous Immortal is planning something extremely important."

"If this matter can be prevented, it might be possible to somewhat reverse the power gap between him and me."

The "him" referred to in the words was naturally the "Dao" part of the Virtuous Immortal, Ho Gan Immortal.

The Faceless Immortal was truly cautious. After more than fifty years of consideration, he still had no intention of revealing himself. Instead, he waited for a good opportunity, to test Li Fan's "sincerity" without revealing himself.

Li Fan's original goal was to meet Ho Gan Immortal, so he didn't care and directly asked about this so-called "good opportunity."

"The Virtuous Immortal... Ho Gan Immortal acts according to his whims. He has no virtue, so everything he thinks and does is attributed to virtue." Perhaps because he felt that the name Li Fan had given to his other self was more fitting, the Faceless Immortal simply changed his address.

"Although to others, and even to me, Ho Gan Immortal's actions seem shocking and go against conscience, in his own eyes, what he does is incomparably correct and unquestionable."

"Ho Gan Immortal's understanding of this concept is supported by a self-consistent logic. Note that Ho Gan Immortal does not think he is truly without virtue. He actually has virtue, but this virtue is contrary to the common understanding and only exists within his own cognition."

"For so many years, no outsider has broken this cognition. He acts according to what he believes is correct, and his flow of virtue becomes stronger, continuing to practice his own ideals. For so many years, Ho Gan Immortal has been repeating this cycle, growing stronger like a snowball."

"But now, there is the best opportunity to subvert his cognition!"

The Faceless Immortal spoke eloquently.

Sensing the faint fluctuations coming from the Profound Sky stone statue, Li Fan pondered, interrupted the Faceless Immortal, and said: "You can actually perceive Ho Gan Immortal's specific movements? It seems I underestimated you before."

"Ho Gan Immortal is not without virtue, and the Faceless Immortal is not without Dao. You two are quite interesting."

"I said earlier that Dao and Virtue separating is not as simple as splitting into two. The intricacies can only be known by ourselves. It is truly not worth mentioning to outsiders." The Faceless Immortal gave a perfunctory explanation and then detailed the great opportunity to intercept Ho Gan Immortal.

It actually touched upon the most fundamental core of Ho Gan Immortal's own moral concept.

"The reason Ho Gan Immortal believes himself to have virtue is that in his eyes, he is the only one who can save the Mountains and Seas. Therefore, all other beings in the Mountains and Seas must yield to his survival, even if it means sacrificing them. It is only right and proper."

"Therefore, he can righteously destroy an entire possibility just for a minuscule improvement in his own strength."

Hearing the Faceless Immortal's words, Li Fan's heart stirred, and a thought flashed through his mind. His eyes narrowed slightly.

However, he did not show it on the surface, merely letting the Faceless Immortal continue.

"The foundation of all his actions is built upon his ultimate salvation of the Mountains and Seas. If this fantasy can be shattered, it will sever his self-circulation of virtue. Even without us taking action, as time passes, his strength will only continue to decline."

"Currently, he is creating boundless slaughter in another possibility within the Mountains and Seas, just to increase his strength again. If he is defeated at this time, causing him to lose his inexplicable confidence, he will be utterly demoralized!"

Li Fan keenly sensed the key point in the Faceless Immortal's words: "At this time... meaning, even if he is defeated normally, it won't shake his self-concept. It must be at a critical moment. So, is he comprehending the Dao now?"

"That's right! Rather than comprehending the Dao, it's more accurate to say he's [cultivating]. Ho Gan Immortal's cultivation method is different from ordinary people. Although he has found an excuse for slaughtering all living beings, saying it's all for the ultimate salvation of the Mountains and Seas, in his heart, he still retains some correct conscience. He knows that what he's doing goes against human ethics. He needs to diminish the influence of his remaining correct conscience on himself while his strength grows."

"Specifically, he deliberately creates a karmic debt of slaughter. When his remaining conscience feels the karma he has created, he will feel guilt and sorrow, and may even enter a state of temporary loss of control."

"But after Ho Gan Immortal suppresses these negative emotions, he can regain his sanity. And the remaining conscience will be consumed. When all conscience is gone, he will have no more flaws. And now, after these years of cultivation, he has very little conscience left."

"Every cultivation is the best opportunity to stop him. I've tried to intervene before, but unfortunately, the power gap was too great..."

"You might as well go and investigate this possibility."

The Faceless Immortal sent a coordinate for a location in the Mountains and Seas, and then his aura completely disappeared.

Perhaps it was to avoid something, he was extremely cautious.

"These two..."

"One Dao, one Virtue."

After thinking for a moment, Li Fan followed the Faceless Immortal's guidance, leaped up, and left the Primordial Possibility.

Heading towards the Mountains and Seas to find his whereabouts.

It was quite far from the Primordial.

Fortunately, in the Mountains and Seas, there was no concept of time passage.

When Li Fan arrived at the destination possibility, he saw a scene of doomsday.

Ho Gan Immortal stood in the center of the shattered star sea, laughing maniacally: "What does it have to do with me, what does it have to do with me!"

He was indifferent to the countless beings perishing around him.

Li Fan could vaguely see that while saying these words, his face indeed showed signs of grief.

It appeared extremely contradictory.

But his body remained unmoving.

Watching the star sea, and even the possibility, being destroyed.

Tears gradually dried, and his expression slowly became resolute.

Even somewhat sinister.

All beings were fleeing and crying out in despair.

Li Fan, who suddenly appeared and was extremely calm at this moment, was extremely conspicuous.

Instantly, Ho Gan Immortal's gaze locked onto Li Fan.

Without any wasted words, his cold gaze directly locked onto Li Fan: "Die!"

In Li Fan's ears, it seemed to be the sound of a wooden door closing, "creak."

It was not an auditory hallucination, but the sound of the collapse of the Heavenly Emperor caused by too many pillars of the Great Dao collapsing simultaneously!

Along with the destruction of the possibility, came the Dao Annihilation tribulation like waves.

The possibility, which was already in a state of doomsday, was completely destroyed by Li Fan's appearance.

Li Fan, naturally, would not feel any self-reproach for this.

Instead, he let out a soft exclamation: "Well done!"
